Omwanzo, Nluku aphattucha pinku na vathi.
Olumwenku waari ohineeyane matthentto na khayaarimo hatha etthu, yaarivo yiizaru vatulu wa pahari yawiicha. Rooho ya Nluku yaari ozukulela vatulu wa maati.
Aphano Nluku khuri: “Yiiyevo nuuru!” Khwiiyavo.
Nluku khoona yoori nuuru yaari yooshapweya; khuvalula nuuru na yiiza.
Nuuru khutthaja “nthana”, yiiza khutthaja “osikhu”. Khuripa khucha, siikhu yamwanzo.
Aphano Nluku khulupa theenya yoori: “Wiiyevo mwaawanyo vakatthi wa maati onvalulaaye maati na maati!”
Nluku khuretta mwaawanyo ovaluliyeeyo maati vathi na vatulu. Khurettikhana etthiipo.
Mwaawanyo opule, Nluku khutthaja “pinku”. Khuripa khucha, siikhu yaphiiri.
Nluku khuri: “Akusanyeye maati apa ari vathi wa pinku vahali vamote epuwe tuulu yawuuma!” Khurettikhana etthiipo.
Tuulu yaya ethiito yawuuma khutthaja nzina la “tuniya”, maati apale aakusanyeyiyeeyo khutthaja n zina la “pahari”. Nluku khoona yoori pi zooshapweya.
Nluku khulupa theenya yoori: “Tuniya yootthele tthuttu: waaza nyaani ziniimaaye peewu na miitthi ziniimaaye mishumo, wakhula nshumo na phunje yaya!” Khurettikhana etthiipo.
Tuniya khootthela tthuttu: nyaani ziniimaaye peewu, miitthi ziniimaaye mishumo. Nluku khoona yoori pi zooshapweya.
Khuripa khucha, siikhu yattaatthu.
Aphano Nluku khuri: “Otulu ziiyewo vimwasikhelo yoori ovaluleye nthana na osikhu! Ziiye alama zinthoonyezaaye elimwe na mwiita, siikhu na nyaakha.
Vimwasikhelo ziriiye otulu ziiye zoomwasikhela vathi.” Khurettikhana etthiipo.
Nluku khuphattucha vimwasikhelo piiri khuulu. Emwasikhelo eti khuulu yaya yoori esala elokozela nthana, eti ttiitthi esala elokozela osikhu. Na theenya khuphattucha matthottowa.
Nluku khutthaawo vimwasikhelo epile otulu yoori zisala zimwasikhela vathi,
na olokozela nthana na osikhu, zaawanye nuuru na yiiza. Khoona yoori pi zooshapweya.
Khuripa khucha, siikhu yanne.
Aphano Nluku khuri: “Mpahari ziiyemo zumpe za waatta za wiiyana ohaayi, na eeyevo anyannyi anvavaaye otulu!”
Nluku khumpa zumpe z'oohaayi khuluzeene za mpahari, na jaati zooshi za zumpe zineettettaaye na ziniitaalaaye mpahari. Khumpa theenya jaati zooshi za anyannyi. Nluku khoona yoori pi zooshapweya.
Nluku khuparikhiya araka: “Mwittheerelane mwaattelane, mwiitaale mpahari, na anyannyi aattelane vatuniya!”
Khuripa khucha, siikhu yathaanu.
Aphano Nluku khuri: “Ziiyemo ntuniya jaati zooshi za zumpe za wiiyana ohaayi, nyama za ntthuttu, mifuwo za vaje na nyama zoojipurula!” Khurettikhana etthiipo.
Nluku khumpa nyama za ntthuttu za wakhula jaati, zoojipurula za wakhula jaati, na mifuwo za wakhula jaati. Khoona yoori pi zooshapweya.
Nluku khulupa theenya yoori: “Nimumpe pinaatamu woonishapihi wa wiiya nkhama Fweeyo! Yoori eeyane owahi wooshintta swi za mpahari na anyannyi o'otulu; mifuwo za vaje na nyama za ntthuttu mpakha nyama zooshi zinjipurulaaye vathi.”
Aphano Nluku khumumpa pinaatamu wa wiiya nkhama Ye; nlume na muukha ompiwa ti Ye.
Nluku khuwaaparikhiya khuwooza yoori: “Mwivokolelane, mwaattelane mwiitaale voolumwenku! Mwiiyane oshintta vatuniya, swi za mpahari, anyannyi o'otulu na nyama zooshi zineettettaaye vathi!”
Nluku khulupa theenya araka: “Yoori mweeyo mwiiyane etthu-yooja, kiniwinkhani nyaani zooshi za ntuniya ziniimaaye peewu, miitthi zooshi ziniimaaye mishumo na phunje zaya.
Kininkha mathapa ooshi nkhama vitthu-zooja za nyama zooshi ziriina ohaayi: anyannyi ooshi o'otulu na nyama zooshi mpakha epile zinjipurulaaye vathi.” Khurettikhana etthiipo.
Nluku khoona yoori pi zooshapweya channu. Khuripa khucha, siikhu yasiitha.
Ti nanna yiishisiweezo ophattuchiwa pinku na vathi na zooshi ziriimo.
Nluku amarisiyeevo khaazi yawe, siikhu yasaapa khuvumula.
Siikhu ethiito yasaapa, Nluku khuparikhiya na khuttakatthisa mwaasa woovumula khwa khaazi yawe aakholiyeeyo yoophattucha.
Eti hatiithi yoophattuchiwa pinku na vathi. Siikhu Mbwana Nnyizinku aphattuchiyeevo pinku na vathi,
vatuniya khawaarivo hatha muutthi wala nyaani zaari zihinootthe, maana Mbwana Nnyizinku aari ahinanyisele vuula vathi na khaarivo hatha ntthu woolima tuniya.
Ila maati aari opuwa vathi khusala anaanisa tuniya yooshi.
Aphano, Nnyizinku khumumpa pinaatamu khwa ottophe wa vathi. Khunvitelela mphula mwawe khumwinkha phuumu y'oohaayi, pinaatamu khwiiya yumpe haayi.
Mbwana Nnyizinku khuzala woorotha nti wa Eeteni, phantte y'ookhu lintthamuwaawo njuwa, khuntthaamo pinaatamu otule aamumpiyeeyo.
Mbwana Nnyizinku khootthisa miitthi za wakhula nanna, zooshapweya woona na zootuva oja mishumo zaya. Vakatthi wa woorotha khuzalavo muutthi woohaayi, na muutthi onjuwisaaye yooshapweya na yootakhala.
N'Eeteni nttumpho waarimo muuttho waari okhuwaraaye woorotha opule; muuttho otthuupo khwaawanyeya khupuwavo nyuuttho mine.
Wamwanzo oniitthiwa Pishoni, opo wazukulela nti wooshi wa Havila, ohali wa waattawo thahapu.
Thahapu za nti opo pi zooshapweya na theenya ewaakho miitthi enlazaaye manlela oonukhela na mawe ootafikhana.
Muuttho opu waphiiri oniitthiwa Kihoni, ozukuleliyeeyo nti wooshi wa Kuushi.
Muuttho opo wattaatthu, onviraaye phantte lintthamuwaawo njuwa ya nti wa Shuuru, oniitthiwa Tiikiri. Opu wanne Efwarathi.
Mbwana Nnyizinku khunthuula pinaatamu otule khunttha nwoorotha wa Eeteni yoori asala alimela na weekesela.
Mbwana Nnyizinku khunruma pinaatamu otule yoori: “Miitthi epi ziriiye nwoorotha mphu oje mishumo zaya woohiina hatha shaakha.
Ila muutthi opo woojuwisa yooshapweya na yootakhala ohije; siikhu onttelaaye oja satakithu ontta ofwa.”
Aphano Mbwana Nnyizinku khuri: “Khahi yooshapweya pinaatamu wiiya otthwe, kintta omumpa pinaatamu wa wiiya nkhama ye asala ankhiza.”
Paata ya Mbwana Nnyizinku wumpa khwa ottophe wa vathi nyama zooshi za ntthuttu na anyannyi apa o'otulu, zooshi khuntiisela Adamu yoori amoone nanna aari weettelaazo otthaja; wakhula yumpe aari otthajaaye, nzina laya laari wiiya nttinttho.
Adamu khutthaja mazina mifuwo za vaje, anyannyi o'otulu na nyama zooshi za ntthuttu. Ila khuhipuwivo hatha moote ya wiiya nkhama ye yaari weettelaaye onkhiza.
Aphano, Mbwana Nnyizinku khuntiisela Adamu osikizi wa waatta. Eettaka olala, khunlaza likhonkolo limote la pavu yawe, aphale vaya aalaziyeevo khuttiyavo na nyama.
Likhonkolo limote la pavu anlaziyeeyo Adamu, Mbwana Nnyizinku khumumpa muukha, khumwinkha Adamu.
Ye khuri: “Ahee! Ntthi likhonkolo la likhonkolo laka na nyama ya nyama yaka. Nka eetthiwaka oriwa muukha, maana alaziwa vamwiili wanlume.”
Ti eto nlume oninlikha papaawe na mamaawe khukusanyeya na muukhaawe oowiiri khwiiya nyama moote.
Oowiiri, Adamu na muukhaawe aari wiiya waazu woohiina haaya.
Nyookha yaari nlavilavi zayita nyama zooshi za ntthuttu Mbwana Nnyizinku ompiyeeyo. Khumuuzela muukha eraka: “Atthi Nluku alupa yoori mwihije mishumo za miitthi zooshi ziriiye nwoorotha mphu?”
Muukha otule khujipu yoori: “Ninaaye ruhusa yooja mishumo za miitthi ziriiye nwoorotha mphu,
ila Nluku anuuza yoori: ‘Nshumo wa muutthi oriiye vakatthi wa woorotha mwihije wala mwihisape. Mwijaru mwintta ofwa.’”
Aphano nyookha khumuuza muukha otule yoori: “Hatha khamwimfwa!
Maana Nluku ajuwa yoori siikhu mwinttelaavo oja nshumo opo antta ofunuwa maasho enu, mweeyo mwinttela wiiya nkhama Ye, ojuwa yooshapweya na yootakhala.”
Muukha khoona yoori muutthi opule waari wooshapweya, mishumo zaya zaari zooshapweyela oja na zaarina fwayita yoojuwisa. Attaapho, khushuma khuja, khumwinkha mannawe na-ye khuja.
Paata ya toowo, oowiiri khufunuwa maasho aya khujuwa yoori ari waazu. Khurukela mathapa a muutthi oniitthiwaaye mfikeera khuretta wiiya kuwo zaya.
N'oosiila shintto ya Mbwana Nnyizinku eettettaka nwoorotha mphule, wakathi wa pheevo ya matulayi njuwa-looveva, pinaatamu na muukhaawe khujivitha na miitthi nwoorotha nttumphule yoori Mbwana Nnyizinku ahiwoone.
Mbwana Nnyizinku khunkhuwela pinaatamu khumuuzela yoori: “Ori vayi?”
Ye khujipu araka: “Keetta osiila shintto yawo nwoorotha mphu, miiyo khoova na khujivitha mwaasa wa wiiya waazu.”
Mbwana Nnyizinku khumuuzela theenya yoori: “Wooziwa paani yoori ori waazu? Nshumo wa muutthi opule kookhattaziyeeyo yoori ohije weetta oja?”
Pinaatamu khujipu yoori: “Muukha otu okinkhiyeeyo yoori asala akikhiza, ti ye akinkhiyeeyo nshumo aya opo miiyo khuja.”
Mbwana Nnyizinku khumuuzela muukha araka: “Niini eto orettiyeeyo?” Muukha khujipu yoori: “Nyookha ti ye ekittettekhiyeeyo miiyo khuja.”
Aphano Mbwana Nnyizinku khuuza nyookha yoori: “Wiiya waretta vitthu epi, woolaanikha ti weyo vakatthi wa mifuwo za vaje na nyama zooshi za ntthuttu, nka weettettanaka erukulu na ojaka ottophe siikhu zooshi z'oohaayi awo.
Kinttela otthaavo wuumani weeyo na muukha; peewu yawo na peewu ya muukha. Peewu ya muukha nka yuuvulalisaka eeshwa yawo, na weeyo nka ottovolaka ekwakuno yaya.”
Mbwana Nnyizinku khumuuza muukha yoori: “Kintta ozitisa thwaapu yawo amana wiimittha ompatthaka mwaana. Weeyo onlawa watakhe onlokozela mannawo, ila mannawo onlawa ooshintte.”
Ye khumuuza Pinaatamu yoori: “Wiiya wansiileza muukhaawo khuja nshumo wa muutthi opu kookhattaziyeeyo, yalaanikha tuniya yooshi mwaasa wa weeyo, nka okholaka khaazi yoolipa yoori opatthe etthu-yooja ohaayi awo wooshi.
Tuniya eniwinkha wakhula nanna ya miiwa, weeyo nka ojaka mishumo za ntthuttu.
Okholaka khaazi yoovujuwela yoori opatthe etthu-yooja yawo mansha awo ooshi. Maana weeyo wompaniwa ottophe, n'oofwa mpakha orutele voottophe.”
Pinaatamu khuntthaja muukhaawe nzina la Haawa, mwaasa wa wiiya maama wa anaatamu ooshi.
Mbwana Nnyizinku khwaattala kuwo za shapala khunwalisa pinaatamu na muukhaawe.
Mbwana Nnyizinku khuri: “Mpakha apha pinaatamu wampattha wiiya nkhama fweeyo, ajuwa etthu yooshapweya na yootakhala. Ye ahilikheleliwe oshuma nshumo wa muutthi w'oohaayi aja yoori eeyane ohaayi wa mileele.”
Paata ya toowo, Mbwana Nnyizinku khumwiikaramo nwoorotha wa Eeteni, yoori asala alima ottophe otthuupule ompaniweeyo.
N'oomwiikaramo pinaatamu nwoorotha phantte lintthamuwaawo njuwa ya Eeteni, khutthaamo kerupiina na phanka ya moottho yaari ozukulelaaye. Ye aarettiye toowo yoori esala yeekesela tarikhi yaari weettaaye okhule oriiwo muutthi w'oohaayi.
Adamu khurapalelana muukhaawe Haawa, khwiimittha khumpattha mwaana khuntthaja nzina la Kayiini. Ye khulupa yoori: “Khwa otakha wa Nnyizinku kampattha mwaana wanlume.”
Khwiimittha theenya khumpattha mwaana nkina wanlume, ttwiiye Kayiini. Khuntthaja nzina la Apeele. Apeele khwiiya makhampuzi wa pwittipwitthi, Kayiini khwiiya namalima.
Siikhu moote, Kayiini khutiisa mishumo za mmashapa oteela omwinkha zaakha Nnyizinku.
Apeele na-ye zwaamu yawe khutiisa pwittipwitthi etile yaari yamwanzo ottheeriwa ya nliphanko mwawe, khushija khuthawula phantte epile zoosamini waya oteela omwinkha zaakha Nnyizinku, Ye khwiiya wootuveliwa ti Apeele na zaakha yawe.
Ila Kayiini na zaakha yawe etile aatiisiyeeyo, Nnyizinku khuhituveliwi. Kayiini khukatipukha khujiinamela.
Nnyizinku khumuuzela araka: “Wakatipukhela-ni khujiinamela?
Amana weeyo weettetta saana akinuukhupalela? Ila amana weeyo oheettetti saana, ojuwe yoori twampi eri vanlako entta wuuwejela yoori ewiirukhele yuushintte. Weeyo enuuhithajiya oshintta twampi yaya eto.”
Aphano Kayiini khumuuza ttwiiye Apeele yoori: “Nlawe ntthuttu.” N'oofiya khunzukuluwela khumuula.
Paata ya toole, Nnyizinku khumuuzela Kayiini araka: “Ttwiiyo Apeele ori vayi?” Khujipu yoori: “Akijuweeni! Namweekesela wa ttwiiyaku ti miyo?”
Nnyizinku khumuuzela theenya araka: “Warettela-ni etthu nkhama eti? Huula ya taamu ya ttwiiyo entta okikhuwela vathi.
Nasaapi ethiiti, woolaanikha ti weyo vatuniya ethiito enywiiyeeyo taamu ya ttwiiyo.
Amana weeyo olima nka ohiruweraka. Vatuniya weeyo nka weettaka ojeettettela nkhama ntthu wootthira.”
Kayiini khumuuza Nnyizinku yoori: “Hukhumu yaka khuluyeene channu akinkhitiri.
Leelo wakiikara vatuniya apha yoori kihiiye vamote na-weyo, miiyo kinttela ojeettettela nkhama namatthira vatuniya na wakhula anttelaaye okisikana ontta okuula.”
Nnyizinku khunjipu yoori: “Wala! Khahiyo toowo! Wakhula otule anttelaaye owuula oniiya woohukhumwiwa swaafu sapa.” Ye khunttha alama vamwiili yoori wakhula aninsikanaaye ahimuule.
Aphano Kayiini khwumwazeyanana Nnyizinku khulawa khwiikhala nti wa Nooti, okhu lintthamuwaawo njuwa phantte ya Eeteni.
Ye khurapalelana muukhaawe, khwiimittha khumpattha mwanawe Enookhi. Kayiini khujeka sitati khutthaja nzina nttintthile la mwanawe Enookhi.
Enookhi khunvokola Eraati, Eraati khunvokola Mehuyayele, Mehuyayele khunvokola Lameekhi
Lameekhi khuwaarala aakha awiri, mmote nzina lawe laari Aada. Otu nkina lawe laari Siila.
Aada khumpattha mwanawe khuntthaja nzina la Yapaali, paapa wa atthu apale aari wiikhalaaye mmaheema aari ofuwaaye nyama.
Ttwiiye nzina lawe laari Yupaali, oto aari paapa wa atthu apale ooshi animpiyaaye tthakare na apale ampiyaaye phivi.
Siila khumpattha mwaana khuntthaja nzina la Tupaali-Kayiini, ye aari funti wa waattala zaana za khoopiri na zuuma. Tupaali-Kayiini aarina nlupuwe aari wiitthiwaaye Naama.
Lameekhi khuwooza aakhaawe yoori: “Aada na Siila! Mwikisiileze aakhaaka: Kamuula ntthu mwaasa wookivulalisa, na shapu mmote mwaasa wookiluwattha.
Amana Kayiini ariphiwa hukhumu swaafu sapa, Lameekhi onttela oriphiwa swaafu sapiini na sapa.”
Adamu khurapalelana muukhaawe theenya khumpattha mwaana khuntthaja nzina la Seethi, Haawa khuri: “Nnyizinku akinkha mwaana nkinoko wonriphelavo Apeele otule ooliweeyo ti Kayiini.”
Seethi na-ye khumpattha mwaana khuntthaja nzina la Enooshi. Wakathi aya otthuupo phi laaziyeevo waaputwiwa nzina la Nnyizinku.
Eti warakha yoovokola wa peewu ya Adamu. Wakathi Nluku amumpiyeeyo pinaatamu, aamumpiye wa wiiya nkhama ye;
nlume na muukha ti ye awompiyeeyo. N'oowompa khuwaaparikhiya. Khuwaatthaja nzina la “anaatamu”.
Adamu afiiyeevo nyaakha miiya na talaathiini khumpattha mwaana wa wiiya nkhama ye na khwa wumpo awe khuntthaja nzina la Seethi.
Paata yonvokola Seethi, Adamu khwiikhala theenya nyaakha miiya naane khuwaapattha aana a waatta aalume na aakha.
Adamu afwa arina nyaakha miiya tiisiya na talaathiini.
Seethi afiiyeevo nyaakha miiya na mithaanu, khunvokola Enooshi.
Paata yonvokola Enooshi, Seethi khwiikhala theenya nyaakha miiya naane na sapa khuwaapattha aana akina aalume na aakha.
Seethi afwa arina nyaakha miiya tiisiya na khumi na miwiri.
Enooshi afiiyeevo nyaakha tiisiini, khunvokola Kenaani.
Paata yonvokola Kenaani, Enooshi khwiikhala theenya nyaakha miiya naane na khumi na mithaanu, khuwaapattha aana akina aalume na aakha.
Enooshi afwa arina nyaakha miiya tiisiya na mithaanu.
Kenaani afiiyeevo nyaakha sapiini, khunvokola Mahalaleeli.
Paata yonvokola Mahalaleeli, Kenaani khwiikhala theenya nyaakha miiya naane na arupayiini, khuwaapattha aana akina aalume na aakha.
Kenaani afwa arina nyaakha miiya tiisiya na khumi.
Mahalaleeli afiiyeevo nyaakha siithiini na mithaanu, khumpattha mwaana khuntthaja nzina la Yareeti.
Paata yonvokola Yareeti, Mahalaleeli khwiikhala nyaakha miiya naane na talaathiini khuwaapattha aana akina aakha na aalume.
Mahalaleeli afwa arina nyaakha miiya naane na tiisiini na mithaanu.
Yareeti afiiyeevo nyaakha miiya na siithiini na miwiri, khumpattha mwaana khuntthaja nzina la Henookhi.
Paata yonvokola Henookhi, Yareeti khwiikhala nyaakha miiya naane, khuwaapattha aana akina aalume na aakha.
Yareeti afwa arina nyaakha miiya tiisiya na siithiini na miwiri.
Henookhi afiiyeevo nyaakha siithiini na mithaanu, khumpattha mwaana khuntthaja nzina la Methuseela.
Paata yonvokola Methuseela, Henookhi khulotta mwentto wa Nnyizinku nyaakha miiya ttatthu, khuwaapattha aana akina aalume na aakha.
Ye eekhaliye nyaakha miiya ttatthu na siithiini na mithaanu.
Henookhi aarina osiilana nwulweene na Nluku. Ye eettiye woophaziwa ti Nluku.
Methuseela afiiyeevo nyaakha miiya na thamaaniini na sapa, khunvokola Lameekhi.
Paata yonvokola Lameekhi, Methuseela khwiikhala nyaakha miiya sapa na thamaaniini na miwiri, khuwaapattha aana akina aalume na aakha.
Methuseela afwa arina nyaakha miiya tiisiya na siithiini na tiisiya.
Lameekhi afiiyeevo nyaakha miiya na thamaaniini na miwiri khumpattha mwaana mmote.
Mwaana otule mmote ampatthiyeeyo khuntthaja nzina la Nuuhi, ye khulupa yoori: “Khwa khaazi zoolwaaza ninkholaazo nilimaka tuniya eti elaaniweeyo ti Nnyizinku, mwaana otu ti ye anttela wiitthaaza rooho zetthu.”
Paata yonvokola Nuuhi, Lameekhi khwiikhala theenya nyaakha miiya thaanu na tiisiini na mithaanu, khuwaapattha aana akina aalume na aakha.
Lameekhi afwa arina nyaakha miiya sapa na sapiini na sapa.
Nuuhi eekhaliye nyaakha miiya thaanu khuwaapattha aana aalume khuwaatthaja mazina: Sheemu, Haamu na Yafeeti.
Wakathi anaatamu aaziyeevo waattelana muulumwenku na khuwaavokola aana aakha,
mahaakhimu khuwoona yoori aakha apale aari ooshapweya, wakhula mmote wa yo khusala awaathuula apale aari owaatakhaaye.
Aphano Nnyizinku khuri: “Akinteela onlikhela pinaatamu phuumu z'oohaayi khwa mileele, maana ye nyama ya taamu; siikhu zawe enttela wiiya nyaakha miiya na eshiriini.”
Wakathi aya opo muulumwenku aarimo atthu awulu-awulu na oozivala, aruteliye wiiyavo theenya. Aari aana aalume aavokoliweeyo pi mahaakhimu n'oorapalelana aana aakha a anaatamu. Aana atthaapo, pa yo aari atthu oozivala na ootafikhana.
Nnyizinku khoona yoori vatuniya zootakhala za anaatamu zeetta ovira zeekezeleyaka; Menttezi aya ooshi aari ooretta vitthu zootakhala wakhula siikhu.
Aphano Nnyizinku khukasirikha mwaasa woomumpa pinaatamu vatuniya, khwiiya woolemeliwa nroho mwawe.
Khuri: “Kintta owaafujavo anaatamu aya apa kiwompiyeeyo voolumwenku apha; waaza anaatamu, nyama, anyanyama, na anyannyi o'otulu, kiwookasirikha mwaasa woowumpa.”
Ila Nuuhi khwiiya ntthu aapatthiiyeeyo rehema omaasho wa Nnyizinku.
Eti hatiithi ya Nuuhi. Vakatthi wa atthu ooshi ye otthwe paasi ti ye ari ntthu w'eekhweeli na washariya, aari weettettelaaye mwentto wa Nluku
Nuuhi awaavokoliye aanaawe aalume attatthu; Sheemu, Haamu na Yafeeti.
Olumwenku waazukuleliwe pi vitthu zootakhala na zoohusuti omaasho wa Nnyizinku.
Nnyizinku khweekesa olumwenku khusala oona ori wooharipweya, maana zumpe zooshi zaari zooharipweya menttezi aya.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Nuuhi yoori: “Kintta wiishisa zumpe zooshi z'oohaayi, vamote na olumwenku aya kipweche.
Weeyo omwaattale aaraka nwulweene na thaapwa za mpila, onremule ontthe kaatthi, onkokotte ontthe piriniisi oje waya na nkatthi.
Omwaattale nanna eti: phiima miiya na talaathiini na thaanu olepa waya, phiima eshiriini na piiri na nuusu owula waya, phiima khumi na ttatthu chanka yaya.
Ontthe tarato enfiyaaye nuusu ya phiima vatulu vaya. Waawanye tarato moote vathi, moote vakatthi, kinoko vatulu, ontthe nlako mpavu mwaya.
Onjuwa! Miiyo kasaleela ozamisa olumwenku wooshi na maati a nnyeri, kiishise zumpe zooshi ziriina phuumu z'oohaayi ziriiye vathi wa pinku. Zooshi ziriiye vatuniya zinttela ofwa.
Ila wahati aka kinretta na-weyo, onttela weetta mmwaaraka, weeyo, muukhaawo, aanaawo na aakhaaya.
Othuule nyama wakhula jaati piiri-piiri, yeelume na yeekha opakhire mmwaaraka mwawo yoori ziiye haayi vamote na-weyo.
Wakhula jaati ya anyannyi, wakhula jaati ya nyama, wakhula jaati ya epile zinjipurulaaye vathi, zooshi piiri-piiri ziiye vamote na-weyo yoori ziiye haayi.
Othuule vitthu zooshi zinjiwaazo opwehe yoori osala oja weeyo na nyama epo zooshi.”
Nuuhi khuretta zooshi epile aarumiweezo ti Nnyizinku.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Nuuhi yoori: “Weeyo na ajamaazo ooshi opakhire mmwaaraka. Vakatthi wa atthu apa ooshi ariivo, Miiyo kawoona weeyo paasi wiiya ntthu washariya.
Othuule nyama za halaali sapa zeelume na sapa zeekha ila epile zoohiiyi za halaali othuule piiri-piiri yeelume na yeekha.
Owaathuule theenya anyannyi sapa eelume na sapa eekha yoori jaati yaya ehaashikhe.
Mmana zivira siikhu sapa kinlawa kanyisele vuula vatuniya siikhu arupayiini nthana na osikhu, kipweteche zumpe zooshi kumpiyeezo.”
Nuuhi khuretta zooshi epile Nnyizinku anrumiyeezo.
Wakathi maati aazamisiyeevo tuniya, Nuuhi aari oretta arina nyaakha miiya sitha.
Ye khupakhira mmwaaraka vamote na muukhaawe, aanaawe na aakhaaya mwaasa wa maati a nnyeri aari oteelaaye ozamisa olumwenku.
Nyama za halaali na zoohiiyi za halaali, anyannyi na nyama epile zinjipurulaaye vathi,
khupakhira mmwaaraka vamote na Nuuhi piiri-piiri zeelume na zeekha, nkhama etthiipo Nnyizinku aamuuziyeezo.
Ziviriyeevo siikhu sapa, maati oozamisa olumwenku khwaaza opuwa vatuniya.
Siikhu Nuuhi afiiyeevo nyaakha miiya sitha, mweezi waphiiri orina siikhu khumi na sapa, khuphutuwa matthatta a vathi ooshi apale awiicha na milako za pinku khufukuwa.
Khunya vuula vatuniya siikhu arupayiini nthana na osikhu.
Siikhu ethiito Nuuhi, muukhaawe, aanaawe Sheemu, Haamu, Yafeeti, na aakha attatthu a aanaawe aarettiye ari mmwaaraka.
Nuuhi aapakhiriye nyama zooshi za ntthuttu, mifuwo zooshi za vaje, nyama epile zooshi zinjipurulaaye, na anyannyi a wakhula jaati na epile zooshi za wiiyana mapaphelo.
Zumpe zooshi ziriina phuumu z'oohaayi khupakhira piiri-piiri mmwaaraka mphule vamote na-ye.
Nyama zooshi zeettiyeemo zaari zeekha na zeelume za wakhula jaati nkhama etthiipo Nluku anrumiyeezo. Nawiisha opakhira, Nnyizinku khufuka nlako wa aaraka.
Nnyeri weeshiye siikhu arupayiini vatuniya. Maati khuvira eekezeleyaka mpakha khweeleela aaraka
Maati eetta ovira atepaka waatta mpakha aaraka otule khusala eeleela vatulu a maati.
Khwaatta channu mpakha khufiyelela ozamisa nyaako.
Maati khuvikana nyaako epile kiyasi ya phiima sapa.
Zumpe zooshi z'oohaayi zaari vatuniya khufwa; anyannyi, mifuwo za vaje, nyama za ntthuttu, epile zinjipurulaaye vathi na anaatamu ooshi.
Zumpe zooshi epile zaariina phuumu y'oohaayi, zaari ovumulaaye voolumwenku apha khufwa.
Nnyizinku khupwetecha zumpe zooshi z'oohaayi zaari vatuniya. Pinaatamu, nyama za ntthuttu, na epile zinjipurulaaye vathi na anyannyi o'otulu zooshi khupwetheya. Khusala Nuuhi otthwe na ajamaaze na nyama epile zaari vamote na-ye mmwaaraka.
Maati aarupaziye vatuniya siikhu miiya na hamusiini.
Ila Nluku khuhinsahawu Nuuhi na nyama epile za ntthuttu na mifuwo za vaje epile aarinaazo mmwaaraka, khuperekha pheevo yoori evitelele vatuniya, maati khwaaza ovwa.
Matthatta apale awiicha na milako za pinku khufukiwa, vuula khwaamusa,
maati khwaaza ovwa vattiitthi-vattiitthi mpakha siikhu miiya na hamusiini.
Siikhu khumi na sapa ya mweezi wasaapa aaraka otule khuphweruwa vanyaako za Araraati.
Maati apale khusala avwa paasi mpakha siikhu yamonsi mweezi wakhuumi khwaaza wooneya mithoma za nyaako.
N'oovira siikhu arupayiini Nuuhi khufukula ettakha ya aaraka etile aattaliyeeyo.
Khumfukulela nakhuku khusala avava azukulelaka mpakha maati ovwa.
Elottelanaka khufukulela jiwa yoori yoone nkhama maati avwa vatuniya.
Ila jiwa etile khuhisikani puuro yoomorela khurutela mmwaaraka, mwaasa yoori tuniya nalelo yaari ehinavuuwe. Jiwa khurutela wa Nuuhi, khusarula nkhono awe khukhola jiwa etile khuvirisa mmwaaraka.
Nuuhi khuvira awejaka mpakha siikhu sapa, khuruma jiwa ethiitile swaafu yaphiiri.
Khuruti njuwa-looveva elumiye nthapa liwishi l'ooluveera, aphano Nuuhi nawoona khujuwa yoori maati avwa vatuniya.
Khuweja theenya siikhu sapa khuruma jiwa ethiitile opheya, ila swaafu eti khuhiruti.
Siikhu yamonsi ya mweezi wa mfunko monsi wakathi Nuuhi aarinaavo nyaakha miiya sitha na mmote, maati apale aazamisiyeeyo tuniya khukakhamela. Nuuhi khufunula tarato ya aaraka khoona yoori nshaka wooma.
Siikhu eshiriini na sapa ya mweezi waphiiri, tuniya khuuma saaneene.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Nuuhi yoori:
“Wiishukhemo mmwaaraka mpho weeyo, muukhaawo, aanaawo na aakhaaya.
Wiishushe nyama zooshi oriinaazo waaza anyannyi, nyama na epi zinjipurulaaye vathi. Osarule zimwazeyele vatuniya, zittheerelane zaattelane.”
Nuuhi na muukhaawe, aanaawe na aakhaaya khwiishukha mmwaaraka mphule.
Khusarulamo nyama epile zooshi zinjipurulaaye vathi, anyannyi ooshi, na zooshi etthiipile zineettettaaye vatuniya, wakhula moote na jaati yaya.
Nawiisha, Nuuhi khunjeka alitaari woorettavo twaha yoomwinkha kafwara Nnyizinku. Ye khuthawula nyama epile kinoko zaya za halaali, na anyannyi a halaali akinoko aya, khushija, khulawa khuretta twaha yoolukuziwa vaalitaari.
Nnyizinku khusiila arufu yonkhurunusha rooho khulupa mwennyeweru yoori: “Akinteela orutela theenya olaani tuniya mwaasa wa pinaatamu, eeyaru pure wootakhala rooho ovokoliwa-wene. Akinteela orutela opwetecha zumpe zooshi nkhama nanna eti kirettiyeezo.
Mmana olumwenku wiiyakavo oniiyana wakathi woozala na wa wuurula, woozizima na wa haari, elimwe na mwiita, nthana na osikhu, vitthu epo khinteela wiisha.”
Nluku khumparikhiya Nuuhi na aanaawe awoozaka yoori: “Mwivokolelane mwaattelane mwiitaale voolumwenku.
Nyama zooshi za voolumwenku, epi za ntthuttu, anyannyi o'otulu, epi zinjipurulaaye vathi, na swi za mpahari, zinttela wiiya zoowoovani mweeyo channu. Zooshi epo mwinttela oshintta.
Zooshi zinoonaaye na zineettettaaye zinttela wiiya etthu-yooja yenu, nkhama etthiipo kiwinkhiyeenini mathapa, zooshi kawinkhani.
Ila mwihije nyama na taamu yaya, maana taamu ohaayi.
Wakhula nyama enimuulaaye ntthu, na pinaatamu animuulaaye nzaawe, anttela ojipu mmakhono Mwaka.
‘Mwaasa yoori Nluku amumpa pinaatamu ajilattanisaka mwennyewe, otule animuulaaye pinaatamu na-ye ontta wuuliwa ti pinaatamu.’
Ila mweeyo mwivokolelane mwaattelane mwiitaale voolumwenku.”
Aphano Nluku khumuuza Nuuhi vamote na aanaawe araka:
“Nasaapi eti Kinretta wahati aka na-weyo na peewu yawo,
na zooshi ziriinaazo ohaayi opakhuwaniyeeyo mmwaaraka ziriiye vamote na-weyo: anyannyi, mifuwo, nyama za ntthuttu na zumpe zooshi za ntuniya.
Kinretta wahati aka na-mweyo; akinteela opwetecha theenya zumpe zooshi na maati a nnyeri, wala tuniya khinteela ozama theenya na maati a nnyeri.”
Nluku khulupa theenya: “Eti alama ya wahati aka miiyo na-weyo na zumpe zooshi ziriiye vamote na-weyo, khwa mileele:
katthaamo nkhankanyama mmawiku yoori wiiye alama ya wahati miiyo na tuniya.
Amana kifinikha pinku na mawiku, khupuwa nkhankanyama,
phi kinttelaaye wuupuwela wahati aka miiyo na-weyo na zumpe zooshi. Khanrutela theenya maati a nnyeri ozamisa zumpe zooshi z'oohaayi.
Nkhankanyama n'oopuwa mmawiku, nka kifikhiraka wahati opule kirettiyeeyo wa mileele miiyo na zumpe zooshi z'oohaayi ziriiye vatuniya.”
Nawiisha Nluku khumuuza Nuuhi yoori: “Eti alama ya wahati kirettiyeeyo miiyo na zumpe zooshi ziriiye vatuniya.”
Aana a Nuuhi aapakhuwaniyeeyo mmwaaraka mphule pi apa: Sheemu, Haamu na Yafeeti. Haamu aari paapa wa Kanaani.
Apa attatthu aari aana a Nuuhi, atthu ooshi amwazeyeliyeeyo vatuniya avokoliwa khwa yo.
Nuuhi aari namalima, ye ti tthakuzi woozala mirayi za wuuva.
Siikhu moote, khunywa viinyu ya nshumo opule khunhapala khuvuleya kuwo zawe zooshi nheema mwawe.
Haamu, paapa wa Kanaani, khuvira nheema khoona owaazu wa papaawe. Khulawa khuwooza attwiize apale awiri aari vaje.
Aphano khulankha Sheemu na Yafeeti khuthuulaza juupa khuvikela mmafuzi mwaya khusala eettetta na enyokonyoko yoori ahoone owaazu wa papaaya n'oofiya khumfinikha.
Wakathi Nuuhi emwaamuwiyeevo viinyu etile, khujuwa mattakhuzi aaviriseliweeyo ti mwanawe otu w'eefutti.
Aphano ye khuri: “Woolaanikha ti Kanaani, onttela wiiya mwiitthwaana wa amwiitthwaana a attwiize.”
Theenya khuri: “Asifwiwe Mbwana Nnyizinku wa Sheemu, anrette Kanaani wiiya mwiitthwaana wa Sheemu.
Nnyizinku anwulise Yafeeti; khapila yawe yiiye vamote na ya Sheemu, Kanaani eeye mwiitthwaana aya.”
Paata yawiisha nnyeri, Nuuhi eekhaliye nyaakha miiya ttatthu na hamusiini.
Nuuhi afwa arina nyaakha miiya tiisiya na hamusiini.
Eti warakha ya peewu ya Sheemu, Haamu na Yafeeti, aana a Nuuhi. Yo aawaapatthiye aana wakathi opule wiishiyeevo nnyeri.
Aana a Yafeeti aari apa: Komeeri, Makooku, Matayi, Yavani, Tupaali, Mesheki na Tirasi.
Aana a Komeeri aari apa: Ashikenazi, Rifwathi na Tokaama.
Aana a Yavani aari apa: Elisha, Tarishishi, Kitimu na Rotanimu.
Khwa aana atthaapo, atthu khumwazeyela nkerekhere wa nttima na mvisura. Eti peewu ya Yafeeti wakhula khapila na lihimo laya na nti aya na luuka yaya.
Aana a Haamu aari apa: Kuushi, Misuri, Puuti na Kanaani.
Aana a Kuushi aari apa: Seepa, Havila, Saapita, Raama na Sapiteeka. Aana a Raama aari apa: Sheepa na Tetaani.
Kuushi khunvokola theenya Ninrooti, otu ti ye aaziyeeyo wiiya ntthu wooshintta vathi apha.
Ye aari namasaya wookhomaala omaasho wa Nnyizinku. Ti eto enlupiwaaye yoori “Ntthu nkhama Ninrooti, namasaya wookhomaala omaasho wa Nnyizinku”.
Ofwalume awe waaza nti wa Babeeli, Ereki na Akati, zooshi epo zaari nti wa Shinaari.
Khulankha nti wa Shinaari khulawa mpakha Ashuuru khujeka sitati ya Neniive, ya Rehopoothi-Yiiri na ya Kaala,
na sitati ya Reseeni, sitati khuluyeene yaari vakatthi wa sitati ya Neniive na ya Kaala.
Misuri khunvokola Aluti, Anaamu, Alehaapi, Anafituhi,
Apaturusi na Akasuluhi (apa pa yo awaavokoliyeeyo Afiliishiti) na Akafitoori.
Kanaani khunvokola Sitooni mwanawe wa mwanzo na Ahiiti,
theenya na Ayepuzi, Amoori na Akirikashi,
Ahivi, Ariki, Asiini,
Aravati, Azemaari na Ahamati. Khwa etthiipo lihimo la Akanaani khumwazeya.
Mwiinano wa Akanaani waaziye Sitooni olawaka Keraari, mpakha Gaaza, na phantte ya Sotooma na Komoora, Atima na Sepooyimu mpakha Laasha.
Apa aari aana a Haamu na mahimo aya, luuka zaya, miti zaya na khapila zaya.
Sheemu nttunkhulu wa Yafeeti, na-ye aawaavokoliye aana; Sheemu aari pwaapu wa aana a Heebere.
Aana a Sheemu aari apa: Elamu, Ashuuru, Arifwakisaati, Luthi na Aramu.
Aana a Aramu aari apa: Wuuzi, Huuli, Keteeri na Maashi.
Arifwakisaati khunvokola Sheela, na-ye Sheela khunvokola Heebere.
Heebere khuwaavokola aana awiri: mmote khuntthaja nzina la Peleekhi mwaasa yoori siikhu zawe tuniya yeettiye waawanyiwa. Otu waphiiri khuntthaja nzina la Yokitaani.
Yokitaani khunvokola Alimotathi, Shelefu, Hazarimawethi, Yeera,
Hatoramu, Yuzaali, Tiikala,
Opaali, Apimayeeli, Sheepa,
Ofiiri, Havila na Yopaapu, ooshi apa aana a Yokitaani.
Apa aari wiikhala waaza nti wa Meesha mpakha nnyaako phantte ya malawa-juwa nti wa Sefaari.
Apa aari aana a Sheemu na mahimo aya, luuka zaya, miti zaya na khapila zaya.
Opu ojama wa aana a Nuuhi, waawanyeyiyeeyo khapila khwa khapila na peewu yaya paata yawiisha nnyeri. Khapila zooshi zimwazeyeliyeeyo voolumwenku zalankha voojama otthuupo.
Wakathi aya opo olumwenku wooshi waarina luuka moote na nanna moote yoottakhula.
Atthu aalankhiye malawa-juwa khusikana nttapo la Shinaari khwiikhala attaapho.
Khusiilana yoori: “Nlaweni nuupe thizolo nooche saaneene.” Thizolo epile khuretta wiiya mawe, piriniisi khunretta wiiya mattakha.
Theenya khuri: “Nlaweni nijeke sitati yawiiyana korofwa khuluyeene enkomaaye pinku, yoori nzina letthu liiye loojuwanikha, nihiiye woomwazeyela olumwenku wooshi.”
Paata ya toole, Nnyizinku khwiishukha yoori oone sitati ya korofwa etile aari ojekaaye atthu apale.
Ye khuri: “Moone! Atthu apa amoteru, ooshi anttakhula luuka moote. Eti arettiyeeyo eetta waaza, khaavo anttelaaye owaakarawela etile awaziyeeyo.
Nlaweni niishukhe navirikanise luuka anttakhulaaye yoori ahisala asiilana mmote na nzaawe.”
Ethiito, khukaraweleya ojekiwa sitati etile, Nnyizinku khuwaamwazela olumwenku wooshi.
Ti eto sitati etile khutthajiwa nzina la “Babeeli”, mwaasa wa Nnyizinku ovirikanisa luuka ya anaatamu ooshi. Attaapho, Nnyizinku khuwaamwazela olumwenku wooshi.
Eti peewu ya Sheemu. Sheemu afiiyeevo nyaakha miiya khunvokola mwanawe Arifwakisaati, nyaakha miwiri paata ya nnyeri ovira.
N'onvokola Arifwakisaati, eekhaliye nyaakha miiya thaanu, khuwaavokola theenya aana aalume na aakha.
Arifwakisaati afiiyeevo nyaakha talaathiini na mithaanu, khunvokola Sheela.
Paata yonvokola Sheela, eekhaliye nyaakha miiya nne na mittatthu, khuwaavokola theenya aana aalume na aakha.
Sheela afiiyeevo nyaakha talaathiini khunvokola Heebere.
N'onvokola Heebere, eekhaliye nyaakha miiya nne na mittatthu, khuwaavokola theenya aana aakha na aalume.
Heebere afiiyeevo nyaakha miiya nne na talaathiini khunvokola Peleekhi.
N'onvokola Peleekhi, eekhaliye nyaakha miiya nne na talaathiini, khuwaavokola theenya aana aalume na aakha.
Peleekhi afiiyeevo nyaakha talaathiini khunvokola Reewu.
N'onvokola Reewu, eekhaliye nyaakha miiya piiri na tiisiya, khuwaavokola theenya aana aalume na aakha.
Reewu afiiyeevo nyaakha talaathiini na miwiri khunvokola Serukhi.
N'onvokola Serukhi, eekhaliye nyaakha miiya piiri na sapa khuwaavokola theenya aana aakha na aalume.
Serukhi afiiyeevo nyaakha talaathiini khunvokola Nahoori.
N'onvokola Nahoori, eekhaliye nyaakha miiya piiri khuwaavokola theenya aana aalume na aakha.
Nahoori afiiyeevo nyaakha eshiriini na tiisiya khunvokola Teera.
N'onvokola Teera, eekhaliye nyaakha miiya na khumi na tiisiya, khuwaavokola theenya aana aalume na aakha.
Teera afiiyeevo nyaakha sapiini, khunvokola Eburamu, Nahoori na Hara.
Eti peewu ya Teera. Teera khunvokola Eburamu, Nahoori na Hara. Hara khunvokola Loothi.
Hara khufwa sitati ya Wuuri, nti wa Babilooniya tuniya aavokoliweewo, ila papaawe khusala ari haayi.
Eburamu na Nahoori khuloola. Muukha wa Eburamu aari wiitthiwa Suhuriiya, na-ye muukha wa Nahoori nzina lawe aari Miilika, mwaana wa Hara, aarina mwaana nkina theenya aari wiitthiwaaye Ishika.
Ila Suhuriiya khaarina aana mwaasa woohiina mavokozi.
Teera khulankha sitati ya Wuuri, nti wa Babilooniya, eettaka Kanaani. Alawaka khunthuula mwanawe Eburamu na ntuuluwe Loothi, mwaana wa Hara, vamote na nkhwewe Suhuriiya, muukha wa Eburamu. Ila afiiyeevo sitati ya Harani khuhivikani, khwiikhala ottuukho.
Teera khufwa Harani arina nyaakha miiya piiri na mithaanu.
Siikhu moote, Nnyizinku khumuuza Eburamu araka: “Olikhe tuniya yawo, na ajamaazo, na vaje wa apapazo olawe tuniya kinttelaaye wuuthoonyeza.
Kinteela wuuretta wiiya paapa wa peewu ya waatta, kinteela wuuparikhiya na onteela wiiya woojuwanikha, kinteela owaaparikhiya atthu akina mwaasa wa weeyo.
Kiniwaaparikhiya apale anuuparikhiyaaye, na kininlaani otule anuulaanaaye. Khwa weyo enteela wiiya zooparikhiyiwa khapila zooshi za voolumwenku.”
Eburamu khulankha khusala alawa nkhama etthiipo Nnyizinku anrumiyeezo. Ye aalawiye vamote na Loothi, wakathi aaliiyeewo Harani aari oretta arina nyaakha sapiini na mithaanu.
Khunthuula muukhaawe Suhuriiya na Loothi mwaana wa ttwiiye, na mali zawe zooshi aariinaazo, vamote na amwiitthwaana awe aawaapatthiyeeyo Harani, khusala alawa tuniya ya Kanaani. N'oofiya tuniya ya Kanaani,
ye khuvira eettettaka tuniya aya etile, khulawa mpakha Shekemu, phantte ya Moore ohali waariiwo muutthi nwulweene. Wakathi aya opule Akanaani aari oretta eekhalaka tuniya ethiitile.
Nnyizinku khunteela Eburamu, khumuuza yoori: “Tuniya eti kinteela winkha peewu yawo”. Aphano Eburamu khunjekela alitaari Nnyizinku attaaphale.
Eeshiyeevo, khusala eetta phantte ya kusini onyaako wa malawa-juwa ya Beetele. N'oofiya onyaako okhule, khweemesa heema yawe. Beetele yaari okhu lintupweelaawo njuwa, Aayi yaari okhu lintthamuwaawo njuwa. Ye khunjekela alitaari Nnyizinku khwaaputu nzina la Nnyizinku.
Aphano, ye khusala avira alawaka mpakha Nikeepu, phantte ya kusini ya Kanaani.
Tuniya ya Kanaani yaapuwiyewo jala ya waatta, aphano Eburamu khulankha khusala alawa tuniya ya Misuri yoori eekhalewo siikhu vattitthiiru.
Asaleelaka ofiya, khumuuza muukhaawe Suhuriiya yoori: “Osiileze, miiyo kajuwacha yoori weeyo o muukha wooshapweya.
Amisuri n'oowoona anttela olupa yoori weeyo o muukhaaka, antta okuula yoori weeyo osale na-yo.
Amana wuuzeliwa olupe yoori nlupwaaka, ahikuule na akikhole saana mwaasa wa weeyo.”
Wakathi Eburamu afiiyeevo, Amisuri khumoona Suhuriiya yoori aari muukha wooshapweya channu.
Mifwalume za Firawuuna, amooniyeevo muukha otule, khulawa omuuza Firawuuna yoori amoona muukha wooshapweya. Pi apho khunthuula khunlawana wa Firawuuna.
Eburamu aakholiwe saana ti Firawuuna mwaasa wa muukha otule, khwinkhiwa pwittipwitthi, mompe, amwiitthwaana aalume na aakha, apuuru na khavalo.
Ila Nnyizinku khunhukhumu Firawuuna, khuntiisela pala ya waatta na ajamaaze, mwaasa wa Suhuriiya muukha wa Eburamu.
Aphano, Firawuuna khunkhuwelisa Eburamu, khumuuzela yoori: “Mwaasa aya niini okirettelaka toono? Wahaakuuziye yoori otu muukhaawo?
Khi apho waari olupaaye yoori ti nlupuwo? Mwaasa wa weeyo ori nlupuwo, ti eto yaakipatthisiyeeyo onrala. Apho muukhaawo otu, onthuule olawe!”
Aphano Firawuuna khuwaaruma atthu awe omperekha Eburamu yoori aleemo mmuti mphule na muukhaawe na vitthu zawe zooshi.
Aphano Eburamu khulaawo Misuri khweetta phantte ya kashikhazini khulawa mpakha Nikeepu, ye na muukhaawe na vitthu zawe zooshi, vamote na Loothi.
Eburamu aari thaajiri nwulweene. Aarina nyama za waatta, na feeta na thahapu.
Ye khulaawo Nikeepu, khulawa phantte ya kashikhazini ajeettettelaka wakhula phantte mpakha nti wa Beetele, attaaphale eemesiyeevo heema yawe omwanzo, nakatthi-nakatthi ya Beetele na Aayi.
Attaaphale anjekiyeevo alitaari, ye khwaaputu nzina la Nnyizinku.
Na-ye Loothi otule aari weettettanaaye Eburamu, aarina pwittipwitthi, mompe na heema za waatta.
Khayaari owaheya wiikhala vamote mwaasa yoori nti opule khawaarina tthuttu yoofiyela ojisa nyama zaya.
Pi apho, khupuwa onyakulisana amakhampuzi a Eburamu na amakhampuzi a Loothi. Wakathi aya opo Akanaani na Aperizi aari oretta eekhalaka nti otthuupule.
Eburamu khumuuza Loothi yoori: “Ohiiyevo ohisiilani miiyo na-weyo, wala amakhampuzi aka na awo, mwaasa yoori ojama etthu mmote.
Tuniya yooshi khiri mmakhono mwawo? Nlawe nimwazeyane, othawule phantte ontakhaaye olawa. Weeyo weettaru nkhono-nkha, miiyo kintta nkhono-nlume, weettaru nkhono-nlume miiyo kintta nkhono-nkha.”
Loothi khulansa maasho awe khoona nttapo la muuttho Yorotaani lihiniishaaye maati liri looripelela mpakha nti wa Zowaari. Nttapo ntthile laari nkhama woorotha wa Eeteni, na loolattanana tuniya ya Misuri. Wakathi aya opo Nnyizinku aarettiye ahinapweche nti wa Sotooma na Komoora.
Aphano, Loothi khuthawula nttapo la Yorotaani, khumwazeyana na Eburamu, khusala alawa phantte ya malawa-juwa.
Eburamu khusala eekhala tuniya ya Kanaani, Loothi khweemesa heema zawe waattamana na Sotooma, kharipu na sitati za nkerekhere wa nttapo la Yorotaani.
Ila atthu a Sotooma aari ootakhala rooho, aari annya-twampi ooziti mmakhono wa Nnyizinku.
Paata ya Loothi olawa, Nnyizinku khumuuza Eburamu araka: Olanse maasho awo attaapho oriivo, weekese kashikhazini na kusini, na okhu lintthamuwaawo njuwa mpakha lintupweelaawo.
Tuniya eto yooshi onoonaaye kinteela owinkha weeyo na peewu yawo khwa mileele.
Kinteela waattisa peewu yawo nkhama mishaka za voolumwenku, nkhama etthiipo ahinteelaaye wiiyavo ntthu wa waalaka mishaka za voolumwenku, na peewu yawo khinteela waalakeya.
Olankhe ozukulele tuniya eti woone olepa waya na owula waya, mwaasa yoori kinttela owinkha weeyo.
Aphano Eburamu khuthamisa heema zawe, khulawa khwiikhala aphale zaariivo miitthi miwulu-miwulu nti wa Manre sitati ya Heporooni. Attaaphale ye khunjekela alitaari Nnyizinku.
Wakathi aya opo Amirafeele aari mfwalume wa Shinaari, Ariyookho mfwalume wa Elazaari, Ketorilameeri mfwalume wa Elamu, na Titaali mfwalume wa Koyiimu,
khulankhaza olawa wuumanana viittha Peera mfwalume wa Sotooma, Piirisha mfwalume wa Komoora, Shinaapu mfwalume wa Aatima, Shemeepere mfwalume wa Zeboyimu, na mfwalume wa sitati ya Peela, yaari wiitthiwaaye Zowaari.
Afwalume apa athaanu khuwaakusanya anajanka aya nttapo la Siitimu (liiyiyeeyo ntthatta la maati majiphwaani).
Mfwalume Ketorilameeri, aawaashinttiye afwalume apale athaanu khwa nyaakha khumi na miwiri, ila mwaakha wakhuumi na ttaatthu aya khunzukuluwelaza.
Mwaakha wakhuumi na nne Ketorilameeri khuta vamote na afwalume apale aaphakanyeyaniyeeyo, khuwaashintta Arefayi o'Ashiteroothi-Karinayimu, Azuuzimu o'Haamu, na Aheemi o'Shave-Kiriyatayimu.
Theenya khuwaashintta Ahoori omwaako wa Seyiiri, khuwiikarisa mpakha Paraani ohali yaaziyeewo yaara.
Arutaka khuviraza Kateeshi waari wiittheliwakaawo Emishipathi, khuwaattapwattha atthu ooshi a nti wa Amalekiita na theenya Amoori aari wiikhalaaye nti wa Hazaazoni-Tamara.
Aphano khulankha mfwalume wa Sotooma, mfwalume wa Komoora, mfwalume wa Atima, mfwalume wa Zeboyimu, na mfwalume wa sitati ya Peela (eti yaari wiitthiwaaye Zowaari), khulankha olawa wuumanisa viittha nttapo la Siitimu.
Aari wuumanaza na Ketorilameeri mfwalume wa Elamu, Titaali mfwalume wa Koyiimu, Amirafeele mfwalume wa Shinaari, na Ariyookho mfwalume wa Elazaari. Aari afwalume athaanu aari wuumananaaye afwalume wane.
Nttapo la Siitimu laarina milipu za waatta za piriniisi. Wakathi aari otthiraavo afwalume a Sotooma na Komoora, anajanka aya eetta okwela mmilipu, apale akinoko aya khutthirela nnyaako.
Afwalume apale wane aashinttiyeeyo khuthuula maali zooshi za Sotooma na Komoora na vitthu-zooja zaya khulawaza.
Na theenya khunthuula Loothi, mwaana wa ttwiiye Eburamu na mali zawe zooshi, mwaasa aya ye aari wiikhala Sotooma.
Aarivo mwinyi mmote oosurukhiyeeyo, ye khulawa khumweeleza zooshi Eburamu Mwiibereewu, aari wiikhalaaye kharipu na miitthi miwulu-miwulu za Manre Mmori. Manre na attwiize, Sikhoole na Aneeri, aari atthu oosiilana na Eburamu.
Asiiliyeevo Eburamu oriwa ntuuluwe akholiwa, khuwaathuula alume miiya ttatthu na khumi na wanaane aawaakhupaliyeeyo, oovokoliwa vaje vawe, khusala aweekarisa afwalume apale wane mpakha nti wa Daani.
Ye khuwaawanya alume apale khuntti-khuntti, khuumanisa viittha osikhu mpakha owaashintta maatuwi aya, khuweekarisa mpakha nti wa Hoopa, phantte ya kashikhazini ya Tamaashiku.
Khuwaanyakanya maali zooshi aathuuliyeeyo, khunthuula Loothi ntuuluwe na mali zawe, vamote na aakha na atthu akinoko aakholiweeyo khuwaarutisa.
Wakathi Eburamu anshinttiyeevo mfwalume Ketorilameeri na afwalume aaphakanyeyaniyeeyo, mfwalume wa Sotooma khusala alawa ompokherela nttapo la muuttho Shaawe liniittheliwaaye “Nttapo la Mfwalume”.
Aarivo mfwalume wa nti wa Salemu, aari wiitthiwaaye Melikiseetekhi. Khutiisa phaawu na viinyu. Ye aari haakhimu wa tiini ya Nluku Nwulu wa Pinkuuni,
khumparikhiya Eburamu araka: “Aparikhiyiwe Eburamu ti Nluku Nwulu wa Pinkuuni, otu ompiye pinku na vathi.
Woottitthimisiwa eeye Nluku Nwulu wa Pinkuuni, otu awinkhiyeeyo owaashintta maatuwi awo.” Aphano, Eburamu khulaza lifunku lakhuumi khwa zooshi epile aataniyeezo, khumwinkha Melikiseetekhi.
Mfwalume wa Sotooma khumuuza yoori: “Miiyo okinkhe atthu paasi. Maali zooshi osalane weeyo.”
Eburamu khunjipu mfwalume araka: “Kalansa makhono aka kinlanselaka Nnyizinku, Nluku Nwulu wa Pinkuuni ompiye pinku na vathi,
na kinlapha yoori akinsalana hatha etthu yaawo, wala luuzi wala nliiza wa jampali, ohiri nawiikhala, olupa yoori ‘Eburamu kanreelisa’.
Miiyo khina etthu moote kintakhaaye, yoohiiyi etile ajiiye atthu aka. Ila apale aaphakanyeyiyeeyo na-miyo, Aneeri, Sikhoole na Manre, apa ana ya wiiyana lifunku laya”.
Paata ya vitthu epile, Nnyizinku anttakhulaniye Eburamu nkatthi wa ezimu amuuzaka yoori: “Eburamu ohoove! Miiyo ki namwaakisa awo, na tthuvo yawo enteela wiiya yooziti owula.”
Eburamu khujipu: “Mbwanaaka Nnyizinku ontakha okinkha-ni na miiyo akina hatha mwaana wa waarithi aka? Antakhaaye orithi vaje vaka ti Elizeeri wa Tamaashiku.
Khukinkheeni mwaana; apho, karumeya wa vaje vaka ti ye anttelaaye orithi vitthu zaka.”
Aphano Nnyizinku khunjipu: “Namarithi vitthu zawo khanttela wiiya oto, ila mwaana woovokoliwa ti weyo ti anttelaaye orithi.”
Khunsarulamo nheema mwawe khumuuza yoori: “Weekese otulu, waalake matthottowa nkhama anaalakeya. Peewu yawo enteela wiiya etthiipo.”
Ye khumwaamini Nnyizinku, na-ye khukhupaliwa ti Nnyizinku wiiya ntthu wa shariya.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Eburamu theenya: “Miiyo ki Nnyizinku kuulaziyeeyo Wuuri nti wa Babilooniya yoori kiwinkhe tuniya eti orithi.”
Eburamu khumuuzela yoori: “Oo Mbwanaaka Nnyizinku, kihakikhi toovi yoori kinteela orithi tuniya eti?”
Nnyizinku khujipu: “Okitiisele mwaana wa mompe, wa puuzi, na wa pwittipwitthi, zooshi za wiiyana nyaakha mittatthu, na theenya likhoko na jiwa moote”.
Ye khutiisa nyama epile zooshi, khusala ashija vakatthi wakhula nyama n'oothata wakhula erikitthili omaasho wa erikitthili kiina yaya. Ila likhoko na jiwa khuhishiji vakatthi.
Mirepo khusala ziishukhela mphule zaariimo nyama epile zooshijiwa, ila Eburamu khusala eekara.
Njuwa leettelaka otupweela, Eburamu khunkhola osikizi wa waatta khusala oona yiiza ya waatta na woova.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza yoori: “Ojuwache yoori peewu yawo enteela omaka nti woohiiyi waaya, enteela orettiwa omwiitthwaana na ohoochiwa nyaakha miiya nne.
Ila miiyo kinteela owaahukhumu atthu apo anttelaaye oretta omwiitthwaana, na enteela olaawo na maali za waatta.
Weeyo onttela wuuluvala ori wooparikhiyiwa na onteela ofwa na heeri.
Paata yoovira nyaakha epo miiya nne, peewu yawo enteela orutela tuniya eti, amana Amoori apa aniikhalaaye nttumphu atepa oretta vitthu zootakhala, miiyo kinteela owaahukhumu na kiweekare.”
Litupweeliyeevo njuwa, waariipiye vathi khupuwa loosi la njocho na mweeke wa moottho khuvira vakatthi wa virikitthili za nyama epile zaashijiweezo.
Siikhu ethiitile, Nnyizinku khuretta wahati na Eburamu, khumuuza yoori: “Tuniya eti kinteela winkha peewu yawo, waaza muuttho wa Misuri mpakha muuttho nwulu oniitthiwaaye Efwarathi,
otthaamo nti wa Akeni, wa Akenizi, wa Akatemoni,
wa Ahiiti, wa Aperizi, wa Arefayi,
wa Amoori, wa Akanaani, wa Akirikashi na wa Ayepuzi.”
Wakathi aya opo, Suhuriiya muukha wa Eburamu khaari ovokola. Ye aarina njaazi mmote wa Misuri aari wiitthiwaaye Hajira.
Siikhu moote, Suhuriiya khumuuza mannawe Eburamu yoori: “Nnyizinku khanikinkha mwaana, apho orapalelane njaazi aka, khinjuweya kimpatthaka mwaana khwa ye.” Asiiliyeevo toole, Eburamu khukhupalela mattakhuzi apale a muukhaawe.
Suhuriiya khunthuula njaazi otule khumwinkha Eburamu yoori eeye muukhaawe waphiiri. Vitthu epi zarettikhana Eburamu arina nyaakha khumi eekhalaka tuniya ya Kanaani.
Eburamu khurapalela na Hajira, ye khwiiya wa wiimittha. Ooniyeevo yoori eemittha khwaaza ontwayifu nhano awe.
Suhuriiya khumuuza Eburamu yoori: “Miiyo kanthuula njaazi aka khuwinkha, ye n'oojuwa yoori eemittha aaza okitwayifu. Okitwayifusha opu anikirettelaaye Hajira, khahi etthu ya shariya, ti weyo onintakhelaaye. Nnyizinku ti aniphuke miiyo na-weyo.”
Eburamu khunjipu Suhuriiya yoori: “Ye nalelo njaazi awo, onrettele khwa nanna ontakhaazo.” Aphano Suhuriiya khwaaza ontarawu Hajira mpakha khufiyelela otthira.
Nlayikha la Nnyizinku khunsikana Hajira n'yaara eemeliye kharipu na naattuuttu wa maati aattameliyeeyo tarikhi ya Shuuri.
Nlayikha ntthile khumuuzela liraka: “Weeyo Hajira njaazi wa Suhuriiya! Onlankha vayi wala ontta vayi?” Ye khujipu: “Keetta otthira vaje wa nhano aka Suhuriiya othuuto.”
Nlayikha khumuuza yoori: “Orutele wa nhano awo, wanshututele.”
Khumuuza theenya yoori: “Kinteela waattisa peewu yawo khwa nanna ehinaalakeyaaye.
Apho wiimitthiyeevo onteela ompattha mwaana ontthaje nzina la Esumayila, mwaasa yoori Nnyizinku oona ohoowa wawo.
Ye onteela wiiya woohisiilaneyi nkhama nyama ya ntthuttu; onteela wiiya muumani wa atthu ooshi, na-yo anteela wuumana na ye, na onteela wiiya wa waattuwana na attwiize.”
Hajira khujuuzela mwennyeweru yoori: “Kamoona Nluku, nalelo kiri haayi?” Aphano khunkhuwelela Nnyizinku nzina liriina maana a “Nluku anikoonaaye”.
Pi apho nlipu aya opule oniittheliwa “Peeri-Lahayi-Rooyi”. Nlipu aya opu ori enakatthi-nakatthi ya Kateeshi na Peereti.
Hajira khumpattha mwaana wa Eburamu. Eburamu khuntthaja mwaana otule nzina la Esumayila.
Wakathi Hajira ampatthiyeevo mwaana otule, Eburamu aarettiye arina nyaakha thamaaniini na sitha.
Wakathi Eburamu afiiyeevo nyaakha tiisiini na tiisiya, Nnyizinku anteeliye khusala amuuza araka: “Miiyo ki Nluku Woowahi Zooshi: weettettele mwentto kintakhaaye miiyo, wiiye ntthu nkemaani,
yoori kirette wahati miiyo na-weyo, na kinteela owinkha peewu ya waatta.”
Aphano Eburamu khukokhora khulawa sijita, Nluku khusala anttakhulana ye araka:
“Wahati opu kinrettanaaye weeyo, phantte yaka kiniwaahiti yoori onteela wiiya paapa wa khapila za waatta.
Waaza leelo nzina lawo khahiyo Eburamu, ila Eburahiima ti linttelaaye wiiya nzina lawo, mwaasa yoori kinttela wuuretta opaapa wa khapila za waatta.
Kinteela waattisa channu peewu yawo, khwa weyo kinretta khapila za waatta, akinoko aya anteela wiiya afwalume.
Wahati opu kinrettaaye na-weyo na peewu yawo, onttela wiiya wa mileele; Miiyo ki Nluku awo na wa peewu yawo.
Kinteela owinkha tuniya eti oniikhalaaye, weeyaru pure mmalapo. Tuniya yooshi ya Kanaani kinteela winkha peewu yawo khwa mileele, na-miyo kinteela wiiya Nluku aya.”
Nluku khurutela omuuza yoori: “Phantte yawo ona yooshututela wahati aka, weeyo na peewu yawo khwa mileele.
Wahati onttelaaye oshuka, waaka Miiyo na-weyo na peewu yawo pi opu: wakhula mwaana wanlume ona yookhiriyisiwa.
Okhiriya waya opo, alama ya wahati aka miiyo na-mweyo.
Wakhula mwaana anvokoliwaaye wanlume vakatthi wa peewu yawo, n'oofiya siikhu yanaane ona yookhiriyisiwa, hatha nkhama karumeya woovokoliwa vaje vawo, mpakha amwiitthwaana apale amalapo a wuuzanyiwa na apale oohiiyi a peewu yawo.
Hatha nkhama pi apa oovokoliwa vaje vawo mpakha apa a wuuzanyiwa ana yookhiriyisiwa. Alama eti yookhiriya vamwiili venu, enthoonyeza wahati aka na-mweyo khwa mileele.
Otule ahinttelaaye okhiriya eekariwemo muumathi mwenu, mwaasa yoori akattha wahati aka.”
Nluku khumuuza Eburahiima theenya yoori: “Muukhaawo khanteela wiitthiwa theenya Suhuriiya, ila nka eetthiwaka Suhura.
Kinteela omparikhiya na kimwinkhe mwaana wawo; khweele, miiyo kinimparikhiya na onteela wiiya maama wa khapila za waatta, afwalume anteela opuwa khwa ye.”
Aphano Eburahiima khukokhora khusijiti, ila khusala ajitheyela nroho mwawe ajuuzelaka toono: “Nlume wa nyaakha miiya eeyane mwaana? Khi Suhura ariina nyaakha tiisiini ate ampatthe mwaana?”
Eburahiima khumuuza Nluku: “Omparikhiye Esumayila, eeye namarithi aka.”
Ila Nluku khunjipu: “Miiyo kiniwuuza khweele yoori, muukhaawo Suhura onteela ompattha mwaana, ontthaje nzina la Esiyaakha. Kinteela oshuka wahati aka na-ye, na peewu yawe entaaye khwa mileele.
Kasiila oveka wawo khwa Esumayila. Kinteela omparikhiya na kinteela omwinkha peewu ya waatta. Ye onteela wiiya paapa wa mifwalume khumi na awiri, khwa ye enteela opuwa theenya khapila ya waatta.
Ila wahati aka kinteela oshuka mmakhono wa Esiyaakha, otu anttelaaye ovokoliwa ti Suhura wakathi otthuupu wa mwaakhani.”
Nawiisha ottakhula na Eburahiima, Nluku khulawa.
Siikhu ethiitile, Eburahiima khunthuula mwanawe Esumayila na ooshi aavokoliweeyo vaje vawe na apale aawuuzanyiyeeyo. Khulawa owaakhiriyisa, nkhama etthiipo Nluku aamuuziyeezo.
Wakathi aakhiriyaziyeevo, Eburahiima aarettiye arina nyaakha tiisiini na tiisiya
na mwanawe Esumayila aari oretta arina nyaakha khumi na mittatthu.
Eburahiima na mwanawe aakhiriyiye siikhu moote,
vamote na apale aavokoliweeyo owawe, mpakha amalapo apale a wuuzanyiwa.
Siikhu moote, Nnyizinku aatiiye ottakhula na Eburahiima vahali zaariivo miitthi miwulu-miwulu za Manre. Yaari elukuluku na yaarivo haari ya waatta, Eburahiima aarettiye eekhaliye vanlako wa heema yawe.
Ye khulansa maasho awe khuwoona alume attatthu eemeliye kharipu. Aphano awooniyeevo khulankhavo aphale vaya, khusala awaatthirela. Awaafiyeliyeevo khukokhora khulawa sijita.
Khuwooza yoori: “Mbwanaaka, nkhama kinaaye sehemu mmakhono mwenu, kinuuvekelani yoori mwihivikane vaje vaka, mwihivumuleeni vattitthiiru.
Mwiikhale vamwiivuuli wa muutthi opu mwivumule, antta otiisiwa maati vattitthiiru moose moolweenu,
wiiya mwavira vaje wa karumeyeenu, kintta weettela etthu ttiitthiiru mwisapeye, yoori mwipatthe kuvu yoorutela safwari yenu.” Yo khujipu yoori: “Kemaani! Erettikhane khwa nanna onlupaazo.”
Aphano Eburahiima khutthira eettaka nheema mwawe khumuuza Suhura yoori: “Othuule miphimo miwulu mittatthu z'oofu wa tiriku yooshapweya, okhatte wooche phaawu wa waakuvavo.”
Nawiisha, khutthirela onzizi wawe khunthuula mwaana wa mompe woonenevacha, khumwinkha karumeyaawe yoori anshije na amwiipikhe wa waakuveyavo.
Eburahiima khuthuula mompe etile yawiipikhiwa saana, manteeka na leethi khuwenkha aletto apale, ye khweemela nshini wa muutthi kharipu na aletto apale eettaka oja.
Yo khumuuzela: “Khi muukhaawo Suhura ori vayi?” Eburahiima khujipu: “Ori nheema mpho.”
Mmote wa yo khuri: “N'oovira mwaakha, kinrutela vaje vawo attaapha, na muukhaawo onretta ampatthiye mwaana.” Suhura aari oretta ari vanlako wa heema onyoko wa Eburahiima, eettaka osiila mattakhuzi apale aari ottakhuliwaaye.
Eburahiima na Suhura aari a wuuluvala na kuvu, na Suhura zanvireliye siikhu zoovokola.
Ye khusala ajitheyela nroho mwawe otthwe ajuuzelaka yoori: “Khwa nanna eti nuuluvaliyeezo miiyo na mbwanaaka, kinteela wiiyana furaha yaya eto?”
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuzela Eburahiima yoori: “Muukhaawo ontheya-ni? Wala alupisiwa-ni yoori ‘kinteela ompattha toovi mwaana kuuluvaliye?’
Ewaapho etthu yoolipa mmakhono wa Nnyizinku? Nkhama etthiipo kilupiyeeyo yoori n'oovira mwaakha kinta wuuthotola, wakathi aya otthuupo Suhura onteela ompattha mwaana wanlume.”
Mwaasa wa woova Suhura khusala akhana yoori: “Akitheyeeni.” Ye khuri: “Khahiye toowo, khweele weeyo watheya.”
Wakathi alume apale attatthu alankhiyeevo eeshukhelaka nti wa Sotooma, Eburahiima alankhiye khusala awaaperekha alawaka oleezanana.
Aphano Nnyizinku khujuuzela mwennyeweru yoori: “Akinta kimuuze Eburahiima etthu kinttelaaye oretta?
Khweele-khweele Eburahiima onteela wiiya paapa w'oomathi nwulweene woowahi; khwa ye, kinteela oparikhiya khapila zooshi za voolumwenku.
Maana miiyo kanthawula ye yoori awaanozele aanaawe na omathaawe, weettettela saana tarikhi ya Nnyizinku, arettaka etile yiiyiye ya shariya na yoolotteya, yoori miiyo Nnyizinku kirette khwa Eburahiima etile kaahitiyeeyo.”
Nnyizinku khumuuza Eburahiima yoori; “Kinsiila nkhuwo yoori atthu a Sotooma na Komoora anretta vitthu zootakhala na twampi zaya pi zooziti.
Kineetta ottuukhu kilawe koone khiima za twampi epo anrettaazo nkhama khweele pi etthiipo kinsiilaazo, kinttela ohakikhi.”
Attaaphale, alume apale awiri khusala alawa Sotooma, ila Nnyizinku khusala ari vamote na Eburahiima.
Eburahiima khunsusela Nnyizinku khumuuzela yoori: “Onttela owooleela vamote anashariya na anapaathuli?
Khi amana eeyawo atthu hamusiini anashariya, ompwecha sitati etile? Khunteela owaaswaamihi mwaasa wa atthu apo hamusiini anashariya?
Ohiiye weeyo wooretta etthu nkhama eto, yoowuuleela vamote anashariya na anapaathuli. Khawaari oteela owaahukhumu anashariya mwaasa wa vitthu zoorettiwa pi anapaathuli. Weeyo o namaphuka w'oolumwenku wooshi, khunteela ophuka na shariya?”
Nnyizinku khujipu araka: “Amana kifiya Sotooma kiwaasikana anashariya hamusiini ari nsitati nttumphule, kinttela oswaamihi sitati yaya etile kiiswa ya yo.”
Eburahiima khurutela ottakhula araka: “Okiswaamihi na ruhusa kiriina yoottakhulana weeyo Mbwanaaka, keeyaru ottophe na fuutha.
Khi amana asaleelaka athaanu yoori afiyele hamusiini, onipwecha sitati etile mwaasa wa apa ansaleelaaye?” Mbwana khuri: “Amana kiwaasikana arupayiini na athaanu akimpwecha.”
Khumuuzela theenya; “Khi amana owaasikana arupayiini?” Mbwana khujipu: “Wala, akimpwechawo mwaasa wa apale arupayiini.”
Khuvira amuuzelaka theenya: “Mbwanaaka, ohikatipukhe amana kirutela ottakhula: khi amana owaasikana anashariya talaathiini?” Mbwana khuri: “Amana kiwaasikanawo talaathiini akinretta hatha etthu.”
Eburahiima khurutela olupa yoori: “Okiswaamihi na nthiti kiriinaayo la wuuttakhulana Mbwanaaka, khi amana owaasikana anashariya eshiriini?” Ye khuri: “Akimpwechawo mwaasa wa anashariya apale eshiriini.”
Khulupa theenya Eburahiima: “Mbwanaaka, ohikatipukhe, kiniwuuzela swaafu moote ethiiti paasi; khi amana owaasikanawo anashariya khumi?” Ye khunjipu: “Akimpwechawo mwaasa wa anashariya apale khumi.”
Nawiisha Nnyizinku ottakhula na Eburahiima, khulankha khusala alawa. Na-ye Eburahiima khurutela owawe.
Malayikha apale mawiri khufiya Sotooma makaaripi, Loothi aarettiye eekhaliye vanlako wa sitati ethiitile, ye nawoona malayikha apale khusala athepeeza atthirelaka. N'oofiyela khukokhora khusijiti.
Khuwooza yoori: “Ambwana zaka kookholani moolu, kintakha mwisapuwe owaka miiyo karumeyeenu; moose moolweenu na mwilale, mwilawe meesho supuyeene.” Yo khujipu yoori: “Khinhithajiya, fweeyo ninwahi olala vaparasa veetakale.”
Loothi khuwaakhanyerela na kuvu mpakha yo okhupali olawa omaka owawe. Ye khurumisa wiipikhiwa etthu-yooja ya nnofu na khoochiwa phaawu yoohiina fwaramento, aletto apale khuja.
Ila ahinalawe olala, eetta ota alume ooshi a sitati ethiitile waaza attunkhulu mpakha mashaapu khuzukulela nyuupa ya Loothi.
Khusala anyakula ankhuwelaka Loothi araka; “Alume apa atiiyeeyo nnyupa mwawo mphu osikhu otthuupu ari vayi? Owaasarulele vaje apha, fweeyo nintakha niwaalalane”.
Loothi khusaruwela vaje, khufuka nlako awe afukelaka onyoko wawe.
Khuwooza yoori: “Safwatali ajamaazaku; mwihirette etthu eto otakhala
Mweyo! Miiyo kinaaye aanaaka awiri ahiniwaajuwaaye alume. Kintta owinkhani atthaapo, mwiwaarettele wakhula etile mwintakhaaye. Ila mwihiwaarettele etthu yootakhala aletto apa ata nnyupa mwaka, na miiyo kina yoowiinanela.”
Yo khuri: “Oleevo apha! Weeyo o mmalapo mmuti mphu, ontakha ojinkhe ofwalume na mmuti mwetthu? Fweeyo nintta wuurettela vitthu zooziti epi naari otakhaaye owaarettela apo.” Aphano yo khunsukhuma Loothi, khusala asusela nlako awe yoori apwechaze.
N'ooretta toole, aletto apale khunkhola Loothi khumfutthela nnyupa khufuka nlako,
na khuwoola maasho alume apale a Sotooma aari vanlako wa Loothi. Waaza attunkhulu mpakha mashaapu khusala apapasela nlako khuhisala asikana.
Alume apale khumuuzela Loothi: “Onaaye ajaama akina nsitati mphu? Oleemo, owaathuule aanaawo, akhwewo, muukhaawo na ooshi apale eeyiye aawo,
mwaasa aya nateela opwecha sitati eti. Nnyizinku asiila nkhuwo nwulweene wa vitthu zootakhala anrettaazo atthu a Sotooma, apha aniruma yoori nite nipweche sitati yaya eti.”
Aphano ye khulawa owooza akhwewe, apale aari weettelaaye owaarala aanaawe yoori: “Mwileemo nsitati mphu, maana Nnyizinku onttela opwecha.” Ila akhwewe apale khusala oona nkhama nzaha.
Lifwajiri, malayikha apale khusala amuuza Loothi antumereraka yoori: “Olankhe nasaapi ethiiti, onthuule muukhaawo na aanaawo oowiiri mwileemo mphu. N'oohiretti toowo, amana etaka hukhumu nsitati mphu mweeyo mwintta ofwa.”
Khusala arupaza, malayikha apale khuwaakhola makhono, ye na muukhaawe na aanaawe oowiiri khuwaalawana othetekele, mwaasa wa Nnyizinku wiiyana huruma na-ye.
Paata yoolaziwamo nsitati mphule, nlayikha limote khumuuza yoori: “Tthira wuusuru ohaayi awo, na oheekese nyuma wala oheemele hatha vahali ohifiyeeni omwaako yoori ohipwetheye.”
Loothi khujipu; “Toowo wala safwatali ambwana zaka!
Wakirettela saana, khukoonela huruma venkivene, khuusuru ohaayi aka. Ila onyaako khu woolepawo, opwechiwa wa sitati eti ontta okisikana kihinafiye.
Kharipu apho ewaapho sitati ttiitthiiru, kinwahi otthirela ottuukho. Hatha nkhama yeetta opushuwa, mwikilikhe kitthirele ottuukho kuusurukhe.”
Nlayikha khujipu yoori: “Kakhupali eto ovekiyeeyo, akinteela opwecha sitati yaya eto olupiyeeyo.
Ila waakuve olawe nasaapi ethiiti, miiyo akinretta hatha etthu, weeyo ohifiyeeni ohali onttaawo.” Ti eto sitati yaya eto eniittheliwaaye Zowaari.
Njuwa litthamuwaka na-ye Loothi afiyaka nti wa Zowaari.
Aphano Nnyizinku khukwisa mawe a moottho otulu, akwiselaka Sotooma na Komoora.
Khupwecha sitati epile na miti zaattamananiyeeyo, na atthu aya apale aari wiikhalaamo na tthuttu yaya.
Ila muukha wa Loothi khuzukuluwa khweekesa onyoko ohali aari olankhaawo, khuthatuwa khwiiya sanamu ya mwiinyu.
Supuyeene Eburahiima aalankhiye khulawa puuro etile aari ottakhulanaavo Nnyizinku.
Khweekesa phantte ya Sotooma na Komoora na miti zooshi za shiini yaya etile, khusala oona loosi la waatta leettaka otthuwela mmuti mphule nkhama njocho lookhoziwa.
Nkatthi woopwecha sitati zooshi za tuniya etile, Nluku khufikhiri etile aavekeliweeyo ti Eburahiima, khumuusuru Loothi vakatthi wa pala yaarettikhaniyeeyo sitati etile aari wiikhalaaye.
Loothi eetta woova wiikhala Zowaari, khuthama na aanaawe oowiiri khusala eekhala omwaako. Oottaatthu khusala eekhala nlikurakuza.
Siikhu moote, mwanawe otu nwulu khumuuza otu nttiitthi yoori: “Papeetthu ooluvala na nti opu niriiyo khaamo alume oonirala yoori niwaapatthe aana, nkhama enrettikhanaazo olumwenku wooshi.
Nlawe nithuule viinyu ninnywise papeetthu ahapaliwe, niwahi orapalelana anivokolele aana, yoori peewu ya papeetthu ehiishe.”
Osikhu otthuupule khuthuula viinyu khunnywisa papaaya, mwaana otu nwulu aya khulawa khulalana papaawe. Papantthu woohijuwi wakathi arapaleliyeevo wala alankhiyeevo.
Mmeesho mwaya, otule nwulu khumuuza ttwiiye: “Taana osikhu karapalelana paapa, apho osikhu opu wa leelo nlawe ninhapalise na weeyo olawe warapalelane zwaamu yawo. Anivokolele aana yoori peewu ya papeetthu ehiishe”.
Osikhu otthuupule khumwinkha papaaya viinyu swaafu yaphiiri, na-ye otu nttiitthi aya khulawa khulalana, theenya papantthu khuhijuwi wakathi arapaleliyeevo wala alankhiyeevo.
Aana apale oowiiri khwiimittha erukulu ya papaaya.
Otu nwulu aya khumpattha mwaana wanlume khuntthaja nzina la Mowaabu, ye paapa wa Amowaabu apa ariiwo mpakha leelo.
Elottelanaka otule nttiitthi aya khumpattha mwaana wanlume khuntthaja nzina la Ben-Ami, ye paapa wa Amooni, apa ariiwo mpakha leelo.
Eburahiima aalankhiye Manre khulawa nti wa Nikeepu, khwiikhala enakatthi-nakatthi ya Kateeshi na Shuuri. Khuthamela theenya nti wa Kerari.
Ottuukhule, Eburahiima aalupiye yoori Suhura nlupuwe, khupe ari muukhaawe. Aphano Apimeleekhi mfwalume wa nti aya opule, khuruma weetteliwa Suhura, ye khunthuula.
Osikhu aya, Nluku khunteela Apimeleekhi khusala amuuza nkatthi wa jozi yoori: “Ontta ofwa mwaasa wa muukha otu onthuuliyeeyo, ye onaaye mannawe.”
Ila Apimeleekhi aari ahinarapalelane muukha otule, ye khujipu: “Mbwana, onttela okuula miiyo na atthu aka woohiivo hatha paathuli?
Ti Eburahiima aakuuziye yoori Suhura nlupuwe! Na Suhura khukuuza etthiipo yoori nlupuwe. Miiyo karetta eti na rooho y'ookemaani woohijuwivo etthu.”
Nluku khunjipu njozi nttumphule yoori: “Miiyo kajuwa yoori vitthu epi waretta na rooho y'ookemaani. Ti eto miiyo kiwiinaneliyeeyo yoori ohikikose, pi apho kihuutakheleeni onsapa muukha oto.
Apho, onrutisele mannawe muukha oto. Ye napiyu, ontta wuulompela yoori ohifwe, ila amana ohinrutiseli kiniwuuza khweele yoori ontta ofwa weeyo na zooshi epi ziiyiye zaawo.”
N'oolankha mmeesho mwaya supu, Apimeleekhi khuwaakhuwela mawaziiri awe khusala awooza epile aalotthiyeezo, yo khwiiya awoova channu.
Nawiisha, khuruma okhuweliwa Eburahiima khusala amuuzela yoori: “Niini eti oniretteliyeeyo? Kookosela-ni okikwiselaka paathuli ya twampi khuluyeene nkhama eti, miiyo na atthu aka? Etthu okiretteliyeeyo khinrettelaniwaka.
Woopuweliye niini okirettelaka vitthu nkhama epi?”
Eburahiima khunjipu: “Miiyo kaari woona yoori atthu a nti opu khanimoova Nluku, antta okuula mwaasa wa muukhaaka.
Na khweele phantte kiina nlupwaaka, mwaana wa paapa ila khahiyo mwaana wa maama. Ti nanna afiyeleliyeeyo wiiya muukhaaka.
Wakathi Nluku akilaziyeemo mmuti wa apapazaku, kaamuuziye muukhaaka yoori: ‘Safwatali kintta wuuvekela, wakhula vahali nimfiyaavo osala olupa yoori nlupwaaka’.”
Aphano Apimeleekhi khuthuula pwittipwitthi, mompe na amwiitthwaana aalume na aakha khumwinkha Eburahiima na theenya khunrutisela muukhaawe.
Apimeleekhi khuri: “Nti opu pu waaka ohiiyane shaakha, wiikhale wakhula vahali ontakhaavo.”
Khumuuza Suhura yoori; “Kamwinkha nlupuwo mizurukhu za feeta alufu, ajamaazo ooshi ajuwe yoori khutthekeeni hatha etthu, na ahiiyevo antakhaaye owaakanyerela.”
Nnyizinku aawaarettiye aakha ooshi a vaje wa Apimeleekhi yoori ahisala avokola, mwaasa wa epile zanrettikhaneliyeeyo Suhura muukha wa Eburahiima. Aphano Eburahiima khunvekela Nluku zwaamu ya Apimeleekhi, Nluku khunvonisa vamote na muukhaawe na akarumeyaawe aakha yoori asala avokola.
<range>
Paata ya toole, Nnyizinku khumparikhiya Suhura, khunrettela etile aamwaahitiyeeyo.
Suhura khwiimittha khumpattha mwaana wa Eburahiima ari wa wuuluvala, wakathi otthuupule Nluku aamuuziyeeyo.
Mwaana otule aavokoliweeyo ti Suhura, Eburahiima khuntthaja nzina la Esiyaakha.
Siikhu yanaane, Eburahiima khunthuula mwaana otule khulawa onkhiriyisa nkhama etthiipo Nluku anrumiyeezo.
Wakathi Eburahiima ampatthiyeevo mwanawe Esiyaakha, aarettiye arina nyaakha miiya.
Suhura khuri: “Nluku akinkha otheya, na atthu ooshi apale anttelaaye osiila anttela otheya vamote na-miyo.
Paani aari waakanyeraaye yoori Eburahiima aari oteela ompatthela mwaana Suhura? Na wuuluvala wawe, miiyo kampatthela mwaana!”
Mwaana otule khusala awula mpakha ofiyelela olikha nziwa. Alikhiyeevo nziwa mwaana otule, papaawe khuretta njampo la furaha.
Ila Suhura khumoona Esumayila mwaana wa Hajira mmisuri, otule aavokoliweeyo ti Eburahiima anveyisaka mwanawe.
Suhura khulawa omuuza Eburahiima yoori: “Omwiikare njaazi otule na mwanawe. Ye khanteela orithi vamote na mwanaka Esiyaakha.”
Eburahiima khwiiya woozinkireya na kuvu na mattakhuzi apale mwaasa wa Esumayila wiiya mwanawe.
Aphano Nluku khumuuza Eburahiima yoori: “Ohizinkireye mwaasa wa mwanawo na njaazi awo, osiileze etile aniwuuzaaye Suhura, mwaasa yoori peewu yawo enttela olankha vakatthi wa Esiyaakha.
Mwaana wa njaazi otule onteela wiiyana omathi wa waatta mwaasa yoori na-ye peewu yawo.”
Mmeesho mwaya, Eburahiima khuthuula phaawu na ttompwiyo ya maati, khunvikelisa Hajira khunleeza vamote na mwanawe. Yo khusala alawa ajeettettelaka n'yaara ya Beeresheba ahijuwaka ohali anttaawo.
Wakathi amwiisheliyeevo maati nttompwiyo, ye khunlikha mwanawe nshini wa muutthi.
Khulankha khulawa khwiikhala ohali woolepawo vattitthiiru na okhule aariiwo mwanawe, mwaasa yoori khaari otakha omoona mwanawe afwaka. Eekhaliye etthiipile, khusala alila.
Nluku khusiila theenya huula ya mwaana otule eettaka olila. Nlayikha la Nluku khukhuwa pinkuuni linkhuwelaka Hajira, khumuuza yoori: “Wakafilikhela-ni Hajira? Ohoove, Nluku asiila huula yawe mwaana oto alilaka vahali ariivo.
Olankhe onlanse mwanawo onkholele nkhono, phantte yawe kinteela waattisa omathaawe.”
Elottelanaka Nluku khunthoonyeza Hajira nlipu wa maati, khulawa khuttekhelela ttompwiyo yawe khunnywisa mwanawe.
Esumayila khusala awula mmakhono wa Nluku. Ye aari wiikhala n'yaara na aari njuwi wa weesa mattetthe.
Aari wiikhala n'yaara ya Paraani, mamaawe khumweekesela muukha wa Misuri khunlooza.
Wakathi aya opo, Apimeleekhi aalokoziwe ti Fikhoole namalokozela wa anajanka, khumuuza Eburahiima yoori: “Nluku ori vamote na-weyo khwa wakhula etile onrettaaye.
Nasaapi ethiiti olaphe khwa nzina la Nluku yoori khunteela okihata miiyo wala aanaaka ama otuulwaka, nkhama etthiipile kuuretteliyeezo zooshapweya, na-miyo okirettele etthiipo na mmuti mphu oniikhalaamo.”
Khujipu Eburahiima araka: “Miiyo kinlapha”.
Attaaphale Eburahiima khusala ajiliza mwaasa wa nlipu aanyakanyiweeyo pi akarumeyaawe Apimeleekhi.
Apimeleekhi khunjipu: “Miiyo akaajuwiyevo etthu na khawaakuuziye, kintta osiilaru nasaapi ethiiti.”
Aphano Eburahiima khuthuula pwittipwitthi na mompe khumwinkha Apimeleekhi. Oowiiri aya khusiilana.
Elottelanaka Eburahiima khuphakula pwittipwitthi sapa za nliphanko lawe.
Apimeleekhi khumuuzela yoori: “Pwittipwitthi epo sapa omphakulaaye maana aya niini?”
Eburahiima khujipu: “Okhupalele pwittipwitthi epi sapa kiniwinkhaaye khwa lifunku looshaahiti yoori nlipu opu ti miyo kithipiyeeyo.”
Pi apho puuro yaya eto eniitthiwaaye Beeresheba, mwaasa yoori oowiiri aya aalaphisaniye attaapho.
Paata yawiisha oosiilana opule Beeresheba okhule aariiwo, Apimeleekhi na Fikhoole namalokozela wa anajanka, khurutela nti wa Afiliishiti.
Eburahiima n'oosala Beeresheba okhule khuzala muutthi wa nkolokope, khumwaaputu Nnyizinku, Nluku wa Mileele.
Ye khwiikhala nti wa Afiliishiti khwa nyaakha za waatta.
Paata yoovira nyaakha, Nluku aamweeziye Eburahiima, khunkhuwela araka: “Eburahiima!” Ye khujipu: “Lapeekha!”
Nluku khumuuza araka: “Onthuule mwanawo Esiyaakha, othuuto mmote oriinaaye onimphetachaaye, olawe mpakha nti wa Moriya, vamwaako oriiye ottuukho kinttelaaye wuuthoonyeza, onrette twaha yoolukuziwa”.
Ye khulankha mmeesho mwaya lifwajiri khunthuula puuru awe khufukavo zaana zawe, khuwaathuula akarumeyaawe awiri na mwanawe Esiyaakha. Khurema khuuni zoolawa orettela twaha yoolukuziwa, khusala alawa ottuukhule Nluku aamuuziyeewo.
Siikhu yattaatthu, Eburahiima khweesa maasho awe khoona puuro etile ari ohali woolepawo.
Ye khuwooza akarumeyaawe apale yoori: “Mwisale attaapha na puuru otu, miiyo na shapu otu nintta aphale, ninttela omwaaputu Nluku. Amana niisha nintta oruti nite niiye vamote na-mweyo.”
Eburahiima khuthuula khuuni epile aari weettelaaye orettela twaha yoolukuziwa, khunttikha Esiyaakha mmafuzi mwawe. Ye khuthuula eesu na moottho khusala alawa.
Esiyaakha khunkhuwela papaawe yoori: “Mweyo paapa!” Ye khujipu: “Lape mwanaka!” Aphano Esiyaakha khumuuzela papaawe: “Nathuula moottho na khuuni, khi pwittipwitthi yoolawa otwahi eri vayi?”
Ye khujipu araka: “Nluku ti ye anjuwaaye pwittipwitthi ninttelaaye orettela twaha yoolukuziwa mwanaka.” Yo khusala alawa vamote.
N'oofiya ohali okhule aathoonyeziweewo ti Nluku, khunjeka alitaari vatulu vaya khuthatelavo khuuni. Khumfuka mwanawe Esiyaakha khunttha vatulu wa khuuni.
Khuthuula eesu, khulansa makhono awe yoori antwahi mwanawe.
Ila nlayikha la Nnyizinku khukhuwa pinkuuni liraka: “Eburahiima! Eburahiima!” Ye khujipu: “Lapeekha!”
Khumuuza yoori: “Ohimwaavulele eesu shapu oto, na ohinrettele hatha etthu. Aphano kinjuwa yoori onimoova Nluku, mwaasa woohikikhattazi mwanawo mmote othuuto oriina.”
Eburahiima khuzukuluwa khoona pwittipwitthi ewayiye manyaka aya valikukhu. Ye khulawa khuthuula khurettela twaha yoolukuziwa khwa zwaamu ya mwanawe.
Aphano khutthaja nzina puuro etile “Nnyizinku ti ye anjuwaaye”. Mpakha eleelo eti oniittheliwavo yoori: “omwaako wa Nnyizinku ti ye anjuwaaye”.
Elottelanaka, nlayikha la Nnyizinku khukhuwa theenya pinkuuni linkhuwelaka Eburahiima.
Khumuuza yoori: “Nnyizinku ari: ‘Kinjilaphela ki mwennyeweru, mwaasa weeyo oretta etile kiwuuziyeeyo, ohikikhattazi mwanawo mmote paasi oriinaayo,
khweele, kinteela wuuparikhiya na kiwinkhe peewu ya waatta nkhama matthottowa o'otulu na mishaka za mmattima, yo anteela othuula nti wa maatuwi aya.
Atthu ooshi a voolumwenku anteela oparikhiyiwa, mwaasa wa peewu yawo, maana weeyo wakishututela.’”
Eburahiima na Esiyaakha khurutela aphale aawaalikhiyeevo akarumeyaawe. Ooshi khurutela Beeresheba ohali Eburahiima aari wiikhalaawo.
N'oovira vitthu epile khuuziwa Eburahiima oriwa: “Miilika avokoleliwa aana ti ttwiiyo Nahoori;
w'oomwanzo aya nzina lawe ti Wuuzi, na ttwiiye Buuzi, khulotteliwa ti Kemuweeli, papaawe Aramu,
Keseeti, Haazo, Pilitashi, Yitalafu, na Betuweeli.”
Betuweeli khunvokola Repeekha. Aana apo wanaane aawaavokoliye ti Miilika na Nahoori ttwiiye Eburahiima.
Nahoori aarina muukha nkinoko aari wiitthiwaaye Rewuma, na-ye anvokoleliye aana; Teepa, Kahaamu, Tahaashi na Maaka.
Suhura eekhaliye nyaakha miiya na eshiriini na sapa.
Khufwa Kiriyati-Aarapa (oniittheliwaawo Heporooni) tuniya ya Kanaani. Eburahiima khusala alila na ojikhupanyera ofwa wa Suhura.
Ye khunlikha muukhaawe ari woofwa, khulawa ottakhulana Ahiiti yoori:
“Miiyo ki mmalapo na ki nletto mmuti mphu; ila kinuuvekelani okinkha ruhusa ya wiiyana vilalo yaka mmuti mwenu mphu, yoori kinzikhemo muukhaaka.”
Ahiiti apale khunjipu Eburahiima yoori:
“Osiileze mbwaneetthu, fweeyo niniwinkha hishima nkhama mfwalume wa Nluku. Apho olawe wanzikhe muukhaawo wakhula vilalo etile enuufwayaaye. Khaavo mmote wa fweyo antakhaaye wuukhattaza khapuri yonzikhavo muukhaawo.”
Aphano Eburahiima khulankha khwiinama omaasho wa Ahiiti, ennyewe nti opule.
Khuwuuza yoori: “Nkhama khweele mwinaaye niiya yookikhupalela onzikha muukhaaka, mwikivekelele Eforoni, mwaana wa Zohaari,
yoori akuuzanyeze likurakuza la Makhipeela liriiye mmwiinano wa nshapa lawe. Miiyo kininripha hisapu yoolikana mooshi moonaka, yoori likurakuza laya nttho liiye vilalo yoowaazikhamo ajamaazaku”.
Eforoni, Nhiiti otule, aarettiye eekhaliye vamote na attunkhulu a sitati ethiitile, ye khunjipu Eburahiima vakatthi wa Ahiiti ooshi aari vanlako wa sitati ethiitile yoori:
“Wala mbwanaaka! Okisiileze, miiyo kiniwinkha nshapa na likurakuza liriiye nttumpho, kiniwinkha atthu ooshi apa ariiye apha eettaka woona. Olawe wanzikhe muufwi awo.”
Eburahiima khwiinama swaafu yaphiiri, omaasho wa atthu apale a mmuti mphule.
Ye khumuuza Eforoni atthu ooshi eettaka osiila yoori: “Safwatali mwikisiileze, kintta oripha hisapu la nshapa ntthile. Okhupalele yoori kiwahi onzikhamo muukhaaka.”
Eforoni khunjipu Eburahiima yoori:
“Okisiileze mbwanaaka! Nti aya opo pu wa mizurukhu za feeta miiya nne. Eto yaya niini miiyo na weeyo? Wanzikhemo muufwi awo.”
Hisapu etile aalupiyeeyo Eforoni atthu ooshi asiilaka, Eburahiima khukhupalela. Khuphima miphimo miiya nne za mizurukhu wa feeta khumwinkha, nkhama etthiipo aari ophimakaazo anamuuzanyisa.
Waaza attaapho nshapa la Eforoni laariiye Makhipeela kharipu na Manre, na likurakuza laariimo na miitthi zooshi khwinkhiwa Eburahiima. Ahiiti ooshi apale aari vanlako wa sitati etile eettaka woona.
<range>
Wakathi enkhiweevo nti aya opule, khunthuula muukhaawe Suhura khulawa khunzikha nlikurakuza la Makhipeela kharipu na Manre eriiye Heporooni, tuniya ya Kanaani.
Khwa etthiipo, khuhakikhiwa nshapa ntthile na likurakuza laya pi Ahiiti wiiya vilalo ya Eburahiima.
Eburahiima aarettiye ooluvaliye arina nyaakha za waatta, Nnyizinku amparikhiyiye khwa zooshi.
Siikhu moote, khumuuza karumeya nwulu wa vaje vawe aari weettettisaaye mali zawe zooshi aariinaazo, araka: “Othuule nkhono awo otthe vathi wa liphaja laka yoori
kuulaphise khwa nzina la Nnyizinku, Nluku wa pinkuuni na vathi, yoori khunteela omweekesa muukha wa nti otthuupu kiniikhalaaye wa wiiya mwaana wa Akanaani.
Ila olankhe olawe nti w'oowaka wamweekese muukha vakatthi wa ajamaazaku, ate eeye muukha wa Esiyaakha.”
Karumeya otule khumuuzela yoori: “Khi amana muukha aya oto ahitakhi ota na-miyo mmuti mphu, kinthuule mwanawo kinlawane nti otthuupo olankhiyeeyo?”
Eburahiima khunjipu: “Phoole! Hatha vattitthiiru ohirette onlawana mwanaka.
Nnyizinku, Nluku wa pinkuuni akilaza vaje wa apapazaku nti wa ajamaazaku khukaahiti na olapha araka: ‘Nti opu kinttela winkha peewu yawo.’ Ye ontta operekha nlayikha lawe yoori luulokoze, omweettele muukha yoori ate araliwe ti mwanaka Esiyaakha.
Amana muukha aya oto ahitakhi ota na-weyo, olapha wawo oniiya woofujeya. Ila ohiiye wonthuula mwanaka onlawana.”
Aphano karumeya otule khuthuula nkhono awe khuttha vathi wa liphaja la Eburahiima mbwanaawe. Khulapha yoori aari weettela oretta etthiipile ooziweezo.
Karumeya otule khuthuula enkamiiya khumi za mbwanaawe na majathi apale enkhiweeyo khusala alawa nti wa Mezapotaaniya sitati ya Nahoori.
Afiiyeevo, njuwa looveva wakathi opule aakha anttelakaaye ottekha maati, khukokhorisa enkamiiya zawe epile onlipu kharipu ya sitati.
Attaaphale khusala alompa araka: “Oh! Nnyizinku, Nluku wa mbwanaaka Eburahiima, kinuuvekela yoori siikhu eti ya leelo okiparikhiye, na onthoonyeze pheta ya waamineya mbwanaaka Eburahiima.
Onikoonelaavo apha kiri wa weemela kharipu na nlipu, aanaakha a atthu a sitati eti antakaavo ottekha maati.
Mwaari othuuto kinttelaaye omuuza yoori: ‘Wiinamise yuuku yawo okimeele maati kinywe,’ ye khulupa yoori: ‘Apa nywa, na kintta onywisa enkamiiya zawo,’ eeye othuuto onthawuleliyeeyo Esiyaakha. Ti etthu enttelaaye okijuwisa yoori wanthoonyeza pheta ya waamineya mbwanaaka Eburahiima.”
Ahineeshe olompa, nasaapiru onimoona Rapekha mwaana wa Betuweeli eettaka ota alankhaka nsitati athuuliye yuuku atthiye valifuzi. Betuweeli aari mwaana wa Miilika muukha wa Nahoori, ttwiiye Eburahiima.
Rapekha aari mwaari wooshapweya channu woohinjuwi nlume, ye khwiishukhela vanlipu khuttekha maati khwiitaaza yuuku yawe khuwelela.
Karumeya otule khulankha khusala antthirela, khumuuza yoori: “Safwatali kimeele maati apo ari n'yuku mwawo kinywe.”
Ye khujipu araka: “Mwiinyi apa mwinywe.” Khurula yuuku khukholelela mmakhono khumwinkha khunywa.
Nawiisha omwinkha maati, khumuuza yoori: “Kinttela ottekha makina theenya kinkhe enkamiiya zenu zinywe mpakha zooshi ziishe”
Nasaapiru khwiitthela maati apale n'yopo zaari onywaamo nyama, khwaakuva khulawa vanlipu ottekha swaafu za waatta yoori zinywe enkamiiya zooshi.
Mwinyi otule khusala anyamaliye amweekesaka mwaari otule saaneene yoori ajuwe nkhama Nnyizinku aparikhiya safwari yawe ama wala.
Ziishiyeevo onywa enkamiiya epile, khulaza kharawu ya thahapu ya karaama sitha na kakhana piiri za thahapu zaari ochiraaye karaama miiya olemela waya khunwalisa mmakhono mwawe.
Khumuuzela yoori: “Weeyo o mwaana waani? Safwatali nkakuuze nkhama wa papaawo ewaakho puuro y'oolalawo miiyo na ashirikhaaka apa.”
Ye khujipu: “Miiyo ki mwaana wa Betuweeli, mwaana wa Miilika na Nahoori.
Onti ewaakho puuro yoolalawo mweeyo, na nyaani za waatta zooja enkamiiya zenu.”
Aphano karumeya otule khukokhora khumwaaputu Nnyizinku,
araka: “Asifwiwe Nnyizinku, Nluku wa mbwanaaka Eburahiima, ahisahaweeni onthoonyeza pheta yawe ya waamineya, maana akilokoza mpakha vaje wa ajamaaze mbwanaaka.”
Aphano mwaari otule khutthira eettaka owawe, khuwooza ajamaaze vitthu zaarettikhaniyeezo.
Rapekha aarina nlupuwe aari wiitthiwaaye Labani. Ye khutthira eettaka onlipu yoori amoone ntthu aya otule.
Mwaasa wa woona kharawu na kakhana aawalisiweeyo nlupuwe, na khusiila vitthu ooziweeyo Rapekha ti nlume otule, ye khulankha khusala alawa omoona nlume otule ottuukhule aariiwo na enkamiiya zawe nshini wa nlipu.
Labani khuri: “Ote okhuno, weeyo wooparikhiyiwa ti Nnyizinku! Weekhalela-ni veetakale apho? Kawaattalelela puuro onti na vahali woopwehavo enkamiiya zawo.”
Labani khuta na karumeya otule mpakha owawe, khuruma wiishushiwa mapwattha vankamiiya epile na khwinkhiwa nyaani yoori zije. Khwinkhiwa maati yoori oose moolu awe na atthu apale aarinaaye.
Nawiisha khutiisiwa etthu-yooja khwinkhiwa, ila karumeya otule khuri: “Akinja kihaazeeni olupa eti kaateeliyeeyo.” Labani khumuuza yoori: “Haya lupa.”
Aphano khwaaza olupa araka: “Miiyo ki karumeya wa Eburahiima.
Nnyizinku amparikhiya venkivene, amwinkha maali khwiiya woojuwanikha; onaaye pwittipwitthi na mompe, feeta na thahapu, akarumeya aalume na aakha, enkamiiya na apuuru.
Suhura muukha wa mbwanaaka Eburahiima, anvokola mwaana ooluvaliye. Mwaana aya otu amwinkha vitthu zooshi ariinaazo.
Mbwanaaka khukilaphisa araka: ‘Nti opu kiniikhalaaye ohimweekesemo muukha wa aana a Akanaani.
Ila olawe wa apapazaku vakatthi wa ajamaazaku wamweekese ottuukho muukha yoori ate araliwe ti mwanaka.’
Aphano miiyo khunjipu mbwanaaka: ‘Khi muukha aya oto amana ahitakhi ota na-miyo?’
Ye khukijipu yoori: ‘Nnyizinku otu kininrumeelaaye ontta operekha nlayikha luulokoze, na ontta oparikhiya safwari yawo yoolawa omweekesa muukha wa wiiya jamaayaku na wa vaje wa apapazaku yoori ate araliwe ti mwanaka.
Amana ofiya wa ajamaazaku yo khuhitakhi owinkha, eti koolaphisiyeeyo entta owiishela.’
Phi kiriyeevo n'oofiya onlipu leelo, khusala kimuuza Nnyizinku kiraka: ‘Oo Nnyizinku! Nluku wa mbwanaaka Eburahiima, nkhama safwari eti kineettaaye otakha wawo, okijaaliwe.
Nasaapi eti miiyo kiri apha nshini wa nlipu opu wa maati; mwaari othuuto antelaaye ottekha maati amana kinvekela yoori: “Kimeele maati ariiye n'yuku mwawo,”
ye khukuuza yoori: “Apa onywe, na kinttela ottekha makina kinkhe nyama zawo,” eeye othuuto muukha aya athawuliweeyo ti Nnyizinku yoori araliwe ti mwaana wa mbwanaaka.’
Ahineeshevo mattakhuzi apale oolompa varoho vaka, kinimoona Rapekha athuuliye yuuku valifuzi vawe eettaka vanlipu ottekha maati, miiyo khumuuza yoori: ‘Safwatali kimeele maati kinywe.’
Ye khwiishusha yuuku yawe nasaapiru khukuuza yoori: ‘Apa onywe, na kintta winkha enkamiiya zawo zinywe.’ Khukinkha miiyo khunywa na khwiinkha enkamiiya zaka khunywa.
Aphano miiyo khumuuzela yoori: ‘O mwaana waani?’ Ye khujipu yoori: ‘Miiyo ki mwaana wa Betuweeli mwaana wa Nahoori na Miilika.’ Ethiito miiyo khunwalisa kharawu vaphula vawe khunwalisa kakhana makhono awe.
Miiyo khukokhora, khwiinama khumwaaputu Nnyizinku, khunshukhurwela Nnyizinku, Nluku wa mbwanaaka Eburahiima akeettettisiyeeyo tarikhi yooshapweya yoori kimweettele mwaana wa ttwiiye mbwanaaka ate araliwe ti mwanawe.
Aphano, nkhama mwatakha onthoonyeza pheta ya waamineya mbwanaaka Eburahiima, mwikuuze. Nkhama khamweepu, mwikuuze kijuwe etthu yooretta.”
Labani na Betuwele khujipu araka: “Epo zalankha wa Nnyizinku, fweeyo khanina etthu yoowaza.
Rapekha aya otu ari apha, onthuule alawe eeye muukha wa mwaana wa mbwanaawo, etthiipo Nnyizinku alupiyeezo.”
N'oosiila mattakhuzi apale karumeya wa Eburahiima khukokhora khwiinama khufiyisa ajihi vathi omaasho wa Nnyizinku.
