Elottelanaka khusarula vitthu za feeta na za thahapu na kuwo khumwinkha Rapekha, khulaza vitthu kiina theenya za mali khumwinkha nlupuwe na mamaawe.
Nawiisha, yo khuja na khunywela khulala mpakha supu. N'oocha karumeya otule khulupa yoori: “Mwikilikhe kirutele wa mbwanaaka.”
Ila nlupuwe Rapekha na mamaawe khumuuza yoori: “Mwaari otu eekhale attaapha na-fweyo nenkawu siikhu khumi, nawiisha osala olawa saana.”
Ye khuri: “Mwihikirupazise maana Nnyizinku ashapweyisa safwari yaka. Mwikilikhe kirutele wa mbwanaaka.”
Aphano yo khunjipu: “Nintta onkhuwela mwaari oto nimuuzele mwennyewe.”
Khukhuweliwa Rapekha khuuzeliwa: “Ontakha olawa na mwinyi otu?” Ye khujipu yoori: “Kakhupali.”
Ajamaaze khuleezanana Rapekha na yaaya awe na karumeya wa Eburahiima na atthu apale aataniyeeyo.
Khuparikhiyiwa Rapekha na mattakhuzi apa: “Weeyo nlupweetthu wiiye maama wa peewu alufu alufu zene; Peewu yawo eto eshintte sitati ya maatuwi aya.”
Rapekha khulankha na akarumeyaawe a aakha khuwela enkamiiya zaya khusala alawa na nlume otule. Attaaphale karumeya khunthuula Rapekha khusala alawa.
Esiyaakha aarettiye arutaka onlipu oniitthiwaaye Layi-Rooyi, aari wiikhala Nikeepu, phantte ya kusini ya Kanaani.
Siikhu moote, njuwa-looveva wakathi Esiyaakha aari othepelaavo mmashapa, khulansa maasho khoona enkamiiya zeettaka ota.
Rapekha khulansa maasho khumoona Esiyaakha, ye khwiishukha vankamiiya vawe.
Khumuuzela karumeya: “Khi mwinyi otule anlankhaaye mmashapa mphule ataka okhuno niriiwo ti paani?” Ye khujipu araka: “Ti mbwanaaka.” N'oosiila toole ye khuthuula nshukwi lawe khujifinikha.
Karumeya khumuuza Esiyaakha zooshi epile ziviriyeezo.
Esiyaakha khunthuula Rapekha khunttha nheema etile yaari ya mamaawe Suhura. Khunrala khwiiya muukhaawe wompheta. Aphano Esiyaakha khumpattha ntthu wonkhiza paata yoofwa mamaawe.
Eburahiima khunrala muukha nkina aari wiitthiwaaye Khetuura.
Ye khunvokolela aana apa: Zimraani, Yokishaani, Medaani, Midiyaani, Ishibaaki na Shuuwa.
Yokshaani khunvokola Sheeba na Dedaani, aana a Dedaani aari Waashuuru, Waletushi na Walewumi.
Aana a Midiyaani aari Eefa, Eferi, Hanooki, Abiida na Eelida. Ooshi apa aari aana na atuulu a Khetuura.
Eburahiima khumwinkha Esiyaakha vitthu zooshi aariinaazo.
Ila aanaawe apale aawaavokoleliyeeyo na aakha akina, ari haayi nalelo, khuwenkha vitthu zaya na-yo, khuweekarela phantte ya malawa-juwa yoori ahiikhale vamote na mwanawe Esiyaakha.
Eburahiima eekhaliye nyaakha miiya na saapiini na mithaanu.
Ye afwa ari wa wuuluvala arina nyaakha za waatta, khulawa khuzikhiwa vamote na ajamaaze apa afwiiyeeyo.
Esiyaakha na Esumayila, khunthuula khulawa khunzikha nlikurakuza la Makhipeela kharipu na Manre, nshapa la Eforoni mwaana wa Zohaari nhiiti.
Nshapa nttintthile oozanyeziweeyo Eburahiima pi Ahiiti, pi ottuukho azikhiweewo ye na muukhaawe Suhura.
Paata ya Eburahiima ofwa, Esiyaakha aari wiikhala nti wa Peeri-Lahayi-Rooyi, Nnyizinku khusala amparikhiya.
Eti hatiithi ya peewu ya Esumayila mwaana wa Eburahiima, aavokoliweeyo ti Hajira wa Misuri karumeya wa Suhura.
Apa mazina a aana aavokoliweeyo ti Esumayila: Nebayoothi, mwaana wa mwanzo wa Esumayila, Kedaari, Adibeeli, Mibisaamu.
Miishima, Duuma na Maasa.
Hadaadi, Teema, Yetuuri, Nafiishi na Kedeema.
Apa aana Esumayila khumi na awiri, pi atthaapo aari afwalume, wakhula mwaana na lihimo lawe na nhali aari omakaamo.
Esumayila eekhaliye nyaakha miiya na talaathiini na sapa. Khufwa khulawa khuzikhiwa vamote na ajamaaze apa afwiiyeeyo.
Peewu yawe yeekhaliye waaza Hawila mpakha Shuuri kharipu na Misuri tarikhi yaweetta Ashuuru. Yo aari woohisiilani na ojama nkina wa Eburahiima.
Eti hatiithi ya peewu ya Esiyaakha mwaana wa Eburahiima: Eburahiima khunvokola Esiyaakha.
Esiyaakha n'oopattha hirimo ya nyaakha arupayiini khunrala Rapekha mwaana wa Betuweeli, nlupuwe Labani. Yo aari Araamu aari wiikhalaaye Paata-Araamu, tuniya ya Mesopotamiya.
Mwaasa wa muukhaawe ohiina mavokozi, Esiyaakha khulompa wa shariyavo anvekelaka Nnyizinku. Ye khusiila lompa yawe Rapekha khwiimittha.
Aana awiri khusala oomana mwiirukulu mwawe. Ye khushanka khusala ajuuzela yoori: “Niini enrettikhanaaye mwiirukulu mwaka, nkhama pi toono keemitthela-ni?” Aphano ye khumuuzela Nnyizinku.
Nnyizinku khunjipu: “Mahimo mawiri pi ariiye mwiirukulu mwawo. Weeyo onttela ovokola khapila piiri zoohisiilani: moote enttela wiiya ya kuvu zayita eti kiina. Nttunkhulu onteela onrumeyela nsimaana.”
Zifiiyeevo siikhu zoopattha ekumi, khuwaavokola aana a maphapo.
Otu woovokoliwa mwanzo aari wookhuttuwa na wa waatta ovuzi, ti maana yootthajiwa nzina la Ezawu.
Elottelanaka khuvokoliwa ttwiiye, nkhono awe okholeliye ekwakuno ya Ezawu. Ti maana yootthajiwa nzina la Yaakhumpa. Ampattikhanaru aana aya apa, Esiyaakha aarettiye arina nyaakha siithiini.
Aana apale khuwula, Ezawu khwiiya namasaya nwulu na aari wontuvela weettetta ntthuttu, ila Yaakhumpa aari ntthu woonyamala wontuvela wiikhala vaje.
Esiyaakha aari ompheta Ezawu, mwaasa wontuvela orafuna nyama epile aari osayaazo. Ila Rapekha aari ompheta Yaakhumpa.
Siikhu moote, Yaakhumpa khwiipikha sekuseku, wakathi aya opo Ezawu aarettiye eettaka orutiru ntthuttu ari wookholiwa ti jala na wooshokhera.
Ye khumuuza Yaakhumpa yoori: “Okinkhe vitthu epo oniipikhaazo zookhuttuwela kije. Kintakha ofwa jala!” Ti eto Ezawu enkhiweeyo nzina la Edomu.
Yaakhumpa khumuuza yoori: “Waaze okuuzanyeza lifunku lawo l'oomwaana w'oomwanzo khapula.”
Ye khumuuza yoori: “Lina fwayita-ni lifunku laya nttho la wiiya mwaana wa mwanzo, miiyo kitakhaka ofwa jala!”
Yaakhumpa khusala ankhanyarela yoori: “Olaphe.” Ye khulapha, khumuuzanyeza Yaakhumpa lifunku lawe l'oomwaana wa mwanzo.
Aphano ye khumwinkha Ezawu phaawu na sekuseku y'eepwiri. Khuja khunywela, khusala alawa safwari zawe. Woohooneli fwayita lifunku l'oomwaana wa mwanzo.
Yaapuwiye jala nti opule nkhama etthiipile yaapuwiyeezo wakathi wa Eburahiima. Ti eto Esiyaakha khulawa nti wa Geraari okutthanana Apimeleekhi mfwalume wa Afiliishiti.
Nnyizinku khunteela, khumuuza yoori: “Ohilawe tuniya ya Misuri; weekhale nti kintakhaaye owuuza.
Ottuukho miiyo kinttela wiiya vamote na-weyo na kinttela wuuparikhiya. Weeyo na peewu yawo kinttela owinkhani nti opo wooshi, kilipiselaka wahati opule kaalaphiyeeyo kimwaahitaka papaawo Eburahiima.
Kinttela waattisa peewu yawo nkhama matthottowa o'otulu, na kinttela winkha tuniya yooshi eti. Mwaasa wa peewu yawo, khapila zooshi za tuniya zinttela wiiya zooparikhiyiwa;
maana Eburahiima asiileza huula yaka, ashututela oruma waka, mwentto aka, kano zaka na masomi aka.”
Aphano Esiyaakha khusala eekhala nti wa Geraari.
Atthu a nti opule n'oomuuzela monkoni wa muukhaawe, ye khuri: “Nlupwaaka.” Mwaasa yoori Rapekha aari wooshapweya, Esiyaakha eetta woova olupa yoori muukhaawe. Ye aari wuupuwela yoori alume a mmuti mphule eetta omuula asale na Rapekha.
Esiyaakha eekhaliye Geraari siikhu za waatta. Siikhu moote, Apimeleekhi mfwalume wa Afiliishiti eetta othurumela veettakha khumoona Esiyaakha ampapasaka muukhaawe.
Aphano Apimeleekhi khunkhuwela Esiyaakha khumuuza yoori: “Otu, khweele muukhaawo! Khi apho waari oraaye nlupuwo?” Ye khujipu yoori: “Kaari woova wuuliwa mwaasa wa ye.”
Apimeleekhi khuri: “Epo zaya niini oniretteliyeeyo? Khi eriwaka ntthu mmote wa fweyo eettiye olalana, weeyo waari onittha paathuli?”
Apimeleekhi khuwooza atthu ooshi yoori: “Wakhula otule antakhaaye onsapa mwinyi otu ama muukhaawe ontta ofwa.”
Esiyaakha khulima nshapa lawe nti otthuupule, mwaasa wa Nnyizinku omparikhiya mwaakha otthuupo khuurula vitthu swaafu miiya zooziti epile aazaliyeezo.
Ye khureela, khusala evira zeekezeleyaka mali zawe, khwiiya thaajiri nwuulweene.
Aarina maphanko a pwittipwitthi, puuzi, a mompe na aarina akarumeya a waatta, ti nanna Afiliishiti laawaatiyeeyo nrima.
Milipu zooshi epile aathipiyeeyo akarumeya a Eburahiima paapa wa Esiyaakha ari haayi, khusirelaza.
Siikhu moote Apimeleekhi khumuuza Esiyaakha yoori: “Oleemo mmuti mphu, maana wareela na kuvu waniziti fweeyo.”
Aphano ye khuthama nti opule, khulawa khumaka nttapo la Geraari khwiikhala ottuukho.
Khuthipa opheya milipu epile zaathipiweeyo wakathi wa Eburahiima, khusireliwa pi Afiliishiti paata yoofwa Eburahiima, Esiyaakha khwinkha mazina milipu epile atthaapale papaawe aatthajiyeeyo.
Siikhu kiina, akarumeyaawe khuthipa mmattapo nttumphule, khunsikana naattuuttu wa maati.
Amakhampuzi a Geraari khusala anyakulisana na amakhampuzi a Esiyaakha araka: “Maati apa pi eetthu,” ti eto Esiyaakha aatthajiyeeyo nzina la Eseki nlipu aya opule, mwaasa yoori weetta wuumaneliwa.
Akarumeyaawe khuthipa nlipu nkina, ila amakhampuzi apale a Geraari khupuwisa wuumani theenya, ye khutthaja nzina la Sitiina (milattu).
Aphano khulaavo aphale vaya khulawa khuthipa nlipu nkina, khuhiivo hatha ntthu mmote wa wuumanelana. Ye khutthaja nzina la Rehopoothi araka: “Aphano Nnyizinku aninkha puuro ya nafwaasi, na ninteela oruwera saaneene nti otthuupu.”
Attaaphale Esiyaakha khulawa Beerisheba.
Osikhu Nnyizinku khunteela khumuuza yoori: “Miiyo ki Nluku wa papaawo Eburahiima. Ohoove, kiri vamote na-weyo. Kintta wuuparikhiya kaattise peewu yawo mwaasa wa papaawo karumeyaaka.”
Attaaphale ye khunjeka alitaari, khwaaputu nzina la Nnyizinku. Khweemesa heema yawe na akarumeyaawe khuthipavo nlipu.
Apimeleekhi aalankhiye nti wa Geraari na shawuriiya awe Ahuzaathi na Fikhoole namalokozela wa anajanka olawa okutthanana Esiyaakha.
Esiyaakha n'oowoona khuwooza yoori: “Mweeyo khamwintuveliwa ti miyo mweettiye okiikara mmuti mwenu. Khi mwatela-ni?”
Yo khunjipu araka: “Neetta woona yoori Nnyizinku ori vamote na-weyo. Khuupuwela yoori enshapweya olapha na winkhana wahati weeyo na-fweyo.
Osiilana waya pi opu: Olaphe yoori khunnirettela zootakhala nkhama etthiipo na-fweyo nihuuretteleeni, noorettela zooshapweya na khuulikha olawa na heeri. Weeyo o wooparikhiyiwa ti Nnyizinku.”
Esiyaakha khuwenkha etthu-yooja yooshapweya khuja khunywela.
Mmeesho mwaya supuyeene khulaphisana. Esiyaakha khuwaaleeza, yo khusala alawa na heeri.
Siikhu ethiitile khuta akarumeya a Esiyaakha oteela omuuza hapari za nlipu opule aathipiyeeyo yoori: “Napattha maati.”
Nlipu aya opule Esiyaakha khutthaja nzina la Sheba. Mpakha leelo sitati yaya etile eniittheliwa Beeresheba.
Wakathi Ezawu apatthiyeevo nyaakha arupayiini khunrala Yudiithi mwaana wa nhiiti aniitthiwaaye Beeri, na Basemaathi mwaana wa nhiiti nkinoko aniitthiwaaye Elooni.
Aakha apo awiri, anshukulikhisiye Esiyaakha na Rapekha.
Esiyaakha ooluvaliye, maasho awe aashokheriye khuhisala oona. Khunkhuwela Ezawu mwanawe otu nwulu araka “Mwanaka!” Ye khujipu: “Lape!”
Khumuuza yoori: “Miiyo kooluvala siikhu kimfwaavo khijuweyeeni.
Othuule nttetthe lawo olawe ntthuttu wasaye nyama.
Wiipikhe saana wookituvelavo okitiisele kije, kuuparikhiye kihinafwe.”
Ezawu khulankha khulawa ntthuttu osaya nyama yoori antiisele papaawe. Rapekha aari onsiila Esiyaakha attakhulanaka mwanawe Ezawu,
ye khumuuza mwanawe Yaakhumpa araka: “Weyo! Kansiila papaawo amuuzaka ttwiiyo Ezawu yoori:
‘Okitiisele nyama ya wiipikhiwa wookituvelavo kije, kuuparikheye mmakhono wa Nnyizinku kihinafwe.’
Mwanaka, osiileze mattakhuzi apa kinuurumaaye, nasaapi eti
olawe oliphanko la nyama wa waathuule aana a puuzi awiri ooneneva, kite kiweepikhe saaneene anttelaaye ontuvela papaawo.
Onlawanele aje, ooparikhiye ahinafwe.”
Yaakhumpa khunjipu mamaawe Rapekha yoori: “Ezawu ti wa waattana ovuzi, miiyo akina.
Paapa amana akipapasela ahikisikanani ovuzi kinttela wiiya ntthu woohata, toowo khankiparikhiya ontta okilaani.”
Mamaawe khumuuza yoori: “Laana yaya eto ti ekikwele miiyo mwanaka. Ila orette eti kiwuuziyeeyo: weettele puuzi epile kuurumiyeezo.”
Ye khulawa khuthuula puuzi khuntiisela mamaawe, khwiipikha wootuvavo waari weettelaaye ontuvela papaawe.
Aphano Rapekha khuthuula kuwo epile zooshapweya za Ezawu mwanawe otule nwulu zaari owawe, khunwalisa Yaakhumpa mwaana otu nttiitthi aya.
Khumfinikha na shapala ya puuzi makhono awe na phantte ya mmwisiko mwawe wahaariimo ovuzi.
Khuthuula etthu-yooja yootuva etile eepikhiyeeyo na phaawu khumwinkha mwanawe Yaakhumpa.
Ye khulawana aphale aariivo papaawe khunkhuwela: “Paapa!” Ye khujipu: “Lape! Weeyo o mwanaka-ni?”
Yaakhumpa khunjipu papaawe: “Miiyo ki Ezawu mwanenu wa mwanzo. Katiisa eti mwaakirumiyeeyo. Mwilankhe mwije nyama eti kitiisiyeeyo, nawiisha mwikiparikhiye.”
Esiyaakha khumuuzela mwanawe yoori: “Wapattha toovi nasaapiru mwanaka?” Ye khujipu: “Nnyizinku Nluku eenu eetta okiperekheza.”
Khumuuza yoori: “Nkakisusele apha kuupapasele, kuujuwe nkhama khweele o mwanaka Ezawu.”
Yaakhumpa khunsusela papaawe. Esiyaakha khusala ampapasela, khumuuza yoori: “Huula ti ya Yaakhumpa, ila makhono pa Ezawu.”
Ye khuhinjuwi mwaasa wa makhono awe wiiyana ovuzi nkhama apa a ttwiiye Ezawu.
Ahinamparikhiye khumuuzela theenya: “Mwanaka Ezawu ti weyeena?” Ye khujipu: “Aa, ti miyo.”
Aphano khuri: “Okitiisele apha nyama yaya eto osayiyeeyo kije, yoori kuuparikhiye.” Yaakhumpa khumweettisela khuja na khumwinkha viinyu khunywela.
Esiyaakha khumuuza yoori: “Okaattame mwanaka okipatikhe.”
Yaakhumpa khumwaattama papaawe khumpatikha. Esiyaakha khusiila muuru wa kuwo zawe, aphano ye khumparikhiya araka: “Muuru wa mwanaka muuru wa nshapa looparikhiyiwa ti Nnyizinku.
Nnyizinku awinkhe mmatte wa pinkuuni na oruwera wa vathi, peewu ya waatta na viinyu ya waatta.
Khapila za waatta zuurumeele weeyo, na mahimo a waatta ookokhorele. Wiiye mbwana wa attwiizo, na aana a mamaawo ookokhorele weeyo. Oolaanikha pi apale anttelaaye wuulaani, na ooparikhiyiwa pi apale anttelaaye wuuparikhiya.”
Paata Yaakhumpa oparikhiyiwa ti Esiyaakha papaawe, ye alaakavo aphale, nasaapiru ttwiiye Ezawu khufiya alankhaka wuusaya.
Na-ye khwiipikha etthu-yooja yootuva khuntiisela papaawe, khumuuza yoori: “Mwilankhe paapa mwije nyama eti keetteliyeeyo osaya mwikiparikhiye.”
Papaawe khumuuzela: “Weeyo o paani?” Ye khuri: “Ti miyo Ezawu, mwanenu otu wa mwanzo.”
Esiyaakha khusuthuwa channu khusala athukumela khulupa yoori: “Khi otule apatthiyeeyo nyama khukitiisela ti paani? Miiyo kaja keesha weeyo ohinate. Kamparikhiya, ti wooparikhiyiwa!”
Ezawu n'oosiila mattakhuzi apale a papaawe khwiiphiiriwa khulila venkivene, khunvekela papaawe yoori: “Na-miyo paapa mwikiparikhiye!”
Ye khulupa yoori: “Aatiiyevo ttwiiyo apha khukittettekha, khuthuula parakha yawo.”
Ezawu khulupa yoori: “Eto swaafu yaphiiri akishinttaka. Ti maana ootthajiwa nzina la Yaakhumpa. Yamwanzo akinyakanya lifunku laka l'oomwaana wa mwanzo. Apho theenya akinyakanya parakha yaka. Paapa khamwinkiparikhiya na miiyo?”
Esiyaakha khujipu: “Miiyo kanthawaza Yaakhumpa yoori eeye mbwanaawo weeyo na ajamaazo ooshi anttela onrumeela ye. Onteela wiiyana tiriku ya waatta na viinyu. Kuurettele niini miiyo mwanaka?”
Ezawu khumuuzela papaawe: “Mweeyo paapa khamwisalaneeni hatha parakha? Na miiyo mwikiparikhiye!” Khusala alila anyakulaka.
Aphano Esiyaakha khunjipu: “Weeyo onttela wiikhala ohali woolepelana na miti zooruweriwa, ohali woothowawo mmatte wa pinkuuni.
Yoori weeyo opatthe meekhazi onttela wuumanana phanka yawo na onttela onrumeela ttwiiyo. Amana ojilipisa ontta olaamo nthwaapu mwaya mphu.”
Ezawu khwiiya wa wiiphiiriwa ti ttwiiye mwaasa wa parakha etile enkhiweeyo ti papaawe. Khusala oopuwela toono: “Siikhu za matthaka a paapa ziri kharipu. Amana afwa miiyo kintta omuula ttwiiyaku Yaakhumpa.”
Wakathi asiiliyeevo Rapekha mattakhuzi apale aari ottakhulaaye mwanawe otu wa mwanzo Ezawu, ye khunkhuwela mwanawe Yaakhumpa otu nttiitthi aya khumuuza yoori: “shawuri ariinaazo Ezawu pi zootakha owuula.
Apho weeyo mwanaka osiile eti kiniwuuzaaye. Otthire nasaapi ethiiti, weette wa nlupwaaka Labani aniikhalaaye nti wa Harani.
Weekhale ottuukho mpakha ttwiiyo omwiishe okatipukha wawe.
Amana omwiishela okatipukha wawe na asahawu eti onretteliyeeyo miiyo kintta wuuperekheza nhupi yoori ote. Akintakha okipwetheya aanaaka oowiiri siikhu moote!”
Aphano Rapekha khulawa omuuza Esiyaakha yoori: “Akituveliweeni ohaayi aka wooshi mwaasa wa aakha a Ahiiti apa awaaraliyeeyo Ezawu. Amana Yaakhumpa na-ye awaarala aakha a tuniya ethiiti miiyo kinhithari ofwa.”
Esiyaakha khunkhuwela Yaakhumpa khumparikhiya, khumuuza yoori: “Ohinrale hatha muukha mmote wa Kanaani.
Olankhe olawe nti wa Paata-Araamu owawe Betuweeli pwapwiyo. Olawe wanrale mwaana wa Labani nlupu wa mamaawo.
Nluku Woowahi Zooshi ooparikhiye, awinkhe mavokozi na peewu ya waatta, yoori khwa weyo epuwe khapila za waatta.
Awinkhe weeyo na peewu yawo parakha etile aahitiweeyo Eburahiima, wiiye mwennyewe nti opu oniikhalaaye nkhama nletto enkhiweeyo Eburahiima ti Nnyizinku.”
Paata ya toole, Esiyaakha khumuuza Yaakhumpa yoori aphano etta. Ye khulawa Paata-Araamu owawe Labani mwaana wa Betuweeli Mwaaramu, nlupuwe Rapekha maama wa Yaakhumpa na Ezawu.
Ezawu aajuwiye yoori Esiyaakha amparikhiyiye Yaakhumpa, khumuuza yoori alawe nti wa Paata-Araamu, amweekese muukha w'oottuukho anrale. Na khusiila yoori papaawe amuuza Yaakhumpa yoori ahinrale muukha wa Kanaani.
Khujuwa theenya yoori Yaakhumpa anshututela papaawe na mamaawe alawa Paata-Araamu.
Ti nanna ye ajuwiyeezo yoori papaawe khaari ontuvela aakha a Kanaani.
Aphano Ezawu khulankha khulawa owawe Esumayila mwaana wa Eburahiima, khunrala Mahalaathi mwaana wa Esumayila, nlupu wa Nebayoothi, oohiiyi aakha apale akina aarinaaye.
Yaakhumpa khulankha Beeresheba khusala alawa Harani.
Eettaka olawa etthiipile, n'ootupweela njuwa ye khufiya puuro yaya eto yoori alale attaapho. Khuthuula liwe laari attaaphale khuretta nsaawu khurapalela.
Khulottha khoona yeemesiwe shikatta vathi, janka yaya yaari okomaaye pinku. Malayikha a Nnyizinku aari owela ethiito na wiishukha.
Nnyizinku ari kharipu na-ye khumuuza araka: “Miiyo ki Nnyizinku, Nluku wa papaawo Eburahiima na wa Esiyaakha. Nti opo orapaleliyeeyo kinteela owinkha weeyo na peewu yawo yooshi.
Peewu yawo enteela wiiya ya waatta nkhama mishaka za voolumwenku, enteela omwazeyela malawa-juwa, makaaripi, kashikhazini na kusini. Khwa weyo na peewu yawo khapila zooshi za voolumwenku enteela oparikhiyiwa.
Woone! Miiyo kiri vamote na-weyo, kinteela owiinanela wakhula vahali oneettaavo, na kinteela wuurutisela tuniya ethiiti, akiniwanswi khihiretteeni epile zooshi kiwaahitiyeezo.”
Yaakhumpa asisimuwiyeevo aphale aari olalaavo khuri: “Khweele, Nnyizinku ori puuro ethiiti, miiyo akaajuwiye.”
Ye khwiiya wa woova channu, khulupa yoori: “Puuro eti ti yawoopisa! Nyuupa ya Nluku, na nlako wa pinkuuni.”
Mmeesho mwaya supuyeene, Yaakhumpa khuthuula liwe ntthile aaphiteeziyeeyo, khweemesa khwiitthela mafuttha vatulu vaya.
Khutthaja nzina puuro yaya etile, la “Beetele”, ila raku sitati yaya etile yaari wiitthiwa “Luuzhu”.
Yaakhumpa khwaahiti yoori: “Amana Nluku eeya vamote na-miyo, eenanela safwari yaka eti, khukinkha etthu-yooja na kuwo zoowala,
khukirutisela vaje wa paapa kiri nkumi, Nnyizinku onteela wiiya Nluku aka.
Liwe ntthi keemesiyeeyo apha nkhama nripu linttela wiiya nyuupa ya Nluku, na wakhula etile onikinkhaaye kiwinkhaka lifunku la khuumi.”
Yaakhumpa khurutela safwari yawe khulawa mpakha nti oriiye phantte lintthamuwaawo njuwa.
Siikhu moote, khweekesa nkerekhere wa nttapo khoona nlipu mmote ozukuleliwe ti maphanko mattatthu a pwittipwitthi zirapaleliye. Waari nlipu zaari onywisiwaavo maati, liwe laari ofinikhaniwakaaye nlipu opule laari liwululene.
Ti eto amakhampuzi aari owejelanakaaye yoori asusise liwe ntthile enkhe nyama zaya maati oonywa, nawiisha khurutiselavo liwe ntthile.
Yaakhumpa khuwoozela amakhampuzi apale araka: “Mweeyo attwiizaku, mwaavayi?” Yo khujipu araka: “Fweeyo nti etthu Harani.”
Ye khuri: “Mwininjuwa Labani ntuulu wa Nahoori?” Yo khujipu araka: “Aa, nininjuwa!”
Khuwoozela theenya yoori: “Nkumi?” Yo khujipu yoori: “Aa, nkumi! Mwanawe Rakeele ti oto antaaye apho na pwittipwitthi za papaawe.”
Yaakhumpa khulupa yoori: “Nalelo khunaripe, khunafiye wakathi wookusanya maphanko. Mwinkhe maati pwittipwitthi epo mwilawe mwajise opheya.”
Ila yo khujipu araka: “Khaninwahi, nina yoowejela pwittipwitthi zooshi zikusanyeye attaapha nisusise liwe ntthi lifinikhaniweeyo nlipu, ninkhe pwittipwitthi zetthu maati zinywe.”
Eettaka ottakhula etthiipile khusala ata Rakeele na pwittipwitthi za papaawe, mwaasa yoori aari nshuki.
Yaakhumpa n'oomoona Rakeele mwaana wa halwiye Labani eettaka ota na pwittipwitthi, khulawa khufunula nlipu khwinkha maati pwittipwitthi za halwiye.
Nawiisha khumwinkha peezhu khusala alila.
Aphano Yaakhumpa khumuuza Rakeele yoori: “Miiyo ki jaama wa papaawo, ki mwaana wa Rapekha.” Ye khutthira alawaka omuuza papaawe.
Labani n'oosiila hapari za Yaakhumpa mwaana wa nlupuwe, khusala atthira alawaka okutthanana. N'onsikana khumpatikha khumpejari, khunthuula khusala alawana owawe. Ye khumuuza Labani zooshi epile zanvireliyeezo.
Aphano Labani khulupa yoori: “Weeyo khweele ojamaayaku, taamu yetthu moote.” Yaakhumpa khwiikhala mpakha wiisha mweezi ari ottuukho.
Elottelanaka Labani khuri: “Hatha nkhama ojamaayaku, onakhola khaazi mahala? Kuuze phakari yawo.”
Labani aarina aanaawe awiri aakha; otu nwulu aari wiitthiwa Liiya. Nttiitthi aya aari wiitthiwa Rakeele.
Liiya aari woosizila maasho, ila Rakeele aari wooshapweya mwiili awe na omaasho wawe.
Yaakhumpa mwaasa wootuveliwa ti Rakeele, khulupa yoori: “Kintta okhola khaazi nyaakha sapa okilooze mwanawo otu nttiitthi aya.”
Labani khujipu yoori: “Kemaani! Ti yooshapweya wuulooza weeyo zayita onlooza ntthu nkinoko. Osala wiikhala attaapha na-miyo.”
Yaakhumpa khukhola khaazi nyaakha sapa yoori anrale Rakeele. Nyaakha epile sapa ye khoona nkhama siikhu vattitthiiru mwaasa wootuveliwa channu.
Ye khumuuza Labani yoori: “Aphano kiloozeni muukhaaka, maana zafiyela siikhu naasiilaniyeezo.”
Labani khuwaakhuwela atthu a waatta a mmuti mphule khuretta njampo.
Ila n'ooripa khunthuula mwanawe Liiya khumwinkha Yaakhumpa khurapalelana.
Labani khumwinkha karumeyaawe Ziilipa mwanawe Liiya yoori asala anrumeela.
Ochiiyeevo, Yaakhumpa khumoona yoori ti Liiya. Ye khulankha olawa omuuzela Labani yoori: “Niini epi okiretteliyeezo? Miiyo akaari okhola khaazi mwaasa wa Rakeele? Khi kiiswa yaya niini okittettekhaka?”
Labani khunjipu yoori: “Fweeyo mmuti mwetthu mphu khanizowereeni onlooza otu nttiitthi nttunkhulu ahinaraliwe.
Amana zivira siikhu sapa za njampo ntthi, nintta wuulooza otu nkina, paata onaahitaavo okikholela khaazi theenya nyaakha sapa.”
Ye khukhupali, khuvira siikhu epile sapa za njampo la harusi ya Liiya, Labani khunthuula Rakeele khunlooza.
Khunthuula karumeyaawe Biila khumwinkha mwanawe Rakeele yoori asala anrumeela.
Yaakhumpa khurapalelana Rakeele khwiiya wontuvela zayita Liiya. Khurutela theenya onkholela khaazi Labani mpakha nyaakha sapa.
Nnyizinku nawoona yoori Yaakhumpa khaari otuveliwa ti Liiya, khumwinkha mavokozi. Ila Rakeele khaari ovokola.
Liiya khwiimittha khumpattha mwaana wanlume, khuntthaja nzina la Ruubeni. Khuri: “Nnyizinku oona ohoowa waka. Aphano phi kinttelaavo ophetiwa ti mannaka.”
Khwiimittha theenya khumpattha mwaana nkinoko, khuntthaja nzina la Simiyooni. Khulupa yoori: “Nnyizinku asiila ohituveli waka, akinkha mwaana nkina.”
Khwiimittha theenya swaafu kiina khumpattha mwaana khuntthaja nzina la Leevi, khulupa yoori: “Aphano mannaka onttela wiiya wookusanyeya na-miyo mwaasa wompatthela aana attatthu.”
Khurutela wiimittha theenya, khumpattha mwaana khulupa yoori: “Swaafu eti kinttela onsifu Nnyizinku.” Ti eto antthajiyeeyo nzina la Yuuda. Aphano khumwiishela mavokozi.
Rakeele ooniyeevo yoori Yaakhumpa khaari ompatthela mwaana, khusala anlilela wiivu ttwiiye. Khumuuza Yaakhumpa yoori: “Okipatthele mwaana, n'oohiiyi etthiipo kintta ofwa!”
Yaakhumpa khumwiiphiira, khumuuza yoori: “Weeyo onikoona nkhama Nluku? Ye ti ahiniwinkhaaye mavokozi.”
Rakeele khumuuza yoori: “Kinaaye karumeyaaka Biila, onthuule othuuto orapalelane yoori ampatthe mwaana zwaamu yaka, kiiye maama khwa ye.”
Rakeele khunthuula Biila khumwinkha Yaakhumpa khwiiya muukhaawe.
Khwiimittha khumpattha mwaana.
Rakeele khulupa yoori: “Nnyizinku akirettela wa shariyavo, asiila lompa yaka akinkha mwaana.” Khuntthaja nzina la Daani.
Biila karumeya wa Rakeele khwiimittha theenya khumpattha mwaana waphiiri.
Rakeele khulupa yoori: “Kaarina viittha khuluyeene na nuunu, ila kanshintta.” Mwaana otule khuntthaja nzina la Nafitaali.
Liiya nawoona yoori alikha ovokola, khunthuula karumeyaawe Ziilipa khumwinkha Yaakhumpa khwiiya muukhaawe.
Ziilipa karumeya wa Liiya, khupattheliwa mwaana ti Yaakhumpa.
Liiya khulupa yoori: “Kashapweyiwa mwaani!” Khuntthaja nzina la Gaati.
Ziilipa karumeya wa Liiya khunvokola mwaana nkinoko theenya.
Liiya khuri: “Kafurahi mwaani! Mpakha aakha akina anteela okuuza yoori kenkhiwa furaha!” Mwaana otule khuntthaja nzina la Asheeri.
Wakathi wa wuurula tiriku Ruubeni aalankhiye khusala alawa omashapa, khusikana mishumo eniitthiwaaye mathunkuja, khuthuula khulawa khumwinkha Liiya mamaawe. Rakeele khunvekela araka: “Safwatali, kimeeleni mathunkuja vattitthiiru apo atiisiyeeyo mwanenu.”
Ye khujipu araka: “Wanthuula mannaka, khootosheeni? Theenya ontakha othuule mathunkuja apa atiisiyeeyo mwanaka?” Rakeele khunjipu araka: “Kemaani! Nlaweni nipatili, mwikinkhe mathunkuja apo, osikhu opu Yaakhumpa mwilawe mwarapalelane mweeyo.”
Njuwa-looveva Yaakhumpa arutaka omashapa, Liiya khunthepeeza khusala amuuza yoori: “Leelo onttela orapalelana miiyo, maana keetta wuurentteri na mathunkuja atiisiyeeyo mwanaka.” N'ooripa Yaakhumpa khulala vamote na Liiya.
Nnyizinku khusiila lompa ya Liiya, khwiimittha khumpattha mwaana wathaanu wa Yaakhumpa.
Liiya khulupa yoori: “Nnyizinku akitthuva mwaasa wonthuula karumeyaaka khumwinkha mannaka.” Ti eto khuntthaja nzina la Esakhaari.
Khwiimittha theenya khumpattha mwaana wasiitha.
Ye khuri: “Nnyizinku akinkha etthu ya fwayita, aphano mannaka onteela otuveliwa venkivene ti miyo mwaasa wompatthela aana sitha.” Ti eto mwaana otule khuntthaja nzina la Zabulooni.
Wiishela waya Liiya khumpattha mwaana nkina wankha khuntthaja nzina la Diina.
Nnyizinku khumuupuwela Rakeele, khusiila lompa yawe khumwinkha mavokozi.
Ye khwiimittha khumpattha mwaana. Khulupa yoori: “Nnyizinku eeshisa haaya yaka.”
Khuntthaja nzina la Yuusufu, alupaka yoori: “Nnyizinku ti akinkhe mwaana nkina.”
Paata ya Rakeele ompattha Yuusufu, Yaakhumpa khumuuza Labani yoori: “Kilikheni kirutele nti kivokoliweeyo.
Mwikinkhe aakhaaka apa kiwaakholeliyeeyo khaazi na aanaaka kilawe. Mweeyo mwinjuwa khaazi kuukholeliyeenini.”
Labani khujipu yoori: “Safwatali nkhama onikisiileza ohilawe, miiyo sako zaka zakuuza yoori Nnyizinku akiparikhiya mwaasa wa weeyo.
Apho okuuze phakari ontakhaaye kisala kuuripha.”
Yaakhumpa khunjipu: “Mweeyo mwinjuwa khaazi kuukholeliyeenini yoori ti ya waatta na nanna kaari oshukisaazo nyama zenu mpakha waatta.
Miiyo kihinate nyama zenu zaari vattitthiiru leelo pi za waatta: Nnyizinku ooparikhiyani mwaasa wa miiyo. Khi ajamaazaku kinttela owaatthantta lini?”
Labani khumuuzela yoori: “Kuuriphe niini?” Khujipu Yaakhumpa: “Mwihikiriphe hatha etthu. Kintta orutela oshukisa nyama zenu amana nisiilana saana.
Leelo kinttela woona maphanko ooshi a nyama zenu, kilazakamo pwittipwitthi zooriipa, zoottweleela na za malepa, puuzi zoottweleela na za malepa. Eto ti enttelaaye wiiya phakari yaka.
Etthiipo enttela okhweya woona okho ninttaawo nkhama ki wa waamineya. Wakathi mwinttelaaye woona nyama zaka, amana yiiyamo nliphanko mwaka puuzi yoottweleela ama yoohiina malepa ama pwittipwitthi yoohiiyi yooriipa, mwintta ojuwa yoori keetta wiiya.”
Labani khuri: “Osiilana wetthu wiiye etthiipo olupiyeezo.”
Siikhu ethiitile, Labani khuphakula puuzi zeelume na zeekha zaariina malepa oolakala, na pwittipwitthi epile zaariina malepa ooriipa khuwenkha aanaawe oshukisa.
Labani khuruma osusisiwa liphanko ntthile, khulawaniwa ohali woolepawo kiyasi ya siikhu ttatthu ntthu ari nsafwari na okhule aariiwo Yaakhumpa. Yaakhumpa khusala ashukisa nyama za Labani epile zaasaliyeezo.
Yaakhumpa khushija virapi piishi za miitthi mittatthu zoofwarikhana khuwaka.
Ye aajuwiye yoori vahali aari onywaavo maphanko a nyama phi vahali zaari opepheranaavo. Ti eto aari otthaakaaye puutta epile zoophaka omaasho waya amana zinywaka.
Amana zipepherana paata yawoona puutta epile, aana zaari owaapatthaaye aari wiiya oophaka, oottweleela, na a malepa.
Yaakhumpa khuphakula nyama epile khuttha mphule zaariimo pwittipwitthi zeekha zoolakala yoori zisala zeekesa okhule ziriiwo epile zooriipa na za malepa za nliphanko la Labani. Khufuwa maphanko awe khuphakula khuhikusanyi na epile za Labani.
Amana zipepheriwaka epile zeekha za ruthupa, ye eetta otthaka puutta omaasho waya vahali zaari onywakaavo yoori zisala ziimittha zoonaka puutta epile.
Ila nawoona yoori nyama eti ti yawootta khaari ottheela puutta. Epile za wootta zaari wiiya za Labani ila epile za ruthupa zaari wiiya za Yaakhumpa.
Wa nanna ethiito aari orettaaye, ye khwiiya thaajiri nwulweene khwiiyana maphanko a waatta a nyama, akarumeya aakha na aalume, nkamiiya na apuuru.
Yaakhumpa khuuziwa mattakhuzi aari olupaaye aana a Labani araka: “Yaakhumpa athuula zooshi paapa aariinaazo, areela mwaasa wa maali za paapa”.
Yaakhumpa khoona yoori Labani khaari omweettettisa saana nkhama aari omweettettisaazo raku.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Yaakhumpa yoori: “Orutele nti wa apapazo okhu ovokoliweewo, miiyo kinttela wiiya vamote na-weyo.”
Yaakhumpa khuruma okhuweliwa Rakeele na Liiya yoori alawe otthuttu okhule aari ojisaawo nyama zawe.
N'oofiya khuwooza yoori: “Kinoona yoori papeenu khanikeettettisa saana nkhama raku. Ila Nluku wa paapa ori vamote na-miyo siikhu zooshi.
Mweeyo mwinjuwa yoori kakhola khaazi ya papeenu khwa kuvu zaka zooshi.
Papeenu khukittettekha na khuzukulisa phakari yaka swaafu khumi, ila Nluku khuhintakheli yoori akirettele zootakhala.
N'oolupa yoori nyama epile zooshi za wiiyana malepa phakari yaka, nyama epile khusala ziwaapattha aana awiiyana malepa paasi. N'oolupa yoori nyama zoottweleela pi zaawo, nyama epile khusala ziwaapattha aana oottweleela.
Nluku othuuto ti ye athuuliyeeyo nyama za papeenu khukinkha miiyo.
N'oofiya wakathi zaari wiimitthaavo nyama epile, kooniye muulottha mirurumpi zaari opepheraaye ziri za malepa, zoottweleela na zooriipa.
Nlayikha la Nluku khukikhuwela muulottha liraka: ‘Yaakhumpa!’ Miiyo khujipu: ‘Lape!’
Nlayikha ntthile khulupa yoori: ‘Olanse maasho awo woone nyama zimpepheriwa pi mirurumpi za malepa, zoottweleela, na zooriipa. Miiyo koonoza mwaasa yoori kinoona zooshi epile Labani anuurettelaazo.
Miiyo ki Nluku otule oopuweleliyeeyo Beetele okhule waavaaziyeewo mafuttha liwe na khukaahiti. Oleemo mmuti mphu nasaapi ethiiti orutele nti ovokoliweewo.’”
Rakeele na Liiya khujipu araka: “Fweeyo khanina hatha etthu yoorithi mmakhono wa papeetthu.
Oninoona nkhama amalapo! Anuuzanyisa, nzurukhu etthu wa mahari wooshi aja.
Maali epi zooshi Nnyizinku alaziyeeyo mmakhono wa papeetthu pi zeetthu fweeyo na aaneetthu. Apho orette zooshi epi Nnyizinku awuuziyeeyo.”
Yaakhumpa khuwaapakhira aanaawe na aakhaawe vankamiiya.
Khuthuula nyama zawe na mali zawe zooshi aapatthiyeeyo Paata-Araamu, khusala alawa wa papaawe Esiyaakha tuniya ya Kanaani.
Wakathi Labani alawiyeevo okasa ovuzi wa pwittipwitthi zawe, Rakeele khwiiya sanamu za papaawe aarettiyeeyo wiiya miluku zawe.
Ti nanna Yaakhumpa anretteliyeezo Labani Mwaarameewu, khutthirawo owawe woohinleezi.
Khutthirisa vitthu zawe zooshi arinaazo, khulokha muuttho wa Efwarathi khusala alawa nti wa nyaako Gileyaadi.
Eviriyeevo siikhu ttatthu, Labani khuuziwa yoori Yaakhumpa atthira.
Ye khuwaathuula ajamaaze khusala amwiikarisa Yaakhumpa mpakha siikhu sapa, khunsikana onyaako wa Gileyaadi.
Aphano Nnyizinku khunlotthisa Labani osikhu eettaka olala yoori: “Phoole! Ohimuuze etthu yooshapweya Yaakhumpa ama yootakhala.”
Labani khunsikana Yaakhumpa eemesiye heema zawe onyaako wa Gileyaadi ye na ajamaaze, n'oofiya khumaka kharipu na attaaphale aamakiyeevo Yaakhumpa.
Ye khumuuzela Yaakhumpa yoori: “Epi okiretteliyeezo niini, zookittettekha khuwaathuula aanaaka nkhama atthu ookholiwa viittha?
Wakittettekhela-ni khutthira sirini? Okijuwisiye khaneetta oleezana na furaha niipaka maliipo, koma na tthakare?
Weeyo khuhikiweji khapula kileezanana aanaaka na atuulwaka! Epi orettiyeezo vitthu zoololo.
Miiyo kinaaye owahi wa wuuhoowisa, ila osikhu wa taana Nluku wa papaawo khukuuza yoori: ‘Phoole! Ohimuuze etthu yootakhala ama yooshapweya.’
Aphano nkhama weeyo watthira mwaasa wa wuunukhela wa papaawo, miluku zaka weeyela-ni?”
Yaakhumpa khunjipu Labani araka: “Keetta woova, kaari wuupuwela yoori mwintta okinyakanya aaneenu.
Amana mwinsikanana ntthu miluku zenu epo, ahiiye haayi. Mashaahiti ajamaazetthu apa; n'oosikana etthu ya wiiya yeenu kirina miiyo mwithuule.” Yaakhumpa khaajuwiye yoori Rakeele ti ye eeyiyeeyo miluku epile.
Labani khuvira nheema wa Yaakhumpa na nheema wa Liiya na etile ya akarumeya apale awiri, ila khuhisikanimo. Asaruwiyeemo nheema wa Liiya, khweetta nheema wa Rakeele.
Rakeele aarettiye atthiiye vathi wa nsaawu wa enkamiiya eekhaleliye. Labani khuwaathola mmaheema wooshimo khuhiwaasikani.
Rakeele khumuuza papaawe yoori: “Mwihikatipukhe mbwanaaka mwaasa woohilankhi n'oowoonani, keetta wiiya mmweezi.” Ye khweekesa miluku zawe epile ila khuhipatthi.
Yaakhumpa khwiiphiiriwa, khusala ammaruwela Labani yoori: “Niini kitthekiyeeyo? Wala kakosa-ni yoofiyelela okiikarisa mwiri wookatipukhawene?
Mapwattha aka ooshi mwathola, mwasikanamo niini ya wiiya yeenu? Nkhama mwasikanamo etthu yeenu mwitiise apha ariivo attwiizaku na attwiizenu aniphuke fweeyo awiri.
Nyaakha eshiriini kiri vamote na-mweyo. Khina pwittipwitthi yenu wala puuzi yenu enaharipweye erukulu yaya na akinarafune hatha pwittipwitthi moote ya liphanko lenu.
Akinootiseleni hatha nyama moote yoovulalisiwa khufwa: miiyo keetta oriphelaka. Mweeyo mwaari oveka oriphiwa wakhula nyama yaari wiiyiwaaye osikhu na nthana.
Nthana keetta ohoowa mwaasa wa haari, osikhu keetta ohoowa mwaasa wookizizima, osikizi khawaari okikhola.
Ti nanna miiyo keekhaliyeeyo vaje venu nyaakha eshiriini: kookholelani khaazi nyaakha khumi na mine yoori eeye mahari a aaneenu oowiiri, na nyaakha sitha kishukisaka nyama zenu phakari yaka yiiyaka nyama etthiipo, ila mweeyo khuzukulisa phakari yaka swaafu khumi.
Eriwaka khaari Nluku wa paapa, Nluku wa Eburahiima otu amooviyeeyo Esiyaakha, wiiya vamote na-miyo, mweetta okiikara woohikinkhi etthu. Ila Nluku khoona ohoowa waka na khaazi kikholiyeeyo, taana osikhu Ye khuulikhisani.”
Labani khunjipu Yaakhumpa yoori: “Aakha apa aanaaka, aanaaya atuulwaka, nyama epo oriina pi zaaka. Zooshi epi onoonaazo pi zaaka. Miiyo kiwaarettele niini aanaaka na aanaaya apa awaavokoliyeeyo?
Apho, nirette wahati miiyo na-weyo, otthuupo wiiye pi oshaahiti etthu.”
Aphano Yaakhumpa khuthuula liwe khweemesa nkhama nripu.
Ye khuwooza ajamaaze yoori: “Mwilokotthele mawe muukele.” Yo khulokotthela, khwiikhala khusala aja nshini wa mawe atthaapale ookeliyeeyo.
Labani khutthaja nzina puuro yaya etile la Yakaare Sahatuuta, na-ye Yaakhumpa khutthaja nzina la Kaleeti.
Aphano Labani khulupa yoori: “Mawe apa nuukeliye apha leelo, oshaahiti etthu miiyo na-weyo.” Ti eto yaari wiittheliwaaye nzina la Kaleeti.
Khusala yiitteliwa theenya nzina la Misipha, mwaasa ye woolupa araka: “Nnyizinku asala aneekesela amana naattuwana.
Amana owaahazula aanaaka na khuweekesa aakha akina oohiiyi yo, hatha nkhama khajuweeni ntthu, wuupuwele yoori Nnyizinku shaahiti etthu.”
Labani khumuuza Yaakhumpa yoori: “Woone mawe apa ariiye apha na nripu ntthi keemesiyeeyo vakatthi vetthu miiyo na-weyo.
Kulu eti ya mawe na nripu, oshaahiti yoori akinteela wiirukhela kaapu yawo oteela wuuharipwela, wala weeyo ohiirukhe otaaka kaapu yaka oteela okiharipwela.
Nluku wa Eburahiima, Nluku wa Nahoori, Nluku wa papaawo ti aniphuke miiyo na-weyo.” Yaakhumpa khulapha khwa nzina la Nluku wa Esiyaakha otule aari omoovaaye.
Yaakhumpa khuretta twaha vamwaako khuwaakhuwela ajamaaze ooshi aariinaaye yoori aje vamote, n'ooja nawiisha khulala vamwaako attaapho.
Mmeesho mwaya lifwajiri Labani khulankha khuwaapejari aanaawe na atuuluwe, khuwaaparikhiya, nawiisha khusala arutela owawe.
Yaakhumpa khulankha khusala alawa safwari yawe khukutthanana malayikha a Nnyizinku.
Ye nawoona khuri: “Eti puuro ya anajanka a Nluku.” Aphale vaya khutthajavo nzina la Manayimu.
Yaakhumpa khuwaaruma akarumeyaawe yoori alokoze wa ttwiiye Ezawu nti wa Seyiiri tuniya ya Edomu.
Khuwaaruma yoori: “Mwilawe mwamuuze mbwanaaka Ezawu yoori karumeyaawo Yaakhumpa alupa toono: ‘Keekhala vaje wa Labani siikhu za waatta mpakha leelo.
Kapatthawo mompe, apuuru, pwittipwitthi na puuzi, akarumeya aalume na aakha. Aphano kinimperekheza hapari epi mbwanaaka yoori akipokherele wooshapweyavo.’”
Akarumeya apale khurutela wa Yaakhumpa khumuuza yoori: “Naalawiye mpakha wa ttwiiyo Ezawu. Nanlikha eettaka ota, ontana atthu awe miiya nne oteela okutthanana weeyo.”
Ye khwiiya wa woova na wooshukulikha, khuwaawanya atthu apale aariina na maphanko a nyama khuntti piiri, pwittipwitthi, puuzi, mompe, na enkamiiya.
Arettaka toowo oopuweliye yoori: “Ezawu amana ata okuumanana khushintta khuntti moote, eti kiina entta otthira.”
Aphano Yaakhumpa khulompa araka: “Nluku wa paapa Eburahiima na Nluku wa paapa Esiyaakha, Oo Nnyizinku okuuziyeeyo yoori: ‘Orutele nti wa apapazo miiyo kinttela oweettettisa saana’,
akinsuhi pheta yawo ya waamineya khwa nanna okikholiyeezo miiyo karumeyaawo; wakathi kaari olokhaavo muuttho Yorotaani miiyo kaathuuliye pakhora yaka paasi, aphano kapattha khuntti piiri za atthu na nyama.
Okuusuru mmakhono wa ttwiiyaku Ezawu, maana kinimoova oteela okuula vamote na aakha apa na asimaana.
Ila weeyo wakaahiti yoori onttela okeettettisa saana, na waattise peewu yaka nkhama mishaka za mmattima epi zihinaalakeyaaye.”
Waari osikhu, ye khulala attaaphale. Mmaphanko wa nyama zawe khuthawulamo nyama zoomwinkha ttwiiye Ezawu:
miiya piiri puuzi zeekha na mirurumpi eshiriini, miiya piiri za pwittipwitthi na mirurumpi eshiriini,
enkamiiya talaathiini zeekha na aanaaya awaamwa, mompe zeekha talaathiini na zeelume khumi, apuuru eekha eshiriini eelume khumi.
Wakhula liphanko la nyama epile khusala amwinkha karumeya mmote, khuwooza yoori: “Mwilokozise, maphanko apa mwaattuwanise.”
Otule aalokoziyeeyo khumuuza araka: “Weeyo onlawa wakutthanane ttwiiyaku Ezawu. Amana awuuzela yoori ‘Nyama epi pi zaani wala weeyo ontta vayi?’
Weeyo onjipu yoori, ‘Pi za karumeyeenu Yaakhumpa, vitthu animperekhezaaye mbwanaawe Ezawu, ye aya ontta ota nyuma wetthu.’”
Khunruma otule waphiiri na wattaatthu na apa akinoko aya aari operekhaaye maphanko a nyama, awoozaka yoori: “Amana mwikutthanana Ezawu, mooshi mwimuuze etthu moote.
Mwihisahawu olupa yoori: ‘Yaakhumpa karumeyeenu ontta ota onyuma wetthu okho.’” Maana Yaakhumpa aari wuupuwela yoori: “Kintta onnyamaza wiiphiiriwa wawe Ezawu mwaasa wa vitthu epi kilokozisiyeezo. Amana kikutthanana talili onteela okipwekherela saana.”
Khulokozisa vitthu epile, ila ye khulala attaaphale aamakiyeevo.
Osikhu otthuupule Yaakhumpa khulankha khuwaathuula aakhaawe oowiri na akarumeyaawe apale awiri aakha, na aanaawe khumi na mmote, khuwaalosa muuttho wa Yabokhi.
Khuwaalosa atthu apale na vitthu zawe zooshi aariinaazo.
Yaakhumpa khusala otthwe, khumpuwelela nlume mmote khusala oomanana mpakha ocha.
Nlume otule ooniyeevo yoori khaari onkhitiri khumpiya n'yuunu mwawe khukurukunyuwa liphaja lawe eettaka wuumana.
Aphano nlume otule khuri: “Okilikhe kilawe wacha.” Ye khuri: “Akinuulikha olawa ohikiparikhiyeeni.”
Nlume otule khumuuzela yoori: “Nzina lawo o paani?” Khujipu araka: “Miiyo ki Yaakhumpa.”
Nlume otule khutukhuru yoori: “Khunteela wiittheliwa theenya nzina la Yaakhumpa, ila nka okhuweleliwaka Ezirayeele. Mwaasa yoori weeyo woomanana Nnyizinku na atthu, khushintta.”
Yaakhumpa khumuuza yoori: “Kakhola moolu kuuzeni nzina lenu.” Ye khujipu araka: “Ontakha oretta-nne nzina laka?” Khumparikhiya attaaphale.
Yaakhumpa khulupa yoori: “Miiyo kamoona Nnyizinku wuuso khwa wuuso ila nalelo kiri haayi.” Ti eto khutthaja nzina puuro etile la Peniyeele.
Yaakhumpa lantthamuweliye njuwa alankhaka Peniyeele eettaka okokoja muulu mmote.
Ti eto mpakha leelo atthu a Ezirayeele khanja ntika wa nyama opu onluttaaye liphaja, mwaasa yaari phantte ya mwiili wa Yaakhumpa waapiiweeyo khukurukunyuwa.
Yaakhumpa khweekesa okhule aari weettaawo khumoona Ezawu eettaka ota na atthu awe miiya nne. Khuwaawanya aanaawe khumwinkha Liiya, Rakeele na akarumeyaawe apale awiri aakha.
Khuwaalokozisa akarumeyaawe apale na aanaaya, khusala alottiwa ti Liiya na aanaawe, khwiishela Rakeele na Yuusufu.
Yaakhumpa khuwaalokozela, khukokhora khwiinama swaafu sapa mpakha nttunkhulu awe ofiya aphale aariivo.
Ezawu khutthira khulawa khumpatikha khumpejari, oowiiri khusala alila.
Ezawu khulansa maasho khuwoona aakha na aana, ye khuuzela yoori: “Khi apa apaani?” Yaakhumpa khunjipu: “Aana apa rehema Nnyizinku amwinkhiyeeyo karumeyeenu.”
Aphano akarumeya apale na aanaaya khumwaattama khukokhora khwiinama.
Elottelanaka Liiya khuta attaaphale na aanaawe khukokhora khwiinama. Wa wiishela aari Yuusufu na Rakeele, na-yo khuta khukokhora khwiinama.
Ezawu khuuzela yoori: “Nyama epile zooshi kisikaniyeeyo ntarikhi ontakhela-ni?” Yaakhumpa khujipu: “Kintakha kipatthe osuhi mmakhono mwenu mbwanaaka.”
Ezawu khulupa yoori: “Miiyo kinaaye pure ttwiiyaku, epo zaawo osalane omwennyewe.”
Yaakhumpa khusala ankhanyarela araka: “Mwihikatthale! Nkhama kinsuhi mmakhono mwenu safwatali pokherani vitthu epi, maana n'oowoonani mweeyo koona nkhama kimooniye Nnyizinku khwa nanna mwituveliweezo ti miyo.
Kinuuvekelani yoori mwipokherele vitthu epi kuutiiseliyeenini mwaasa yoori Nnyizinku akiparikhiya, akinkha zooshi epile kinhithajiyaaye.” Ye khunkhanyarela Ezawu mpakha okhupali.
Ezawu khuri: “Nlawe nivire neettettaka.”
Ila Yaakhumpa khuri: “Mbwanaaka, mwinjuwa yoori aana apa nalelo asimaana na kinaaye pwittipwitthi na mompe zinaamwisaaye. Amana kikhanyarela weettettisa channu zooshi zintta ofwa siikhu moote.
Apho mwilokoze mbwanaaka, miiyo kintta ota vattiitthi-vattiitthi khwa mwentto wa aanaaka na nyama zaka, mpakha ofiya nti wa Seyiiri.”
Ezawu khuri: “Kintakha atthu aka akina kuulikhele weeyo.” Yaakhumpa khuuzela yoori: “Mwaasa wa niini? Khinhithajiya. Ethiiti mwikipokhereliyeeyo saana paasi.”
Siikhu ethiitile Ezawu khulankha khusala arutela owawe Seyiiri.
Yaakhumpa khulankha khusala alawa Sokoota. Ottuukhule khujeka nyuupa yawe na mazizi a nyama zawe. Ti eto atthajiyeevo nzina la Sokoota.
Yaakhumpa arutiyeevo Paata-Araamu khufiya Shekemu tuniya ya Kanaani ari nkumi, khweemesa heema zawe kharipu ya sitati ethiitile.
Khuuzanya phantte moote ya nshapa puuro ethiitile eemesiyeevo heema zawe, na aana a Hamori, paapa wa Shekemu, khwa hisapu miiya nzurukhu wa feeta.
Attaaphale khunjeka alitaari khuntthaja “Nluku yoori Nluku wa Ezirayeele.”
Siikhu moote, Tiina mwaana wa Yaakhumpa na Liiya, aalankhiye olawa owaathotola aanaakha a nti otthuupule.
Shekemu mwaana wa Hamori nhiivi mfwalume wa nti aya opule, n'oomoona, khunkhola khunjansili.
Erettiyeevo toole khwiiya wootuveliwa ti Tiina mwaana wa Yaakhumpa, khumpheta, khumuuza mattakhuzi oomwiitthaaza rooho.
Shekemu khumuuza Hamori papaawe yoori: “Mwakuurele mwaari otu kinrale.”
Wakathi Yaakhumpa asiiliyeevo yoori mwanawe Tiina ajansiliwa ti Shekemu, aarettiye aanaawe ari ntthuttu ashukisaka nyama. Ye khunyamala khusala awaaweja aanaawe mpakha oruti.
Khulankha Hamori paapa wa Shekemu olawa ottakhulana Yaakhumpa.
Wakathi arutiyeevo aana a Yaakhumpa ntthuttu, n'oosiila vitthu epile yo khwiiya ooshanka channu, khuweephiira mwaasa yoori Shekemu aarettiye etthu yoopatthisa haaya vakatthi wa Meezirayeele, onjansili mwaana wa Yaakhumpa; eto etthu yahaari orettiwaayo.
Hamori khuwooza yoori: “Mwanaka Shekemu atuveliwa ti mwanenu, apho safwatali mwinlooze eeye muukhaawe.
Nirette ojama; aaneenu awaarale aaneetthu, na apa eetthu awaarale eenu.
Mwiikhale vamote na-fweyo, nti opu pu weetthu mwithawule wakhula phantte mwintakhaaye. Mwiikhale nttumphu mwirette zanshara zenu mpakha muuzanye nti eenu.”
Aphano Shekemu khumuuza papaawe Tiina na alupuwe yoori: “Safwatali mwikikhupalele mattakhuzi apa, kintta owinkhani wakhula etile mwinttelaaye olupa.
Mwilupe mahari a waatta a mwanenu na tthuvo mwintakhaaye, kintta wuuriphani khwa nanna mwintakhaazo okuuza, ila mwikilooze.”
Aphano aana a Yaakhumpa khunjipu Shekemu na papaawe wonhatavo, mwaasa wonjansili nlupwaaya Tiina.
Khunjipu yoori: “Khaninwahi onthuula nlupweetthu khunlooza nlume woohikhiriyi koma, enttela wiiya haaya.
Fweeyo ninkhupali wuuloozani nlupweetthu amana alume ooshi a mmuti mwenu eeya ookhiriya koma nkhama fweeyo.
Toowo phi ninttelaavo wuuloozani aaneetthu na-fweyo owaarala aaneenu, ninttela wiikhala vahali vamote niiye ojama mmote.
Ila amana mwihikhupali okhiriya koma, nintta onthuula mwanetthu nileemo mmuti mwenu.”
Mattakhuzi apale Hamori na mwanawe Shekemu khukhupalela.
Shekemu, shapu wooshitahiwa pi atthu ooshi a vaje wa papaawe, khuhirupazi khulawa khuretta etile aavekeliweeyo mwaasa wontuvela mwaana wa Yaakhumpa.
Hamori na mwanawe Shekemu khulankha khulawa vanlako wa sitati ethiitile owooza alume ooshi araka:
“Atthu apa pi oosiilaneya, nlaweni niwaalikhe eekhale mmuti mwetthu mphu arettaka zanshara zaya. Nti opu nwulweene ewaamo puuro eniwaafiyelaaye, anilooze aanaaya na-fweyo niwaalooze aaneetthu.
Ila yo ankhupali wiikhala vamote na-fweyo khwiiya ajamaazetthu amana alume ooshi akhiriya koma nkhama etthiipo na-yo akhiriyiyeezo.
Nyama zaya zooshi na mali zaya zooshi zinttela wiiya zeetthu; nlaweni nikhupalele shawuri zaya yoori eekhale vamote na-fweyo.”
Alume ooshi apale aakusanyeyiyeeyo vanlako wa sitati khukhupalela mattakhuzi apale aalupiyeeyo Hamori na mwanawe Shekemu; alume ooshi a sitati ethiitile khukhiriya koma.
Siikhu yattaatthu, wakathi alume apale aari woonachaavo olwaaza, aana awiri a Yaakhumpa, Simiyooni na Leevi alupuwe Tiina, khuthuula phanka zaya, khweetta nsitati mphule woohijuwiwi ti hatha ntthu. Khuwoola alume ooshi.
Khumuula Hamori na mwanawe Shekemu. Khunthuulawo Tiina owawe Shekemu khusala alawa.
Khuta aana a Yaakhumpa apale akina ositati ottuukhule ooliiweewo atthu, khuttapwattha vitthu za mali mwaasa woojansiliwa nlupwaaya.
Khuthuula liphanko la pwittipwitthi, la puuzi, mompe, na apuuru, na vitthu zaari nsitati nttumphule na epile zaari omashapa.
Yo khuwaathuula aakha na aanaaya na vitthu zooshi za mali zaari mmamanyupa mwaya.
Aphano Yaakhumpa khumuuzela Simiyooni na Leevi yoori: “Mweeyo mwakizinkula! Mwaretta yoori atthu apa aniikhalaaye nti otthuupu, Akanaani na Apirizi asala eephiiriwa ti miyo. Fweeyo khanaatteeni, yo amana akusanyeya ateela okuumanana antta okuula na ajamaazaku.”
Yo khujipu araka: “Ti yooshapweya yo onretta omalempe nlupweetthu?”
Nluku khumuuza Yaakhumpa yoori: “Olankhe olawe Beetele weekhale ottuukho, wanjekewo alitaari wa Nluku otu oopuweleliyeeyo wakathi waari ontthiraavo ttwiiyo Ezawu.”
Yaakhumpa khuwooza ajamaaze na atthu apale aariina yoori: “Mweeselele okho miluku zenu epo zoohifwayi mwiriinaazo, mwijitwaharishe mwiwale kuwo kiina.
Nilankhe nilawe Beetele, ottuukho kinlawa kanjekewo alitaari woomwaaputuvo Nluku otu aakipuweleliyeeyo siikhu epile kaari mmashakha, otu aakilokoziyeeyo tarikhi zooshi kiviriyeezo.”
Yo khumwinkha Yaakhumpa miluku zaya zooshi epile zoohifwayi aariinaazo, na pirinku epile aawaliyeeyo aakha ooshi, ye khuthuula khuthipela nshini wa muutthi nwulweene waari nti wa Shekemu.
Wakathi yo alankhiyeevo alawaka, Nluku khuweeshushela woova atthu a sitati epile aattamananiyeezo, mphule aari oviraamo, yo khuhiweekarisi aana a Yaakhumpa.
Yaakhumpa khufiya na atthu awe ooshi nti wa Luuzu oniitthiwaaye Beetele, tuniya ya Kanaani.
Khunjeka alitaari, puuro yaya etile khutthajavo nzina la Nluku wa Beetele mwaasa yoori Nluku aajithoonyeziye attaaphale wakathi opule Yaakhumpa aari ontthiraavo ttwiiye.
Deebora, yaaya wa Rapekha khufwa, khuzikhiwa kharipu ya Beetele nshini wa muutthi nwulweene oniittheliwaaye Alooni-Pakuuti.
Yaakhumpa n'ooruti Paata-Araamu, ari Beetele, Nluku ampuweleliye swaafu yaphiiri khumparikhiya.
Khumuuza yoori: “Nzina lawo o Yaakhumpa ila waaza leelo walikha, aphano nzina lawo o Ezirayeele.” Ti nanna Nluku antthajiyeeyo nzina la Ezirayeele.
Nluku khumuuza theenya araka: “Miiyo ki Nluku Woowahi Wooshi, mwivokolelane na mwaattelane. Khwa peewu yawo weeyo enteela opuwa khapila na khuntti ya khapila za waatta na anlawa apuwevo afwalume.
Nti kimwinkhiyeeyo Eburahiima na Esiyaakha kinteela owinkha weeyo na peewu yawo.”
Nawiisha ottakhulana Yaakhumpa, Nluku khulawa.
Yaakhumpa khweemesa nripu la mawe vahali attaaphale aattakhulaniyeevo Nluku. Khwiitthela viinyu nripu laya ntthile na khuvaaza mafuttha.
Ye khutthaja nzina la Beetele puuro yaya etile aari ottakhulanaavo Nluku.
Yo khulankha Beetele, nalelo ahinafiye Efwarata Rakeele khwiiyana tafwawuthi khuluyeene ya woona olwaaza asaleelaka ompattha mwaana.
Oonaka olwaaza channu, mwaatani khumuuza yoori: “Ohoove! Weeyo wampattha mwaana nkina theenya wanlume.”
Ettaka oshakhi ahinattiye phuumu, khuntthaja nzina mwaana otule la Benooni, ila papaawe na-ye khuntthaja nzina la Bejami.
Aphano Rakeele khufwa khulawa khuzikhiwa tarikhi ya Efwarata (yiiyiye Belemu).
Yaakhumpa khutthaavo alama ya nshuhuti vakhapuri ya Rakeele, mpakha leelo eti liwaapho.
Ezirayeele khulankha khuvikana korofwa ya Eeteri khulawa khweemesa heema zawe.
Siikhu moote, Ezirayeele eekhalaka nti otthuupule, mwanawe Ruubeni khulawa khulalana Biila, mwiitthwaana otule aari muukha nkina wa papaawe, ila hapari epile khumfiyela papantthu. Ezirayeele aarina aana khumi na awiri.
Aana aavokoleliweeyo Liiya ti Yaakhumpa pi apa: wamwanzo ti Ruubeni, alottiwaka ti Simiyooni, Leevi, Yuuda, Esakhaari na Zabulooni.
Aana aavokoleliweeyo Rakeele: ti Yuusufu na Bejami.
Na-ye aana a Biila karumeya wa Rakeele pi apa: Daani na Nafitaali.
Aana a Ziilipa karumeya wa Liiya pi apa: Gaati na Asheeri. Aari atthaapo aana a Yaakhumpa awaapatthiyeeyo nti wa Paata-Araamu.
Aphano Yaakhumpa khurutela wa papaawe nti wa Manre kharipu na Kiriyati-Aarapa wiiyiye Heporooni, ohali aari wiikhalaawo Eburahiima na Esiyaakha.
Esiyaakha eekhaliye nyaakha miiya na thamaaniini.
Afwa ari wa wuuluvala arina nyaakha za waatta, aanaawe Ezawu na Yaakhumpa khunzikha.
Eti peewu ya Ezawu anjuwaniwaaye nzina la Edomu.
Ezawu khuwaarala aakha a Kanaani. Mmote aari wiitthiwa Aada aari mwaana wa Elooni, nhiiti. Nkinoko aari wiitthiwa Olipama mwaana wa Anahi ntuulu wa Zipiyooni Nhiivi,
na Basemaathi mwaana wa Esumayila nlupuwe Nepayoothi.
Aada aavokoleliwe mwaana ti Ezawu khuntthaja nzina la Elifazi, na Basemaathi khunvokola Rewele.
Na Olipama khunvokola Yewuushi, Yalaamu na Koora. Apa aari aana Ezawu awaavokoliyeeyo tuniya ya Kanaani.
Ye khuwaathuula aakhaawe na aanaawe na atthu ooshi aari wiikhalanaaye na vitthu zooshi aapatthiiyeezo tuniya ya Kanaani waaza pwittipwitthi zawe, puuzi na mompe zawe zooshi, khumwazeyanana ttwiiye Yaakhumpa khulawa khwiikhala nti nkina.
Ye khuthama mwaasa wa nti opule aari wiikhalaaye khawaarina etthu-yooja yoofiyela oja nyama zaya zooshi, mali zaya zaari za waatta khuhisala ewaheya wiikhala vahali vamote.
Ezawu, otu aniitthiwaaye Edomu, khuthama khulawa khwiikhala onyaako wa Seyiiri.
Eti peewu ya Ezawu paapa wa Meedomu aniikhalaaye onyaako wa Seyiiri.
Apa mazina a aana a Ezawu: Elifazi mwaana wa Aada muukha wa Ezawu, Rewele mwaana wa Basemaathi muukha wa Ezawu.
Apa mazina a aana a Elifazi: Teemani, Omari, Zeefo, Katamu na Kenaazi.
Tinna, muukha nkina wa Elifazi mwaana wa Ezawu, aavokoleliwe mwaana aari wiitthiwaaye Amaleekhi. Apa atuulu a Aada muukha wa Ezawu.
Apa aari aana a Rewele: Nahathi, Zeera, Shaama na Miiza. Apa atuulu a Basemaathi muukha wa Ezawu.
Apa aana a Olipama muukha wa Ezawu, mwaana wa Anahi, ntuulu wa Zipiyooni: Yewuushi, Yaalamu, na Koora.
Apa mahaakhimu a mahimo a peewu ya Ezawu: Elifazi, mwaana wamwanzo wa Ezawu, aanaawe aari apa: Haakhimu Teemani, haakhimu Omari, haakhimu Zeefo, haakhimu Kinaazi,
haakhimu Koora, haakhimu Katamu, na haakhimu Amaleekhi. Apo aari mahaakhimu a peewu ya Elifazi nti wa Edomu. Aari atuulu a Aada.
Aana a Rewele, mwaana wa Ezawu aari apa: Haakhimu Nahathi, haakhimu Zeera, haakhimu Shaama na haakhimu Miiza. Apa mahaakhimu a Rewele nti wa Edomu na atuulu a Basemaathi muukha wa Ezawu.
Aana a Olipama muukha wa Ezawu, aari apa: Haakhimu Yewuushi, haakhimu Yaalamu na haakhimu Koora. Apa mahaakhimu a peewu ya Olipama muukha wa Ezawu mwaana wa Anahi.
Ooshi apa mahaakhimu na aana a Ezawu otu anjuwaniwaaye nzina la Edomu.
Apa aana a Seyiiri, nhoori aari wiikhalaaye nti otthuupule; Lotaani, Shobaali, Zipiyooni, Anahi,
Diishoni, Eseeri na Diishani. Apa aari mahaakhimu a nti wa Hoori, aana a Seyiiri nti wa Edomu.
Aana a Lotaani aari apa: Hoori, Hemani, na Tinna nlupu wa Lotaani.
Aana a Shobaali aari apa: Aluvani, Manahati, Ebali, Shefo na Onamu.
Aana a Zipiyooni aari apa: Aaya na Anahi othuuto ooneliyeeyo nlipu wa maati oolukuza n'yaara ashukisaka apuuru za papaawe Zipiyooni.
Aana a Anahi aari apa: Diishoni na Olipama.
Aana a Diishoni aari apa: Hemetaani, Eshipaani, Ethirani na Keerani.
Aana a Eseri aari apa: Bilani, Zaawani na Akani.
Aana a Diishani aari apa: Wuuzi na Araani.
Apa aari mahaakhimu a Ahoori: Lootani, Shopali, Zipiyooni, Anahi,
Diishoni, Eseeri na Diishani. Apa aari mahaakhimu a ahoori, ti nanna aawanyeyiyeezo mahimo aya nti wa Seyiiri.
Apa afwalume aariina yenzi nti wa Edomu ahineeyevo hatha mfwalume mmote wa mwiizirayeele.
Beela mwaana wa Bewoori ti ye aathawaliyeeyo tuniya ya Edomu, sitati yawe yaari wiitthiwa Dinaapa.
N'oofwa Beela, khuthawala Yobaabu mwaana wa Zeera wa sitati ya Bozara.
Yobaabu khufwa, khuthawala Hushaamu wa nti wa Temaani.
Khufwa Hushaamu, khuthawala Hadaadi mwaana wa Bedaadi aawaashinttiyeeyo Amidiyaani nti wa Mowaabu. Sitati yawe yaari wiitthiwa Avithi.
Hadaadi khufwa, khuthawala Samula wa nti wa Masareka.
Samula khufwa, khuthawala Shawulu wa nti wa Rohopoothi waattameliyeeyo muuttho Efwarathi.
Shawulu khufwa, khuthawala Baali-Hanani mwaana wa Akiboori.
Afwiiyeevo Baali-Hanani mwaana wa Akiboori khuthawala Hadaari, sitati yawe yaari wiitthiwa Paawu, muukhaawe aari Mehetabeeli mwaana wa Matereeti ntuulu wa Mezahaabu.
Mahaakhimu apa aari a peewu ya Ezawu, na mahimo aya na miti zaya: Haakhimu Tinna, Aluvani, Yeteeti,
Oholipama, Elaahi, Pinoni,
Kenaazi, Temaani, Mibizaari,
Makidiyeeli na Iramu. Apa aari mahaakhimu a Edomu; wakhula mmote aari wiikhala puuro etile aari othawalaaye. Meedomu ooshi peewu ya Ezawu.
Yaakhumpa aari wiikhala tuniya ya Kanaani ottuukho aasaafireliyeewo papaawe.
Eti hatiithi ya peewu ya Yaakhumpa. Yuusufu arina nyaakha khumi na sapa, aari nshuki wa pwittipwitthi na puuzi za papaawe vamote na attwiize aana a Biila na Ziilipa, aakha a papaawe. Yuusufu eetta omuuzaka papaawe vitthu zootakhala aari orettaazo attwiize.
Ezirayeele aari ompheta Yuusufu zayita aana apale akinoko aya, mwaasa yoori ampatthiye ooluvaliye. Khunsonela ajapi ya kisawu za waatta.
Attwiize nawoona yoori oniiya ophetiwa ti papaaya zayita yo, khwaaza wiiphiiriwa ti ye khuhisala awahi onttakhulana saana.
Siikhu moote, Yuusufu khulottha jozi, n'oowooza attwiize yo khutepa wiiphiiriwa ti ye.
Ye khuwooza yoori: “Mwisiileze jozi kilotthiyeeyo!
Kalottha niri mmashapa nifukaka misama za tiriku, nsama aka khweemela, misama zenu mweeyo khuzukulela khwiinamela opu waaka.”
Attwiize khumuuzela yoori: “Apho niri weeyo onttela wiiya mfwalume etthu fweeyo? Ama niri ti weyo onttelaaye onilokozela?” Khutepa wiiphiiriwa mwaasa wa jozi etile na mattakhuzi awe.
Khurutela olottha khuwooza attwiize yoori: “Kalottha theenya! Njuwa, mweezi na matthottowa khumi na limote zikiinameliye.”
N'oomuuza papaawe na attwiize, papaawe khunshowera araka: “Jozi-ni eto olotthiyeeyo? Niri miiyo, attwiizo na mamaawo ninteela wuukokhorela weeyo?”
Waaza attaapho attwiize khuwaata nrima na-ye, papaawe khusala apheleleza vitthu epile varoho vawe.
Siikhu moote, attwiize Yuusufu aalawiye oshukisa nyama za papaaya kharipu ya sitati ya Shekemu.
Aphano Ezirayeele khumuuza Yuusufu araka: “Attwiizo anshukisa nyama kharipu ya Shekemu. Apho kintakha yoori weeyo olankhe olawe ottuukho.” Ye khujipu: “Kemaani, kasiila paapa.”
Papaawe khumuuza: “Wawoone nkhama akumi na nyama zaya, ote okuuze.” Yaakhumpa oninrumaru aarettiye ari mmujokowa wa Heporooni, Yuusufu khulankha khusala alawa Shekemu.
Asaleelaka ofiya Shekemu khuthowelela. Khusikaniwa ti mwinyi mmote eettaka ojeettettela ntthuttu khumuuzela yoori: “Weyo! Oneekesa-ni?”
Ye khunjipu araka: “Kiniweekesa attwiizaku; safwatali kuuzeni ohali anshukisaawo nyama zaya?”
Mwinyi otule khujipu yoori: “Apha avikanavo, kawaasiila araka: ‘Nintta Dotaani.’” Yuusufu khusala aweekesa, khuwaasikana asaleelaka ofiya Dotaani.
Attwiize n'oomoona eettaka ota, ari peetiwene ahinawaafiyele khuwaza shawuri zoomuula.
Yo khuuzana yoori: “Ahee! Namalottha nwulu oto ontta ota!
Aphano akhweya. Nlaweni nimuule nimweeselele valiphotto nalupe yoori eetta orafuniwa ti nyama za ntthuttu. Noone olottha wawe vahali onttelaaye wiishelavo.”
Ruubeni n'oosiila khumwaakisela khulupa yoori: “Nihimwankameze!”
Khulupa theenya yoori: “Nihimuule. Nimweeselele vanlipu oriiye n'yaara mpho, ila mwihinvulalise.” Ye alupaka toowo, aariye amuusuru ttwiiye arutele wa papaawe ari haayi.
Yuusufu n'oowaafiyela attwiize, yo khunvula ajapi etile yooshapweya aawaliiyeeyo,
khuntthempa khumweeselela vanlipu woohiivo hatha etthu na oohivo maati.
Yo khwiikhala yoori aje, khuwoona annya-zanshara eettaka ota ari ohali woolepawo, annya-esumayila aari olankhaaye Kileyaati na enkamiiya zaya apakhiriye viluko, paalasamu, na mafuttha oonukhela eettaka Misuri.
Yuuda khuwoozela attwiize yoori: “Ena fwayita-ni omuula ttwiiyetthu khunvitha?
Nihimuule, niwoozanyeze annya-esumayila apo, maana ye ti ttwiiyetthu, taamu yetthu moote.” Attwiize apale akinoko aya khukhupalela.
Khunlazavo vanlipu aphale aamweeseleliyeevo, khuwoozanyeza annya-esumayila aari oviraaye, a nti wa Midiyaani, na nzurukhu eshiriini wa feeta. Yo khunthuula khusala alawana Misuri.
Wakathi Ruubeni aruteliyeevo vanlipu aphale, khuthurumelavo khuhinsikanivo, attaaphale khuvarula kuwo zawe athoonyezaka yoori ori nhuzuni.
Khurutela aphale aariivo attwiize khuwooza yoori: “Mweyo! Shaapu otule khaavo vanlipu aphale! Kiri toovi?”
Khuthuula ajapi ya Yuusufu, khuula puuzi moote, taamu yaya khuttukunttela.
N'ooretta toole, khuthuula ajapi etile ya waatta kisawu khumweettisela papaaya, khumuuza yoori: “Ajapi eti neetta olokottha. Nkoonani nkhama khahiyo ya mwanenu.”
Ezirayeele khufwahamu khuri: “Ajapi ya mwanaka! Khweele-khweele nyama yoohusuti yeetta omuula khunrafuna.”
Aphano Yaakhumpa khuvarula kuwo zawe khuwala saakhu khusala anlilela mwanawe siikhu za waatta.
Aanaawe ooshi aalume na aakha khuteela onzuru, ila ye khukatthala ozurwiwa waya alupaka yoori: “Kiniikhala woolila etthiipi mpakha olawa okutthanana mwanaka aahera.” Khwiiya wonlilela mwanawe Yuusufu.
Wakathi aya opo Amidiyaani aarettiye amuuzanyisiye Yuusufu wa Potifwaari nttunkhulu wa anamweekesela a Firawuuna.
Wakathi aya opo Yuuda aamwazeyananiye attwiize khusala eekhala wa mwinyi mmote aari wiitthiwaaye Hiira nti wa Atulaamu.
Ottuukho Yuuda ansikaniyeewo mwanankha mmote aari mwaana wa nkanaani aari wiitthiwaaye Shuuwa, ye khunrala.
Khwiimittha khumpattha mwaana khuntthaja nzina la Eeri.
Khwiimittha theenya khumpattha mwaana nkina khuntthaja nzina la Onaani.
Khurutela theenya khumpattha mwaana khuntthaja nzina la Shela, ompattikhanaru Yuuda aarettiye ari nti wa Kezipu.
Ye khumweekesa muukha aari wiitthiwaaye Tamaara khunlooza mwanawe Eeri.
Ila Nnyizinku khuhintuveli thwapiya za Eeri, khufiyelela omuula.
Aphano Yuuda khumuuza Onaani yoori: “Onrale muukha wa marehemu ttwiiyo, ompatthele aana yoori ttwiiyo eeyane peewu khwa weyo.”
Ila Onaani aajuwiye yoori aana aari weettelaaye opattikhana, khaari weettela wiiya awe. Ti eto, amana arapalelana muukha wa ttwiiye, zina yawe aari wiitthelaka vathi yoori ahiwaapatthe aana eeya a ttwiiye.
Nnyizinku khuhisala zintuvela vitthu epile aari orettaazo khufiyelela omuula.
Aphano Yuuda khumuuza Tamaara muukha wa mwanawe yoori: “Orutele wa apapazo ori nankhwele onwejaka mwanaka Shela owula.” Ye aalupiye toowo mwaasa woomoovisa mwanawe Shela ofwa. Tamaara khulawa khwiikhala wa papaawe.
Ziviriyeevo siikhu za waatta, khufwa muukha wa Yuuda mwaana wa Shuuwa, nawiisha matthaka khulankha na swaahipu awe Hiira wa nti wa Atulaani, khusala alawa owoona atthu apale ari okasaaye ovuzi wa nyama zaya nti wa Tinna.
Khuuziwa Tamaara yoori: “Nkhwewo ontta ovira, oneetta Tinna olawa okasisa nyama zawe.”
Khuvula kuwo zawe epile aawaliyeezo z'oonankhwele, khujifinikha nshukwi yoori ahijuwiwe, khulawa khwiikhala vanlako wa sitati ya Enayimu waattamana na tarikhi ya Tinna. Ye aarettiye toowo mwaasa woojuwa yoori Shela awula, ila khwiiya ahinalooziwe.
Yuuda n'oomoona khumwaakanyerela omalempe, mwaasa yoori aajifinikhaniye nshukwi omaasho wawe.
Ye khunkhuwela araka: “Nkatu! Kinuutakha, kuulalane.” Ye ahijuwaka yoori ti nkhwewe muukha wa mwanawe. Tamaara khumuuzela yoori: “Amana kilalana weeyo onikinkha-ni?”
Yuuda khunjipu yoori: “Kintta wuuperekheza puuzi moote ya nliphanko mwaka.” Tamaara khuri: “Aayo! Kasiila. Ila okilikhele etthu kinwahaaye waamini yoori onlawa wakiperekheze puuzi yaya eto.”
Ye khumuuzela araka: “Kuulikhele niini?” Tamaara khujipu yoori: “Okilikhele peetthe yawo, mfukho awo na pakhora eto oriina mmakhono mwawo.” Yuuda khumwinkha zooshi epile anvekeliyeezo, khunlalana khwiimittha.
Nawiisha Tamaara khurutela owawe khuvula nshukwi khuwala kuwo zawe epile z'oonankhwele.
Yuuda khuthuula puuzi khumwinkha swaahipu awe Hiira yoori alawane athuule vitthu epile anlikheliyeeyo muukha otule, ila ye khuhinsikani.
Hiira khuwoozela atthu a nti aya opule yoori: “Ori vayi malempe otule aniikhalakaaye ntarikhi?” Yo khujipu araka: “Mmuti mphu khaamo hatha malempe wa wiiya wa nttumphu.”
Ye khurutela wa swaahipu awe Yuuda, khumuuza yoori: “Akinsikaneeniwo, atthu a nti aya opule akuuza yoori khaawo hatha malempe wa wiiya wa mmuti nttumphule.”
Yuuda khulupa yoori: “Ti asalane epile kimwinkhiyeezo yoori ehikikwele paathuli, miiyo kaaperekhiye puuzi yaya, ila weeyo khuhinsikani ye aya.”
N'oovira nyeezi mittatthu, khuuziwa Yuuda yoori: “Nkhwewo Tamaara araruwa, apha eemittha.” Ye khuri: “Athuuliwe alawe alukuziwe!”
Athuuliweevo alawaka olukuziwa, khumperekheza nhupi nkhwewe araka: “Erukulu eti kiriina ti ya mwennyewe vitthu epi.” Khulupa theenya yoori: “Moone pakhora eti, mfukho opu na peetthe eti nkhama mwininjuwa mwennyewe.”
Yuuda nawoona vitthu epile khulupa yoori: “Ye ti wa shariya zayita miiyo, maana kamwaahitiye oraliwa ti mwanaka Shela.” Na Yuuda khuhiruteli orapalelana.
Ofiiyeevo wakathi woopattha ekumi, mwiirukulu mwawe aarimo aana awiri.
Apatthaka ekumi otu mmote aya khusarula nkhono awe mmote, mwaatani khuthuula luuzi lookhuttuwa khumfukela khuri: “Otu ti eeyiye tthakuzi woosaruwa.”
Otule aasaruliyeeyo nkhono awe khurutiselamo, khusaruwa otule ahaasaruliyeeyo, mwaatani khuri: “Huu! Wapattha toovi tarikhi yoosaruwa?” Khuntthaja nzina la Pereezi.
Aphano, khusaruwa ttwiiye otule aafukeliweeyo luuzi lookhuttuwa nkhono awe, khutthajiwa nzina la Zeera.
Yuusufu aathuuliwe khulawaniwa Misuri pi annya-esumayila. N'oofiya khuuzanyeziwa Potifwaari mmisuri, karumeya nwulu wa Firawuuna, namalokozela wa anamweekesela.
Nnyizinku aari vamote na Yuusufu, khunjaaliwa eekhalaka Misuri vaje wa mbwanaawe.
Mbwanaawe otule khoona yoori Nnyizinku ori vamote na Yuusufu, wakhula etthu aari orettaaye Nnyizinku eetta onjaaliwa,
Yuusufu khwiiya woofwayi mmakhono wa Potifwaari khumwinkha ottunkhulu wa weettettisela vaje vawe na mali zawe zooshi.
Paata yoomwinkha ottunkhulu wa vaje vawe na wa mali zawe zooshi, Nnyizinku khuparikhiya vaje aphale mwaasa wa Yuusufu. Parakha ya Nnyizinku yeeshukheliye khwa zooshi epile aariinaazo, waaza vaje mpakha mmashapa mwawe.
Zooshi aariinaazo nttunkhulu aya khwiiya Yuusufu, Potifwaari khaari ojali hatha etthu yoohiiyi etthu-yooja etile ari ojakaaye. Yuusufu aari wooshapweya wumpo na wa weeziwa.
N'oorettikhana vitthu epile, muukha wa Potifwaari khwaaza ontakha Yuusufu. Siikhu moote khumuuza yoori: “Weeyo nlawe wakilalane.”
Ye khukatthala, khumuuza muukha wa mbwanaawe yoori: “Moone! Mbwanaaka khanjali vitthu za vaje apha; zooshi ariinaazo, ziri mmakhono mwaka.
Khaavo mmote akizitiyeeyo miiyo vaje apha, khayiivo hatha etthu moote akikhattaziyeeyo ila mweeyo wala, mwaasa yoori mwa muukhaawe. Etthu yootakhala nkhama eto, kirette mwaasa wa niini? Toowo kintta onkosa Nnyizinku!”
Wakhula siikhu muukha otule eetta onkhanyarela yoori alawe anlalane, ila Yuusufu khuhisala ansiileza na khusala anwerawera.
Siikhu moote, ye khuvira nnyupa olawa okhola khaazi zawe, aarettiye ahiwo hatha mwiitthwaana mmote.
Muukha wa Potifwaari khukhola orempo awe khumuuza yoori: “Haya okilalane!” Yuusufu khunlikhela orempo awe mmakhono mwawe khutthirela vaje.
Muukha otule ooniyeevo yoori atthira khulikha orempo awe,
khuwaakhuwela akarumeya khuwooza yoori: “Mmoone! Mwiibereewu otu atiisiweeyo ti mannaka aaza onitarawu. Aaviriye okatthi waka khusala atakha okilalana, ila miiyo khusala kikhuwa kinyakulaka.
Ye nawoona yoori keetta onyakula khukilikhela orempo awe khutthirela vaje.”
Ye khupweha orempo opule mpakha mbwanaawe ota.
Wakathi atiiyeevo khumuuza mattakhuzi apale araka: “Mwiitthwaana awo otule wa mwiibereewu onitiiseliyeeyo apha, aakiteeliye khusala atakha okilalana.
Kikhuwiyeevo ye khukilikhela orempo awe khutthira.”
Paata yoosiila mattakhuzi apale aari wuuziwaaye ti muukhaawe, araka: “Mwiitthwaana awo vitthu akiretteliyeezo pi epo,” ye khukasirikha venkivene.
Khuruma weetteliwa Yuusufu khulawa khutthiiwa nkalapooso, nttumpho mfwalume Firawuuna aawaafukeliyeemo atthu awe.
Ila Nnyizinku ari vamote na Yuusufu anthoonyezaka pheta ya waamineya, nttunkhulu wa anamweekesela kalapooso khunkola saana.
Khumwinkha ottunkhulu Yuusufu wa anamfukeliwa ooshi, khwiiya namalokozela vitthu zooshi za nkalapooso mphule.
Nttunkhulu wa anamweekesela a kalapooso etile khuhisala ajali hatha etthu, zooshi zaari mmakhono wa Yuusufu mwaasa yoori Nnyizinku aari vamote na-ye; na wakhula etile aari orettaaye aari wiiya woojaaliwa.
Paata yoovira vitthu epile, namootela zoonywa za mfwalume na namuupa-phaawu khunkosa mbwanaaya, mfwalume wa Misuri.
Firawuuna khwiiya wa wiiphiiriwa pi annya-khaazi awe apo awiri; nttunkhulu wa wootela zoonywa na nttunkhulu wa wuupa phaawu.
Khuruma olawa ofukeliwa nkalapooso ya nttunkhulu wa anamweekesela, nttumphule aafukeliweemo Yuusufu.
Nttunkhulu wa anamweekesela khumwinkha Yuusufu atthu apale awiri yoori asala awaatthantta, yo khwiikhala siikhu za waatta nkalapooso.
Osikhu mmote oowiri khulottha, wakhula jozi yaarina maana aya, etile ya namuupa-phaawu na ya namootela zoonywa.
Mmeesho mwaya supu Yuusufu khulawa owaathotola, khuwaasikana ari ooshukulikha.
Aphano ye khuwoozela annya-khaazi a Firawuuna apale aafukelaniweeyo araka: “Leelo mwakafilikhela-ni?”
Yo khunjipu yoori: “Neetta wiiyana jozi khuhiivo ntthu wootaphulela maana aya.” Yuusufu khujipu yoori: “Ila Nluku paasi ti ye anttelaaye otaphulela jozi epo, kuuzeni jozi zaya epo.”
Nttunkhulu wa wootela zoonywa khumuuza jozi yawe Yuusufu araka: “Kaalotthiye okiteeliye nrayi wa wuuva omaasho waka.
Orina virapi ttatthu za waaleya na khwiima mishumo zaari ottokotthaaye miwawa-miwawa.
Pilawuri ya Firawuuna eri mmakhono mwaka. Miiyo khuthuula mishumo za wuuva khuvinyela mpilawuri mphule kimwinkha mmakhono mwawe.”
Yuusufu khuri: “Maana a jozi yawo eto pi apa: virapi ttatthu enlupa siikhu ttatthu.
Nkatthi wa siikhu ttatthu Firawuuna ontta wuulazamo nkalapooso orutele khaazi yawo ya wootela zoonywa za mfwalume na omwinkha pilawuri mmakhono mwawe, nkhama etthiipo waari orettakaazo raku.
Ila amana zooshi ziweettettelaka saana ohikisahawu, kinuuhirimiza yoori okoonele huruma omuuze mfwalume monkoni wa miiyo, okaawuni yoori kileemo nkalapooso mphu.
Miiyo keetta wiiyiwa nti wa Meebereewu khutiisiwa mmuti mphu khweeseleliwa nkalapooso hatha etthu kihiretteeni.”
Asiiliyeevo nttunkhulu wa wuupa phaawu yoori Yuusufu aataphuleliye jozi etile wooshapweyavo, ye khumuuza yoori: “Na-miyo kinaaye yaaka, kalottha kipwecheriye phaawu khelenke ttatthu.
Khelenke eti ya vatulu zaarimo wakhula nanna ya phaawu epile zontuvela Firawuuna, ila anyannyi khusala ajoropoja ziri veeshwa vaka.”
Aphano Yuusufu khunjipu yoori: “Jozi yawo eto maana pi apa, khelenke ttatthu epo enthoonyeza siikhu ttatthu.
Nkatthi wa siikhu ttatthu etthiipo, Firawuuna onlawa athomeye eeshwa mmutthi, mwiili awo osala ojoropojiwa pi anyannyi.”
Siikhu yattaatthu yaari siikhu Firawuuna aari orettaaye mwaakha, ye khujisa njampo na annya-khaazi awe ooshi, khuruma okhuweliwa apale aari nkalapooso namuupa-phaawu na namootela zoonywa.
Namootela zoonywa khurutiseliwa khaazi yawe ya wootela na yoomwinkha pilawuri Firawuuna mmakhono mwawe.
Ila Firawuuna khunthomeya namuupa-phaawu nkhama etthiipile aalupiyeezo Yuusufu.
Aphano namootela zoonywa otule khuhinfikhiri Yuusufu khunsahawu eperepere.
Eviriyeevo nyaakha miwiri, Firawuuna khulottha ari nshini wa muuttho oniitthiwaaye Niilu.
Mmuttho nttumpho zivuuwakamo mompe sapa zooneneva na zooshapweya khusala zittepula nyaani.
Elottelanaka theenya khusala zivuuwamo mmuttho Niilu mompe sapa zootakhala za wootta, khulawa khwiiya vamote na epile zaavuuwiyeeyo omwanzo.
Epile zootakhala za wootta khurafuna epile zooshapweya zooneneva, attaaphale Firawuuna khusisimuwa.
Khurutela olala khulottha theenya, misaasi sapa za tiriku zooshapweya za wiitaala zaari owulaaye vanchina limote.
Elottelanaka khoona misaasi sapa za maveya a tiriku a wuuma oolukuziwa ti pheevo ya n'yaara.
Misaasi epile sapa za maveya khumiza epile za wiitaala na zooshapweya. Firawuuna khusisimuwa khujuwa yoori eetta olottha.
N'oocha mmeesho mwaya supu, nafusi yawe khwiiya yooshukulikha, khurumisa olawa okhuweliwa anamajintta ooshi na anampiya sako a Misuri. Firawuuna khuwooza jozi alotthiyeeyo, ila khuhiivo hatha ntthu mmote aajuwiiyeeyo otaphulela waya.
Aphano namootela zoonywa khumuuza Firawuuna yoori: “Leelo kafikhiri koosa zaka.
Siikhu moote mweephirisiweeyo pi annya-khaazi eenu mwaarumisiye ofukeliwa miiyo na nttunkhulu wa wuupa phaawu nkalapooso wa nttunkhulu wa anamweekesela.
Osikhu mmote fweeyo awiri khulottha wakhula ntthu jozi yawe, wakhula jozi yaarina maana aya.
Ila nkalapooso nttumphule aarimo shapu mmote wa mwiibereewu aari mwiitthwaana wa nttunkhulu wa anamweekesela, fweeyo khumweeleza jozi zetthu epile ye khutaphulela.
Khurettikhana zooshi nkhama etthiipile aanuuziyeezo: miiyo khurutiseliwa khaazi yaka, otu nkina khuheyiwa.”
Firawuuna khuruma olawa okhuweliwa Yuusufu, khulaziwamo nkalapooso nasaapiru. Khunyoola ttevu zawe khuwala kuwo kinoko khulawaniwa wa Firawuuna.
Ye khumuuza Yuusufu yoori: “Miiyo keetta olottha jozi moote khuhipuwi hatha ntthu mmote wookitaphulela. Ila khusiila yoori weeyo amana wuuziwa jozi onwahi otaphulela maana aya.”
Ye khunjipu Firawuuna araka: “Miiyo akina owahi, ila Nnyizinku onwahi wuutaphulelani wooshapweyavo.”
Aphano Firawuuna khusala amuuza jozi etile Yuusufu yoori: “Kalottha keemeliye nshini wa Niilu.
Mmuttho mwaya mphule khusala zivuuwamo mompe sapa zooshapweya na zooneneva khusala zittepula nyaani nshini wa Niilu.
Theenya khuvuuwa mompe sapa za wootta zootakhala. Nti wooshi wa Misuri akinoone mompe zootakhala nkhama epo.
Mompe zaya etthiipile zootakhala na za wootta khumiza mompe epile zooneneva na zooshapweya,
ila khusala zumpuwa nkhama zihijeeni etthu nalelo, khwiiya za wootta na zootakhala nkhama zaariizo. Ethiito miiyo khusisimuwa.
Khurutela olala khulottha theenya misaasi sapa za tiriku zooshapweya za wiitaala zaari owulaaye vanchina limote.
Elottelanaka khoona misaasi sapa za maveya a tiriku a wuuma oolukuziwa ti pheevo ya n'yaara.
Misaasi epile sapa za maveya khumiza epile za wiitaala na zooshapweya, miiyo khuwooza anamajintta ila khuhiivo hatha mmote aawahiyeeyo otaphulela.”
Aphano Yuusufu khumuuza Firawuuna yoori: “Jozi zenu epo z'oopiri enlupa etthu moote paasi, Nluku eetta wuuthoonyezani eti anttelaaye oretta.
Mompe epo sapa zooshapweya zinlupa nyaakha sapa. Misaasi sapa zooshapweya na-yo zinlupa nyaakha sapa. Jozi zaya epo mooteru.
Mompe epo sapa za wootta na zootakhala zaavuuwiyeeyo ziwelela aphale zaariivo epile zooshapweya enlupa nyaakha sapa. Misaasi epo sapa za maveya zaalukuziweeyo ti pheevo ya n'yaara, khumiza epile zooshapweya enlupa nyaakha sapa za jala.
Mattakhuzi apa kiniwuuzaanini mfwalume, Nluku eetta wuuthoonyezani etile anttelaaye oretta.
Nyaakha sapa tuniya ya Misuri enteela oruwera venkivene.
Ila theenya zinlawa zate nyaakha sapa za jala, oruwera opo onlawa wasahawiwe. Jala yaya eto enlawa yashintte nti aya opu.
Khunteela ofikhireliwa oruwera opule, mwaasa wa jala enttela wiiya yootepa waatta tuniya eti ya Misuri.
Eto mwilotthisiweeyo swaafu piiri enlupa yoori Nluku alakela na onretta woohirupazi.
Apho mweeyo mfwalume, mwinthawule ntthu mmote woojuwa na wa akhili eeye nttunkhulu wa weettettisa tuniya eti ya Misuri.
Mwirette etthiipo, mwiwaattheemo attunkhulu mmuti mphu asala alokotthela phantte ya thaanu za vitthu zinuuruliwaazo tuniya ya Misuri, khwa nyaakha epo sapa zooruweriwa.
Yo ana yookusanya epile anttelaazo opattha nyaakha epo zooruwera, theenya ekusanyiwe tiriku yooshi epwehiwe yiiye mmakhono wa Firawuuna, yiiye etthu-yooja ya mmasitati.
Vitthu-zoojiwa zaya epo zinttela orumeyeliwa nyaakha epo sapa za jala enttelaaye ota tuniya ya Misuri yoori jala eto ehishintte tuniya eti.”
Firawuuna na mashawuriiya awe khoona yoori akhili epile za Yuusufu pi zooshapweya.
Ye khuwooza mashawuriiya awe yoori: “Naari oteela ompattha ntthu nkhama otu wa weettettisiwa ti rooho ya Nluku?”
Firawuuna khumuuza Yuusufu araka: “Wiiya Nluku oothoonyeza vitthu epi, khaavo nkinoko aya wa akhili na woojuwa nkhama weeyo.
Weeyo ti ye onttelaaye wiiya nttunkhulu wa vaje vaka, atthu apa ariivo ooshi nka ashututelaka mattakhuzi awo, ila nkatthi woofwalume miiyo ki nttunkhulu zayita weeyo.
Mpakha nasaapi eti kawinkha ottunkhulu wa tuniya eti ya Misuri yooshi.”
Aphano, Firawuuna khuvula peetthe yawe khunwalisa Yuusufu, khuruma yoori awalisiwe kuwo zooshapweya na nkufu wa thahapu mmwisiko mwawe.
Khupakhiriwa mmwikukutta opule waphiiri, khulokoza anamalaleya alupaka yoori: “Mwinkokhorele!” Yuusufu enkhiweeyo ottunkhulu wa Misuri yooshi.
Khulupa theenya Firawuuna amuuzaka Yuusufu yoori: “Miiyo ki Firawuuna, ila khina mmote antakhaaye oretta etthu tuniya eti ya Misuri ahaazeeni wuusikana weeyo.”
Firawuuna khuntthaja Yuusufu nzina la Zafenathi-Paneeya. Khunlooza muukha aari wiitthiwaaye Asenaathi, mwaana wa Potifweera, nttunkhulu wa tiini ya Ooni. Aphano Yuusufu khuzukulelisiwa tuniya yaya etile yooshi ya Misuri.
Ye azaka khaazi ya mfwalume Firawuuna aarettiye arina nyaakha talaathiini na sitha, khunleeza Firawuuna khwaaza weettetta miti zooshi za Misuri.
Nkatthi wa nyaakha sapa epile zooruwera tuniya etile khuruweriwa tiriku ya waatta.
Yuusufu khukusanya tiriku yooshi yaaruweriweeyo khwa nyaakha sapa tuniya ya Misuri khupweha mmasitati. Wakhula mashapa apale aattameliye sitati, tiriku yaari wuuruliwaaye yaari opwehiwa ottuukho.
Yuusufu khukusanya tiriku ya waatta yahaari waalakeyaaye nkhama mishaka za mmattima, khulikha waalaka mwaasa wa waatta channu.
Ehinafiye nyaakha epile za jala, muukha wa Yuusufu Asenaathi, mwaana wa Potifweera, khuwaapattha aana awiri.
Otu wa mwanzo Yuusufu khuntthaja nzina la Manaase, alupaka yoori: “Nluku akisahawisa ohoowa waka na vaje wa apapazaku.”
Otu waphiiri aya khuntthaja nzina la Efwarayiimu, khulupa yoori: “Nluku akirizikhiya nti opu kihoowiyeeyo.”
Aphano nyaakha epile sapa zooruweriwa tuniya ya Misuri khwiisha.
Khufiya nyaakha epile sapa za jala aalupiyeeyo Yuusufu. Khupuwa jala tuniya yooshi, ila miti za Misuri zaarina etthu-yoojiwa.
Wakathi epariziyeevo jala Misuri, atthu ooshi khunvekela Firawuuna etthu-yoojiwa. Ila ye khuwooza atthu ooshi a Misuri yoori: “Mwilawe mwakutthanane Yuusufu. Wakhula etile anttelaaye owuuzani mwirette ethiito.”
Yuusufu nawoona yoori jala yamwazeyela tuniya yooshi khufukulela tiriku etile aapwehiiyeeyo, khusala awoozanyeza Amisuri mwaasa yoori jala etile yaashinttiye.
Atthu a tuniya kiina aari ota Misuri oteela wuuzanya tiriku wa Yuusufu, mwaasa yoori jala yaamwazeyeliye olumwenku wooshi.
Yaakhumpa n'oojuwa yoori Misuri ewaakho etthu-yoojiwa, khuwooza aanaawe araka: “Mwineekesana yoori niini?
Kasiila oriwa Misuri ewaakho tiriku, apho mwilawe moozanye nite nijilelane nihifwe jala.”
Aphano khulankha attwiize Yuusufu khumi khusala alawa Misuri wuuzanya tiriku.
Yaakhumpa khunkhattaza Bejami ttwiiye Yuusufu owaalotta attwiize amoovisaka ompattha etthu yootakhala.
Aana a Yaakhumpa khulawa wuuzanya tiriku nkhama etthiipo aari olawaazo atthu akina, maana tuniya yooshi ya Kanaani yaarina jala.
Yuusufu nttunkhulu wa Misuri, ti ye aari owoozanyezaaye tiriku atthu ooshi a mmuti. Attwiize n'oofiya khunkokhorela ajihi zaya khufiisa vathi.
Wakathi awooniyeevo khuwaajuwa, ila khumpuwa nkhama ahiwaajuweeni. Khusala awoozela awaatuturuchaka araka: “Mweeyo! Mwinlankha vayi?” Yo khunjipu “Ninlankha tuniya ya Kanaani, naateeliye wuuzanya etthu-yoojiwa.”
Yuusufu khuwaajuwa attwiize ila yo khuhinjuwi.
Ye khupayini jozi epile aawooziyeeyo khuri: “Mweeyo mw'aahankawaani! Mwaateeliye ojuwa siiri za mmuti mwetthu mphu.”
Yo khunjipu araka: “Wala mbwaneetthu! Fweeyo akarumeyeenu naateeliye wuuzanya etthu-yoojiwa.
Fooshi papeetthu mmote, n'aatthu awaamineya. Khahi n'aahankawaani.”
Yuusufu khusala akhanyarela owooza yoori: “Wala mweeyo mwateela ojuwa kiphenyo za mmuti mwetthu mphu.”
Yo khuri: “Fweeyo ninlankha tuniya ya Kanaani, niri aana khumi na awiri paapa mmote. Otu w'eefutti aya nasaapi eti asala onti na paapa, ila otu nkina aya afwa.”
Khurutela owooza araka: “Pi etthiipo kilupiyeezo! Mweeyo mw'aahankawaani!
Apho kintakha kiwooneni. Kinlapha khwa ohaayi wa Firawuuna, yoori khamwinlaavo apha mwihintiiseeni ttwiiyenu oto w'eefutti.
Mwinrume ntthu mmote amweettele, ila apa akina ansalaaye anttela ofukeliwa. Noone nkhama mattakhuzi apa mwilupiyeeyo pi ookhweele. Ila mmana ehiiyi toowo kinlapha khwa ohaayi wa Firawuuna yoori phi mwinttelaavo ojuweya wiiya ahankawaani.”
Ye khuwaattha nkalapooso siikhu ttatthu.
Siikhu yattaatthu khuwooza yoori: “Miiyo kinimoova Nluku, apho nkhama mweeyo mwintakha wuusuru nafusi zenu, mwiri toono:
nkhama mw'aatthu awaamineya mwinlikhe ttwiiyenu mmote nkalapooso, apa akina athuule tiriku awenkhe ajamaazenu ahifwe jala.
Mwikitiisele ttwiiyenu oto w'eefutti kihakikhi nkhama mattakhuzi enu pi ookhweele, mwirettaru toowo khamwinuuliwa. Yo khukhupalela oretta epile ooziweezo.”
Aphano khusala oozana yoori: “Khweele ninaaye paathuli mwaasa wa ttwiiyetthu. Maana wakathi aashankiyeevo aanivekeliye yoori nimoonele huruma ila fweeyo khuhitakhi, apha t'iiti na-fweyo anipatthiyeeyo matteso apa.”
Ruubeni khujipu araka: “Miiyo akaalupiye yoori shapu oto mwihinrettele vitthu zootakhala? Ila mweeyo khuhitakhi okisiileza! Apho nina yoojipu mwaasa w'oofwa wawe.”
Yo khaari ojuwa yoori Yuusufu aari osiila epile aari ottakhulaazo, mwaasa yoori attakhulaka aarivo ntthu aari otaphulelaaye.
Yuusufu khuwaasusa vattitthiiru khusala alila. Nawiisha khurutela attaaphale khusala attakhula, aphano khunthawula Simiyooni khuruma yoori afukiwe eettaka omoona.
Elottelanaka Yuusufu khuwaaruma anakhaazi awe wiitaaza tiriku visurupa za attwiize na owaarutisela nzurukhu aya sirini atthaaka mvisurupa nttumpho, na owenkha etthu-yooja ntarikhi. Khurettiwa etthiipo.
Khuthuula visurupa epile wakhula ntthu khuttha vapuuru vawe khusala alawa.
N'oofiya vahali aalaliyeevo, mmote khufukula esurupa yawe yoori alazemo etthu-yoojiwa enkhe puuru yawe, khusikana nzurukhu awe ori mwiisurupa nttumphule.
Khuwooza attwiize yoori: “Moone! Nzurukhu aka karutiseliwa, opu ori mphu!” Aphano yo khusuthuwa khusala athukumela na woova oozelanaka yoori: “Niini epi Nluku aniretteliyeezo?”
N'oofiya wapapaaya Yaakhumpa tuniya ya Kanaani, khusala amuuza zooshi za waavireliyeezo araka:
“Nttunkhulu wa Misuri eetta onituturucha anuuzaka yoori n'aahankawaani.
Ila fweeyo khujipu yoori: ‘Khahi n'aahankawaani n'aatthu awaamineya.
Niri khumi na awiri paapa mmote, mmote afwa, nkina aya w'eefutti asala onti na paapa tuniya ya Kanaani.’
Aphano nttunkhulu wa nti aya opule khunuuza yoori: ‘Mwinlikhe ttwiiyenu mmote attaapha, toowo phi kinttelaavo ojuwa yoori mweeyo mw'aatthu awaamineya: mwithuule etthu-yoojiwa mwilawe mwawenkhe ajamaazenu ahifwe jala.
