Mwitaaka mwintiise ttwiiyenu otu w'eefutti aya, kaamini yoori mweeyo khahi mw'aahankawaani ila mw'aatthu awaamineya. Ttwiiyenu kintta wuurutiselani, kiwinkheni ejaaza yooretta zanshara zenu mmuti mphu.’”
Wakathi afukuliyeevo visurupa zaya, wakhula esurupa khusikanamo mfukho wa nzurukhu, yo na papaaya nawoona nzurukhu opule khusala oova.
Aphano papaaya khulupa yoori: “Mweeyo! Mwintakha okiishisela aanaaka. Yuusufu ti otule aashikhiyeeyo, Simiyooni khaavo apha na Bejami mwintakha onthuula theenya! Zooshi epo othunku aya ti miyo kinoonaaye.”
Ruubeni khumuuza papaawe yoori: “Mwikinkhe miiyo khanaashikha kininrutisa, amana kihinrutisi mwiwoole aanaaka apale awiri.”
Yaakhumpa khujipu araka: “Akinintakhisa Bejami olawa na-mweyo, Yuusufu afwa, ye ti asaliyeeyo. Amana empattha etthu yootakhala ntarikhi okho mwineettaawo, mwintta okishukhelisa aahera na pwi zaka kirina huzuni yoototheliwa ti mweyo.”
Jala etile yeetta otepa yaattaka mmuti.
N'ooweeshela tiriku etile aalaziyeeyo Misuri, papaaya khuwooza yoori: “Mwirutele theenya Misuri moozanye etthu-yoojiwa.”
Ila Yuuda khujipu araka: “Kiniwuuzani khweele, nttunkhulu wa Misuri anihirimiza channu yoori nihirutelewo nihinlawaneeni ttwiiyetthu otu w'eefutti.
Amana mwinlikha ttwiiyetthu olawa na-fweyo, ninlawa noozanye etthu-yooja yenu.
Ila amana mwihininkhi khaninlawa, maana nttunkhulu oto anuuza yoori amana nihinlawani ttwiiyetthu nihirutelewo.”
Ezirayeele khuwoozela: “Mwamuuzela-ni yoori mwinaaye ttwiiyenu nkina? Mwakitothela pala khuluyeene.”
Yo khujipu araka: “Mwiinyi oto eetta onuuzela yoori anijuwe fweeyo na ajamaazetthu. Khuvira anuuzelaka theenya yoori: ‘Papeenu ori haayi? Mwinaaye ttwiiyenu nkina theenya?’ Fweeyo naarina yoojipu epile aari onuuzelaazo. Fweeyo naajuwiye yoori onttela oniila onlawana ttwiiyetthu?”
Aphano Yuuda khumuuza papaawe yoori: “Mwinlikhe shapu otu kilawena miiyo nasaapi ethiiti, nihifwe jala fweeyo na-mweyo na aaneetthu.
Mwikikhupali miiyo, kinjaahiti omwiinanela na ontthantta. Amana kihinrutisi ari nkumi, kiniiyana paathuli ohaayi aka wooshi mmakhono mwenu mweeyo.
Eriwaka khanaarupaziye nka nilawiye niruteliyewo swaafu yaphiiri.”
Aphano Ezirayeele, papaaya khuwooza yoori: “Nkhama pi etthiipo khina nanna kiina. Mwithuule vitthu zooshapweya za mmuti mphu, waaza paalasamu, asali, viluko, mafuttha oonukhela, na vitthu kiina nkhama amentowa, mwilawe mwamwinkhe mwiinyi oto.
Mwithuule nzurukhu wa feeta swaafu piiri na opu mwisikaniyeeyo mvisurupa mwenu mwilawane, khinjuweya eettiye ovonyela.
Mwinthuule ttwiiyenu mwilawe mwakutthanane mwiinyi oto.
Nluku Woowahi Wooshi amwinkhe wiiyana huruma na-mweyo, yoori oorutiseleni ttwiiyenu otu nkina na anlikhe Bejami ate. Maana, amana miiyo akaashikha aanaaka kinsala etthiipo woohiina mwaana.”
Yo khuthuula vitthu epile enkhiweezo na nzurukhu vamote na Bejami khusala alawa Misuri wa Yuusufu.
Yuusufu n'oomoona Bejami ari vamote na attwiize khumuuza karumeyaawe nwulu yoori: “Owaathuule atthu apa owaalawane owaka, yashijiwe nyama yiipikhiwe, yo anttela oja na-miyo nthana opu.”
Ye khuretta etthiipile ooziweezo, khuwaathuula atthu apale khuwaalawana owawe Yuusufu.
Yo n'oofiya owawe Yuusufu khusala oova oopuwelaka yoori: “Talili natiiseliwavo mwaasa wa nzurukhu opule naarutiseliweeyo swaafu etile yamwanzo mvisurupa mwetthu. Ye ontakha onihukhumu, aniphuke anirette wiiya amwiitthwaana zawe, aninyakanye apuuru etthu.”
Khumweettela karumeya w'oowawe Yuusufu yoori anttakhulane vanlako.
Khulupaza yoori: “Safwatali mbwaneetthu! Swaafu etile naatiiyeeyo apha yamwanzo naateeliye wuuzanya etthu-yoojiwa.
Ila n'oofiya vahali naalaliyeevo, naafukuliye visurupa zetthu wakhula mmote wa fweyo khusikanamo omilomo waya nzurukhu opule naateeliyeeyo wuuzanyela etthu-yoojiwa ori woolikana. Apha, naateeliye orutisa,
na theenya natana nzurukhu nkinoko yoori nuuzanyele etthu-yoojiwa. Khaninjuweeni nlupa aatthiiyeemo nzurukhu aya opu mvisurupa mwetthu.”
Aphano karumeya otule khujipu araka: “Mwihoove na wala mwihisuthuwe. Nluku otu weenu mweeyo na otu wa papeenu ti ye atthiiyeemo nzurukhu mvisurupa mwenu, ila miiyo kaapokhereliye nzurukhu opule mwaataniyeeyo.” Karumeya khumfukulela Simiyooni khuntiisa attaaphale aariivo attwiize.
Nawiisha khuwaathuula khuwaavirisa nnyupa wa Yuusufu, khuwenkha maati khoosa moolu aya na khwinkha etthu-yoojiwa apuuru aya.
Attwiize Yuusufu khwaattalela tthuvo epile aataniyeezo khusala anwejela, maana aajuwiye yoori nthana aari oteela oja vamote na-ye.
Wakathi Yuusufu afiiyeevo owawe, yo khweettela tthuvo epile aatiisiyeezo khumwinkha khukokhoraza omaasho wawe khufiisa ajihi zaya vathi.
Ye khuwenkha hapari, nawiisha khuwoozela yoori: “Papeenu otule mwaakuuziyeeyo nalelo ori haayi?” Owaakho nkumi?
Yo khunjipu yoori: “Karumeyeenu papeetthu ori haayi, owaakho nkumi.” Yo khukokhora khwiinama.
Ye khulansa maasho awe khumoona ttwiiye Bejami mwaana wa mamaawe. Khuwoozela yoori: “Ttwiiyenu otu mwaari onlupaaye w'eefutti ti othuutu?” Ye khumuuza Bejami yoori: “Nluku awinkhe rehema mwanaka!”
Yuusufu khwiiyana furaha khuluyeene mwaasa wa ttwiiye, khusala atakha olila, nasaapiru khulaavo khweetta okatthi wawe khusala alila.
Nawiisha, khufuushula khurutela vansana ari woojiitthaaza khulupa yoori: “Mwininkhe etthu-yoojiwa.”
Khusaruliwa etthu-yoojiwa meeza mattatthu, mamote a Yuusufu, makina a attwiize na makina a Amisuri aari ottuukho. Mwaasa yoori yaari haraamu atthu a Misuri oja na Meebereewu.
Attwiize Yuusufu khwiikhala vameeza kharipu na-ye, khuthataanya waaza nttunkhulu mpakha efutti, khusala eekesana mmote na nzaawe ari ooshanka.
Yuusufu khuruma winkhiwa etthu-yoojiwa ethiitile enkhiweeyo vameeza vawe, sahani ya Bejami khuziti swaafu thaanu sahani za attwiize. Yo khuja, khunywa, khufurahi vamote na Yuusufu.
Yuusufu khunruma karumeya nwulu wa vaje vawe yoori: “Wiitaaze saaneene etthu-yoojiwa visurupa za atthu apa anwahaaye othuula, ottheemo nzurukhu aya omilomo wa visurupa zaya.
Nawiisha, othuule pilawuri yaka ya feeta otthe omilomo w'eesurupa y'ootu w'eefutti aya na nzurukhu aya opo atiisiyeeyo wuuzanyela tiriku.” Karumeya otule khuretta etthiipo ooziweezo ti Yuusufu.
Mmeesho mwaya supuyeene, attwiize Yuusufu khunleeza khuthuula apuuru aya khusala alawa.
N'oolaazamo nsitati mphule ahinafiyaze peetiwene, Yuusufu khunruma karumeyaawe yoori: “Olankhe nasaapi apha owaatthirele atthu apale eettiye aphale, amana owaasikana wa woozele yoori: Oretteliwa vitthu zooshapweya mweeyo mwinripha zootakhala?
Mweeyela-ni pilawuri ya mbwanaaka? Khahiyo ethiito annywelakaaye na anjuwanaaye vitthu zoorettikhana? Mweeyo mwaretta vitthu zootepa otakhala.”
Ye khuwaatthirela mpakha owaasikana khuwooza etthiipile ooziweezo ti Yuusufu.
Yo khujipu araka: “Mwaasa aya niini mbwaneetthu alupaka toowo? Fweeyo akarumeyaawe khaninwahi oretta vitthu zaya epo!
Onuupuwela yoori fweeyo nawahi orutisa nzurukhu Kanaani naasikaniyeeyo omilomo wa visurupa zetthu? Toowo n'aatthu ninwahaaye wiiya feeta ama thahapu ya vaje wa mbwanaawo?
Apha niriivo, karumeya otule onttelaaye onsikanana pilawuri eto afwe. Fweeyo ninttela osala niri amwiitthwaana za mbwaneetthu.”
Ye khuri: “Kakhupali epo mwilupiyeezo, ila othuuto kinttelaaye onsikanana ti ye anttelaaye wiiya mwiitthwaana aka, mweeyo khamwiniiyana hatha koosa.”
Wakhula ntthu khupakhula esurupa yawe khupweha vathi khufukula nasaapiru.
Karumeya otule khwaaza weekesa mwiisurupa y'ootu nwulu khwiishela esurupa y'ootu w'eefutti aya. Attaaphale khusikana pilawuri etile mwiisurupa ya Bejami.
N'ooretta toole, khuvarula kuwo zaya, khupakhira opheya visurupa zaya vapuuru khusala arutela ositati ottuukhule.
Yuuda na attwiize n'oofiya owawe Yuusufu khunsikana ye ari ottuukho, khukokhora khwiinama attaaphale aariivo Yuusufu.
Yuusufu khuwoozela yoori: “Mwarettela-ni etthu eti? Mweeyo khamwinjuwa yoori ntthu nkhama miiyo kinwahi woona vitthu nkhama epo?”
Yuuda khujipu araka: “Niwuuze niini mbwanaaka! Apho nijihakikhi toovi? Nluku avithula twampi zetthu. Aphano n'aamwiitthwaana za mbwaneetthu nkhama otule asikananiweeyo pilawuri.”
Yuusufu khulupa yoori: “Miiyo akinwahi oretta etthu aya eto! Othuuto asikananiweeyo pilawuri yaka ti ye anttelaaye wiiya mwiitthwaana aka, mweeyo mwirutele wapapeenu na heeri.”
Yuuda khunsusela Yuusufu khumuuza yoori: “Safwatali mbwanaaka! Mwinlikhe karumeyeenu awuuzeni nttakhuzi na mwihinkatipukhele, mwaasa yoori mweeyo mwiri nkhama Firawuuna mwennyeweene.
Mbwanaaka mwaawoozeliye akarumeyeenu mwiraka: ‘Mwinaaye papeenu na ttwiiyenu?’
Fweeyo khujipu yoori: ‘Ninaaye paapa ila ooluvala na ninaaye ttwiiyetthu w'eefutti apattikhaniyeeyo paapa ooluvaliye. Aarina ttwiiye afwa, ye asala otthwe wuumamani wawe, ti woophetiwa na kuvu ti papaawe.’
Mweeyo mwaawaarumiye akarumeyeenu yoori antiise mwite mwimoone khwa maasho enu.
Ila fweeyo khuujipuni mweeyo mbwanaaka: ‘Mwaana oto khanwahi olikhiwa ti papaawe. Amana ampwetheya, papantthu ontta ofwa.’
Ila mweeyo khunuuza yoori: ‘Amana mweeyo mwihintiisi mwihirutelevo vaje vaka apha.’
N'oofiya onti, fweeyo khumuuza papeetthu mattakhuzi apale mwaanuuziyeeyo mbwaneetthu.
Nawiisha ye khuniruma yoori mwirutelewo mwilawe moozanye etthu-yoojiwa.
Fweeyo khumuuza yoori: ‘Khaninwahi orutelawo nihilawaneeni ttwiiyetthu otu wa w'eefutti, amana nihilawani khaninlawa okutthanana mwiinyi oto.’
Karumeyeenu papeetthu khunuuza yoori: ‘Mweeyo mwinjuwa yoori muukhaaka akipatthela aana awiri,
otu mmote akaashikha mpakha leelo eti akinamoone. Kakhupali yoori ooliwa ti nyama ya ntthuttu khunrafuna.
Amana mwinlazavo otu n'ompattha etthu yootakhala, mwintta okiishukhelisa aahera na pwi zaka kirina huzuni yoototheliwa ti mweyo.’
Aphano amana nirutela onti ninlikha ye, nintta omuulaana huzuni papeetthu, mwaasa yoori mwanawe animphetachaaye. Akarumeyeenu anttela ompatthisa papaaya wiishukhela aahera na pwi zawe arina huzuni.
<range>
Olikha eto, miiyo kamwaahiti paapa yoori kininrutisa, amana kihinrutisi kookosani ohaayi aka wooshi.
Apho kinuuvekela yoori safwatali, miiyo kintta osala kiri mwiitthwaaneenu mbwanaaka zwaamu ya shapu otu, mwinlikhe ye arutele onti na attwiize.
Toowo kinttela orutela toovi wapaapa woohilawani shapu otu? Miiyo akinwahi woona ari mmatteso paapa.”
Nawiisha Yuuda ottakhula, Yuusufu khusala oojeela ojilipisela. Khuwooza akarumeyaawe ooshi olaavo, khuhiivo hatha ntthu ajijuwisaka attwiize.
Ye khusala alila anyakulaka mpakha khufiyelela osiila Amisuri, hapari epile khufiya wamfwalume Firawuuna.
Ye khuwooza attwiize yoori: “Miiyo ki Yuusufu! Nkahayani, paapa ori haayi?” Attwiize khuhisala awahi onjipu mwaasa yoori aari ooshanka channu.
Khuwooza attwiize yoori: “Mwisusele apha kiriivo.” Yo khunsusela khuwooza yoori: “Miiyo ki Yuusufu, otule mwaamuuzanyisiyeeyo khutaniwa Misuri.
Apho mwihishanke wala mwihishowerane mwaasa wookuuzanyisa khutaniwa okhuno. Ila Nluku eettiye okilokozisa yoori muusuru nafusi zenu.
Zavira nyaakha miwiri za jala mmamiti mphule ila zasala theenya nyaakha mithaanu atthu ahinteelaaye olima wala wuurula.
Nluku akiperekha vakatthi venu mweeyo yoori kuusuru ohaayi eenu muulumwenku mphu na apa anttelaaye ovokoliwa.
Khahiyo mweeyo mwikiperekhiye okhuno, ila Nluku ti ye akiperekhiye, khukiretta wiiya nkhama paapa wa Firawuuna, na nttunkhulu wa vaje vawe na tuniya ya Misuri.
Mwaakuve mwirutele wapaapa mwamuuze yoori: Mwanenu Yuusufu alupa yoori: Nluku akinkha ottunkhulu wa Misuri yooshi. Ate okhuno, ahirupaze!
Mwite mwiikhale nti wa Gosheni kharipu na-miyo, mweeyo na atuulwenu, aaneenu, pwittipwitthi zenu, mompe zenu, na vitthu zenu zooshi mwiriinaazo.
Ottuukho kisala kiwinkhani etile enuuhithajiyaanini, mweeyo na vaje venu na zooshi mwiriinaazo yoori mwihihoowe, maana zasala nyaakha epi mithaanu za jala.
Mweeyo mwinikoona na maasho enu, na ttwiiyaku Bejami onikoona, yoori khweele ti miyo kinlupaaye mattakhuzi apa.
Mwilawe mwamuuze paapa owahi kiriina Misuri na zooshi epile mooniyeezo. Apho mwaakuve mwilawe mwantiise ottuukhuno.”
Yuusufu khumpatikha ttwiiye Bejami khusala alila, na-ye Bejami khumpatikha khusala alila.
Nawiisha khuwaapejari attwiize ooshi khusala alila. Attaapho attwiize phi awahiyeevo ottakhula na-ye.
Hapari epile khumfiyela Firawuuna, yoori attwiize Yuusufu ata. Firawuuna n'oosiila khwiiya wootuveliwa vamote na akarumeyaawe.
Aphano Firawuuna khumuuza Yuusufu yoori: “Owooze attwiizo: Athuule nyama zaya arutele tuniya ya Kanaani.
Amweettele papeenu na ajamaazenu ooshi ate okhuno. Miiyo kintta owenkha puuro swaafi mmuti mphu, yoori asala aja vitthu zootuva zinruweriwaaye nttumphu.
Athuule mikukutta za Misuri ethiiti aweettele aanaaya, aakhaaya na papeenu.
Mwihiiyane hatha shaakha na mali zenu zooshi mwiriinaazo, maana vitthu zooshapweya za tuniya yooshi ya Misuri zinttela wiiya zeenu.”
Aana a Yaakhumpa khuretta etthiipile. Yuusufu khuwenkha mikukutta nkhama etthiipile aalupiyeezo Firawuuna, khuwenkha vitthu-zooja ntarikhi alawaka.
Wakhula ntthu khumwinkha kuwo pheeya ila Bejami khumwinkha miiya ttatthu za nzurukhu wa feeta na kuwo thaanu pheeya.
Khuperekha apuuru khumi zipakhiriye vitthu zaariiwo Misuri zootuva yoori alawe enkhiwe papaawe, khuperekha theenya apuuru khumi zipakhiriye tiriku na phaawu na vitthu kiina za akhipa yoori asala aja ntarikhi.
Nawiisha, khuleezana na attwiize yo khulankha khusala alawa, ye khuwooza yoori: “Mwihishowerane ntarikhi.”
Yo khulankha Misuri khusala alawa Kanaani wa papaaya Yaakhumpa.
N'oofiya khumuuza papaaya yoori: “Yuusufu nalelo ori haayi, nttunkhulu wa Misuri yooshi!” Yaakhumpa n'oosiila khuzileya mwaasa woohaamini.
Ila nawuuziwa mattakhuzi apale aalupiyeeyo Yuusufu, na khoona mikukutta epile aaperekhiyeezo yoori zilawe zanthuule papaawe, rooho yawe khutamo.
Yaakhumpa khulupa yoori: “Mwanaka ori haayi! Kintta olawa kamoone kihinafwe.”
Ezirayeele khuthuula vitthu zawe zooshi aariinaazo, khulawa mpakha Beresheba. N'oofiya okhule, khuretta twaha anrettelaka Nluku aari omwaaputwaaye papaawe, Esiyaakha.
Nluku anteeliye Ezirayeele osikhu nkatthi wa jozi khusala ankhuwela araka: “Yaakhumpa! Yaakhumpa!” Ye khujipu yoori: “Lapeekha!”
Ye khuri: “Miiyo ki Nluku, Nluku wa papaawo. Ohoove olawa tuniya ya Misuri, maana khwa weyo kinttela opuwisa khapila khuluyeene.
Miiyo kinlawa vamote na-weyo Misuri na kinlawa koorutisele mmuti nttumphu. Amana ofwa Yuusufu ti ye anttelaaye ophulula maasho awo.”
Aphano, Yaakhumpa khulankha nti wa Beresheba na aanaawe na aakhaaya na aanaaya khupakhira mmikukutta epile zaaperekhiweeyo ti Firawuuna.
Khuthuula maphanko a nyama, na mali zaya zooshi epile aapatthiyeeyo tuniya ya Kanaani, Yaakhumpa khusala alawa Misuri na ajamaaze ooshi.
Aanaawe aalume na aanaaya, aanaawe aakha na-yo na aanaaya, ajamaaze ooshi khuwaathuula khusala alawa Misuri.
Apa mazina a meezirayeele, Yaakhumpa na ajamaaze aalawaniyeeyo Misuri: Ruubeni, mwaana wamwanzo wa Yaakhumpa.
Aana a Ruubeni pi apa: Enookhi, Phaalu, Hezorooni na Khariimu.
Aana a Simiyooni pi apa: Yemuweeli, Yamiini, Ohaati, Yakhini, Sohaari na Shawuuli mwaana wa nunu mmote wa Kanaani.
Aana a Leevi pi apa: Geerishoni, Kohaathi na Meraari.
Aana a Yuuda pi apa: Eeri, Onaani, Sheela, Pereezi na Zeera. Eeri na Onaani afwa tuniya ya Kanaani. Aana a Pereezi pi apa: Hezorooni na Hamuuli.
Aana a Ezakaari pi apa: Toola, Phuuva, Yashuubu na Shimrooni.
Aana a Zabulooni pi apa: Seredi, Elooni, na Yaleeli.
Apa atuulu na aana a Yaakhumpa aawaavokoliyeeyo na Liiya nti wa Paata-Araamu, ohintthiimo mwanawe Tiina. Ooshi aari talaathiini na attatthu.
Aana a Gaadi pi apa: Sefiyooni, Haaki, Shuuni, Esbooni, Eeri, Aroodi na Areeli.
Aana a Asheeri pi apa: Imunna, Eshwiiva, Eshwiivi, Beriiya na ttwiiye Zeera. Aana a Beriiya pi apa; Hepeere na Malikiyeeli.
Apa aana a Yaakhumpa na Ziilipa, karumeya otule Labani aamwinkhiyeeyo mwanawe Liiya. Ooshi aari khumi na sitha.
Aana a Rakeele muukha wa Yaakhumpa aari apa: Yuusufu, na Bejami.
Asenaathi mwaana wa Potifweera, nttunkhulu wa tiini ya Ooni aavokoleliwe aana awiri ti Yuusufu tuniya ya Misuri, Manaase na Efwarayiimu.
Aana a Bejami pi apa: Beela, Beekheri, Ashibeeli, Geera, Naamani, Eehi, Rooshi, Muupimu, Huupimu na Haridi.
Apa aana a Rakeele aavokoleliweeyo ti Yaakhumpa, ooshi aari khumi na wane.
Mwaana wa Daani aari Hushimu.
Aana a Nafitaali pi apa: Yaseeli, Kuuni Yeseeri, na Shileemu.
Apa aana a Yaakhumpa na Biila, karumeya otule Labani aamwinkhiyeeyo mwanawe Rakeele. Ooshi aari sapa.
Atthu ooshi apale aalawaniyeeyo Yaakhumpa Misuri aari ajamaaze, ohiwaatthiimo aakha a aanaawe, aari siithiini na sitha atthweene.
Owaatthaamo aana a Yuusufu aavokoliweeyo tuniya ya Misuri, ojama wooshi wa Yaakhumpa waari wa atthu saapiini.
Aphano Yaakhumpa khunlokozisa Yuuda wa Yuusufu, yoori alawe amuuze anthepeeze nti wa Gosheeni. Afiiyeevo nti wa Gosheeni,
Yuusufu khuthuula nkukutta awe khusala alawa okutthana na papaawe, Ezirayeele. N'oomoona khuntthirela khulawa khumpatikha, khuvira wakathi wa waatta eettaka olila.
Yaakhumpa khumuuza Yuusufu yoori: “Aphano kiwooniyeevo yoori ori haayi, kimfwa kihina shaakha.”
Yuusufu khuwooza attwiize na ajaama a papaawe yoori: “Kintta wa Firawuuna kamuuze yoori attwiizaku na ajamaaze paapa apa aari wiikhalaaye tuniya ya Kanaani, ata mmuti mphu.
Kinttela omuuza yoori yo amakhampuzi, ataaka atiisa nyama zaya, pwittipwitthi, mompe na vitthu zaya zooshi ariinaazo.
Amana Firawuuna arumisa oteela okhuweliwa mweeyo, na awuuzelani yoori ‘Mwinkhola khaazi-ni?’
Mwinjipu yoori: ‘Fweeyo akarumeyaawo khaazi yetthu oshukisa nyama, waaza osimaana etthu mpakha apha, nkhama etthiipo aari orettaazo apapazetthu.’ Toowo, mwintta okhupaleliwa wiikhala nti wa Gosheeni, mwaasa yoori amakhampuzi ooshi pi ootarawiwa pi a Misuri.”
Yuusufu khulankha olawa omuuza Firawuuna yoori: “Paapa na attwiizaku ata ari nti wa Gosheeni, atana maphanko a nyama, mompe, pwittipwitthi na vitthu zaya zooshi ariinaazo.”
Khuwaathuula attwiize athaanu olawa owaajuwisa Firawuuna.
Aphano Firawuuna khuwoozela attwiize Yuusufu araka: “Mwinkhola khaazi-ni?” Yo khunjipu yoori: “Mbwaneetthu, fweeyo khaazi yetthu oshukisa nyama nkhama apapazetthu apa aviriyeeyo.
Fweeyo nateela wiikhala mmuti mphu siikhu vattitthiiru, mwaasa yoori tuniya ya Kanaani yeetta opuwawo jala ya waatta nyama zetthu khuhisala ziiyana etthu-yooja. Safwatali wa safwatali, mwinilikhe niikhale nti opu wa Gosheeni.”
Aphano Firawuuna khulupa yoori: “Papaawo na attwiizo ata wiiya vamote na-weyo.
Tuniya ya Misuri eri mmakhono mwawo. Apho, papaawo na attwiizo owenkhe Gosheeni ti yiiyiye phantte yooshapweya ya mmuti mphu, eekhale ottuukho. Na amana woona yoori vakatthi wa ajamaazo awaapho atthu ariina akhili, owenkhe ottunkhulu wa mompe zaka.”
Yuusufu khunthuula papaawe Yaakhumpa khulawa onjuwisa Firawuuna, Yaakhumpa khumparikhiya.
Firawuuna khumuuzela Yaakhumpa araka: “Mwina nyaakha mikavi?”
Yaakhumpa khunjipu araka: “Kinaaye nyaakha miiya na talaathiini, keettaka osaafiri kijeettettelaka. Nyaakha epi kivirisiyeeyo vattitthiiru na pi zootakhala, mpakha apha akinafiye nyaakha epile eekhaliyeezo amarehemu apapazaku.”
Aphano Yaakhumpa khumparikhiya Firawuuna, nawiisha khuruti.
Yuusufu khumwinkha meekhazi papaawe na attwiize phantte yooshapweya ya tuniya ya Misuri waattamana na nti wa Ramesesi, nkhama etthiipile Firawuuna aalupiyeezo.
Ye khumwinkha papaawe na attwiize na ajamaaze ooshi etthu-yooja, yowaafiyela wakhula ntthu na aanaawe.
Khuthowa etthu-yooja tuniya ya Misuri mpakha Kanaani yooshi. Atthu khusala akureya mwaasa wa jala waatta.
Aphano Yuusufu khukusanya nzurukhu wooshi, opule waari orumeeliwaaye Misuri na wa Kanaani opule waari wuuzanyeliwaaye tiriku, khulawa khupweha owawe Firawuuna.
Wakathi wiishiyeevo nzurukhu wa Kanaani na Misuri, khulankha Amisuri khulawa onvekhela Yuusufu araka: “Safwatali, oninkhe etthu-yooja nihifwe onoonaka mwaasa woohiina nzurukhu.”
Yuusufu khujipu araka: “Nkhama mweeyo khamwina nzurukhu, mwikitiisele nyama zenu nipatili na etthu-yooja.”
Amisuri khuthuula pwittipwitthi zaya, mompe, khavalo, na apuuru aya, khulawa khumwinkha Yuusufu, ye khuwenkha etthu-yooja aari weettelaaye oja mwaakha wooshi.
Mwaakha aya opule khwiisha, mwaakha nkina khurutelawo wa Yuusufu olawa omuuza yoori: “Mbwaneetthu khaninoona etthu yoovitha, nzurukhu etthu waniishela, nyama zetthu p'iipile niwinkhiyeenini. Khanisalaneeni hatha etthu, nasalana mwiili etthu na mashapa etthu paasi.
Ohinilikhe nifwaka na mashapa etthu apwecheyaka weettaka woona. Wuuzanye mashapa etthu na-fweyo aya, oninkhe etthu-yooja. Toowo niniiya amwiitthwaana za Firawuuna na mashapa eetthu anttela wiiya awe. Oninkhe peewu yoozala yoori nipatthe wiiyana meekhazi, nihifwe jala na nti etthu ohiiye yaara.”
Khwa nanna ethiito Yuusufu khuuzanya mashapa ooshi a Misuri khwiiya a Firawuuna. Amisuri ooshi aarina yawuuzanyisa mashapa aya mwaasa wa jala yeetta otepa yaattaka, nti wooshi khwiiya wa Firawuuna.
Yuusufu khuwaaretta omwiitthwaana atthu ooshi a phantte yooshi ya Misuri.
Ila mashapa a attunkhulu a tiini khoozanyiye mwaasa yoori yo aari winkhiwa etthu-yooja ti Firawuuna, ti etthu ahoozanyiseliyeeyo mashapa aya.
Aphano Yuusufu khuwooza atthu yoori: “Mwikisiileze! Kawuuzanyani mweeyo na miti zenu zooshi. Waaza leelo mweeyo na mashapa enu anttela wiiya a Firawuuna. Peewu eti mwilawe mwazale.
Wakhula etile mwinttelaaye oruwera mwisala mwithuula lifunku la thaanu mwimwinkha Firawuuna. Mafunku apa mane mwinsalanaaye mwisala mwija mweeyo na aaneenu na atthu apale mwiniikhalanaaye. Kinoko khupweha yoori mwirette peewu.”
Yo khujipu araka: “Weeyo mbwaneetthu wanuusuru, wanirettela vitthu zooshapweya, fweeyo nakhupali na rooho zetthu zooshi wiiya amwiitthwaana za Firawuuna.”
Yuusufu khulaleya kano moote eriivo mpakha leelo eti, yoori lifunku la thaanu la vitthu zooshi zinruweriwaazo tthi la Firawuuna. Mashapa apale paasi a attunkhulu a tiini khuhinkhiwi wiiya awe.
Meezirayeele khuthamela Misuri nti wa Gosheeni. Ottuukho khupatthawo meekhazi khuvokolelana khwaattelana.
Yaakhumpa eekhaliye tuniya ya Misuri nyaakha khumi na sapa, nyaakha eekhaliyeezo Yaakhumpa ohaayi awe wooshi zaari miiya na arupayiini na sapa.
Ooniyeevo yoori mansha awe asala vattitthiiru khunkhuwela mwanawe Yuusufu khumuuza yoori: “Nkhama onikipheta othuule nkhono awo otthe vathi wa liphaja laka, olaphe nkhama onteela oretta na pheta ya waamineya etile kuuvekeliyeeyo, yoori ohikizikhe tuniya ethiiti ya Misuri.
Amana kifwa okilazemo tuniya eti olawe wakizikhe nti opule azikhiweewo apapazaku, kilawe keeye vamote na-yo.” Yuusufu khujipu araka: “Kinttela oretta etthiipo mwikirumiyeezo.”
Aphano Yaakhumpa khunkhanyerela yoori alaphe, Yuusufu khulapha, Yaakhumpa khwiinamela ovishwa w'oolili.
Wakathi ziviriyeevo vitthu epile, khuuziwa Yuusufu oriwa: “Papaawo nlwele.” Ye khulankha khusala alawa omoona, alawaka khuwaathuula aanaawe awiri, Manaase na Efwarayiimu.
Khuuziwa Yaakhumpa yoori: “Mwanenu Yuusufu ontta ota oteela owoona.” Ezirayeele khujilipisela khulankha khwiikhala voolili.
Aphano Yaakhumpa khumuuza Yuusufu: “Nluku Woowahi Wooshi aakipuweleliye nti wa Luuzu tuniya ya Kanaani khukiparikhiya,
akuuzaka yoori: ‘Kinteela owinkha mavokozi na kaattise peewu yawo yoori khwa weyo epuwe khuntti za waatta na kinkhe nti opu peewu yawo khwa mileele.’
Aanaawo apa awiri avokoliweeyo Misuri miiyo kihinate, Manaase na Efwarayiimu apa aya pi aka aanaaka, nkhama etthiipo Ruubeni na Simiyooni eeyiyeezo aanaaka.
Ila apa onttelaaye owaavokola theenya anttela wiiya awo apa pa yo anttelaaye orithi zwaamu ya attwiizaya.
Kirutaka Paata-Araamu akifwela muukhaaka Rakeele tuniya ya Kanaani, kiri ntarikhi kisaleelaka ofiya nti wa Efwarata. Miiyo khunzikha phantte ya tarikhi ya Efwarata oniitthiwaawo Belemu.”
Ezirayeele n'oowoona aana a Yuusufu khuuzela araka: “Khi apa apaani?”
Yuusufu khunjipu papaawe yoori: “Apa aana akinkhiyeeyo Nluku mmuti nttumphu.” Ezirayeele khulupa yoori: “Okitiisele apha kiriivo yoori kiwaaparikhiye.”
Maasho awe Ezirayeele khaari woona saana mwaasa wa wuuluvala, Yuusufu khuwaathuula aana apale khumwaattamisela pwapwaaya, ye khuwaapatikha khuwaapejari.
Ezirayeele khumuuza Yuusufu yoori: “Wala akaari wuupuwela yoori kaari oteela woonanana weeyo theenya, ila Nluku akinoza mpakha aanaawo!”
Elottelanaka Yuusufu khuwaalazavo aana apale vamakutha wa pwapwaaya khwiinama khufiyisa ajihi yawe vathi.
Yuusufu khuwaathuula aanaawe oowiiri, Efwarayiimu nkhono-nlume phantte ya nkhono-nkha wa Ezirayeele, Manaase khunthuula nkhono-nkha phantte ya nkhono-nlume wa Ezirayeele khunttha khuwaattamisela pwapwaaya.
Ezirayeele khookola nkhono awe weelume veeshwa wa Efwarayiimu, otu nttiitthi aya, nkhono-nkha khuttha veeshwa wa Manaase otu nwulu.
Aphano khumparikhiya Yuusufu araka: “Nluku otu anrumeyeliyeeyo apapazaku, Eburahiima na Esiyaakha, Nluku otu ankishukaaye ohaayi aka wooshi mpakha leelo,
Nlayikha ntthi likilaziyeemo nkatthi wa vitthu zootakhala, liwaaparikhiye asimaana apa. Khwa yo livuwisiwe nzina laka na mazina a apapazaku, Eburahiima na Esiyaakha, eeyane peewu ya waatta vatuniya.”
Wakathi Yuusufu amooniyeevo papaawe athuuliye nkhono awe nlume khuttha veeshwa wa Efwarayiimu, ye khuhintuveli. Khulazavo nkhono-nlume wa papaawe veeshwa va Efwarayiimu khuttha veeshwa va Manaase.
Khumuuza papaawe yoori: “Khahiyo toowo paapa, otu ti ye eeyiye nttunkhulu, apho nkhono-nlume mwinttheele othuuto veeshwa vawe.”
Ila papaawe khuhitakhi khuri: “Miiyo kinjuwa mwanaka etthu kinrettaaye. Manaase onttela wiiya khuntti khuluyeene na onteela wiiyana peewu ya waatta, ila ttwiiye otu nttiitthi onteela onziti ye, peewu yawe enttela wiiya khuntti za waatta.”
Aphano khuwaaparikhiya siikhu ethiitile araka: “Atthu a Ezirayeele anteela owaaparikhiya azaaya arumeyelaka mazina enu araka: ‘Nluku ooretteni nkhama Efwarayiimu na Manaase.’” Paata ya toowo, khunwulisa Efwarayiimu zayita Manaase.
Elottelanaka, Ezirayeele khumuuza Yuusufu yoori: “Apha miiyo nasaapi kimfwa, ila Nluku onttela wiiya vamote na-mweyo na ti ye anttelaaye wuurutiselani nti wa apapazenu.
Apho kawinkha nti w'oonyaako wa Shekemu weeyo owaazitiyeeyo attwiizo, etile kiwaanyakanyiyeeyo amoori kuumananaka phanka yaka na mattetthe aka.”
Yaakhumpa khuwaakhuwela aanaawe khuwooza yoori: “Mwite apha kiwuuzeni vitthu zinttelaaye orettikhana siikhu epo zintaazo.
Mwisusele apha mwisiile aana a Yaakhumpa, mwinsiileze papeenu Ezirayeele.
Weeyo Ruubeni, mwaana woomwanzo aka, kuvu zaka, nshumo woomwanzo woojikhitiri wooshapu aka, mwanzo wooshitahiwa channu na wookhomaala.
Weeyo o wootumpunyeya nkhama maati a mpahari, omwanzo awo wafujeya, mwaasa woolalana muukha wa papaawo, waphuja voolili wa papaawo.
Na-ye Simiyooni na Leevi, ntthu na ttwiiye, phanka zaya puntukhi zoorettana vitthu zoohusuti.
Shawuri zaya miiyo akeepu, na rooho yaka khiri vamote na-yo, mwaasa wa wiiphiiriwa waya awoola atthu khushija ttottopwa za mompe za watthu mwayiini.
Woolaanikha wiiye wiiphiiriwa waya yo, maana pu woowali, woolaanikha yiiye katapu yaya yo, maana pi zookhomaala. Kinlawa kawaaphakulevo vakatthi wa khapila ya Yaakhumpa, kiwaamwazelaka vakatthi wa Ezirayeele.
Weeyo Yuuda, attwiizo anteela wuuttottopela; onttela owaashintta maatuwi awo, aana a papaawo anlawa awiinamele weeyo.
Yuuda, mwaana wa siipa, amana akhola nyama khininsuruwa; onlattanana siipa nwulweene arapaleliye, paani amminyalaaye khunlansa?
Khweele Yuuda khanteela onyakanyiwa ofwalume awe, wala pakhora y'oofwalume eriiye mmwinyoka mwawe, mpakha ate mwennyewe ofwalume, otu anttelaaye oshututeliwa pi atthu ooshi.
Ye onteela ofukelela puuru yawe vanrayi wa wuuva, na mwaanaaya anfukelele veerapi yooshapweya ya nrayi otthuupo. Kuwo zawe nka afulanaka viinyu na ajapi yawe nka afulanaka taamu ya wuuva.
Maasho awe anttela wiiya awaara mwaasa woonywa viinyu ya wuuva, meeno awe anttela wiiya oolakala mwaasa w'oonywa leethi.
Zabulooni onttela wiikhala phantte ya phwaani, onttela wiiya patari ya makalawa; mwiinano awe onlawa mpakha nti wa Sidooni.
Ezakaari puuru wookhomaala arapaleliye vakatthi wa mapwattha mawiri.
Wakathi ooniyeevo yoori tuniya etile yaari ya shirehe na yooshapweya ovumula, ye khwiinamisa mafuzi awe khuvikela mapwattha, khusala akhola khaazi nkhama mwiitthwaana.
Daani, onteela ophuka washariyavo khapila yawe nkhama lihimo limote la Ezirayeele.
Ye onteela wiiya nkhama nyookha eniiyaaye nshini wa tarikhi. Nkhama evili yoovithaalela enlumaaye ekwakuno ya khavalo, namweettettisa khavalo khukwana enyokonyoko.
Oo Mbwanaaka! Miiyo kinweja nusura yawo!
Gaadi onteela wuumananiwa pi annya-viittha ila ye eettaka owiikarisa.
Vitthu-zoojiwa za Azeeri enttela wiiya za nnofu, ye nka avahaka etthu-yooja ethiitile ensuhaaye oja afwalume.
Nafitaali nazoro woojitaphula aniwaapatthaaye aana ooshapweya.
Yuusufu muutthi wa wiima channu waattameliyeeyo nshini wa maati, virapi zaya khurapela vatulu wa muuri.
Maatuwi awe anlawa amuumanane amwiikarisaka na mattetthe aya,
ila nttetthe lawe tthi lookhomaala, makhono awe pi oozivala khwa kuvu za Nwali wa Yaakhumpa, khwa kuvu za Nshuki nwulu, Mwaako wa Ezirayeele,
khwa kuvu za Nluku wa papaawo, Nluku Woowahi Wooshi. Ye ooparikhiye weeyo Yuusufu na parakha za pinkuuni, na parakha za mmaati ariiye vathi w'oolumwenku, na parakha za nyama za waatta na parakha zoovokola.
Parakha za papaawo pi za waatta zayita parakha epile za nyaako epi za raku, na maali za nyaako mittiitthi za mileele. Parakha zooshi epi ziiye veeshwa wa Yuusufu mpakha vaajihi va otule athawuliweeyo vakatthi wa attwiize.
Bejami miiji woosaya, supuyeene ontta okhola nyama na orafuna, njuwa looveva na waawanya epile zinsalaazo.”
Pi atthaapa mahimo khumi na mawiri a Ezirayeele, na mattakhuzi aawooziyeeyo papaaya awaaparikhiyaka, na amwinkhaka wakhula ntthu parakha yawe etile yaamweeziyeeyo.
Elottelanaka Yaakhumpa khuwooza araka: “Kinttela ofwa kilawe kazikhiwe vamote na ajamaazaku apa afwiiyeeyo. Mwakizikhe vamote na apapazaku nlikurakuza liriiye mmashapa wa Eforoni Nhiiti,
nttintthile liriiye Makhipeela kharipu ya Manre tuniya ya Kanaani, nttinttho Eburahiima oozanyeziweeyo ti Eforoni Nhiiti yoori yiiye vilalo yawe.
Ottuukho azikhiweewo Eburahiima na muukhaawe Suhura, na-ye Esiyaakha na muukhaawe Rapekha na theenya ottuukho phi kinzikhiyeewo Liiya.
Nshapa laya na likurakuza laya nttho oozanyaniye Ahiiti.”
Nawiisha mattakhuzi apale aari owoozaaye aanaawe, Yaakhumpa khurutisela moolu awe voolili khurapalela khwiittha phuumu khufwa.
Yuusufu khumwiinamela papaawe omaasho wawe khumpejari khusala alila.
Elottelanaka khuwooza anamajisa thiipa awe yoori anvaaze thiipa ya paalasamu papaawe yoori ahivutte; yo khuretta etthiipo.
Ottukuntteliwa thiipa Ezirayeele weeshiye siikhu arupayiini, nkhama etthiipo aazowereliyeezo Amisuri. Yo eeshiye siikhu saapiini ari mmatthaka.
Nawiisha matthaka apale, Yuusufu khuwooza attunkhulu apale aari wiikhalanaaye Firawuuna araka: “Kookholani moolu mwilawe mwamuuze Firawuuna yoori;
Paapa ahinafwe, aakilaphisiye yoori: ‘N'oofwa kilawe kanzikhe attaapho azikheweevo ajamaaze tuniya ya Kanaani.’ Safwatali mwikilikhe kilawe kanzikhe ottuukho nawiisha kintta ota.”
Firawuuna khunjipu araka: “Wiiya oolaphisiye etta wanzikhe papaawo.”
Aphano Yuusufu khulankha khusala alawa onzikha papaawe vamote na attunkhulu, akarumeya ooshi a Firawuuna na mamunu-munu ooshi a tuniya ya Misuri.
Aalawiye vamote na ajamaaze Yuusufu na attwiize, na ajaama ooshi a Yaakhumpa aasaliiyeeyo aari asimaana na pwittipwitthi na mompe.
Atthu aalawiye mmwikukutta akina vakhavalo, atthu aalawiyeeyo aari a waatta.
Afiiyeevo nti wa Ataati oriiye phantte ya malawa-njuwa ya muuttho Yorotaani, khwiikhala siikhu sapa Yuusufu ari mmatthaka wa papaawe eettaka olila.
Wakathi Akanaani apale aari wiikhalaaye ottuukhule awooniyeevo Amisuri apale eettaka olila nti wa Ataati yo khuri: “Olila opu anlilaaye Amisuri apa nwulweene.” Pi apho khutthaja nzina aphale vaya la Apeele-Misurayiila, eniiyaaye malawa-njuwa ya muuttho Yorotaani.
Aana a Yaakhumpa khuretta etthiipile aawooziyeezo ahinafwe.
Khunthuula khunlawana tuniya ya Kanaani khulawa khunzikha nlikurakuza la Makhipeela waattamana na Manre, nshapa nttintthile Eburahiima oozanyaniyeeyo Eforoni Nhiiti yoori asala awaazikhawo ajamaaze.
Nawiisha ozikha, Yuusufu khurutela Misuri vamote na attwiize na atthu ooshi apale aalawaniyeeyo ozikha.
N'oofwa papaaya, attwiize Yuusufu khuri: “Talili Yuusufu khana liphuta varoho vawe mwaasa wa vitthu epile nanretteliyeezo zootakhala, na-ye khanteela onirettela etthiipo?”
Attwiize khumperekheza nhupi Yuusufu yoori: “Papaawo ahinafwe aanirumiye
yoori niwuuze toono: ‘Safwatali, owaaswaamihi attwiizo khwa koosa na twampi epile ooretteliyeezo mwaasa woohuukholi saana.’ Apho nasaapi eti ninuuvekela yoori, oniswaamihi koosa zetthu, fweeyo niiyiye akarumeya a Nluku otu aari omwaaputwaaye papaawo.” Ye n'oosiila mattakhuzi apale khusala alila.
Aphano khuta attwiize khwiinama khukokhora anvekelaka nswammaha araka: “Nata n'aamwiitthwaana awo.”
Yuusufu khuwooza yoori: “Wala mwihikoove. Miiyo aki Nluku.
Khweele mweeyo mwaakiwazeliye shawuri zootakhala. Ila Nluku khuzukulisa khwiiya zooshapweya. Khwa toowo Nluku awoosuru atthu a waatta mpakha leelo eti.
Apho mwihoove. Miiyo kintta wuukholani mweeyo na aaneenu.” Khwa etthiipo Yuusufu khuwaanyamaza attwiize, mattakhuzi apale aawooziyeeyo aawaafiiye nroho mwaya.
Yuusufu aari wiikhala Misuri vamote na ajaama a papaawe, ye eekhaliye nyaakha miiya na khumi.
Khuwoona aana a Efwarayiimu peewu yattaatthu, theenya khuwaathuula aana a Makhiiri, mwaana wa Manaase, khuwaattha vamoolu vawe.
Yuusufu ahinafwe khuwooza attwiize yoori: “Apha miiyo kinttela ofwa, ila Nluku onteela owaawunini oolazenimo mmuti mphu oolawaneni tuniya etile aamwaahitiyeeyo alaphaka yoori onteela omwinkha Eburahiima, Esiyaakha na Yaakhumpa.”
Ye khuwaalaphisa aana a Ezirayeele araka: “Kiniwuuzani khweele, Nluku onteela owaawunini. Amana zirettikhana epo zaya, mwilawaka nti aya opo mwithuule makhonkolo aka.”
Yuusufu afwa arina nyaakha miiya na khumi. Khuvaaziwa thiipa ya paalasamu mwiili awe yoori ahivutte, khutthiiwa mwiiluza khuzikhiwa tuniya ya Misuri.
Apa mazina a aana a Yaakhumpa eettiyeeyo Misuri, wakhula ntthu na ajamaaze:
Ruubeni, Simiyooni, Leevi, Yuuda;
Ezakaari, Zebulooni, na Bejami;
Daani, Nafitaali, Gaati, na Asheeri.
Aana na atuuluwe Yaakhumpa ooshi aalawaniyeeyo aari sapiyiini; ila Yuusufu aari Misuri ottuukho rakuzeene.
Ziviriyeevo siikhu zawaatta, Yuusufu khufwa na attwiize apale na peewu ya etile.
Ila meezirayiilu apale aasaliyeeyo khuvokolelana khweekezeleya khwaattelana khwiiya okhomaala mpakha khufiyelela omwazeyela mmuti mphule wooshimo.
Aphano Misuri khuthawala mfwalume nkinoko ahaari ojuwaaye hatha etthu monkoni wa Yuusufu.
Aphano ye khuwooza atthu awe yoori: “Mwiwoone meezirayiilu pi awaattelana na ookhomaala zayita fweeyo.
Nlaweni niwaalazele olavilavi yoori ahitepe waattelana, ehiri amana enipuwela viittha yo akusanyeya na maatuwi eetthu anirinkaanyela atthiramo mmuti mphu.”
Aphano amisuri khuwaaretta yo wiiya anamalokozela a khaazi za nkuumu yoori apatthe owaahukhumu na khaazi zoolipa. Khwa etthiipo meezirayiilu khunjekela Firawuuna sitati piiri za sakafu zaari wiitthiwaaye Pito na Rameesi.
Nakhataalikha zaama aari ohukhumwiwaavo, pi aari otepaavo waattelana, tiito amisuri khuwaapattha woova mwaasa wa meezirayiilu;
aphano amisuri khwaaza owaakholisa khaazi zoolipa.
Khweekezela hukhumu muuhaayi mwaya, khwa owenkha khaazi zoolipa nkhama omeya ottophe na waattala thizolo, na okhola khaazi zooshi za mmashapa. Zooshi aari okholisiwa khwa oviitthwaana wootakhalavo.
Mfwalume wa Misuri khuttakhulana anamavokoza a meepereewu aariwitthiwaaye Siifwara na Puuwa yoori:
“Amana mwiwaawunaka meezirayiilu atakhaka ovokola, mwisala mwiwoona aanaaya. Eeyaru aalume, mwisala mwiwoola, ila eeyaru aakha, mwisala mwiwaalikha wiiya haayi.”
Ila anamavokoza apale khumoova Nluku khuhiretti etile ooziweeyo ti mfwalume wa Misuri, khusala awaalikha aana alume wiiya haayi.
Aphano mfwalume wa Misuri khuwaakhuwela khuwoozela yoori: “Mwaari toovi owaalikha aana aalume wiiya haayi?”
Anamavokoza apale khujipu yoori: “Aakha a meezirayiilu afwarikhana na apa a Misuri. Yo pi oojikhitiri, ampattha ekumi ahinafiyevo hatha namavokoza.”
Nluku khwiiya wemaani khwa anamavokoza apale, na meezirayiilu khusala avira eekezeleyaka wookhomaalavo.
Mwaasa wa anamavokoza apale omoova Nluku, ye khuwenkha owahi wa wiiyana ojama waya.
Tiito Firawuuna khuwaaruma atthu awe ooshi yoori: “Wakhula mwaana wa meepereewu anvokoliwaaye eeyaru wanlume amweeselele mmuttho oniitthiwaaye Niilu, ila eeyaru wankha asala anlikha.”
Mwinyi mmote wa lihimo la Leevi anraliye muukha wa lihimo limote na ye.
Khumwiimitthisa khunvokolela mwaana. Amooniyeevo yoori aari wooshapweya khunvitha khwa nyeezi mittatthu.
Nawoona yoori khayaari owaheya ovira anvithaka theenya, khuthuula khelenke ya tteketthe khumattha na piriniisi khuntthaamo mwaana otule, khulawa khunttha ntteketthe nkhome wa muuttho Niilu.
Nlupuwe mwaana otule eemeliye toole sirini yoori oone niini yaari weettelaaye onrettikhanela.
Mwaana wankha wa Firawuuna khwiishukhela mmuttho olawa woowa, ajaazi awe aarina khusala avira nkhome wa muuttho, ye khoona khelenke etile eri ntteketthe khunruma njaazi awe khweettela.
Afunuliyeevo, khunsikanamo mwaana eettaka olila. Khumoonela huruma khuri: “Mwaana otu tuwa meezirayiilu.”
Aphano, nlupuwe mwaana otule khumwaattama mwaana wa Firawuuna khumuuzela yoori: “Onuupuwela toovi? Ontakha miiyo kilawe kankhuwele nunu mmote mwiizirayiilu ate asala amwaamwisa?”
Mwaana wa Firawuuna khunjipu yoori: “Haya etta.” Aphano mwanankha khulawa onkhuwela maama wa mwaana othuutule.
Aphano, mwaana wa Firawuuna khumuuza yoori: “Onthuule mwaana otu omwaamwise zwaamu yaka, kintta wuuripha phakari yawo.” Nunu otule khunthuula mwaana khusala amwaamwisa.
Paata ya mwaana otule owula khuntiisela mwaana wa Firawuuna khunretta wiiya mwanawe. Khuntthaja nzina la Munsa, araka: “Maana koolaza mmaati.”
Siikhu moote, wakathi Munsa apatthiyeevo omwinyi, khulankha khulawa wa attwiize meepereewu khoona khaazi yoolipa aari okholisiwaaye na theenya khumoona mmisuri aari ompiyaaye na onvulalisa mwiipereewu.
Khweekesa okhuno na okhuno nawoona yoori khaari otawo hatha ntthu, khumuula mmisuri otule khunttukuttha vanshaka.
Siikhu yaphiiri khuwaasikana meepereewu awiri oomanaka khumuuza otule aariina paathuli yoori: “Onimpiyela-ni nzaawo?”
Ye khumuuzela yoori: “Paani awinkhiyeeyo onamalokozela weetthu ama onamaphuka? Ontakha okuule nkhama omuuliyeezo mmisuri otule?” Munsa khoova khuri: “Ee, ajuwa etthu kirettiyeeyo!”
Firawuuna nawuuziwa vitthu epile khujilakelela omuula Munsa; ye khutthira khulawa mpakha nti wa Miitiya khwiikhala nshini wa nlipu.
Namalokozela a tiini wa Miitiya aarina aanaawe sapa aakha, yo khuteela ottekha maati atthe n'yopo mwaya enkhe nyama za papaaya.
Aphano khuta mishuki mikina khusala aweekara, ila attaaphale Munsa khulankha khusala awaakisa na khwinkha maati nyama zaya.
Wakathi aruteliyeevo wa papaaya Rewele, ye khuwoozela yoori: “Leelo mwaruti supuyeene mwaasa wa niini?”
Yo khujipu yoori: “Mmisuri mmote ti anaakisiye mmakhono wa mishuki mikina na othuuto khunittekhela maati khunywisa nyama zeetthu.”
Khuuzeliwa ti papaaya yoori: “Apha yaya ori vayi? Mwanlikhelani? Mwankhuwele ate aje na fweeyo.”
Munsa khukhupalela na khutakha wiikhalana mwinyi otule, mwanawe aari wiitthiwaaye Zipoora khunlooza.
Zipoora khunvokola mwaana, Munsa khuntthaja nzina la Yeerisoni alupaka yoori: “Kasaafirela nti wa malaponi.”
Ziviriyeevo siikhu zawaatta khufwa mfwalume wa Misuri; atthu a Ezirayiilu khusala asisimira na okhuwa monkoni wa oviitthwaana, nkhuwo aya opule khunfiyela Nluku.
Nluku noosiila osisimira waya opule khufikhiri wahati aarettaniyeeyo Eburahiima, Esiyaakha na Yaakhumpa.
Nluku khuwoona meezirayiilu khumweeleya tafwawuthi aariinaayo.
Munsa aari oshukisa nyama za nkhwewe Yeeturu, namalokozela a tiini wa Miitiya; siikhu moote khuthuula nyama khusala eettana phantte kiina ya n'yaara khufiya mpakha va mwaako wa Nluku, waari wiitthiwaaye Hereebe.
Attaapho khumpuwelela nlayikha la Nnyizinku va nlimi la moottho waari olankhaaye vakatthi wa muutthi. Munsa khweekesa khoona yoori moottho weetta okholela ila muutthi opule khawaari olukula.
Aphano ye khuri: “Vitthu zootikinisa kintta attaaphale kilawe koone, moottho ontta okholela ila muutthi opule khunlukula mwaasa aya niini?”
Nnyizinku khumoona yoori ye eetta waattama muutthi opule, olawa woona, Nluku khunkhuwela enakatthi-nakatthi ya muutthi otthuupule araka: “Munsa! Munsa!” Ye khujipu araka: “Lapeekha!”
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza yoori: “Ohaattamevo apha! Ovule mmoolu mpho jampali zawo maana puuro yaya eti oriivo ttakatthiifu.”
Khurutela olupa yoori: “Miiyo ki Nluku wa papaawo, Nluku wa Eburahiima, Nluku wa Esiyaakha na Nluku wa Yaakhumpa.” Munsa khufinikha wuuso awe maana aari woova omweekesa.
Nnyizinku khulupa yoori: “Khweele khweele kinoona nanna anhukhumwiwaazo atthu aka Misuri na kasiila nkhuwo aya mwaasa wa khaazi ankholisiwaazo pi anamalokozela a Firawuuna na kinjuwa yoori antta ohoowa;
tiito kiishukhiyeeyo oteela owuusuru mmakhono wa amisuri na kiwaalazakamo mphu kiwaalawanaka nti wooshapweya na nwulweene, ohali liniittikhaawo leethi na asali; ottuukho aniikhalaawo akanaani, ahiiti, amoori, aperizi, amwiivi na ayepuzi.
Maana nkhuwo wa atthu a Ezirayiilu wakifiyela miiyo, na kinoona nanna amisuri aniwaahukhumwaazo.
Kinuuruma nasaapi ethiiti Misuri wa Firawuuna, wawaalazewo atthu aka meezirayiilu.”
Aphano Munsa khulupa amuuzaka Nluku yoori: “Ki paani miiyo woolawa wa Firawuuna olawa owaalazawo meezirayiilu?”
Nluku khunjipu yoori: “Miiyo kiniiya vamote na-weyo. Eto ti alama yoori keetta wuuruma: Amana owaalazawo atthu Misuri wate vamwaako attaapha okaaputu.”
Munsa khumuuzela Nluku yoori: “Miiyo amana kilawa vakatthi wa meezirayiilu kiwooza kiraka: ‘Nluku wa apapazenu akiruma vakatthi-venu,’ khi amana akuuzela yoori: ‘Nzina lawe paani?’ Kiwooze niini?”
Nluku khumuuza Munsa araka: “MIIYO TI MIIYO. Owooze etthiipo meezirayiilu, yoori: ‘MIIYO TI MIIYO ti akirumiyeeyo vakatthi venu.”
Nluku khulupa theenya amuuzaka Munsa yoori: “Wawooze meezirayiilu yoori: ‘Nnyizinku, Nluku wa apapazenu Nluku wa Eburahiima, Nluku wa Esiyaakha na Nluku wa Yaakhumpa, akiruma vakatthi ve.’ Nttho ti nzina linsalaaye kuupuwelaniwaka peewu khwa peewu mileele.”
“Olawe wawaakusanye attunkhulu a meezirayiilu, owooze yoori Nnyizinku, Nluku wa amarehemu apapazenu, Eburahiima, Esiyaakha na Yaakhumpa aakipuweleliye khukuuza yoori: ‘Khweele khweele, Miiyo kinoona tafwawuthi zenu na kinjuwa etthu anuurettelaanini a Misuri.
Miiyo kaahiti wuulazanimo nhukhumu za amisuri kiweettaneni nti wa akanaani, wa ahiiti, wa amoori wa aperizi wa amwiivi na wa ayepuzi nti oniitthaaye leethi na asali.’
“Attunkhulu anteela wuusiileza. Olankhe na attunkhulu a atthu aya atthaapo mwilawe wa Firawuuna wamuuze yoori: ‘Nnyizinku, Nluku wa meepereewu eettiye oniteela. Apho onilikhe nilawe neettette mwentto wa siikhu ttatthu neette n'yaara namwinkhe twaha Nnyizinku, Nluku etthu.’
Miiyo kinjuwa yoori mfwalume wa Misuri khanteela wuulikhani olawa woohiiyi khwa okhanyareliwa pi nkhono woowahi.
Nakatalikha kinteela wookola nkhono aka kiwaavulaze amisuri khwa vitthu zootikinisa zooshi kinttelaazo oretta vakatthi vawo, paata ya toowo ontta wuulikhani olawa.
Na kinteela owenkha amisuri wiiyana niiya na atthu apa na amana mwilaakawo, khamwinlaawo makhono-ru.
Aakha ooshi ana ya owaavekela anamwaattamanana aya na apale aawaamakeliyeeyo vitthu za feeta na za tahapu, na kuwo za owaawalisa aaneenu, aalume na aakha. Khwa etthiipo mwintta ovulula maali zooshi za amisuri.”
Munsa khunjipu Nnyizinku araka: “Wala yo khanteela okhupalela, na khanteela okisiileza, na anlupa yoori: ‘Nnyizinku khoopuweleleeni!’”
Nnyizinku khumuuzela Munsa araka: “Eto oriina mmakhono niini?” Ye khuri: “Pakhora.”
Aphano khumuuza yoori: “Weeselele vathi!” Ye khweesa khuthatuwa khwiiya nyookha Munsa khutthira.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa theenya yoori: “Wookole nkhono awo okhole nkhira aya.” Khookola nkhono awe khukhola, khurutela wiiya pakhora.
“Eto ti ya owaakhupalisa yoori oopuweleliye Nnyizinku, Nluku wa amarehemu apapazaya, Nluku wa Eburahiima, Nluku wa Esiyaakha, Nluku wa Yaakhumpa.”
Nnyizinku khumuuza theenya yoori: “Otthe nkhono awo vamweyo!” Khutthaavo, alazakavo khwiiyana maaharaja khulakala nkhama liwiku.
Nnyizinku khumuuza theenya yoori: “Othuule nkhono awo opheya otthe vamweyo.” Khutthaavo, noolazavo khurutela wiiya sawasawa na mwiili awe wooshi.
Nnyizinku nalelo khuvira amuuzaka araka: “Amana yo ahikhupaleli ama ahitakhi, alama yamwanzo, yaphiiri anteela okhupalela.
Ila amana nalelo eeya ahinakhupalele alama epo piiri wala khuhuusiilezi, ottekhe maati vattitthiiru a mmuttho Niilu, wiitthele tuulu, antta othatuwa maati aya apo a tuulu eeye taamu.”
Aphano Munsa khumuuza Nnyizinku yoori: “Oo, Mbwana, thanku raku miiyo akinwahi ottakhula saana; mpakha nasaapi eti waaziyeevo ottakhulana miiyo, amana kittakhulaka kintta okukuma.”
Nnyizinku khunjipu yoori: “Paani amwinkhiyeeyo milomo pinaatamu? Paani amwinkhiyeeyo ottakhula wala paani awuumpiyeeyo apale ohisiili? Wala apale awoona ama apale ohooni? Khahiyo miiyo Nnyizinku?
Apho olawe, Miiyo kinttela wiiya vamote na milomo zawo na kinuunozela etthu onttelaaye ottakhula.”
Ye khujipu araka: “Oo Mbwanaaka, kinuuvekela yoori onrume ntthu nkina.”
Aphano Nnyizinku khumpattha katapu khwa Munsa, khumuuza yoori: “Weeyo khuna ttwiiyo Arawu, nleevi? Miiyo kinjuwa yoori ye onwahi ottakhula saaneene. Nasaapi eti ye ontta ota oteela okutthanana weeyo, ye onttela wiiya woofurahi amana oosikana.
Weeyo onttela ottakhulana omuuze mattakhuzi anttelaaye olupa; miiyo kintta owaawunini moowiiri yoori mwittakhule na kiwuuzeni etthu yooretta.
Arawu onttela ottakhulana atthu khwa zwaamu yawo, onttela wiiya nlomo awo, weeyo onttela wiiya nkhama Nluku khwa ye.
Othuule pakhora eti mmakhono, ti ethiiti onttelaaye orettana alama za minjuza.”
Aphano Munsa khurutela wa nkhwewe Yeeturu khumuuza yoori: “Safwatali, kilikheni kilawe Misuri kawoone ajamaazaku nkhama nalelo ari haayi.” Yeeturu khujipu araka: “Olawe na heeri.”
Nnyizinku aamuziye Munsa ari Miitiya yoori: “Orutele Misuri maana ooshi apale aari otakhaaye owuula afwa.”
Aphano Munsa khunthuula muukha awe na aanaawe khuwaattha va puuru vawe khusala arutela Misuri. Mmakhono mwawe aathuuliye pakhora ya Nluku.
Nnyizinku khumuuza theenya Munsa yoori: “Miiyo kawinkha owahi wooretta minjuza zawaatta. Amana orutelawo Misuri wiiye woojitthenka yoori orette omaasho wa mfwalume wa nti aya opule minjuza zaya epo, ila miiyo kinlawa koomise rooho yawe ahiwaalikhe atthu apo olawa.
Omuuze Firawuuna oraka: ‘Nnyizinku alupa toono: Ezirayiilu mwanaka wamwanzo.
Miiyo kalupa yoori: “Onlikhe mwanaka alawe akaaputu.” Ila weeyo amana okatthala kintta omuula mwanawo wamwanzo.’”
Eettaka Misuri vahali aamakiyeevo ntarikhi Nnyizinku khunteela Munsa yoori amuule.
Ila Zipoora khuthuula liwe loothokolowa khushija shapala ya soola ya mwanawe khupiyana moolu a Munsa. Khuri: “Weeyo omannaka miiyo khwa taamu.”
Zipoora khuri: “Omannaka khwa taamu,” athoonyezaka okhiriya opule. Wakathi otthuupule Nnyizinku khunlikha Munsa.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Arawu yoori: “Olawe n'yaara wakutthanane Munsa.” Ye khulawa khukutthanana va mwaako wa Nluku, khunchelisa.
Munsa khunthatelela Arawu zooshi epile Nnyizinku anrumiyeezo omuuza, na khumuuza alama zooshi za minjuza arumiweeyo oretta.
Aphano Munsa na Arawu khulawa khuwaakusanya attunkhulu ooshi a meezirayiilu.
Arawu khuwooza zooshi Nnyizinku amuziyeeyo Munsa. Nawiisha naye Munsa khuretta alama za minjuza vakatthi wa atthu apale,
yo khukhupali. Wakathi ajuwiyeevo yoori Nnyizinku awoopuweliye meezirayiilu na aawoniye nanna aari ohoowaazo yo khwiinama khwaaputu.
Paata ya toole Munsa na Arawu khulawa ottakhulana Firawuuna amuuzaka yoori: “Nnyizinku, Nluku wa meezirayiilu alupa toono: ‘Owaalikhe atthu aka alawe akirettele njampo n'yaara.”
Firawuuna khujipu araka: “Nnyizinku paani wonshututela miiyo khuwaalikha olawa meezirayiilu? Akininjuwa Nnyizinku aya na akiniwaalikha meezirayiilu olaamo mphu.”
Munsa na Arawu khukhanyarela araka: “Nluku wa meepereewu ettiye oniteela, safwatali onilikhe nilawe narette safwari ya siikhu ttatthu neettaka n'yaara, namwinkhe twaha Nnyizinku, Nluku etthu, noohiiyi etthiipo antta oniteela marati ama ontta onuula na phanka.”
Aphano mfwalume wa Misuri khumuuza Munsa na Arawu yoori: “Mwaasa aya niini mweeyo mwiwantipwaka atthu na khaazi zaya? Haya! Mwilawe mwakhole khaazi zoolipa.”
Theenya Firawuuna khulupa yoori: “Atthu apa pi awaatta ila mwintta owaalikhisa okhola khaazi zaya.”
Siikhu ethiitile Firawuuna khuwenkha nrumo anamalokozela awe na masuphayi anakhaazi, araka:
“Waaza leelo ethiiti mwihirutele owenkha malala awaattalana thizolo nkhama mwaari orettaazo; asala alawa weekesa eenyewe.
Ila mwiwaakhanyarele waattala thamani ethiitile aari waattalakaaye, mwihiwaavukule hatha etthu; apa aya anamaviliwa, ti eto aaziyeeyo okhuwa araka ‘ninttela omwinkha twaha Nluku etthu.’
Mweekezele khaazi yaya yoolipa yoori ashikheye ahisiileze vitthu zoohatiwa.”
Anamalokozela na masuphayi khulawa khuwooza atthu apale yoori: “Firawuuna alupa toono: ‘Nilikhe owinkhani malala.
Mwilankhe mwilawe mwawooze yoori alawe akusanye malala nhali anwahaaye opatthamo, na khaazi yenu yoolipa khinteela ovukuwavo hatha etthu.”
Aphano atthu apale khumwazeyela nti wooshi wa Misuri khukusanya nyaani khwa zwaamu ya malala.
Anamalokozela a khaazi khuwaattitta awoozaka yoori: “Mwiishise khaazi khwa nanna mooziweezo okhola wakhula siikhu wakathi opule mwaari winkhiwaavo malala.”
Khujalitiwa masuphayi ameezirayiilu apale atthomiweeyo pi anamalokozela a anakhaazi a Firawuuna, na khusala oozeliwa yoori: “Mwaasa aya niini mwihiishisaka khaazi yenu ya waattala thizolo taana wala leelo nkhama mwaari orettazo raku?”
Aphano masuphayi a meezirayiilu khulawa ojiliza wa Firawuuna yoori: “Mwaasa aya niini owaatthanttaka toono akarumeya awo?
Malala khaninkhiwa na ninuuziwa waattala thizolo. Woone, nintta ojalitiwa; ila atthu awo pi ariina paathuli.”
Ila Firawuuna khujipu yoori: “Anamaviliwa! Mweeyo oviliwa! Tiito mwinraaye; ‘Nintakha olawa omwinkha twaha Nnyizinku.’
Nasaapi ethiiti mwirutele okhaazi. Khamwinteela opokhera malala! Ila mwina yawuupa thizolo thamani ethiito mwaari wuupakaaye!”
Masuphayi apale a meezirayiilu khujuwa yoori aari nhukhumu, mwaasa woosiila yoori ahivukule thamani ya thizolo ooziweeyo waattala wakhula siikhu.
Paata ya masuphayi apale noolaavo aphale aariivo Firawuuna, khunsikana Munsa na Arawu eettaka owaaweja.
Yo khulupa yoori: “Nnyizinku ti awooneni na oophukeni; maana mweeyo mwaniretta fweeyo wiiya atthu awiiphira omaasho wa Firawuuna na wa akarumeya awe khuwenkha phanka mmakhono mwaya yoori anuule.”
Aphano Munsa khuzukuluwela wa Nnyizinku khumuuza yoori: “Oo Mbwana, wawaahukhumwelani atthu apa? Khi wakirumeliyeeni?
Maana thanku kilawiyeevo ottakhulana Firawuuna khwa nzina lawo yoori ontta owaahukhumu atthu apa, weeyo khawaarettiye hatha etthu yoori owaataphule!”
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Aphano attaapha ontta woona etthu kinttelaaye onrettela Firawuuna, khwa nkhono aka woowahi ontta owaalikha olawa, khwa nkhono aka woowahi ontta owiikara mmuti mwawe.”
Nluku khumuuza theenya yoori: “Miiyo ki Nnyizinku.
Kampuweleliye Eburahiima, Esiyaakha, na Yaakhumpa nkhama Nluku wa Owahi Wooshi, ila akiwaalikheeni okijuwana nzina la Nnyizinku.
Na theenya kaarettaniye wahati aka wa owenkha nti wa Kanaani, nti aari wiikhalaaye ari aletto.
Nasaapi eti kasiila ojiliza wa meezirayiilu atthaapo amisuri awaarettiyeeyo oviitthwaana na kafikhiri wahati aka karettaniyeeyo.
Nakatalikha owooze meezirayiilu yoori: Miiyo ki Nnyizinku na kinteela owaalazamo nkatthi wa oviitthwaana arettiweeyo pi amisuri. Kiwaataphule khaazi zoolipa epo enkhiweezo na kiniwoosuru na nkhono wookhomaala na owahi nwulweene na hukhumu.
Kinuuthuulani mwiiye atthu aka na-miyo kiiye Nluku enu, aphano pi mwinttelaavo ojuwa yoori miiyo ki Nnyizinku, Nluku enu kuulaziyeenini vathi wa khaazi zoolipa mwenkhiweeyo pi amisuri.
Na kinuuthuulani kiweettaneni nti kaalaphiyeeyo omwinkha Eburahiima, Esiyaakha na Yaakhumpa; apho kiniwinkhani mweeyo wiiye wenu. Miiyo ki Nnyizinku.”
Munsa khuwooza etthiipo meezirayiilu, ila yo khuhitakhi onsiileza, mwaasa wa othunku na hukhumu aari woonaayo nkatthi wa oviitthwaana.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa araka:
“Olawe wamuuze Firawuuna mfwalume wa Misuri yoori awaalikhe meezirayiilu aleemu mmuti mwawe.”
Munsa khunjipu Nnyizinku araka: “Meezirayiilu khanikisiila, khi nannani anttelaaye okisiileza Firawuuna, khupe miiyo kihijuwaka ottakhula saana?”
Ila Nnyizinku anrumiye Munsa na Arawu, yoori awooze meezirayiilu na Firawuuna, mfwalume wa Misuri, yoori etta orumiwa owaalazawo meezirayiilu Misuri.
Attunkhulu a ojama aari apa: Aana a Ruubeni, mwaana nwulu wa Yaakhumpa aari apa: Enookhi, Phaalu, Hesherooni, na Khariimu; opu pi waari ojama wa Ruubeni
Aana a Simiyooni aari apa: Yemuweeli, Yamiini, Ohaati, Yakhiini, Zowaari na Shawaali mwaana wa nunu mmote wa Kanaani; opu pi waari ojama wa Simiyooni.
Apa mazina a aana a Leevi khwa ovokoliwa waya: Yeerisoni, Kowaati, na Meraari. Leevi eekhaliye nyaakha miiya na talaathiini na sapa.
Aana a Yeerisoni khwa ojama aya pi apa, Lipiini na Simeeyi.
Aana a Kowaati pi apa: Anraawu, Izaari, Heporooni na Uziili. Kowaati eekhaliye nyaakha miiya na talaathiini na mittatthu.
Aana a Meraari pi apa; Mali na Muushi. Ntthi laari lihimo la Leevi khwa nanna ya ovokoliwa waya.
Anraawu khunrala Yokipeeti nlupu wa papaawe, khunvokolela Arawu na Munsa, Anraawu eekhaliye nyaakha miiya na talaathiini na sapa.
Aana a Izaari pi apa: Koora, Nefekhe, na Zikiiri.
Aana a Uziili pi apa: Mizayeele, Elizaafwa, na Sithiiri.
Arawu anraliye Elisheepa mwaana wa Aminataapi, nlupu wa Nashooni; ye khunvokolela Nataapi, Apiiwu, Elizaari na Itamaari.
Aana a Koora pi apa: Asiiri, Elikana na Apiyasaafi; ntthi laari lihimo la Akoora.
Elizaari, mwaana wa Arawu, khunrala mwaana mmote wa Putiyeele, khunvokola Fineeya; apa pi attunkhulu a ojama wa Leevi.
Ti Arawu na Munsa atthaapo Nnyizinku awaarumiyeeyo yoori: “Mwilazewo Misuri lihimo la meezirayiilu.”
Pi atthaapo, Munsa na Arawu, anttakhulaniyeeyo Firawuuna mfwalume wa Misuri na niiya ya owaalazawo meezirayiilu.
Siikhu Nnyizinku attakhulaniyeevo Munsa ari nti wa Misuri,
Nnyizinku aamuziye yoori: “Miiyo ki Nnyizinku. Omuuze Firawuuna mfwalume wa Misuri zooshi epile kiniwuuzaaye.”
Munsa khunjipu Nnyizinku araka: “Miiyo akinttakhula saana; Firawuuna onttela okisiila toovi?”
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Miiyo kooretta wiiya nkhama Nluku khwa Firawuuna na ttwiiyo Arawu wiiya nkhama napiyu awo.
Weeyo omuuze zooshi epile kuurumiyeeyo, na ttwiiyo Arawu amuuze Firawuuna awaalikhe meezirayiilu aleemo mmuti mwawe.
Ila miiyo kinteela wuumisa rooho ya Firawuuna na kinteela wenkeza alama zaka na vitthu zaka zootikinisa nti wa Misuri.
Ye khanteela wuusilezani, ila miiyo kinteela wookola nkhono aka khwa Misuri, na khwa khaazi khuluzeene za ophuka, kinteela owaalazawo Misuri atthu a Ezirayiilu.
Phi amisuri anttelaavo ojuwa yoori miiyo ki Nnyizinku, amana kookola nkhono aka khwa Misuri kiwaalazavo meezirayiilu vakatthi vaya.”
Munsa na Arawu khuretta etthiipo Nnyizinku awaarumiyeezo.
Wakathi aattakhulaniyeevo Firawuuna Munsa aarina hirimu ya nyaakha thamaaniini, Arawu aarina hirimu ya nyaakha thamaaniini na mittatthu.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa na Arawu yoori:
“Amana Firawuuna awuuzani yoori: ‘Mwirette minjuza awahi wuukhupalini,’ omuuze Arawu: ‘Athuule pakhora yawo eeselele enakatthi ya Firawuuna,’ pakhora ya eto entta othatuwa yiiye nyookha.”
Aphano Munsa na Arawu khulawa mpakha wa Firawuuna, noofiya khuretta etthiipile Nnyizinku aawaarumiyeeyo. Arawu khuthuula pakhora etile khweeselela enakatthi ya Firawuuna na mashawuriiya awe pakhora etile khuthatuwa khwiiya nyookha.
Aphano naye Firawuuna khuruma olawa okhuweliwa ajuwi na anamajintta; na yo khuretta etthiipo khwa majintta aya.
Wakhula mmote wa yo khusala eesa pakhora yawe na othatuwa nyookha, ila pakhora ya Arawu khumiza pakhora epile.
Ila Firawuuna khuumisa rooho yawe khuhitakhi owaasiileza, nkhama etthiipo Nnyizinku aalupiyeezo.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Rooho ya Firawuuna tiya nthiti khanteela owaalikha atthu apo olawa.
Olawe wakutthanane Firawuuna supuyeene; ye onlawa woowa omuttho. Weemele nshini wa muuttho osala onweja, olawaka othuule pakhora yawo mmakhono etile yaathatuwiyeeyo nyookha.
Omuuze yoori: Nnyizinku, Nluku wa meezirayiilu, akiruma owuuza yoori: Owaalikhe atthu aka alawe akaaputu n'yaara, mpakha leelo khuntakha okisiileza.
Nnyizinku alupa toono: Ethiito ti enttelaaye wuujuwisa yoori miiyo ki Nnyizinku: khwa pakhora eti kiriina mmakhono kintakha kipiye maati a Nniilu athatuwe eeye taamu.
Swi ziriiye mmuttho zinteela ofwa zooshi, osala onukhamo woohifwayivo. Aphano amisuri ewaapatthe enanaari ya onywa maati a mmuttho mphule.”
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa theenya yoori: “Omuuze Arawu athuule pakhora yawo ookolele nkhono maati a Misuri, a mmuttho na mpakha a mmatthatta na a mmazuuku athatuwe eeye taamu, Misuri yooshi yiitaale taamu, mpakha zoopo za thaapwa na za mawe.”
Munsa na Arawu khuretta nkhama etthiipo Nnyizinku awaarumiyeezo. Arawu khushashula pakhora etile, khujapha maati a mmuttho Firawuuna ari attaapho na mashawuriiya awe, maati apale ooshi khuthatuwa taamu.
Swi zooshi zaariimo mmuttho mphule khufwa khusala onukhamo woohifwayivo, Misuri khuhisala owahi onyweyawo maati a mmuttho mwaya mphule nti wooshi waarina taamu.
Nayo anamajintta a Misuri khuretta etthiipo na ojuwa waya woojivitha, ila rooho ya Firawuuna nalelo khusala eri yawuuma khuhitakhi onsiileza Munsa na Arawu nkhama etthiipo Nnyizinku aalupiyeezo.
Firawuuna khuzukuluwa khusala alawa owawe khuhijali epile zaya.
Amisuri ooshi khulawa khuthipa nshini wa muuttho yoori apatthe maati oonywa, maana maati apale a mmuttho khaari onyweya.
Zaaviriye siikhu sapa paata ya Nnyizinku othatusha maati apale a mmuttho.
Nawiisha Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Olawe wa Firawuuna wamuuze yoori Nnyizinku alupa toono: Owaalikhe atthu aka alawe akaaputu.
Amana weeyo ohitakhi owaalikha olawa, kintta operekha pala ya anaphulu nti awo wooshi.
Mmuttho Niilu wooshimo anttela ottheerelanamo anaphulu awaatta, awelele afiye owawo okatthi wawo mpakha voolili vawo na mmanyupa wa mashawuriiya awo mpakha wa atthu awo ooshi na mphule enkhattiwaamo na enoochiwaamu phaawu.
Anaphulu aya apo anttela wuuteela weeyo na mashawuriiya awo na atthu awo ooshi.”
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa araka: “Omuuze Arawu yoori: Wookole nkhono awo othuule pakhora wookolele mmuttho, mmilipu na mmatthatta yoori owaawelelise anaphulu Misuri yooshi.”
Arawu khookolela nkhono yawe maati a Misuri, anaphulu khuwelela khufinikha nti wooshi wa Misuri.
Aphano anamajintta na ojuwa waya woojivitha khuwaapuwisa anaphulu Misuri yooshi.
Firawuuna khuruma olawa okhuweliwa Munsa na Arawu khuwooza yoori: “Mwinvekele Nnyizinku akilaze anaphulu apa miiyo na atthu aka, yiiyaru etthiipo kintta owaalikha atthu apa alawe amwinkhe twaha Nnyizinku.”
Munsa khumuuza Firawuuna yoori: “Ruhusa ti yawo ya okuuza lini ontakhaaye yoori kuulompele weeyo na mashawuriiya awo, atthu awo ooshi, yoori weeyo na vaje vawo mwilaziwe anaphulu asale mmuttho paasi.”
Firawuuna khujipu araka: “Meesho.” Munsa khuri: “Enttela wiiya etthiipo ojipwiyeezo opatthe ojuwa yoori khaavo anlikananaaye Nnyizinku Nluku etthu.
Anaphulu antta wuulikha weeyo, vaje vawo, mashawuriiya awo na atthu awo; anttelaaye osala pi apale ari mmuttho paasi.”
Aphano, Munsa na Arawu khulaavo aphale aarivo Firawuuna, Munsa khunvekela Nnyizinku mwaasa wa anaphulu, nkhama etthiipo aasilaniyeezo na Firawuuna.
Nnyizinku khujipwelela oveka wa Munsa; anaphulu apale ooshi aari mmanyupa, vaje na mmashapa khufwa.
Khulokottheliwa khuukeliwa nti opule khusala onukha woohifwayivo.
Ila wakathi Firawuuna ajuwiyeevo yoori avumula, khurutela wuumisa rooho yawe khuhinsiilezi theenya Munsa na Arawu, khwa epile alupiyeezo Nnyizinku.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Omuuze Arawu: Athuule pakhora yawo ookole nkhono ajaphe lifufu la vathi, lithatuwe liiye shaawa khwa Misuri yooshi.”
Khuretta etthiipo; Arawu khookola nkhono awe na pakhora etile khujapha lifufu ntthile khuthatuwa khwiiya shaawa khuweetaala atthu mpakha nyama na nti aya opule wooshi khwiitaala shaawa.
Anamajintta khweezelela etthiipo na ojuwa waya woovitheya ila khuhiwahi othatusha; shaawa epile khusala evira eweetaalaka atthu na nyama.
Aphano anamajintta apale khumuuza Firawuuna yoori: “Eti yaala ya Nluku,” ila rooho yawe Firawuuna khuumisa khuhitakhi owaasiileza, nkhama etthiipo Nnyizinku aalupiyeezo.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Olankhe supuyeene wakutthanane Firawuuna ye onlawa omuttho, omuuze yoori: Nnyizinku alupa toono: Owaalikhe atthu aka alawe akaaputu.
Amana weeyo ohiwaalikhi atthu aka olawa, kintta wuuperekheza pala ya mempe zawaatta yoori ziwiiphirise weeyo, mashawuriiya awo, atthu awo na mmavaje mwaya. Manyupa a Misuri na vathi anluwatthaavo zinttela wiitaalavo mempe.
Ila siikhu yaya etile kinttela otthantta khwa nanna yoofwarikhana nti wa Gosheeni, okhule aniikhalaawo atthu aka; khinteela opuwawo hatha pala moote ya mempe, yoori weeyo ojuwe yoori miiyo Nnyizinku kiri mmuti nttumphu.
Kinlawa kawaafwarikhanise atthu aka na atthu awo. Meesho entta opuwa alama ya eto.
Nnyizinku khuretta etthiipo, mempe zawaatta khwiitaala nnyupa wa Firawuuna na mmanyupa wa mashawuriiya awe, nti wooshi khwiiya wootapanyeya mwaasa wa mempe.
Aphano Firawuuna khuruma okhuweliwa Munsa na Arawu khuwooza yoori: “Mwilawe mwamwinkhe twaha Nluku enu, mmuti nttumphu.”
Ila Munsa khujipu araka: “Khahi yoolikana fweeyo oretta toowo, maana twaha ninttelaaye omwinkha Nnyizinku Nluku eetthu, ti yoohifwayi khwa amisuri, amana niretta twaha nkhama eto anoonaaye ohifwayi, amisuri antta onuula na mawe.
Nina yooretta safwari ya siikhu ttatthu niri ntarikhi neettaka n'yaara olawa omwinkha twaha Nnyizinku, Nluku etthu, nkhama etthiipo anuuziyeezo.”
Aphano Firawuuna khulupa yoori: “Kintta wuulikhani mwilawe, mwamwaaputu Nnyizinku, Nluku enu n'yaara, ila mwiheette peetiwene, noofiya mwikilompele namiyo.”
Munsa khujipu yoori: “Nasaapi eti amana kilaavo vakatthi vawo kinttela onvekela Nnyizinku; meesho mempe epo entta owaattuwa weeyo na mashawuriiya awo na atthu awo, ila safwatali ohikittettekhe theenya ohiwaalikhi atthu apa olawa omwinkha twaha Nnyizinku.”
Aphano Munsa khulaavo vakatthi wa Firawuuna khunvekela Nnyizinku.
Nnyizinku khujipu lompa ya Munsa, mempe epile khumwaattuwa Firawuuna na mashawuriiya awe mpakha atthu awe, khuhisali hatha mempe moote.
Ila nalelo khusala ari wa wuumisa rooho, khuhitakhi owaalikha atthu apale olawa.
Nawiisha Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa araka: “Olawe wa Firawuuna wamuuze yoori: Nnyizinku, Nluku wa meepereewu, alupa toono: Owaalikhe atthu aka alawe akaaputu.
Amana weeyo nalelo ohitakhi owaalikha olawa na khukhanyarela owaakhattaza,
ojuwe yoori nkhono wa Nnyizinku ontta otiisa pala yawoopisa khwa nyama zawo ziriiye omashapa, khwa khavalo zawo, khwa apuuru awo, khwa nkamiiya zawo, khwa mompe zawo mpakha pwittipwitthi zawo.
Na Nnyizinku onteela ophakula nyama za amisuri na epi za meezirayiilu, yoori ehifwe hatha nyama moote ya meezirayiilu.”
Nnyizinku atthoma wakathi araka: “Meesho Nnyizinku ontta oretta mmuti mphu etile aahitiyeeyo.”
Mmeesho mwaya Nnyizinku khuretta etthiipo: nyama za amisuri zooshi khufwa, ila za meezirayiilu hatha moote khuhifwi.
Firawuuna khunruma ntthu olawa woona, khusikana hatha moote ya meezirayiilu ehifweeni; ye khuumisa rooho khuhitakhi owaalikha olawa atthu apale.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa na Arawu yoori: “Mwisavule fuutha ya vamafiya yawiitaala mmakhono Munsa amwazele otulu, Firawuuna ari attaapho.
Entta othatuwa yiiye lifufu khwa nti wooshi wa Misuri, puupa entta owaapuwa atthu mpakha nyama, Misuri yooshi.”
Yo khuthuula fuutha ya vamafiya khulawa wa Firawuuna; Munsa khumwazela fuutha etile otulu, puupa khuwaapuwa atthu mpakha nyama.
Wala anamajintta khuhisala awahi omwaattama Munsa, mwaasa wa makhwatta, awaapatthiyeeyo vamote na amisuri ooshi.
Ila Nnyizinku khuumisa rooho ya Firawuuna, ye khuhinsiili Munsa na Arawu nkhama etthiipo Nnyizinku amuuziyeeyo.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Olankhe supuyeene olawe wakutthanane Firawuuna, omuuze oraka: Nnyizinku, Nluku wa meepereewu, alupa toono: “Owaalikhe atthu aka alawe akaaputu.
Olikha toowo, swaafu eti pala yaka yooshi kinuutiisela omweenyewe, na mashawuriiya awo na atthu awo, yoori ojuwe yoori khina eeyiye nkhama miiyo olumwenku wooshi.
Maana miiyo kinwahi wookola nkhono aka khuulwaaza weeyo na atthu awo khwa pala yaari owahaaye wuulazavo voolumwenku.
Ila miiyo kinuulikha weeyo ori haayi yoori kithoonyeze owahi waka, yoori nzina laka lilaleyiwe mmuti wooshimo.
Nalelo ontta ojikhutupulana atthu aka, khuntakha owaalikha alawa?
Ila meesho wakathi otthuupu, kinlawa kanyise vuula ya mawe ehinanyeke nti opu wa Misuri thanku owaziwe mpakha leelo.
Apho owaarume atthu awo alawe alokotthele nyama zawo ziriiye omashapa na vitthu zawo ziriiyo waaza atthu mpakha nyama ziriiyo. Amana ohilaziwo otana onti, khunyeliwa vuula ya mawe entta ofwa.”
Akarumeya a Firawuuna aari woovaaye nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku khwaakuva khulawa khuwaalazawo, aviitthwaana aya mpakha nyama zaya khulawa khupwehiwa.
Ila apale ahaari woovaaye nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku khuwaalikha amwiitthwaana aya na nyama zaya omashapa.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Olanse makhono awo yoori ewaanyele vuula atthu, nyama, na miitthi zooshi za ntthuttu nti wooshi wa Misuri.”
Munsa khulansa pakhora yawe khuthoonyeza otulu, Nnyizinku khuvumisa taari na vuula ya mawe, Nnyizinku khwiishusha ozerima na taari khwa nti opule wa Misuri na vuula ya mawe khusala enya.
Vuula ya mawe na taari khuvuma yoopakhanyeya na mawe awoopisa ehinanyeke Misuri yooshi thanku ewaziwe.
Misuri yooshi vuula etile khutapanya vitthu zaari mmashapa, waaza atthu, nyama na mathapa mpakha miitthi zooshi za ntthuttu.
Khusala nti wa Gosheeni paasi, okhule aari wiikhalaawo meezirayiilu, okho khayaanyiyewo vuula ya mawe.
Aphano Firawuuna khuruma olawa okhuweliwa Munsa na Arawu khuwooza yoori: “Swaafu eti kakosa. Nnyizinku ti wa shariya, ila miiyo na atthu aka, na makaafiri.
Mwilompe wa Nnyizinku, maana ottitthima wa Nluku na mawe ankwaaye a vuula pi awaatta, miiyo kintta wuulikhani mwilawe mwiheekesele etthu kiina theenya.”
Munsa khujipu yoori: “Amana miiyo kilaamo nsitati mphu kintta wookolela nkhono aka wa Nnyizinku. Taari enyamale na vuula yaamuse yoori weeyo ojuwe yoori olumwenku pi wa Nnyizinku.
Ila weeyo na akarumeya awo, miiyo kinjuwa yoori khamwinimoova Nnyizinku Nluku.”
Alikutawu na ntthama zaharipweya mwaasa ntthama waarina phunje na alikutawu aaleyiye.
Naye tiriku khayaaharipweyiye maana yaari ehinootthe.
Munsa khulaavo aphale aariivo Firawuuna na nsitati mphule, khumookolela nkhono Nnyizinku, taari na vuula khwiisha.
Firawuuna nawoona yoori taari na vuula zeesha khurutela okufuru oomisaka rooho yawe na mashawuriiya awe.
Ari wawuumisa rooho etthiipo, khuhiwaalikhi meezirayiilu olawa, nkhama etthiipo Nnyizinku aamuziyeezo Munsa.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Olawe wakutthanane Firawuuna, maana miiyo koomisa rooho yawe na rooho za mashawuriiya awe, yoori miiyo kithoonyeze alama zaka epo vakatthi vaya yo,
na yoori mwiwaathatelele aaneenu na atuulwenu nanna miiyo kiwaahukhumwiyeezo amisuri na minjuza zootikinisa kirettiyeezo vakatthi vaya, khwa etthiipo pi mwinttelaavo ojuwa yoori miiyo ki Nnyizinku.”
Aphano Munsa na Arawu khulawa okutthanana Firawuuna, yo khumuuza yoori: “Nnyizinku, Nluku wa meepereewu alupa toono: ‘Mpakha lini weeyo okatthalaka ojipushuwisa mmakhono mwaka miiyo? Owaalikhe atthu aka alawe akaaputu.
Amana okhanyarela ohitakhi owaalikha atthu aka olawa, meesho kintiisa pala ya Mapalaka mmuti mwawo.
Yo anteela ofinikha vathi ohisala wooneyavo, maana anteela orafuna zooshi epile zaalikhiweeyo ti vuula ya mawe mpakha na miitthi epile zinphutuwaazo mmashapa;
anttela wiitaala nnyupa mwawo na mmanyupa wa mashawuriiya awo na wa amisuri ooshi. Vitthu amarehemu apapazenu ahooneeni siikhu epo eekhaliyeezo mphu mpakha leelo.” Elottelanaka Munsa khulankha khulaavo aphale aariivo Firawuuna.
Aphano mashawuriiya a Firawuuna khusala alupa yoori: “Mpakha lini ntthu otu anituturushaka? Owaalikhe atthu apa alawe amwaaputu Nnyizinku Nluku aya. Khiniweeleya yoori Misuri yatapanyeya?”
Aphano khuthuuliwa Munsa na Arawu opheya khulawaniwa mpakha wa Firawuuna, ye khuwooza yoori: “Ettani mwamwaaputu Nnyizinku, Nluku enu. Oweje, anlawaaye paani?”
Munsa khujipu yoori: “Ninlawa na mashaapu etthu, na anakhuuluvale etthu, aaneetthu, pwittipwitthi zeetthu mpakha mompe zeetthu. Maana ninttela onrettela njampo Nnyizinku eetthu.”
Firawuuna khuwooza yoori: “Mweeyo mwinttela onhithajiya Nnyizinku amana kuulikhani olawa na aakha enu na aana enu! Eto enthoonyeza yoori mweeyo mwinwaza shawuri zootakhala.
Khahiyo toowo! Mwilawe alume-ru mwamwaaputu Nnyizinku maana eto ti waakivekeliyeeyo.” Munsa na Arawu khwiikariwa aphale aariivo Firawuuna.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Wookolele nkhono nti wa Misuri yoori ate nazope vathi apha arafune mathapa ooshi ariimo na zooshi epile zaalikhiweeyo ti vuula ya mawe.”
Munsa khookola pakhora yawe ookolelaka nti wa Misuri, Nnyizinku khutiisa pheevo ya ntulayi khuvuma nthana wooshi mpakha osikhu. Noocha pheevo etile khutana nazope.
Misuri yooshi khwiitaala nazope-ru woohilikhi hatha vahali, aari awaatta venkivene. Aari ahinapuwewo nkhama apo na paata ya opo khapuwiyewo theenya nkhama apo.
Maana aafinikhiye phantte zinki za Misuri mpakha nti wooshi khwiiya wooriipa. Khurafuna zooshi epile zaalikhiweeyo ti vuula ya mawe, mathapa na mishumo za miitthi woohisali hatha etthu piishi waaza mmitthi mpakha mmashapa, nti wooshi wa Misuri.
Firawuuna khuruma olawa okhuweliwa Munsa na Arawu woohirupazi, khuwooza yoori: “Kankosa Nnyizinku, Nluku enu na kookosani mweeyo!
Apho kinuuvekelani yoori mwikiswaamihi twampi yaka swaafu eti theenya na mwinvekele Nnyizinku, Nluku enu yoori akilaze pala eti yoofwiwa.”
Munsa paata ya olaavo aphale vaya aariivo Firawuuna khunvekela Nnyizinku.
Aphano Nnyizinku khuvumisa pheevo yawaatta ya phalalazi, ethiito khukhupa mapalaka ooshi khwiitthela mpahari yookhuttuwa; khuhisalimo hatha lipalaka mmote nti opule wa Misuri.
Ila nalelo Nnyizinku khuumisa rooho ya Firawuuna; ye khuhitakhi owaalikha meezirayiilu olawa.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Makhono awo olansele pinkuuni yoori Misuri yooshi yiiye yoofinikhiwa ti yiiza yookhomaala.”
Munsa khookolela nkhono awe otulu, Misuri yooshi khufinikhiwa ti yiiza yookhomaala khwa siikhu ttatthu.
Khuhisala oonana mmote na nzaawe, khaarivo mmote aaliyeevo vahali aariivo khwa siikhu ttatthu; ila meezirayiilu ooshi mmanyupa mwaya yaarimo nuuru.
Aphano Firawuuna khunkhuwela Munsa khumuuza yoori: “Ettani mwamwaaputu Nnyizinku enu. Ila esale pwittipwitthi zenu na mompe zenu paasi; ila aakha na aana mwilawane.”
Munsa khujipu yoori: “Weeyo ona ya oninkha nyama za orettela twaha na olukuza, yoori nimwinkhe Nnyizinku, Nluku eetthu.
Na nyama zeetthu nilawaka nintta othuula hatha likhope khalinsala, maana ninttela orumeyela etthiipo yoori nimwaaputu Nnyizinku Nluku eetthu, khanijuweeni nyama-ni ninttelaaye omwaaputu-na Nnyizinku mpakha ofiya.”
Ila Nnyizinku khuumisa rooho ya Firawuuna, ye khuhitakhi owaalikha olawa.
Firawuuna khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Oleevo apha na ohirutelevo theenya! Siikhu onttelaavo okoona theenya ontta ofwa.”
Munsa khuri: “Walikanisa! Akinteela woona theenya wuuso awo.”
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Kinimperekheza pala moote theenya Firawuuna na Misuri yooshi. Khwa ethiito ye onlawa awaalikhe olaamo mmuti mphu mpakha onlawa aweekaremo eperepere.
Apho owooze meezirayiilu ooshi, waaza alume mpakha aakha, yoori awaavekele anamwaattamanana aya vitthu za feeta na za tahapu.”
Nnyizinku khuwaaretta yoori atthu awe apatthe wooneliwa-vahali pi amisuri. Theenya Munsa aari nlume nwulweene nti opule wa Misuri, waaza mmaasho wa mashawuriiya a Firawuuna mpakha wa atthu ooshi.
Munsa khuri: “Nnyizinku alupa toono: ‘Osikhu layili kinvira Mmisuri.
Aana ooshi aalume amwanzo a nti wa Misuri anttela ofwa, waaza mwaana wa mwanzo wa Firawuuna, anttelaaye orithi khukulu ya mfwalume, mpakha mwaana wa mwanzo wa njaazi ankholaaye khaazi yoochila na aana a mwanzo a nyama zaya.
Misuri yooshi onlawa wapuwewo olila nwulweene; waari ohinapuwewo na ohinttelaaye opuwawo theenya.
Ila khwa meezirayiilu, waaza atthu mpakha nyama, wala mwanapwa khanlawa owahowula.’ Paata ya toowo, mwinttela ojuwa yoori Nnyizinku awavirikanisa amisuri na meezirayiilu.
Aphano mashawuriiya awo ooshi apa, anlawa akeekese na akikokhorele, akivekelaka yoori: ‘Olawe na atthu awo ooshi.’ Attaaphale miiyo kinttela olaawo!” Munsa na okatipukha wawe channu khulaavo aphale aariivo Firawuuna.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Firawuuna khanteela wuusiilani, yoori minjuza zaka zeekezeleye nti wa Misuri.”
Munsa na Arawu khuretta minjuza epile zooshi khwa Firawuuna; ila Nnyizinku khukhomaaza rooho ya Firawuuna, khuhisala atakha owaalikha olaamo mmuti mphule meezirayiilu.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa na Arawu nti wa Misuri yoori:
“Opu ona ya wiiya mweezi wa mwanzo wa mwaakha khwa mweeyo.
Munsa na Arawu ana ya olupa yoori: “Ajaama ooshi a Ezirayiilu, siikhu ya khuumi ya mweezi otthuupu, alume ooshi ana yoovalula nshapi la pwittipwitthi leelume ya wakhula liphanko ya wakhula nyuupa.
Ojama amana wiiya vattitthiiru ohinwahaaye orafuna nyama yooshi, ona yoowaalaleya anamwaattamanana aya apale a kharipu awaameele nyama enwahaaye owaafiyela khwa hisapu ya atthu aya.
Nyama yaya enttelaaye othawuliwa ena ya wiiya yeelume ya mwaakha mmote, yoohiirakali hatha vahali. Ena ya wiiya pwittipwitthi ama puuzi.
Mwipwehe mpakha siikhu khumi na nne ya mweezi, mpakha wakathi ajaama ooshi a meezirayiilu anttelaaye oshija njuwa leettelaka otupweela.
Mwittukunttele taamu yaya vatulu na mpavu wa milako za manyupa, apale mweeyo mwirafuniyeemu nyama.
Osikhu otthuupo mwina ya orafuna nyama yoomanikhiwa va moottho, na mathapa oowaawa na phaawu yoohiina fwaramento.
Mwihirafune nyama piishi wala yawiipikhiwa, ila yoomanikhiwa va moottho waaza eeshwa, moolu na marupo aya.
Mwihisalise hatha etthu efiya supu; amana esala mwilukuze.
Mwiwale, nzako n'yuunu, jampali mmoolu na mwikholele pakhora mmakhono, mwirafune wawaakuvavo; otu paashikowa wa Nnyizinku.
Maana osikhu aya otthuupo kinttela ovira nti wa Misuri na kiwoole aana ooshi amwanzo aalume waaza atthu mpakha a nyama, na kiwaahukhumu a miluku ooshi a Misuri: Nnyizinku ti Miiyo!
Taamu mwivaziyeeyo milako zenu enttela wiiya alama yoori ethoonyeze manyupa mwiniikhalaaye, amana kiwaavulalisaka amisuri, miiyo kinttela woona taamu kisala kuuvikanani wooheemeli yoori mwihiiye wootapanyiwa ti pala yaya eto.
Mwitthapele siikhu ethiito nkhama njampo la tiini muupuwelele yoori ti miiyo, Nnyizinku, kirettiyeeyo epo. Mweeyo na peewu yenu mwina yooretta njampo la paashikowa khwa mileele.
Nkatthi wa siikhu sapa mwina yooja phaawu yoohiina fwaramento. Siikhu yamwanzo mwilazemo fwaramento mmanyupa mwenu, maana wakhula otule anttelaaye oja etthu yawiiyana fwaramento, ntthu aya oto ontta wiikariwa vakatthi wa meezirayiilu.
Siikhu yamwanzo na siikhu yasaapa ona yawiiyavo nthukumano ttakatthiifu, ahiiyevo hatha ntthu mmote antakhaaye okhola khaazi siikhu zaya epo, woohiiyi wenttekhezela etthu-yoojiwa ya wakhula siikhu; mwina yooretta ethiito paasi.
Mwirette njampo la phaawu yoohiina fwaramento, maana siikhu yaya ethiito ti kilaziyeeyo nti wa Misuri mahimo a atthu ooshi a meezirayiilu. Mwitthapele siikhu yaya eto wiiye nrumo wa mileele, waaza wa apaapa mpakha wa aana aya.
Mwina yoorafuna phaawu yoohiina fwaramento makaaripi siikhu yakhuumi na nne ya mweezi wamwanzo mpakha makaaripi siikhu zeettettaka eshiriini na moote.
Siikhu epi sapa ahiiyevo ntthu mmote anttelaaye wiiyana fwaramento owawe. Wakhula antakhaaye oja etthu ya wiiyana fwaramento ontta wiikariwa muujama wa meezirayiilu, hatha nkhama mmalapo ama nnyunti.
Mwihije hatha etthu ya wiiyana fwaramento mmanyupa mwenu wooshimo, ila mwina yooja phaawu yoohiina fwaramento.”
Munsa khuruma okhuweliwa attunkhulu a atthu ooshi a meezirayiilu khuwooza yoori: “Mwinthawule nshapi la pwittipwitthi yoori ajaama ooshi a Ezirayiilu ashije pwittipwitthi ya Paashikowa.
Mwithuule zankalala mwinaanise na taamu eriiye mpasiya mwittukunttele milako zenu vatulu na mpavu mwaya. Ahiiyevo hatha ntthu mmote antakhaaye osaruwa nnyupa mwawe mpakha ocha.
Maana Nnyizinku aviraka mmuti mphule yoori awoole amisuri; amana oona taamu etile mwittukuntteliyeeyo nlako enu phantte na phantte na vatulu vaya, Nnyizinku onttela ovira attaapho khanlawa onlikha namatapanya ovira mmanyupa mwenu yoori awuuleeni.
Mwipwehe nrumo opu mweeyo na aana enu ooshi khwa mileele.
Amana mwifiya nti opule Nnyizinku awahitiyeenini owinkhani, mwina yooretta njampo ntthi.
Aaneenu amana awuuzelani yoori: ‘Njampo laya ntthi maana aya niini?’
Mwiwaajipu yoori: ‘Twaha ya Paashikowa wa Nnyizinku, aviriyeeyo vatulu wa manyupa a meezirayiilu nti wa Misuri, na khwiinanela manyupa eetthu wakathi aari owoolaavo amisuri.” Attaaphale meezirayiilu khukokhora khumwaaputu Nnyizinku.
Meezirayiilu khulaavo, khulawa khuretta nanna ethiitile Nnyizinku amuuziyeeyo Munsa na Arawu.
Aphano osikhu layili, Nnyizinku khuwoola aana ooshi amwanzo a misuri, waaza mwaana wamwanzo wa Firawuuna, namarithi ofwalume awe, mpakha mwaana wamwanzo wa napherezu aari nkalapooso na theenya aana amwanzo a nyama.
Osikhu otthuupule, Firawuuna na mashawuriiya awe ooshi na amisuri ooshi khulankha na wapuwiye olila nwulweene, maana khayaarivo nyuupa yahaafwiweemo.
Osikhu otthuupule Firawuuna khuruma okhuweliwa Munsa na Arawu khuwooza yoori: “Mwileemo nasaapi mmuti mwaka, mweeyo na meezirayiilu! Mwilawe mwamwaaputu Nnyizinku enu, nkhama etthiipo mwivekiyeezo.
Mwithuule pwittipwitthi zenu mompe zenu na puuzi zenu, nkhama mwaalupiyeezo na mwikiparikhiye theenya.”
Amisuri aari owaakhanyarela atthu apale yoori aleemo mmuti mphule, alupaka yoori: “Amana mwihiliimo fooshi fweeyo nintta ofwa!”
Aphano atthu apale khuthuula tiriku yookhattiwa yoohiina fwaramento, khuputaputela pasiya yaya vakuwo khuvikela mmafuzi.
Meezirayiilu khushututela nrumo wa Munsa, khuwaavekela amisuri vitthu za feeta za tahapu na kuwo.
Nnyizinku khuwaaretta atthu awe wooneliwa huruma pi amisuri, khwa nanna awenkhiyeevo etile avekiyeeyo; khwa etthiipo khuvulula maali zooshi za amisuri.
Meezirayiilu khulankha khusala alawa mwentto khuvira Rameesi eettaka Sukooti. Aari alume alufu miiya sitha, ohiwaalaki aakha na aana.
Khuntti khuluzeene zoofwarikhana za amalapo aawaalottiye, na theenya maphanko mawulu-mawulu a nyama, mompe, pwittipwitthi na puuzi.
Khoocha phaawu zoohiina fwaramento khwa tiriku etile aathuuliyeeyo Misuri, maana khayaarina fwaramento mwaasa wawiikariwa Misuri, khuhiwahi otthenkeza etthu-yoojiwa.
Meezirayiilu eekhaliye Misuri nyaakha miiya nne na talaathiini.
Siikhu ethiito afisiyeevo nyaakha miiya nne na talaathiini, atthu ooshi a Nnyizinku eetta olaawo Misuri.
Waari osikhu wa weekesela wa Nnyizinku yoori awaalazewo meezirayiilu Misuri wooshiwo. Tiito, osikhu nkhama otthuupu na yo anttela ojeekesela na ojama aya ontaaye mileele.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa na Arawu yoori: “Epi kano za Paashikowa: ahiiyevo hatha mmalapo mmote anttelaaye onja.
Mwiitthwaana wawuuzanyiwa ona yonja Paashikowa, amana eeya wookhiriya.
Ila apale eettiye omaka na apale aateeliye okhola khaazi ahinje.
Mweeyo mwina yonja nnyupa nttumpho aattaliweemo, mwihithuule hatha phittula moote mwisarulelaka vaje, wala mwihipweche hatha likhonkolo la nyama mwinttelaaye orafuna.
Atthu ooshi a Ezirayiilu ana yontthapela Paashikowa.
Wakhula mmalapo anikhalaaye nttumphu antakhaaye oretta njampo ntthi la Paashikowa wa Nnyizinku, mwina yowaakhiriyisa alume ooshi a muujama mwaya; apo ana yontthapela nkhama aana a muujama. Ahiiyevo ntthu woohikhiriyi anttelaaye ontthapela.
Kano ethiito enttela orumeyeliwa pi anyunti na amalapo apale amakiyeemo.”
Meezirayiilu ooshi khuretta nkhama etthiipo Nnyizinku amuuziyeezo Munsa na Arawu.
Siikhu ethiitile Nnyizinku khuwaalazawo meezirayiilu Misuri, khuwaatthenkeza lihimo khwa lihimo.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori:
“Okithawulele aana aalume ooshi a mwanzo. Aana aalume a mwanzo a meezirayiilu pi aka, khahiyo aana-ru paasi na nyama zooshi za mwanzo zeelume.”
