Aphano Munsa khuwooza atthu yoori: “Mwifikhirele siikhu eti mweeyo mwiliyeewo Misuri, nti opule mwarettiweeyo omwiitthwaana, maana Nnyizinku oolazaniwo okhule khwa owahi wa makhono awe. Tiito mwihije hatha etthu yootthiiwa fwaramento.
Siikhu ethiiti ya mweezi wa Habibi mweeyo mwintta olaawo Misuri.
Amana Nnyizinku oofisani nti wa akanaani, wa ahiiti, wa amoori, wa amwiivi na wa ayepuzi nti opule alaphaniyeeyo amarehemu apapazetthu yoori aari oteela owinkhani, nti liniittikhaawo leethi na asali, mweeyo mwina yooretta njampo ntthi mweezi otthuupu.
Nkatthi wa siikhu sapa mwina yooja phaawu yoohiina fwaramento siikhu yaya eti ya saapa mwitthapele njampo la Nnyizinku.
Mwije phaawu yoohiina fwaramento nkatthi wa siikhu sapa epo, mwihithuule hatha etthu yawiiyana fwaramento wala mmuti mwenu ehiiyemo.
Siikhu yaya etile wakhula mmote ona yoomuuza mwanawe yoori: “Mwaasa wa epi Nnyizinku oretteliyeenini mwilankhaka Misuri.”
Epi enttela wiiya nkhama alama ya mmakhono mwawo na opheleleza wa mmwishwa mwawo yoori oruma wa Nnyizinku wiiye vanlimi vawo, maana Nnyizinku oolaza Misuri khwa nkhono awe woowahi.
Mwishututele nrumo opu khwa siikhu etthomiweeyo, mwaakha khwa mwaakha.
Amana Nnyizinku oofisani nti wa akanaani na khuwinkhani, nkhama etthiipo alaphaniyeeyo mweeyo na amarehemu apapazenu,
mwinthawulele Nnyizinku aana ooshi amwanzo ovokoliwa aalume. Nyama za mwanzo ovokoliwa zooshi zeelume za maphanko enu pi za Nnyizinku.
Mwiwoosuru aana a puuru ooshi a mwanzo mwipatilanaka pwittipwitthi, ila amana mwihitakhi owoosuru waya, mwivuje siiko zaya. Mwiwoosuru theenya aana enu ooshi aalume amwanzo.
Meesho amana aaneenu awuuzelani yoori: ‘Maana aya niini?’ Mwiwooze yoori: ‘Khwa oowahi wa nkhono awe, Nnyizinku anilazawo Misuri, nti narettiweewo oviitthwaana.
Wakathi Firawuuna aari okhijilaaye na okatthala onilikha olaawo, Nnyizinku khuwoola aana ooshi a mwanzo aalume mpakha aana a mwanzo a nyama. Tiito kinimwinkhaaye twaha Nnyizinku aana aalume a vitthu zooshi na niniwoosuru aaneetthu ooshi a mwanzo ovokoliwa.’
Eto enttela wiiya nkhama alama mmakhono mwenu na nthoonyezo wa vaachihi venu yoori Nnyizinku anilaza Misuri na owahi wa nkhono awe.”
Wakathi Firawuuna awalikhiyeevo olaawo meezirayiilu, Nluku khawaavirisiye tarikhi ya Afiliishiti, yeettiye wiiyaru tarikhi yoofupheya. Khulupa yoori: “Yo amana awoomanana, talili anttela owaza orutela Misuri.”
Etthiipile, Nluku khuwaazukulelisa atthu apale n'yaara mphule, phantte ya pahari yookhuttuwa. Meezirayiilu khulaawo Misuri khujitthenka yoori oomane.
Munsa khuthuula makhonkolo a Yuusufu, mwaasa aalaphisaniye na aana a meezirayiilu wakathi aalupiyeeyo yoori: “Weekhweele Nluku onta awaakiseni mweeyo, amana mwilawaka mwithuulewo makhonkolo aka.”
Meezirayiilu khulankha Sukooti khulawa khumaka Eeta, ohali yaaziyeewo yaara.
Nnyizinku aari vamote na yo, nthana aari owaalokoza nkhama nripu la liwiku yoori eettette saana ntarikhi; amana wiiya osikhu eetta owaalokoza na nuuru ya nripu la moottho amwasikhelaka tarikhi; etthiipo pi aari owahaaye weettetta nthana na osikhu.
Nripu la liwiku ntthile khalaari owaasusa meezirayiilu nthana, wala nripu la moottho opule osikhu khalaari owaasusa.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori:
“Owooze meezirayiilu yoori asapuwe alawe amake kharipu ya Piharoote enakatthi-nakatthi ya Mikotooli na pahari. Mwamake nshini wa pahari omaasho ya Baale-Zefooma.
Paata ya toole Firawuuna khusala oopuwela yoori meezirayiilu antta ojeettettela athowelela n'yaara.
Khwa etthiipo kinlawa koomise rooho ya Firawuuna, ye onlawa awiikariseni, paata ya toowo miiyo kinlawa kattitthimisiwe vakatthi wa Firawuuna na anajanka awe ooshi. Amisuri anlawa ajuwe yoori miiyo ki Nnyizinku.” Meezirayiilu khuretta etthiipo.
Ila wakathi ooziweevo mfwalume wa Misuri yoori meezirayiilu atthira, ye na anakhaazi awe khuzukulisa akhili zaya na khulupa yoori: “Niini nirettiyeeyo? Nawaalikha meezirayiilu olawa anaashikha amwiitthwaana etthu!”
Aphano mfwalume khuruma weetteliwa nkukutta awe wa viittha na anajanka awe.
Khuthuula theenya mikukutta miiya sitha epile zookhomaala na mikukutta zooshi za Misuri na anamalokozela ooshi.
Nnyizinku khukhomaaza rooho ya Firawuuna mfwalume wa Misuri, khusala aweekarisa meezirayiilu aaliiyewo khwa nanna wooshinttavo.
Firawuuna khusala aweekarisa na khavalo zawe zooshi, mikukutta zawe zooshi na anakhavalo awe na anajanka awe, khuwaasikana amakiye nshini wa pahari kharipu ya Piharoote omaasho wa Baale-Zefooma.
Firawuuna asaleelaka owaasikana, meezirayiilu khweekesa nyuma khuwoona amisuri eettaka ota phantte etile aariiwo. Khuwaapattha woova channu, khusala ankhuwela Nnyizinku.
Na khumuuzela Munsa yoori: “Misuri zeetta othowawo vilalo tiito onilaziyeewo yoori nite nifwele n'yaara mphu? Niini eti weeyo oniretteliyeeyo, yoonilazawo okhu?
Tiito nawuuziyeeyo Misuri yoori: ‘Onilikhe niiye aviitthwaana amisuri! Afwataali wiiya amwiitthwaana amisuri ehiiyeeni ofwa n'yaara.”
Munsa khuwaajipu atthu apale yoori: “Mwihoove, mwiiye wookhomaala na moone nusura Nnyizinku anttelaaye wuutiselani leelo. Maana khamwinttela owoona theenya amisuri apa mwiniwoonaaye leelo.
Nnyizinku onttela wuumana mwaasa wa mweeyo, mwiiye woonyamala.”
Khulupa theenya Nnyizinku amuuzaka Munsa yoori: “Mwaasa aya niini mwikikhuwelaka miiyo? Owooze meezirayiilu avire alawaka.
Weeyo olanse pakhora yawo ojaphe maati, antta waawanyeya yoori meezirayiilu alokhe eri tuulu yawuuma.
Miiyo kinttela wuumisa rooho za amisuri, yo anttela wuulottelelani mpahari nttumpho. Miiyo kinttela wiiya woottitthimisiwa amana kinshintta mfwalume wa Misuri na anajanka awe ooshi na mikukutta zawe zooshi za nvittha na anakhavalo awe ooshi.
Amisuri anttela ojuwa yoori miiyo ki Nnyizinku amana kittitthimisiwa khwa Firawuuna na mikukutta zawe na anakhavalo awe.”
Aphano nlayikha la Nluku ntthile lawaalokoziyeeyo atthu a Ezirayiilu khuwaalikha khurutela nyuma waya; theenya nripu la liwiku khuwaalikha khurutela nyuma waya,
khwiiya vakatthi wa amisuri na meezirayiilu. Liwiku laari wiiya looripa phantte ya amisuri khusala liwaamwasikhela meezirayiilu; mwaasa wa ethiito khuhisala liwaattamanisa meezirayiilu na amisuri osikhu wooshi.
Munsa khookolela nkhono awe pahari, Nnyizinku khuvumisa pheevo zookhomaala za ntulayi osikhu wooshi mpakha pahari waawanyeya khupuwa mishaka zawuuma mwaasa wa waawanyeya wa maati.
Meezirayiilu khulokha vakatthi wa maati khwa mishaka zawuuma, khupuwa muuri phantte ya nkhono nlume na nkhono nkha.
Amisuri khusala aweekara na khavalo zaya zooshi, mikukutta zaya za nvittha na anakhavalo ooshi a Firawuuna khusala awaalotta mpakha vakatthi wa pahari.
Osaleelaka ocha nkatthi wa nripu la moottho na la liwiku, Nnyizinku khuwoona anajanka amisuri khuwaakarawela.
Khuretta etthu yoophara maroota za mikukutta za amisuri nkhama ahaari ojuwaaye weettettisa na khusala akhuwa araka: “Nlaweni niwaatthire meezirayiilu! Nnyizinku ontta wuumanana amisuri khwa zwaamu yaya yo.”
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Wookolele nkhono awo khwa pahari, yoori maati awaakhutele amisuri na mikukutta zaya na anakhavalo aya.”
Munsa khookolela nkhono awe pahari osaleelaka ocha, maati khurutela etthiipile aariizo. Wakathi amisuri aari ariiye atthire, khukutthanana maati a pahari, aphano Nnyizinku khuwaakhutela na pahari.
Maana maati aarutiye khukhutela mikukutta na anakhavalo, na anajanka ooshi a Firawuuna eeshukheliyeeyo mpahari; hatha mmote khaarutiye.
Ila meezirayiilu khulokha pahari etile eettaka oluwatthela mishaka, maati aari nkhama muuri phantte ya nkhono nlume na phantte ya nkhono nkha.
Etthiipile Nnyizinku khuwoosuru meezirayiilu siikhu etile mmakhono wa amisuri, na meezirayiilu khuwoona amisuri ari oofwa mmattima wa pahari etile.
Meezirayiilu khoona owahi nwulweene wa Nnyizinku na khumoova Nnyizinku aya na khunkhupali Nnyizinku na Munsa karumeya awe.
Aphano Munsa na aana a meezirayiilu khumwiipela liipo ntthi, Nnyizinku yoori: “Kinimwiipela Nnyizinku, mwaasa yoori ashintta wooshapweyavo, khutupweeza mpahari khavalo na anakhavalo aya.
Nnyizinku ti kuvu yaka na liipo laka, ye ti nusura yaka! Ye ti Nluku aka na miiyo kininsifu, ti Nluku wa papaaka na miiyo kinimwaaputu!
Nnyizinku ti naviittha, nzina lawe ti Nnyizinku.
Khutupweeza mpahari mikukutta za nvittha na anajanka a Firawuuna; anamalokozela awe apale awaakhupaliyeeyo khukhuteliwa ti pahari yookhuttuwa.
Maati apale awiicha khuwaakhutela khwiiya oozama nkhama mawe.
Oo Nnyizinku, nkhono nlume awo onaaye owahi nwulweene; Oo Nnyizinku, nkhono nlume awo wawaashijela maatuwi.
Khwa owula wa ofwalume awo wawaakhitiri maatuwi awo, katapu yawo khuwaaja nkhama malala.
Khwa ovitelela wa phula yawo maati na mawipi ajikusanya khujakhuwa nkhama muuri, vathi wa pahari khwiiya awuuma nkhama liwe la manlela.
Maatuwi khusala alupa yoori: ‘Niweekarise niniwaasikana niwaanyakanye maali nafusi zeetthu zinlawa zatoshiwe pi yo, nasarule phanka yeetthu na makhono eetthu niniwaatapanya.’
Khuperekha pheevo yawo, na pahari khuwaafinikha. Khuzama nkhama chumpwi mpahari wawiichamo.
Khaziivo miluku zinlikananaaye weeyo oo Nnyizinku. Khaavo woottitthimisiwa woottakatthifu, wawoopisa khwa oretta vitthu zootikinisa na oretta minjuza.
Wookoliye nkhono nlume awo nti khuwaamiza.
Khwa pheta yawo wawaalokoza atthu awo apale owoosuruyeeyo; na kuvu zawo, khuwaattha puuro yawo yoottakatthifu.
Khapila khusiila epile onrettaazo, khusala zithukumela na woova. Afiliishiti khuwaapattha huzuni.
Attunkhulu a Meedomu khwiiya ooshanka na anamalokozela a amowaabu khuwaapattha othukumela; akanaani khuwaapattha otteettheya.
Osuthuwa na woova khuwaapattha khwa owahi wa nkhono awo, khuhisala asakhinyeya nkhama mawe mpakha ovira atthu awo, Oo Nnyizinku, mpakha ovira atthu apale owoozanyiyeeyo.
Oo Nnyizinku, weeyo oniwalawana na waweekhaze vamwaako wa eritho yawo puuro ttakatthiifu nyuupa yawo ojekiyeeyo na makhono awo.
Nnyizinku mfwalume wa mileele.”
Wakathi khavalo za Firawuuna na mikukutta zawe za nvittha na anakhavalo awe eettiyeevo mpahari, Nnyizinku khuwaazamisa a Misuri na maati a pahari etile; ila meezirayiilu aaviriye mwentto aluwatthelaka mishaka zawuuma vakatthi wa pahari.
Nhupiri Miiriyamu nlupuwe Arawu khuthuula nttowu na aakha ooshi khusala anlotta eettaka opiya na wiina.
Miiriyamu aari owaajipu eettaka wiipa araka: “Nimwiipele Nnyizinku, mwaasa yoori ashintta wooshapweyavo. Khutupweeza mpahari khavalo na anakhavalo aya.”
Aphano Munsa khuwaalokoza meezirayiilu waaza pahari yookhuttuwa mpakha n'yaara ya Shuuri. Siikhu ttatthu eettaka weettetta n'yaara ahipatthaka maati.
Aphano khufiya Maara, ila khuhiwahi onywa maati ottuukho mwaasa wa owaawa. Ti maana aya wiittheliweeyo nzina la Maara.
Tiito meezirayiilu khusala amwaapa Munsa araka: “Ninttela onywa-ni?”
Munsa khunkhuwela Nnyizinku ye khuthoonyeziwa muutthi khuthuula khweeselela mmaati khwiiya ootuva. Puuro etile ya Maara Nnyizinku khuwenkha kano na oruma na khuweeza,
awoozaka yoori: “Mweeyo amana mwinsiileza Nnyizinku, Nluku enu na osiileza etile enintuvelaaye na khusiileza mirumo zawe na khushututela kano zawe zooshi, khamwiniiyana hatha orati opule kiwaatiseliyeeyo amisuri, maana miiyo ki Nnyizinku anvonisaaye.
Aphano khufiya nti wa Elimu, ottuukho zaariiwo milipu khumi na miwiri na mikokonoothi sapiyiini; khumaka ottuukho khwaattamela maati.
Mahimo a atthu a meezirayiilu khulankha nti wa Elimu khulawa mpakha yaara ya Siimu, eriiye enakatthi-nakatthi ya Elimu na Sinaayi. Zaari siikhu khumi na thaanu ya mweezi wa phiiri paata ya olaawo Misuri.
N'yaara mphule mahimo a atthu a meezirayiilu khusala amwaapa Munsa na Arawu.
Alupaka yoori: “Afwataali nkhono wa Nnyizinku onuuleeliye Misuri! Maana okhu fweeyo naari wiiya nshini wa vikhalako za nyama na naari ojaka etthu-yoojiwa woohiivo hatha shaakha mpakha orupala, ila mweeyo khunitiisa n'yaara mphu yoori mwinuule jala fooshi fweeyo.”
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Miiyo kintta okwisa etthu-yoojiwa ya pinkuuni. Atthu nka asaruwaka na olokotthela wakhula siikhu khwa khiima eniwaafiyelaaye siikhu yaya etile, khwa etthiipo kinttela oweeza yoori kiwoone nkhama yo anshututela kano yaka.
Siikhu ya sitha mwina yoolokotthela swaafu piiri zayita epile mwinlokotthelakaaye siikhu kiina zaya.”
Aphano Munsa na Arawu khuwooza meezirayiilu ooshi yoori: “Makaaripi mwinttela ojuwa yoori ti Nnyizinku oolaziyeenini nti wa Misuri,
meesho supu mwinttela woona siifwa ya Nnyizinku maana asiila waapa wenu. Fweeyo na paani mwinnaapaaye?”
Khurutela olupa theenya araka: “Nnyizinku oniwinkhani nyama yoorafuna makaaripi na etthu-yoojiwa ya supu yoori mwirupale, maana asiila waapa wenu. Fweeyo na a paani? Mweeyo khamwinnaapa fweeyo, ila Nnyizinku.”
Munsa khumuuza Arawu yoori: “Wuuze mahimo a atthu ooshi a meezirayiilu oraka: Mweette mmakhono wa Nnyizinku, maana asiila waapa wenu”.
Arawu eettaka ottakhulana meezirayiilu, ooshi khusala eekesa phantte ya n'yaara na siifwa ya Nnyizinku khupuwa mmawiku,
na Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori:
“Kinsiila waapa wa meezirayiilu, ila owaajipu yoori: ‘Njuwa leettelaka otupweela mweeyo mwinrafuna nyama, na supu mwiniiyana-yoojiwa ya wuutoshani. Toowo mwinttela ojuwa yoori miiyo ki Nnyizinku Nluku enu.”
Makaaripi khupuwa khwaali khwiitaala aphale aamakiyeevo, supu waarivo mmatte phantte yaya etile.
Wakathi mmatte opule wuumiyevo, vathi aphale khupuwa vitthu nkhama mavalako zoolattanana cheelu vatulu wa nshaka.
Wakathi meezirayiilu ooniyeevo vitthu epile, khwaaza wuuzelana atthaaporu araka: “Niini epiza?” Maana khaari ojuwa etthu yaari orettikhanaaye. Elottelanaka, Munsa khuwooza yoori: “Eti etthu-yoojiwa Nnyizinku awinkhiyeenini yoori mwije.
Nnyizinku khurumisa yoori: ‘Wakhula mmote wa mweeyo ona yookusanyela epile antakhaaye yoori aje, khwa hisapu ya atthu ariina vaje vawe, ttompwiyo piiri wakhula ntthu.”
Meezirayiilu khuretta etthiipo ooziweezo; akina khukhupa zawaatta, akina vattitthiiru.
Wakathi aphimiyeeyo na ttompwiyo, otule aalokottheliyeeyo zawaatta na otule alokottheliyeeyo vattitthiiru ooshi khupattha sawa-sawa. Wakhula mmote aapatthiye epile aari ohithajiyaaye oja.
Munsa khuwooza yoori: “Ahiiyevo hatha mmote antakhaaye opweha yoori aje meesho.”
Ila yo khuhinsiilezi Munsa, akina khulikha vattitthiiru mana aya yoori aje mmeesho mwaya; ochiyeevo khwiitaala nyunku na khusala anukha. Munsa khuwaakatipukhela yo venkivene.
Wakhula siikhu supu, yo eetta olokotthaka epile aari otakhaaye oja, maana haari ya njuwa yeetta othulushaka etile yaari osalaaye vathi.
Siikhu ya siitha, khulokottha swaafu piiri, theenya ttompwiyo phiiri khwa wakhula ntthu; attunkhulu a atthu khulawa omuuza Munsa.
Khuwaajipu Munsa araka; “Nnyizinku aruma yoori: ‘Meesho enttela wiiya siikhu yoovumula, Saapatu ttakatthiifu ya Nnyizinku etile mwintakhaaye wuumisa vamoottho muumise na etile mwintakhaaye wiipikha na maati, mwiipikhe, zooshi zinttelaaye osala mwipwehe mpakha mmeesho mwaya.”
Khupweha mpakha mmeesho mwaya nkhama etthiipo Munsa aalupiyeezo; wala khuhivutti na hatha nyunku khuhiina.
Aphano Munsa khulupa yoori: “Mwije leelo maana Saapatu ttakatthiifu ya Nnyizinku maana leelo khamwinsikanavo hatha etthu valipuwa.
Siikhu sitha mwina yoolokotthela ila siikhu ya saapa, Saapatu, khazinteela wiiyavo.”
Siikhu ya saapa aalankhiye atthu onlawa olokottha ila khuhisikani.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Mpakha lini mwikhijilaka oshututela mirumo zaka na kano zaka?
Moone yoori Nnyizinku awinkhani Saapatu, tiito siikhu ya siitha oniwinkhani etthu-yoojiwa ya siikhu piiri yoori siikhu ya saapa wakhula ntthu eeye attaaphale aniiyaavo ahiiyevo ntthu antakhaaye weettetta.”
Aphano atthu apale khuvumula siikhu ya saapa.
Atthu a Ezirayiilu khutthaja etthu-yoojiwa etile nzina la mana. Zaari nkhama peewu ya phunje zoolakala zootuva nkhama mishikoto za asali.
Munsa khulupa araka, “Nnyizinku aruma yoori: ‘Mwilokotthele mana apa ttompwiyo moote mwipwehe, yoori khapila entaaye yoone etthu-yoojiwa mwenkhiweeyo ti Nnyizinku wakathi oolaziyeenini Misuri.”
Aphano Munsa khumuuza Arawu yoori: “Othuule ttompwiyo moote ya mana, otthe mmakhono wa Nnyizinku, yoori epweheliwe khapila eto entaaye.”
Khwa oshututela etile Nnyizinku aamuuziyeezo Munsa, Arawu khuthuula mana apale khuttha mmakhono wa oshaahiti wa Mbwana.
Meezirayiilu khuja mana nyaakha arupayiini mpakha ofiya nti waari wiikhaleyaaye; khuvira ajaka mpakha ofiya mmwiinano wa Kanaani.
Mphimo waari ophimaniwaaye mana waari wiitthiwa ttompwiyo, phantte ya khuumi ya eefwa.
Mahimo a atthu a meezirayiilu khulaamo n'yaara ya Siimutta, khusala eettetta avumulaka alawaka, nkhama etthiipo aarumiyeeyo Nnyizinku. Khumaka Refidimu ila khaariwo maati oonywa.
Mwaasa wa ethiito khusala anyakulisana na Munsa araka: “Oninkhe maati oonywa.” Ye khuwaajipu yoori: “Mwaasa wa niini mwinyakulisanaka na miiyo? Mwinimweezelani Nnyizinku?”
Ila atthu apale aarina nnyottha khusala omwaapa Munsa araka: “Waanilazeliyeniwo Misuri? Ontakha onuula na nnyottha na aana eetthu na nyama zeetthu?”
Aphano Munsa khunyakula ankhuwelaka Nnyizinku araka: “Kiwaarettele niini atthu apa? Ansaleela okivonya na mawe!”
Nnyizinku khunjipu yoori: “Olokoze, olawe wawaathuule attunkhulu a atthu a meezirayiilu na wiiyane pakhora mmakhono ethiito waapiyaniyeeyo muuttho Niilu, olawe.
Woone, Miiyo kinttela wiiya ottuukho vatulu wa liwe la Horeepe. Weeyo opiye liwe laya, nttinttho lintta olaza maati yoori atthu apo anywe.” Munsa khuretta etthiipile, attunkhulu a meezirayiilu eettaka omoona.
Puuro yaya etile khutthaja nzina la Maasa na Mariiba, maana aphale vaya meezirayiilu aanyakulisananiye na khumweeza Nnyizinku araka: “Nnyizinku ori vamote na fweeyo ama wala?”
Elottelanaka khuta Amalekiita oteela owoomanana meezirayiilu nti wa Refidimu.
Aphano Munsa khumuuza Yoshuwa yoori: “Owaathawule atthu aalume oomanane Amalekiita. Meesho kinttela wiiya vatulu wa mwaako na pakhora ya Nluku mmakhono mwaka.”
Yoshuwa khulawa wuumanana Amalekiita nkhama etthiipile Munsa aalupiyeeyo. Munsa, Arawu na Huri khuwelaza vatulu wa mwaako.
Amana Munsa alansa makhono awe meezirayiilu eetta oshintta, amana eeshusha makhono awe Amalekiita ti aari oshinttakaaye.
Amana makhono a Munsa ashokhera, Arawu na Huri eetta othuulaka liwe yoori Munsa eekhalevo. Oowiiri khukholelela makhono a Munsa, mmote nkhono nkha nkina nkhono nlume yoori makhono a Munsa eeye aweemela mpakha njuwa otupweela.
Yoshuwa khuwaashintta sawasawa anajanka a Amalekiita na phanka.
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Waatikhe hapari epi nkithaapu yoori zisala zuupuweleliwa na omuuze Yoshuwa yoori Amalekiita anttela wiiya oosahawiwa khwa mileele vathi wa olumwenku.”
Munsa khunjeka alitaari na khuntthaja yoori: “Nnyizinku akinkha oshintta”,
na khuri: “Nkhono mmote vakhukulu ya Nnyizinku; Nnyizinku ori nvittha na Amalekiita khapila khwa khapila.”
Aphano Yeeturu, haakhimu wa Miitiya, nkhwewe Munsa, khusiila vitthu zooshi Nluku anretteliyeeyo Munsa vamote na atthu a Ezirayiilu khwa nanna Nnyizinku awaalaziyeewo Misuri.
Raku, Munsa amperekhiye Zipoora muukha awe owawe nkhwewe Yeeturu, ye khumpwekherela,
vamote na aana awe awiri. Mmote aya aari wiitthiwa Yeerisoni, maana aalupiye yoori “Miiyo kaasafireliye nti wa malaponi”;
nkina aari wiitthiwa Elizeeri, maana aalupiye yoori: “Nluku wa paapa ti eeyiye awuni yaka na akaawuni khwa phanka ya Firawuuna.”
Aphano Yeeturu nkhwewe Munsa na muukhaawe Munsa na aanaawe awiri khulawa n'yaara omwaako wa Nluku okhule Munsa aamakiyeewo.
Yeeturu khurumisa nhupi wuuziwa Munsa yoori: “Miiyo, nkhwewo, kata na muukhaawo na aanaawo awiri.”
Aphano Munsa khumwaattama nkhwewe khumwiinamela khumpatikha, khusala oozelana hapari mmote na nzaawe eettaka ovira nheema.
Elottelanaka Munsa khwaaza omuuza nkhwewe vitthu zooshi Nnyizinku anretteliyeeyo Firawuuna na amisuri mwaasa wa pheta ya meezirayiilu na tafwawuthi zooshi akholiyeeyo ntarikhi na nanna Nnyizinku awaataphuliyeeyo.
Yeeturu noosiila mattakhuzi apale ooshapweya Nnyizinku awaretteliyeeyo meezirayiilu, awaataphulaka mmakhono wa amisuri, khwiiya woofurahi.
Yeeturu khulupa yoori: “Woottottopeliwa eeye Nnyizinku, ootaphuliyeenini mmakhono wa amisuri na mmakhono wa Firawuuna na khuwaataphula atthu awe vathi wa nkhono wa amisuri.
Leelo kajuwa yoori Nnyizinku nwulweene zayita miluku zooshi, maana khwa vitthu epile aari ojikhutupulanaaye atapanya.”
Aphano Yeeturu nkhwewe Munsa, khuretta twaha yoolukuziwa khwa Nluku; khuta Arawu na attunkhulu ooshi a meezirayiilu, yoori aje etthu-yoojiwa na nkhwewe Munsa omaasho wa Nluku.
Mmeesho mwaya Munsa khwiikhala yoori aphuke onyakulisana wa atthu, atthu apale khweemela ya supu mpakha makaripi.
Wakathi nkhwewe ooniyeevo epile aari owaarettelaaye atthu apale, khuri: “Eto onrettaayo niini? Weekhalela-ni atthu ooshi khweemela na khuuzukulela otthowe ya supu mpakha makaripi?”
Aphano Munsa khumuuza nkhwewe yoori: “Mwaasa aya atthu apa anikiteela miiyo okuuzela vitthu za Nluku.
Amana eeyana milattu zaya, antta okiteela yoori kiphuke mmote na nzaawe na kiwoozaka mwentto wa Nluku na kano zawe.”
Nkhwewe Munsa khulupa yoori: “Eto onrettaaye khahiyo yooshapweya oretta.
Weeyo na atthu awo mwinttela oshokhera, maana khaazi yaya eto ti yoolipa channu; khunwahi oretta otthowe.
Osiile huula yaka! Miiyo kiniwinkha shawuri na Nluku ti eeye vamote na weeyo. Wiiye weeyo namalokozela wa atthu omaasho wa Nluku na othuula tafwawuthi zaya zooshi khwa Nluku.
Owooze mwentto na kano na owaajuwise tarikhi ya weettettela na khaazi ya okhola.
Ila weeyo vakatthi wa atthu apo, owaathawule atthu a makhaamu ooretta etthu, oomoova Nluku, atthu a haakhi eniweephiraaye ophattha fwayita ya haraamu. Owenkhe ottunkhulu wa atthu alufu wa atthu miiya wa atthu hamusiini wa atthu khumi.
Yo anttela wiiya vakatthi wa atthu yoori asala aphuka tafwawuthi zaya. Nka ootiiselaka weeyo tafwawuthi epile zoolipa; epile zookhweya anttela waattalela ottho. Amana oretta toowo enttela wiiya yookhweya khaazi yawo, maana yo anttela wuulikhela otthowe.
Amana weeyo oretta etthiipo, nkhama Nluku anrumaazo, nka owahaka oshintta tafwawuthi zaya epo na atthu apa ooshi eettaka orutela onti tafwawuthi zaya ziri zawaattaleliwa.”
Munsa khukhupalela wuuziwa ti nkhwewe na khuretta etthiipile ooziweeyo ti ye.
Khuwaathawula atthu amakhaamu vakatthi wa meezirayiilu ooshi khuwaaretta wiiya anamalokozela atthu aya apale; nttunkhulu wa atthu alufu, wa atthu miiya, wa atthu hamusiini, na wa atthu khumi.
Apa khwiiya nkhama anamaphuka awakhula siikhu, atafwawuthi za atthu. Amana wiiya mwaasa woolipa aari weettiseliwaka Munsa, amana ziiya zookhweya aari ophukaka atthaapo.
Aphano Munsa khuleezanana nkhwewe Yeeturu khusala arutela owawe.
Mweezi wa ttaatthu siikhu ethiitile, paata ya aana a meezirayiilu olaawo Misuri, khufiya mpakha n'yaara ya mwaako Sinaayi.
Noolaawo Refidimu, khulawa mpakha n'yaara ya Sinaayi, meezirayiilu khulawa khumaka ottuukho omaasho wa mwaako Sinaayi.
Elottelanaka Munsa khuwela vamwaako yoori akutthanane Nluku. Nnyizinku khunkhuwela vamwaako attaaphale araka: “Olupe mattakhuzi apa wuuzaka peewu ya Yaakhumpa, atthu ooshi a meezirayiilu yoori:
‘Mweeyo moona etthu kiwaaretteliyeeyo amisuri na nanna kiwaathamisiyeeyo nkatthi wa mapaphelo a saaka kijitiiselaka miiyo.
Aphano, amana mwikishututela wawaamineyavo mwisiila huula yaka na khuthokorela wahati aka, mweeyo mwinttela wiiya atthu aka, ootafikhana zayita khapila kiina, maana olumwenku wooshi pi waka.
Mweeyo mwinttela wiiya ofwalume aka wa anamalokozela a tiini na khapila ttakatthiifu.’ Apo pi mattakhuzi onttelaaye owooza meezirayiilu.”
Munsa khuruti khulawa khuwaakhuwela attunkhulu ooshi atthu a meezirayiilu na khuwooza zooshi Nnyizinku anrumiyeeyo olupa.
Atthu ooshi khujipu wa swaafu moote yoori: “Ninretta zooshi Nnyizinku arumiyeezo.” Aphano Munsa khulawa khumuuza Nnyizinku mattakhuzi ajipwiyeeyo atthu apale.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Woone! Kinttela wuuttakhulana weeyo nkatthi wa liwiku looriipa yoori atthu amana akisiila kittakhulanaka weeyo asala ookhupali khwa mileele.” Aphano Munsa khumuuza Nnyizinku mattakhuzi ooziweeyo pi atthu apale.
Nnyizinku khurutela omuuza theenya Munsa araka: “Olawe vakatthi wa atthu apo, wawaattakatthise leelo na meesho. Yo ana ya ofula kuwo zaya,
yoori eeye oolikana siikhu ya ttaatthu, maana siikhu ya ttaatthu Nnyizinku onttela wiishukha vamwaako Sinaayi, mooshi mweeyo mwimoone.
Otthe mwiinano nkerekhere wa mwaako na owooze atthu yoori: ‘Eeyane phoole ya ohiweli mwaako na ohisapi. Otule anttelaaye osapa mwaako ona ya wuuliwa;
ohinsape na nkhono ila onvonye na mawe ama nttetthe, hatha nkhama ntthu ama nyama, khiniiya haayi.’ Ila amana nlope livuma swaafu moote apho pi anttelaavo owela.”
Munsa khwiishukhela aphale aariivo atthu apale khuwaattakatthisa na yo khufulaza kuwo zaya.
Khuwooza atthu apale yoori: “Mwiiye woolikana ovirisa siikhu ya ttaatthu. Ila ahiiyevo antakhaaye okutthanana muukha awe.”
Noocha, siikhu ya ttaatthu khupuwa taari na ozerima, liwiku looriipa khufinikha mwaako na khuvumisiwa nlope channu. Atthu ooshi khuwaapattha woova aphale aarivo.
Munsa khuwaalazavo atthu apale aphale vaya yoori akutthanane Nluku, yo khulawa khweemela waattamanana mwaako.
Mwaako Sinaayi wooshi weetaaliye loosi, maana Nnyizinku eeshukheliye attaapho na moottho, na loosi laya leetta owela nkhama loosi la vanjocho na mwaako wooshi weetta othukumela channu.
Ovuma wa nlope weetta ovira otepaka, elottelanaka Munsa khuttakhula na huula ya Nluku khunjipu.
Nnyizinku khwiishukhela vatulu wa mwaako Sinaayi, khunkhuwela Munsa vatulu attaaphale Munsa khuwelela khulawa.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Wiishukhe wawooze atthu apo yoori ahivikane mwiinano atakhaka omoona Nnyizinku. Amana avikana enkeene antta ofwa.
Hatha nkhama anamalokozela a tiini amana amwaattamelaka Nnyizinku ana yoojittakatthisa. Amana ahijittakatthisi Nnyizinku ontta owaatapanya.”
Aphano Munsa khumuuza Nnyizinku yoori: “Atthu khanwahi owela vamwaako Sinaayi maana weeyo waanilikhisiye oraka: ‘Mwirette mwiinano omaasho wa mwaako mwiphakule.”
Nnyizinku khunjipu Munsa amuuzaka yoori: “Wiishukhe orutele owela theenya, operekhiwaka ti Arawu. Ila anamalokozela a tiini na atthu ahirukhe mwiinano yoori awelele apha ariivo Nnyizinku, amana aretta toowo Nnyizinku ontta owaatapanya.”
Aphano Munsa khwiishukha khulawa owooza atthu apale.
Nluku alupa mattakhuzi ooshi apa araka:
“Miiyo ki Nnyizinku, Nluku awo, kuulaziyeeyo nti wa Misuri ohali waarettiweewo omwiitthwaana.
Ohiiyane miluku mikina omaasho waka miiyo.
Ohijaattalele sanamu wala ratarato ya etthu ya otulu wala ya vathi ama vathi a mmaati.
Ohikokhorele wala ohaaputu, maana Miiyo ki Nnyizinku, Nluku awo; kintakha wiiye waka paasi, kinoonaaye twampi za apaapa na kifikhirelaka twampi zaya khwa aana aya mpakha khapila ya ttaatthu ama yanne ya apale aari okiphiirisaaye,
ila kintthantta na tthakaraka mpakha khapila alufu epile zinikiphetaaye na zinshututelaaye mirumo zaka.
Ohilupe nzina la Nnyizinku Nluku awo mahala, maana Nnyizinku khanlawa onlikha ahinhukhumweeni otule anlupaaye nzina lawe mahala.
Wuupuwele Saapatu yoori siikhu ttakatthiifu.
Ona yookhola khaazi zawo zooshi siikhu sitha,
ila siikhu ya saapa Saapatu ti yomwinkha Nnyizinku Nluku awo, siikhu yaya eti ohikhole hatha khaazi moote, waaza weeyo, mwanawo wa nlume ama wankha, wala mwiitthwaana awo wala njaazi awo, wala nyama zawo wala aletto ariiye nlikokoro mwawo.
Maana khwa siikhu sitha, Nnyizinku eetta wumpa pinku na vathi, pahari na vitthu zooshi ziriimo, ila Saapatu khuvumula. Paata ya toowo, Nnyizinku khuparikhiya Saapatu ya etile na khuttakatthisa.
Onshitahi papaawo na mamaawo, yoori wiikhale siikhu zawaatta vathi apha Nnyizinku, Nluku awo awinkhiyeeyo.
Ohuule.
Ohiraruwe.
Ohiiye.
Ohinlokoveze nzaawo.
Ohilazele omaashokopho vaje wa nzaawo, wala muukha wa nzaawo, wala amwiitthwaana ama ajaazi awe, wala mompe zawe ama puuru zawe na wala etthu moote etile yiiyiye yawe.”
Wakathi atthu apale aari osiilaavo taari na ozerima na ovuma wa nlope na khoona mwaako olazaka loosi, ooshi khusala athukumela mpakha osusela petiwene.
Khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Weeyo ottakhulane ye, fweeyo nintta osiila. Ila Nluku amana attakhulana fweeyo nintta ofwa.”
Munsa khuwooza atthu apale yoori: “Mwihoove! Nluku aateeliye oweezani, yoori mwisala mwimoova na ooweraweriseni twampi.”
Ila atthu apale nalelo khwiiya peetiwene, Munsa khusala avira aattamelaka liwiku ntthile looriipa aariivo Nluku.
Nnyizinku khumuuza Munsa yoori: “Owooze meezirayiilu mattakhuzi apa yoori: ‘Mweeyo moona na maasho enu yoori pinkuuni kattakhulana mweeyo.
Mwihaattale miluku za feeta wala miluku za tahapu yoori mwikiphakanyane.
Mwikaattalele alitaari wa mattophe mwirettevo twaha ya olukuziwa na zaakha za heeri, pwittipwitthi na mompe zenu wakhula vahali mwinrettaavo nka mwifikhirelaka nzina laka, kintta wuuteelani mweeyo na kuparikhiyeni.
Amana mwikijekela alitaari wa mawe mwihinjekane mawe ooshijaniwa zaana, eeyaru mawe awaattaliwa saana mwintta onkufurwela.
Mwihinwele na shikatta alitaari aka amana mwinjekaka, maana mwintta onfulamela.










































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Siikhu moote Nnyizinku anrumiye Yuunusa mwaana wa Amitayi yoori:
“Olankhe olawe sitati khuulu ya Neniive, walaleye ottuukhu, yoori miiyo kinjuwa zooshi zootakhala zaya anrettaazo.”
Ila Yuunusa asiiliyeevo toole, khuwaza otthirela tuniya yoolepelana Neniive, antthiraka Nnyizinku. Khulawa mpakha sitati ya Yoope khusikana pankaya vapatari, yaari weettaaye Taarisi. Khuripha pasaji yawe, khweetta mpankaya yoori atthirele Taarisi, antthiraka Nnyizinku.
Aphano, alawaka, Nnyizinku khuperekha pheevo ya waatta na pahari khutakhala khusala esaleela opwecheya pankaya.
Mamalinyero ooshi khwiiya awoova, wakhula mmote wayo khusala akhuwa anvekelaka nluku awe, yoori apatthe wuusurukha, na khusala atupweeza mapwattha aya mpahari, yoori eveyaveye pankaya yaya. Wakathi aya opo Yuunusa, aarettiye eeshukheliye mpurawu eettaka olala ajisahawiye.
Nahota khwiishukhela mpurawu mphule aari olalaamo Yuunusa, khumuuzela yoori: “Weeyo! Onlala-ni? Olankhe onvekele nluku awo! Khinjuweya anoonelaka huruma yoori anuusuru nihifwe.”
Paata ya toole, mamalinyero khusiilana yoori: “Nlaweni neekese nasipu, ninjuwe nlupa otu anitotheliye hasara eti.” Yo khweekesa nasipu etile, khusala emoona Yuunusa.
Khuuzeliwa Yuunusa: “Weeyo o nlupa onitotheliyeeyo hasara eti. Nkanuuze! Weeyo onkhola khazi-ni? Wala onlankha vayi? Nti awo nti-ni? Ama lihimo lawo lihimo-ni?”
Ye khujipu araka: “Miiyo ki Mwipereewu, kinimwaaputu Nnyizinku, Mwennyewe pinku, otu ompiye nti na pahari.”
Elottelanaka Yuunusa khuwooza yoori aari ontthira Nnyizinku. Wakathi ajuwaziyeevo etthu yaari onrettikhanelaaye, yo khwiiya ootepa woova, na khumuuzela Yuunusa: “Apho niini orettiyeeyo!”
Pheevo yeetta otepa yaattaka, khufiyelela mamalinyero omuuzela Yuunusa: “Yoori pheevo na pahari eshapweye, fweeyo nuurettele niini?”
Yuunusa khujipu araka: “Miiyo kajuwa yoori pheevo eti yapuwelela mwaasa wa miiyo. Apho, mwikitthempe mwikeeselele mpahari. Mwirettaru toowo, mwintta woona pahari na pheevo zinyamaliye.”
Ila mamalinyero apale khuhintupweezazi, khwaaza ofuttha reemu na kuvu zaya zooshi yoori afiye vathi. Khuhisala ewaheya, mwaasa yoori pahari yeetta ovira etepaka otakhala.
Yo khukhuwa ankhuwelaka Nnyizinku araka: “Oo, Nnyizinku, ohinilikhelele nifwaka mwaasa wa pinaatamu otu, na ohinikwisele paathuli ofwa wa mwinyi otu. Zooshi zarettikhana khwa nanna olakeliyeezo.”
Nawiisha khuntthempaza Yuunusa khumweeselela mpahari. Aphano pahari na pheevo, zooshi khunyamala.
Ooniyeevo toole, mamalinyero ooshi khwiiya awoova channu na khumwaaputu Nnyizinku. Khunrettelaza twaha na theenya ahiti.
Amweeselelaziyeevo mpahari, Nnyizinku khuperekha swi khuluyeene yoori emmize Yuunusa, ye khwiiya mmatthupo wa swi siikhu ttatthu nthana na osikhu.
Ari mmatthupo wa swi, ye khwaaza olompa anshukhurwelaka Nnyizinku awe:
“Nhuzuni mwaka kankhuweliye Nnyizinku, na aakijipwiye. Mithili za ahera kaakhuwiye na waasiiliye huula yaka.
Waakitupweeziye mpahari wa wiichamo, nkatthi wa khilintti, nziko wa maati khukizukulela, na mawipi awo khukikhutela.
Miiyo khulupa yoori keekareliwa peeti-wene na omaasho wawo weeyo Nnyizinku. Kinta kirutele woona theenya nyuupa yawo yoottakatthiifu?
Maati khukifiya vakhulo, khilintti khukizukulela na mirawa khukizokonzela eeshwa yaka.
Khuzama mpakha vanchina la nyaako, tuniya ya vathi, puuro enimfukelaaye ntthu khwa siikhu zooshi. Ila weeyo Mbwanaaka Nnyizinku khuusuru nafusi yaka nkhapuri mphule.
Wakathi kaari osaleelaavo ofwa, koofikhiriye weeyo Nnyizinku, khuuperekheza lompa yaka, yoori efiye nnyupa mwawo woottakatthiifu.
Apale anaputwaaye sanamu zoohiina fwayita, antarawu tthakaraka ya Nnyizinku.
Ila miiyo kinteela wuushukhurwela Nnyizinku na maliipo a siifwa na owinkha twaha, na kinteela oretta eti kaahitiyeeyo, maana nusura ti yaawo weeyo Nnyizinku.”
Aphano, Nnyizinku khuruma swi etile, yoori yanchuwe Yuunusa nshini wa nttima.
Aphano Nnyizinku khunruma Yuunusa swaafu ya phiiri yoori:
“Olankhe olawe sitati khuulu ya Neniive, walaleye ottuukhu mattakhuzi apa kinuurumaaye.”
Ye khulankha khulawa Neniive, nkhama etthiipo Nnyizinku anrumiyeezo. Neniive yaari sitati khuluyeene ntthu aari wiishishaaye siikhu ttatthu eettaka weettetta mwentto.
Ila ye n'oofiya sitati etile eettettiye siikhu moote, alaleyaka yoori: “Nkatthi wa siikhu arupayiini Nnyizinku onteela opwecha Neniive.”
Aneniive khwiiya wonkhupali Nluku khulaleyana yoori afuke, waaza attunkhulu mpakha asimaana, ooshi khuwalaza saakhu.
Hapari epile za Yuunusa zamfiyeliye mfwalume wa Neniive, ye khwiishukha vakhukulu yoohaakhimu, khuvula kuwo zoofwalume khuwala saakhu na khwiikhala vafuutha.
Aphano khuruma olaleyiwa Neniive yooshi yoori: “Khwa nzina la mfwalume na mawaziri awe: Ahiiyevo atha ntthu mmote antakhaaye oja na onywa, wala ojisa na onywisa nyama zawe, mompe zawe ama pwittipwitthi zawe.
Atthu ooshi awale saakhu, na awalise nyama zaya, na akhuwe khwa nzina la Nluku na kuvu zaya zooshi. Attharuwe oretta vitthu zootakhala na ohusuti.
Khinjuweya Nluku omwiishelaka wiiphiiriwa wawe, anoonele huruma yoori nihifwe.”
Wakathi Nluku ooniyeevo yoori alikhaza oretta vitthu zootakhala, ye khulikha etile aari wuupuwelaaye owaarettela na khuhiwaahukhumu.
Erettiyeevo toole, Yuunusa khuhintuveli etile yaya, na khwiiya wookatipukha.
Ye khusala amuuza Nnyizinku araka: “Oo Nnyizinku aka, khahiyo eti kaalupiiye nalelo kiri onti? Ti ethiito yaakipatthisiyeeyo otthira keettaka Taarisi. Miiyo kaajuwiye yoori weeyo o Nnyizinku wa tthakaraka na wa huruma, woovilela na woopheta channu, onaahitaaye ohukhumu ila khulevelela mmana wiiyavo othupwiya.
Aphano Mbwanaaka okilaze nafusi yaka, kinhithari ofwa kihiiyeeni wiiya haayi.”
Ye Nnyizinku khulupa: “Weeyo onaaye shariya yookatipukha?”
Yuunusa aalawiye khwiikhala mashaarikhi ya sitati ethiitile. Khujeka lipantta lawe, khwiikhala vamwiivuuli, khusala aweja etthu-ni yaari weettelaaye orettikhana sitati etile.
Aphano, Nnyizinku khootthisa nrayi khurapela vatulu valipantta aphale aariivo Yuunusa, yoori eeye vamwiivuuli na aawuneye haari. Nrayi opule waamwinkhiye furaha ya waatta Yuunusa.
Ila mmeesho mwaya supuyeene, Nluku khumperekha mwanyanyama khurafuna nrayi opule, khuuma.
Etthamu-tthamu ya njuwa, Nluku khuperekha pheevo ya mashaarikhi yoolukuza channu, naye njuwa khusala lipiyela veeshwa vawe Yuunusa, khusala asaleela ozileya. Eviriyeevo toole, ye khusala ajitakhela ofwa, na khuri: “Toono afwataali ofwa ehiiyeeni wiiya haayi.”
Ila Nluku khumuuzela Yuunusa: “Weeyo onaaye shariya yookatipukha mwaasa wa nrayi?” Ye khujipu: “Ayo, kinaaye! Na ki wookatipukha kintakha hatha ofwa.”
Aphano Nnyizinku khumuuza: “Weeyo onoonela huruma nrayi opo, ohikholeleeni khaazi wala ohiwuliseeni, woottha osikhu mmote na osikhu nkina khufwa.
Ila Neniive awaakho atthu anzitaaye eshiriini wa miiya alufu, ahinjuwaaye othawula etthu yooshapweya wala etthu yootakhala, na nyama za waatta. Miiyo akaari oteela wiiyana huruma na sitati khuluyeene etile?”





















































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Eti warakha ya peewu na mazina aya a amarehemu a phantte ya Yinsa Al-Masiihu, peewu ya Daawuuda na Eburahiima.
Eburahiima khunvokola Esiyaakha; Esiyaakha khunvokola Yaakhumpa; Yaakhumpa khunvokola Yuuda na attwiize;
Yuuda khunvokola Pereezi na Zeera, mamaawe aari Tamaara; Pereezi khunvokola Hezorooni, Hezorooni khunvokola Arawu;
Arawu khunvokola Aminataapi; Aminataapi khunvokola Nashooni; Nashooni khunvokola Salimooni;
Salimooni khunvokola Bowaazi, mamaawe aari Rahaape; Bowaazi khunvokola Obeedi, mamaawe aari Ruuti; Obeedi khunvokola Yeese;
na Yeese khunvokola mfwalume Daawuuda. Daawuuda khunvokola Seleyimaana, mamaawe aari muukha wa Uriiya;
Seleyimaana khunvokola Ropowaawu; Ropowaawu khunvokola Apiiya; Apiiya khunvokola Aasa;
Aasa khunvokola Zhuzaafwa; Zhuzaafwa khunvokola Joraawu; Joraawu khunvokola Uziiya;
Uziiya khunvokola Jotaawu; Jotaawu khunvokola Akaaze; Akaaze khunvokola Ezakiiya;
Ezakiiya khunvokola Manaase; Manaase khunvokola Amooni; Amooni khunvokola Joziiya;
Joziiya khunvokola Jekoniiya na attwiize, wakathi eekareliweeyo Babilooniya.
Paata ya weettaniwa Babilooniya: Jekoniiya khunvokola Sheyalitiyeeli; Sheyalitiyeeli khunvokola Zorobabeeli;
Zorobabeeli khunvokola Apiwuute; Apiwuute khunvokola Eliyakhiimu; Eliyakhiimu khunvokola Azoori;
Azoori khunvokola Satookhi; Satookhi khunvokola Akiini; Akiini khunvokola Eliwuuti;
Eliwuuti khunvokola Eliyazaari; Eliyazaari khunvokola Maata; Maata khunvokola Yaakhumpa;
na Yaakhumpa khunvokola Yuusufu, manna wa Mariyamu, otule anvokoliyeeyo Yinsa, othuuto aniitthiwaaye Al-Masiihu.
Khwa etthiipo waaviriye ojama khumi na nne waaza va Eburahiima mpakha Daawuuda, na khumi na nne waaza va Daawuuda mpakha va okholiwa olawaniwa Babilooniya, na khumi na nne waaza Babilooniya mpakha va ovokoliwa wa Yinsa.
Ovokoliwa wa Yinsa Al-Masiihu pi toono. Mariyamu ari wooposiwa ti Yuusufu ahinarapalelane, khwiimittha khwa Rooho Ttakatthiifu.
Ila Yuusufu, mposi awe, khwiiya ntthu wa shariya na woohitakhi ontwayifusha, ye khulakela sirini okayiri onrala.
Ila, paata ya wuupuwela vitthu epile, khumpuwelela nlayikha la Mbwana nkatthi wa olottha, khumuuza yoori: “Yuusufu, mwaana wa Daawuuda, ohoove ompokhera Mariyamu wiiya muukhaawo, maana ye eemittha khwa Rooho Ttakatthiifu.
Ye onteela ompattha mwaana, weeyo ontthaje nzina la Yinsa, maana ye onteela owoosuru atthu awe khwa twampi zaya.”
Zooshi epo enteela orettikhana yoori ziretteye zooshi epile Mbwana alupiyeeyo khwa napiyu yoori:
“Mwaari onteela wiimittha ampatthe mwaana, anttelaaye wiitthiwa Emanuweele, enlupaaye yoori ‘Nluku ori vamote na fweeyo’.”
Paata ya olankha, Yuusufu khuretta etile nlayikha la Mbwana laamuziyeeyo khumpokhera Mariyamu muukhaawe.
Ye khaarapalelaniye mpakha ompattha mwaana. Khuntthaja nzina la Yinsa.
Paata ya Yinsa ovokoliwa Belemu ya Yudeya yenzi ya mfwalume Herooti, ajuwi alankhiye malawa-juwa khuta Yeruzaleemu.
Khuuzela yoori: “Mwaana ntteetthe otu avokoliweeyo, mfwalume wa mayaahuuti ori vayi? Fweeyo noona ntthottowa lawe malawa-juwa nateela omwaaputu.”
Wakathi mfwalume Herooti asiiliyeevo epo zaya, khwiiya woovelavela, na atthu ooshi a Yeruzaleemu.
Aphano khuwaakusanya mahaakhimu a tiini ooshi na anamanozela a kano, khuwoozela vayi aari weettelaawo ovokoliwawo Al-Masiihu.
Yo khunjipu yoori: “Belemu ya Yudeya, maana napiyu aatikha toono:
‘Weeyo Belemu, ya nti wa Yudeya, weeyo hatha vattitthiiru khahi owoohafwiifweya khwa sitati khuulu za Yuuda, maana khwa weeyo onteela opuwa mfwalume anttelaaye oweettettisa atthu aka a Ezirayiilu.’”
Herooti khuwaakhuwela ajuwi sirini khuwoozela wakathi laapuwiyeeyo ntthottowa nttho.
Aphano khuwaaruma Belemu awoozaka yoori: “Mwilawe mweekese ojuwa saaneene monkoni wa mwaana oto, na amana mwinsikana, mwite mwikuuze yoori na miiyo kilawe kamwaaputu.”
Paata ya onsiila mfwalume yo khusala alawa, ntarikhi khoona ntthottowa nttintthile ooniyeeyo malawa-juwa, khulokoza khulawa khweemela puuro etile aariivo mwaana.
Noorutela woona ntthottowa ntthile, khwiiya oofurahi venkivene.
Khuvira nnyupa mphule khunsikana mwaana na Mariyamu mamaawe, khukokhora khumwaaputu. Nawiisha, khufukula maphuta aya khumwinkha tthuvo: Thahapu, ovupa, na mafuttha oonukhela.
Khuuziwa muulottha yoori ahirutele wa Herooti, khurutela owaya khwa tarikhi kiina.
Paata ya ajuwi olawa, nlayikha la Mbwana khumpuwelela Yuusufu muulottha khumuuza yoori: “Olankhe, onthuule mwaana oto na mamaawe, otthirele Misuri. Weekhale ottuukho mpakha miiyo kiwuuze, maana Herooti onteela omweekesa mwaana oto yoori amuule.”
Aphano ye khulankha, khunthuula mwaana na mamaawe osikhu, khweetta Misuri.
Ottuukho eekhaliyeeyo mpakha Herooti ofwa. Khwa etthiipo khuretteya etile Mbwana alupiyeeyo khwa napiyu yoori: “Kankhuwela mwanaka aari nti wa Misuri.”
Herooti ooniyeevo yoori attettekhiwa ti ajuwi, khwiiya wookatipukha, khuruma wuuliwa aana ooshi a nyaakha miwiri zeettaka vathi, Belemu na miti zawaattamanana nkhama wakathi otthuupo ooziweeyo pi ajuwi.
Aphano khurettikhana epile zaalupiweeyo ti napiyu Yeremiiya:
“Khusiileya huula nti wa Rama ya olila na ojikhupanyisa nwulweene; aari Rakeele awaalilelaka aana awe akatthalaka ozurwiwa, mwaasa wa ooshi ofwa.”
Paata ya Herooti ofwa, nlayikha la Mbwana khumpuwelela Yuusufu muulottha Misuri,
khumuuza yoori: “Olankhe, onthuule mwaana na mamaawe, olawe Ezirayiilu, maana apale aari otakhaaye omuula afwa.”
Ye khulankha, khunthuula mwaana na mamaawe, khweetta nti wa Ezirayiilu
Ila noosiila yoori Arikileewu mwaana wa Herooti ti asalaniyeeyo ofwalume wa papaawe, khwiiya wa woova weettawo. Nawuuziwa muulottha, khweetta nti wa Kalileya.
Khusala eekhala sitati eniitthiwaaye Nazareeti, yoori erettikhane epile zaalupiweeyo pi manapiyu araka: “Ye onteela wiitthiwa Nnazare.”
Siikhu zaya epile khupuwa Yaahaya Namoosa, alaleyaka n'yaara ya Yudeya.
Ye aari okhuwa araka: “Mwithupwiye, Ofwalume wa pinkuuni ori kharipu.”
Maana otu ti otule alupiweeyo ti napiyu Ezaaya yoori: “Huula enkhuwa n'yaara eraka: ‘Mwitthenkeze tarikhi ya Mbwana na mookolele miphiitelo zawe.’”
Kuwo za Yaahaya zaattalaniwe ovuzi wa nkamiiya, na aari owalaka nzako wa shapala n'yuunu. Etthu yoojiwa yawe aari mapalaka na asali ya ntthuttu.
Atthu a nti wa Yeruzaleemu na a Yudeya na miti zooshi za nkerekhere ya Yorotaani aari onteela ye.
Yo aari otukhuru twampi zaya, nawoosiwa ti Yaahaya mmuttho Yorotaani.
Wakathi ye awooniyeeyo mafwarizeewu na masatukhi enkeene ataaka aphale aari woosaavo, khuwooza yoori: “Ojama wa evili! Ti paani awuuziyeeni otthira katapu entaaye?
Mwithoonyeze khwa khaazi zenu yoori weekhweele mwathupwiya twampi zenu!
Khahiyo olupa yoori: ‘Eburahiima ti marehemu papeetthu,’ ila miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori, khwa liwe ntthi Nluku onwahi owaattala aana a Eburahiima.
Nshokha lanoliwa latthiiwa nshini wa mitathaari za miitthi. Wakhula muutthi ohiniimaaye mishumo zooshapweya ontta oshijiwa weeseleliwe va moottho.
“Miiyo kiniwoosani na maati khwa othoonyeza othupwiya wa twampi zenu. Ila paata ya miiyo onta ntthu ariinaaye owahi zayita miiyo, hatha akinsuhi shitaha yawe wala akina makhaamu oothuula jampali zawe. Ye onttela owoosani na Rooho Ttakatthiifu na moottho.
Ye ontana fosholo mmakhono mwawe onteela ophakula tiriku na maveya. Tiriku atthe va sakafu vawe, maveya akhoze va moottho ohinzimaaye.”
Aphano Yinsa khulankha Kalileya khuta o Muuttho Yorotaani oteela woosiwa ti Yaahaya.
Yaahaya khusala atakha okatthala araka: “Miiyo ti kinhithajiya woosiwa ti weeyo, onikiteela toovi miiyo?”
Ila Yinsa khunjipu yoori: “Olikhe etthiipo, yoori erettikhane shariya yooshi.” Yaahaya khukhupalela.
Yinsa nawoosiwa, khuvuuwa, nasaapiru pinku khufukuwa, khoona Rooho Ttakatthiifu yiishukhaka nkhama jiwa khummorela.
Huula ya olankha pinkuuni khuri: “Otu mwanaka wompheta, na wookituvela channu!”
Aphano Yinsa khuthuuliwa ti Rooho Ttakatthiifu khweettaniwa n'yaara, yoori alawe azayiniwe ti sheethwani.
Paata ya ofuka siikhu arupayiini nthana na osikhu, khunkhola jala
Aphano Sheethwani khumwaattama khumuuza yoori: “Nkhama weeyo o Mwaana wa Nnyizinkhu, orume mawe apo athatuwe eeye phaawu.”
Ila Yinsa khunjipu araka: “Yaatikhiwa yoori: ‘Khahiyo phaawu paasi enimwinkhaaye ntthu ohaayi, ila nttakhuzi looshi linlankhaaye nkhanyo wa Nluku.’”
Elottelanaka, sheethwani khumweettana sitati ttakatthiifu, khunweza phantte yawiishela olepa ya Nyuupa Yoosifwiwamo,
khumuuza yoori: “Nkhama o mwaana wa Nluku, ojeeselele vathi aphale. Maana yaatikhiwa yoori: ‘Ye ontta oruma malayikha awe awiinanele, atthaapo antta wuukholelela na makhono aya yoori ohikwakwanttuwe va liwe.’”
Yinsa khunjipu yoori: “Theenya yaatikhiwa yoori: ‘Ohimweeze Mbwana, Nluku awo.’”
Sheethwani khunthuula khumweettana va mwaako mmote woolepa venkivene khunthoonyeza ofwalume wooshi wa olumwenku na siifwa yaya.
Khumuuza yoori: “Amana okikokhorela khukaaputu kintta owinkha zooshi.”
Yinsa khumuuza yoori: “Oleevo, Epiliisi! Maana yaatikhiwa yoori: ‘Omwaaputu Mbwana, Nluku awo, na onrumeyele othuuto paasi.’”
Aphano sheethwani khumwaattuwa, khuta malayikha oteela onrumeyela.
Wakathi Yinsa asiiliyeevo yoori Yaahaya afukiwa, khurutela Kalileya.
Khulaawo Nazareeti khulawa khwiikhala Kafwaranaawu, yaari nshini wa pahari, nti wa Zebulooni na Nafitaali,
yoori erettikhane etile yaalupiweeyo ti napiyu Ezaaya yoori:
“Nti wa Zebulooni, na nti wa Nafitaali, tarikhi ya pahari, kaapu ya Yorotaani, Kalileya ya amalapo!
Atthu aari wiikhalaaye n'yiiza oona nuuru khuluyeene; khwa apale aari wiikhalaaye miti za mwiivuli wa ofwa, amwasikheliwa ti nuuru.”
Waaza attaapho Yinsa khwaaza olaleya hapari zawe alupaka yoori: “Mwithupwiye, maana ofwalume wa pinkuuni ori kharipu.”
Eettaka weettetta nshini wa Pahari ya Kalileya Yinsa khuwoona attwi awiri: Simawu, anitthiwaaye Pheeturu, na ttwiiye Antere. Yo aari weeselela matthavi aya mpahari, maana yo aari anamajiya.
Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Mwikilotte, miiyo kintta wuurettani o namajiya a atthu.”
Nasaapiru yo khulikha matthavi aya khusala anlotta.
Eettaka olawa etthiipile khuwoona attwi akina awiri: Tiyaaku, mwaana wa Zepeteewu, na Yaahaya, ttwiiye. Yo aari mmwaatiya na papaaya Zepeteewu, attalelaka matthavi aya, Yinsa khuwaakhuwela.
Nasaapiru yo khunlikha papaaya na mwaatiya, khunlotta.
Yinsa eettettiye Kalileya yooshi asomisaka mmasinakooka, atafusiraka hapari zooshapweya za ofwalume na avonisaka marati ooshi vakatthi wa atthu
Hapari monkoni wa ye khumwazeyela Siiriya yooshi, atthu khusala awaatiisa ooshi apale aarina marati, aari olwaaziwaaye na ohoochiwa ti masheethwani, anajilejile, anasupiyaani, ye noowaavonisa.
Atthu enkeene khusala anlottelela olankha Kalileya, Tekapooli, Yeruzaleemu, Yudeya na a nti wa phantte kiina ya Yorotaani.
Awooniyeevo atthu apale waatta, Yinsa khuwela va mwaako na khwiikhala. Anakhiyoni awe khususela aphale aariivo,
Ye khusala awaasomisa, araka:
“Ooparikhiyiwa pi apale eeyiye asikhini nroho, maana ofwalume wa pinkuuni pi waaya.
Ooparikhiyiwa pi apale anlilaaye, maana anteela ozurwiwa.
Ooparikhiyiwa pi apale oojipushuwisa, maana yo anteela orithi olumwenku.
Ooparikhiyiwa pi apale ariina jala na nnyottha la shariya, maana anteela orupala.
Ooparikhiyiwa pi apale ariina tthakaraka, maana na-yo anteela wooneliwa tthakaraka.
Ooparikhiyiwa pi apale ariina rooho yoopakusiwa, maana yo anteela omoona Nluku.
Ooparikhiyiwa pi apale oolevelela, maana anteela wiitthiwa aana a Nluku.
Ooparikhiyiwa pi apale anlupatthiwaaye mwaasa wa haakhi, maana Ofwalume wa pinkuuni pi waaya.
Ooparikhiyiwa ti mweeyo amana mwittukhaniwaka na olupatthiwa, na wakhula zootakhala empuwaaye khwa mweeyo mwaasa wa miiyo.
Mwifurahi na mwitthape, maana tthuvo yenu pinkuuni khuluyeene, maana khwa nanna etthiipo awaalupatthiye manapiyu aviriyeeyo khapula ya mweeyo.
“Mweeyo mwa mwiinyu wa olumwenku. Ila amana olikha onyuunya waya, onrutiseleya toovi? Khuniiyana hatha fwayita, woohiiyi wiitthiwa khusala oluwattheliwa pi atthu.
Mweeyo mwa nuuru ya olumwenku. Sitati yoojekiwa va mwaako khinvitheya.
Khina ankhozaaye khantteya khuttha nyuku. Entthiiwa vahali wawooneyavo yoori ewaamwasikhele atthu apale aniiyaaye nnyupa
Nakatalikha nuuru yenu mweeyo yaare vakatthi wa atthu, yoori oone khaazi zenu ansifu Papeenu ariiye pinkuuni.
“Mwihuupuwele yoori kateela wiishisa kano za Munsa ama masomi a manapiyu, akaateeliye wiishisa, ila omarisela.
Kiniwuuzani khweele yoori: Erivo etthiipi pinku na vathi khina nanna entakhaaye waashikha nenkawu alama yiisheliye ya kano ama nttottonka, mpakha zooshi erettikhane.
Wooshi otule anttelaaye okhijilela oruma, hatha nkhama weetta opushuwa, na khuwaanozela akinoko oretta etthiipo, onteela wiitthiwa yoori woopepheya muufwalume wa pinkuuni; ila wakhula otule anshututelaaye na khusomisa oruma waya opu, onteela wiitthiwa yoori nwulweene muufwalume wa pinkuuni.
Maana miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori shariya yenu amana ehiziti ya mafwarizeewu na ya anamanozela a kano, hatha vattitthiiru khamwinteela weettamo muufwalume wa pinkuuni.
“Mweeyo mwasiila vitthu ooziweeyo amarehemu apapazenu yoori: ‘Mwihuule; wakhula anuulaaye oneekesela ophukiwa.’
Ila miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori wakhula aninkatipukhelaaye ttwiiye oneekesela ophukiwa naye, na wakhula aninttukhanaaye ttwiiye ona ya olawaniwa wa afwalume ophukiwa. Na otule animuuzaaye ttwiiye yoori: ‘nlolo!’ oninsuhi weetta vamoottho wa motthooni.
Nakatalikha, amana weettelaka winkha zaakha va alitaari khufikhiri yoori ttwiiyo ona etthu varoho na-weyo,
olikhe zaakha yawo va alitaari attaapho, olawe wasiilane na ttwiiyo, nawiisha ote operekhe saana zaakha yawo.
Amana ntthu atakha wuulawana onyuupa wa anamaphuka, osiilanane saana ntthu aya oto ntarikhi mweettaka olawa, maana noohijuwi saana weeyo onttela winkheleliwa wa namaphuka, namaphuka awinkhelele wa namweekesela kalapooso na ye aweeselele nkalapooso.
Miiyo kiniwuuza khweele yoori khunlaamo ohiripheeni nzurukhu otthuupo onttelaaye wuuziwa.
“Mweeyo mwasiila elupiwaka yoori: ‘Ohiraruwe.’
Ila miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori wakhula animweekesaaye muukha na ontakha varoho vawe, anrarusha.
Nkhama liisho lawo la phantte ya nkhono nlume lintta wuukosisa, olazemo weesele oje. Afwataali wuupwetheya phantte yawo moote ya mwiili awo zayita mwiili awo wooshi weeseleliwa motthooni.
Nkhama nkhono awo nlume ontta wuukosisa, oshije weesele. Afwataali wuupwetheya phantte yawo moote ya mwiili awo woohiiyi mwiili awo wooshi weeseleliwa motthooni.
“Yaatikhiwa theenya yoori: ‘Otule animwaashaaye muukhawe ona ya omwinkha talakha.’
Ila miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori wooshi otule animwaashaaye muukhaawe, ehiriwaka etta oraruwa, oniiyana paathuli ya onruma oraruwa, na otule aninralaaye muukha aya otule wa waashiwa ontta onrarusha.
“Mweeyo mwasiila etthu ooziweeyo amarehemu apapazenu yoori: ‘Mwihilaphe woovonyeyavo, ila mweettettise olapha mwirettiyeeyo omaasho wa Mbwana.’
Ila miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori: mwihilaphe hatha vattitthiiru wala khwa vitthu za pinkuuni maana khukulu ya Nluku;
wala khwa vitthu za vathi maana phi anvumulisaavo moolu awe, wala khwa Yeruzaleemu maana sitati ya Mfwalume nwulu.
Wala ohilaphele khwa eeshwa yawo maana weeyo khunwahi olakaza wala oriipisa hatha nyuuli yawo moote.
Entosheleza olupa yoori ‘ayo’ amana yiiya ‘ayo’, na ‘wala’ amana yiiya ‘wala’; noozitisa apho enlankha wa Sheethwani.
“Mweeyo mwasiila etile elupiwe yoori: ‘Liisho khwa liisho na liino khwa liino.’
Ila miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori: mwihikhanyarele ojiripha khwa atthu apale anuurettelaanini zootakhala. Amana ntthu oopwakula nlaku limote onzukulisele ntthi likina.
Amana ntthu atakha wuulawana wa anamaphuka na wuuvula kameza yawo, omwinkhe theenya ajapi yawo.
Amana ntthu ookhanyarela othuula lipwattha khwa kiyasi ya phiima alufu moote, othuule phiima alufu piiri.
“Amana ntthu oovekela etthu, omwinkhe; ohinnoze enyokonyoko otule anuuvekelaaye omwiipaasha.
Mweeyo mwasiila olupiwa yoori: ‘Omphete namwaattamanani awo, omwiine atuwi awo.’
Ila miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori, mwiwaaphete maatuwi enu na mwiwaalompele apale anuulupatthanini,
yoori mweeyo mwiretteye wiiya aana a Papeenu ariiye pinkuuni. Maana ye oniwaatthamushela njuwa apale anrettaaye zooshapweya na apale anrettaaye zootakhala. Na oniwenkha vuula anashariya na apale ohitakhi shariya.
Amana mwiwaaphetaka apale anuuphetaanini paasi, tthuvo-ni mwiineekeselaaye wiiyana? Anamariphisa lumpuru nayo khanretta etthiipo?
Na amana mwiiwaachelisaka maswaahipu paasi, mwinrettani yooziti? Hatha na amalapo anretta etthiipo.
Nakataalikha mwiiye atthu khaamili, nkhama etthiipo eyiyeeyo khaamili Papeenu wa pinkuuni.
“Mwiiyane phoole na oretta khaazi zenu za shariya vahali aniiyavo atthu akina yoori mwisifwiwe pi yo. Amana mwiretta toowo, khamwiniiyana hatha tthuvo ya Papeenu wa pinkuuni.
“Nakataalikha, amana mwinkha zimola mwihithuule nlope khusala mwilaleya, nkhama anrettaazo manaafikhi mmasinakooka na mmaliinya, atakhaka yoori asifwiwe pi akina aya. Miiyo kiniwuuza khweele yoori yo apokhera tthuvo yaya.
Ila amana weeyo winkha zimola, nkhono awo nkha ohijuwe etthu orettiyeewo nkhono nlume awo,
yoori zimola yawo yiiye siiri. Toowo, Papaawo otule anoonaaye epile enrettiwaaye sirini, ontta wuutthuva.
“Na amana mwilompaka, mwihiiye nkhama manaafikhi. Yo owaatuvela weemela khusala alompa nsinakooka, mmatarikhi, atakhaka yoori ooniwe pi akinoko aya. Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori yo apokhera tthuvo yaya.
Ila amana weeyo olompaka, weette okatthi wawo ofuke nlako awo, onvekele Papaawo ahinooneyaaye. Aphano, othuuto ontta wuutthuva.
Na amana olompaka, khahiyo orutela mattakhuzi mamoteru ooheleyi swaafu zawaatta, nkhama anrettaazo amalapo. Yo anaakhipwela yoori mwaasa wa waattisa ottakhula Nluku ti aniwaasiilaavo.
Mwihiiye nkhama atthaapo, maana khapula mweeyo mwihinaveke Papeenu onretta ajuwe etthu mwinihithajiyaaye.
Nakataalikha, mweeyo amana mwilompaka mwisala mwiri toono: ‘Papeetthu oriiye pinkuuni, littitthimisiwe nzina lawo loottakatthifu,
wiishushe ofwalume awo, mattakhelo awo arettikhane vathi apha nkhama etthiipo enrettikhanaazo otulu!
Oninkhe wakhula siikhu etthu-yoojiwa ninihithajiyaaye.
Oniswaamihi koosa zeetthu nkhama etthiipi na-fweyo nininswaamihaaye wakhula otule annikosaaye,
na ohinilikhelele nizayiniwaka, ila nuusuru khwa ntakhali, [maana ofwalume, owahi, na siifwa zooshi pi zawo, mileele. Amiina.]’
Maana amana mwiwaaswaamihi anaatamu koosa zaya, Papeenu wa pinkuuni naye ontta wuuswaamihini,
ila amana mwihiswaamihanaka, Papeenu wa pinkuuni naye khanuuswaamihini koosa zenu.
“Amana ofuka, ohithoonyeze wuuso wa huzuni nkhama anrettaazo manaafikhi, yo antta ozukulisa wuuso aya yoori akina aya apatthe ojuwa yoori afuka. Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori nooretta toowo apokhera tthuvo yaya.
Ila weeyo amana ofuka, osala woosa wuuso awo, na khushamula nyuuli zawo,
yoori akinoko ahijuwe yoori wafuka, ila Papeenu, anoonaaye vitthu za siiri, ye ontta ojuwa yoori wafuka na othuuto ontta wuutthuva.
“Ohikusanye maali vathi apha, oriivo oshuwa, na kuuthu enwahaaye oharipu, na ariivo manantarawu oophenya khwiiya.
Ila okusanye maali pinkuuni, ottuukho oshuwa na kuuthu ehinwahaawo oharipu wala nantarawu ahimphenyelaawo khwiiya.
Maana attaapho eniiyaavo maali zawo, rooho yawo nayo eniiya attaapho.
“Maasho khantteya ya mwiili. Amana maasho awo eeya ooshwapweya, mwiili awo oniiyana nuuru;
ila amana maasho awo eeya oohishapweyi, mwiili awo wooshi oniiya n'yiiza. Nakataalikha, amana nuuru oriinaaye ezukuluwa yiiya yiiza, yiiza yaya eto eniiya khuluyeene!
“Khaavo ntthu anwahaaye owaarumeyela a mbwana awiri, mwaasa yoori ontta omwiiphiirisa mmote, antuvelise otu nkina; ama oniiya wa waamineya khwa otu mmote, antarawu otu nkina. Khinwaheya onrumeyela Nluku na nzurukhu.
“Tiito, kiniwuuzanini yoori: Mwihiiye woovelavelela ohaayi enu, khwa etthu-yoojiwa ama yoonywiwa; wala mwiili enu monkoni wa etthu ya owala. Ohaayi enu waziti etthu-yoojiwa. Na mwiili enu waziti kuwo.
Mwiwoone anyannyi otulu: Khanzala, khanuurula wala khana sakafu; ila Papeenu wa pinkuuni oniwaajisa. Nakataalikha mweeyo mwinaaye fwayita zayita anyannyi.
Paani wa mweeyo anwahaaye weekezela mansha awe hatha nkhama eetta oshukulikhela?
Khi mwinvelavelelani kuwo? Moone nanna enwulaazo miitthi za ntthuttu na maluwa aya: yo khazinkhola khaazi, wala khazinsona.
Ila wekhweele miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori, Seleyimaana na oshapweya wawe khawaleeni kuwo zooshapweya nkhama maluwa apa.
Moone, Nluku onwalisa nyaani za ntthuttu leelo ziniiyaavo meesho khulukuziwa, onuuwalisani mweeyo channu atthu oopushuwa amini!
Nakataalikha mwihishukulikhe, mwiraka: ‘Ninja niini?’ Ama ‘ninnywa niini?’ Ama ‘ninwala niini?’
Maana amalapo pi anshukulikhelaaye vitthu nkhama epo; ila Papeenu ariiye pinkuuni onjuwa yoori enuuhithajiyani epo zaya.
Apho, mweekese khapula Ofwalume wa Nluku na shariya yaya, zooshi epo mwintta winkhiwa.
Nakataalikha mwihishukulikhele siikhu ya meesho, maana meesho entana tafwawuthi zaya. Wakhula siikhu eniiyana otakhala waya.
“Mwihimphuke nzeenu yoori mwihiphukiwe.
Maana khwa khiima ethiito omphukanaaye, na-weyo omphukiwa khwa khiima ethiito; mphimo otthuupo onrumeyelaaye owaaphimelanaka azaawo, na-yo anuuphimelana otthuupo.
“Mwaasa aya niini woonaka etutu eriiye mmaasho wa ttwiiyo, ila khuhooni lipikhi liriiye mmaasho mwawo?
Nanna-ni onimuuzaaye ttwiiyo yoori: ‘Kintakha kuulaze etutu eriiye mmaasho mwawo,’ khupe weeyo orina lipikhi mmaasho mwawo?
Naafikhi! Olazemo khapula lipikhi liriiye mmaasho mwawo, aphano ontta woona saaneene khuwahi olazamo etutu eriiye mmaasho wa ttwiiyo.
“Mwihiwenkhe vitthu ttakatthiifu anapwa, antta wuuzukuluwelani na oolumeni, wala mwiheeselele kuluwe mawe ootafikhana mwirettaru toowo entta oluwatthela.
“Mwiveke, mwintta winkhiwa; mweekese, mwintta opattha; mwipiye nlako, mwintta ofukuleliwa.
Maana wakhula anvekaaye oninkhiwa, aneekesaaye ompattha, ampiyaaye nlako ontta ofukuleliwa.
“Paapa-ni mmote wa mweeyo, anraaye mwanawe anvekeliye phaawu khumwinkha liwe?
Ama anvekeliye swi khumwinkha nyookha?
Mweeyo mwa atthu ootakhala rooho, mwinjuwa owenkha vitthu zooshapweya aaneenu. Papeenu ariiye pinkuuni, atepa owenkha vitthu zooshapweya apale aninvekelaaye.
Wakhula etile enuutuvelaanini oretteliwa, na-mweyo mwiwaarettele etthiipo azeenu, maana kano na manapiyu anlupa etthiipo.
“Mwivire nlako woophunyeya, maana nlako nwulweene na tarikhi yoomwazeya eninlokoza ntthu motthooni, enkeene anvira nlako otthuupo.
Tarikhi na nlako oninkhaaye ohaayi wa mileele nttithiiru, na atthu vattitthiiru ti anttelaaye oviravo.
“Phoole na manapiyu oojipanka, yo anuuteelani mweeyo awaliye shapala ya pwittipwitthi, ila nkatthi ari miiji zooluma.
Khwa mishumo zaya mwinteela owaajuwa. Khunshumeya wuuva mmiiwa, wala mmuuyu khinshumiwamo ekhuuwa.
Khwa etthiipo wakhula muutthi wooshapweya oniima mishumo zooshapweya, na muutthi wootakhala oniima mishumo zootakhala.
Khinretteya muutthi wooshapweya wiima mishumo zootakhala, wala muutthi wootakhala wiima mishumo zooshapweya.
Wakhula muutthi ohiniimaaye mishumo zooshapweya ontta oshijiwa khweeseliwa va moottho.
Khwa etthiipo mwinteela owaajuwa khwa mishumo zaya!
“Khahiyo ooshi apale anikiitthaaye yoori: ‘Mbwana, Mbwana,’ anttelaaye weettamo muufwalume wa pinkuuni, ila otule anrettaaye matakhelo a Paapa ariiye pinkuuni.
Amana efiya siikhu yaya eto enkeene, anlawa akuuze yoori: ‘Mbwana, Mbwana! Fweeyo nahupiri khwa nzina lawo, neekara masheethwani khwa nzina lawo, na khwa nzina lawo naretta minjuza.’
Aphano miiyo kilupe saaneene yoori: ‘Akuujuweenini. Mwikisuse, anamaretta zootakhala.’
“Wakhula otule ansiilaaye nttakhuzi laka na khushututela onlattisaniwa ntthu wa akhili ajekiye nyuupa yawe khuthipa khuttha vanchina la mawe;
