khunya vuula, khwiitaaza nyuuttho khuvuma pheevo khusakhinya nyuupa etile, khuhikwi, maana nchina laya laari va mawe.
Wakhula otule ansiilaaye nttakhuzi laka khuhishututeli onlattisaniwa ntthu woololo ajekiye nyuupa yawe va nshaka;
khunya vuula, khwiitaaza nyuuttho, khuvuma pheevo khupiya nyuupa etile, khupwaluwa, khupwecheya”.
Wakathi Yinsa eeshiyeevo ottakhula, khuntti epile khwiiya zootikinisiwa khwa masomi awe,
maana aari osomisa nkhama ntthu ariinaaye ofwalume, woohiiyi nkhama anamanozela a kano.
Wakathi eeshukhiyeevo va mwaako, khuntti khuluyeene yeetta onlotta.
Nasaapiru khuta namaaharaja mmote khumwaattama, khumwaaputu akokhoriye khulupa yoori: “Mbwana, onwahi okitwaharesha!”
Yinsa khookola nkhono awe, khunsapa khuri: “Katakha, ti otwaharesheye!” Nasaapiru ye khwiiya wootwaharesheya khwa maaharaja.
Aphano Yinsa khumuuza yoori: “Vitthu epi ohinthatelele hatha ntthu. Ila olawe, wajithoonyeze wa namalokozela a tiini na olaze zaakha etile Munsa alupiyeeyo yoori yiiye oshaahiti.”
Wakathi Yinsa afiiyeevo sitati ya Kafwaranaawu, eetta oteeliwa ti nttunkhulu wa anajanka, anvekelaka yoori amwaawuni.
Khumuuza yoori: “Mbwana, karumeya aka ori onti, onaaye supiyaani, ontta ohoocheya venkivene.”
Yinsa khumuuza yoori: “Miiyo kinlawa kanvonise.”
Nttunkhulu wa anajanka otule khunjipu yoori: “Mbwana, miiyo akinsuhi wuupokherela vaje vaka. Ila olupe nttakhuzi limote paasi, karumeya aka ontta ovona.
Maana na-miyo ki ntthu kiriiye vathi wa ofwalume na ki nlokozi wa anajanka. Kinimuuza mmote yoori: ‘Olawe,’ khulawa; khumuuza nkina yoori: ‘Ote,’ ye khuta. Kinimuuza karumeya aka yoori: ‘Orette khata,’ ye khuretta.”
Yinsa noosiila epo zaya, khushanka, khuwooza apale aari onlottaaye yoori: “Kiniwuuzani khweele: Akinsikaneeni Ezirayiilu ntthu ariina amini nkhama eti.
Miiyo kiniwuuzani, atthu enkeene a khipula na malawa-juwa, anttela wiikhala va meeza na Eburahiima, Esiyaakha, Yaakhumpa muufwalume wa pinkuuni.
Ila apale aari weettelaaye orithi ofwalume wa Nluku anttela weeseleliwa oje, n'yiiza nhali onttelaaye wiiyamo olila na oluma meeno.”
Yinsa khumuuza nttunkhulu wa anajanka otule yoori: “Olawe owawo, entta orettikhana nkhama etthiipo okhupaliyeezo.” Wakathi otthuupule karumeya awe khwiiya woovona.
Yinsa khweetta owawe Pheeturu ottuukho khumoona nkhwewe Pheeturu arapaleliye ari nlwele hooma.
Yinsa khunsapa nkhono awe, hooma etile khumwiisha. Khulankha khusala anrumeyela.
Paata ya otupweela njuwa, khutiiseliwa anamasheethwani awaatta, ye khusala eekara masheethwani khwa nttakhuzi lawe khuwaavonisa alwele ooshi.
Khwa etthiipo khurettikhana epile zaalupiweeyo ti napiyu Ezaaya yoori: “Ye athuula marati etthu na apwechera moolwele etthu.”
Yinsa noowoona atthu awaatta anzukuleliye, khuwaaruma anakhiyoni awe olokhela kaapu ya ntthatta.
Aphano namanozela wa kano mmote khumwaattama khumuuza yoori: “Mwaaliimu, kintta wuulotta wakhula vahali oneettaavo.”
Yinsa khunjipu araka: “Ananthala anaaye maphotto aya anyannyi anaaye vijaaro zaya, ila Mwaana wa Pinaatamu khana vahali woovumulisavo eeshwa yawe.”
Nakhiyoni awe mmote khuri: “Mbwana, waaze okilikha kilawe kanzikhe paapa.”
Yinsa khujipu araka: “Okilotte, owaalikhe ananfwa awaazikhe ananfwa aya eenyewe.”
Yinsa apakhiriyeevo mmwaatiya anakhiyoni awe khunlotta.
Nasaapiru, pheevo yawoopisa khusala evuma mpahari, mwaatiya khusala ozamisiwa ti mawipi, Yinsa ettaka olala.
Anakhiyoni awe khunsusela khusala anlansa, ankhuwelaka araka: “Mbwana, onuusuru nasaleela ofwa!”
Ye khuwoozela yoori: “Mwinoovani? Atthu oopushuwa amini!” Ye khulankha khushowera pheevo etile na pahari, zooshi khunyamala.
Ooshi khusala ashankiye na khulupa yoori: “Otu aya paani hatha anrumaaye pheevo na pahari khunshututela?”
Wakathi afiiyeevo phantte kiina, ya Jerazeenu, khunteela anamasheethwani awiri, alankhiyeeyo ovilalo. Yo aari oowali, khina aari oviraaye tarikhi ya etile.
Aphano, yo khusala anyakula araka: “Onnitakhelani fweeyo, Mwaana wa Nluku? Wata okhuno oteela onoopopisa, ohinafiye wakathi aya?”
Kharipu ya aphale vaya laarivo liphanko la kuluwe.
Aphano masheethwani apale khunvekela Yinsa yoori: “Nkhama onniikara, oniikarile nliphanko la kuluwe.”
Yinsa khulupa yoori: “Apho mwilawe!” Masheethwani apale khulawa khweetta nkuluwe, liphanko looshi khwiishukela va ntthatta khuttuluwa khufwa.
Atthu apale aari oshukaaye kuluwe epile khutthira khulawa mmuti, khulupa zooshi mpakha epile zaarettikhaniyeeyo khwa anamasheethwani apale awiri.
Atthu ooshi a mmuti mphule khusala alawa okutthanana Yinsa, nonsikana, khunvekela amuuzaka yoori aleemo mmuti mwaya.
Yinsa noopakhira mmwaatiya, khulokha ntthatta khweetta sitati ya owawe.
Khutiisiwa nasupiyaani attattikheliwe va nrepa. Wakathi ooniyeevo amini ya atthu apale antiisiyeeyo, khumuuza nasupiyaani otule yoori: “Ominyale, mwanaka! Twampi zawo zaswaamihiwa.”
Noolupa toowo anamanozela a kano khwaaza waapa araka: “Ntthu otu ontta okufuru!”
Yinsa noojuwa etthu aari wuupuwelaaye yo, khuwooza yoori: “Mwaasa wa niini mweeyo muupuwelaka nroho mwenu vitthu zootakhala?
Apho yookhweya ti tiivi? Olupa yoori: ‘Waswaamihiwa twampi zawo,’ ama olupa yoori: ‘Olankhe weettette?’
Mwijuwe yoori Mwaana wa Pinaatamu onaaye ruhusa ya oswaamihi twampi vathi apha” khumuuza nasupiyaani otule yoori: “Olankhe, othuule nrepa lawo olawe owawo.”
Khulankha khusala alawa owawe.
Paata ya atthu woona vitthu epile khuwaapattha woova, khunsifu Nluku, awenkhiyeeyo anaatamu ofwalume nkhama opo.
Elottelanaka Yinsa khulaawo okhule waya, khumoona mwinyi mmote aniitthiwaaye Matewuzhu eekhaliye ariphisaka lumpuru, khumuuza yoori: “Okilotte!” Ye khulankha khunlotta.
Yinsa eekhaliyeevo va meeza owawe Matewuzhu, anamariphisa lumpuru enkeene na anatwampi aatiiye khwiikhala attaapho vamote na anakhiyoni awe.
Mafwarizeewu nawoona toole khuwoozela anakhiyoni awe araka: “Mwaasa wa niini mwaaliimu enu ajaka na anamariphisa lumpuru na anatwampi?”
Yinsa noosiila, khulupa yoori: “Akumi khaninhithajiya tothoro, ila alwele.
Mwilawe mwanozeliwe maana a nttakhuzi linlupaaye yoori: ‘Kintakha tthakaraka, khahiyo twaha.’ Maana miiyo akawaateeliye anashariya, kawaateeliye anatwampi.
Aphano khuta anakhiyoni a Yaahaya omuuzela yoori: “Fweeyo na mafwarizeewu ninfuka, khi anakhiyoni awo ahisala afuka mwaasa wa niini?”
Yinsa khujipu yoori: “Enretteya toovi ofuka anamalaleyiwa harusi, namaposa ari attaapho? Zinlawa zafiye siikhu anttelaaye othuuliwa mposi, na siikhu zaya etthiipo anlawa afuke.
“Khina antthaaye yaapa ya tarapu pheeya kuwo ya raku, maana entta ofutthela kuwo etile evaruwe.
Wala khinthuliwa viinyu pheeya khutthiiwa nttompwiyo ya shapala ya raku, nooretta toowo entta ophutuwa, viinyu yiittikhe, ttompwiyo yaya eharipweye. Ila viinyu pheeya entthiwa nttompwiyo pheeya, na toowo zoopiiri zintta opweheya.”
Ettaka ottakhula etthiipile, khutavo nttunkhulu wa tiini, khunkokhorela na khumuuza yoori: “Mwanaka wankha afwa nasaapi ethiiti; nlawe wanttheele nkhono ontta osisimuwa.”
Yinsa khulankha khusala anlotta na anakhiyoni awe.
Attaaphale, aarivo muukha mmote aarina nyaakha khumi na miwiri emwiittikhaka taamu, khuta onyoko wa Yinsa khusapa ajapi yawe.
Maana ye eettiye ojilakelela yoori: “Kisaparu ajapi yawe paasi, kintta ovona.”
Azukuluwiyeevo Yinsa khumoona khumuuza yoori: “Ofurahi, mwanaka wankha; amini yawo yoovonisa. Wakathi otthuupule muukha otule khwiiya woovona”.
Afiiyeevo owawe nttunkhulu wa tiini khuwaasiila atthu eepaka liipo la miifwa na enkeene ari ootapanyeya,
Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Mwisaruwe! Otu khafweeni, ontta olala.” Ooshi khusala antheya.
Paata ya atthu apale osusa, ye khuvira khunkholela nkhono, khunlansa.
Hapari epile khumwazeyela nti opule wooshi.
Noolaavo aphale vaya, ananhooni awiri khusala anlotta akhuwaka araka: “Mwaana wa Daawuuda, noonele huruma!”
Yinsa noofiya owawe, ananhooni apale khumwaattama, ye khuwoozela yoori: “Mweeyo mwinkhupali yoori miiyo kinaaye owahi wa oretta epo zaya?” Yo khujipu yoori: “Ayo, Mbwana!”
Yinsa khuwaasapa maasho aya araka: “Erettikhane khwa matakhelo amini yenu!”
Maasho aya khwiiya oovona. Aphano Yinsa khuwooza na kuvu yoori: “Phoole ahiiyevo anttelaaye ojuwa epi.”
Yo khulawa, khumwaza hapari zawe epile nti opule wooshi.
Paata ya olaavo aphale, namasheethwani ahaari ottakhulaaye khutiiseliwa Yinsa.
Noomwiikara sheethwani otule, ye khwaaza ottakhula. Khuntti etile khwiiya yooshanka na khuri: “Khinarettikhane vitthu nkhama epi Ezirayiilu.
Ila mafwarizeewu aari olupa yoori: “Oniikara masheethwani khwa owahi wa mfwalume wa masheethwani.”
Yinsa aari weettetta sitati zooshi na mmwanttiwa. Ye aari osomisa mmasinakooka, na olaleya hapari monkoni wa ofwalume wa Nluku, na ovonisa wakhula nanna ya marati na moolwele mawulweene a atthu.
Paata ya woona khuntti zawaatta, khoonela huruma, maana zaari zoovelavela na zawanswiwa, nkhama pwittipwitthi zoohiina nshuki.
Aphano khuwooza anakhiyoni awe yoori: “Wuurula nwulweene, ila anakhaazi vattitthiiru.
Apho, mwinvekele Mweenyewe wuurula awaaperekhe anakhaazi a wuurula.”
Khuwaakhuwela anakhiyoni awe apale khumi na awiri, khuwenkha owahi wa wiikara masheethwani, na ovonisa moolwele na marati ooshi.
Apa mazina a anakhiyoni khumi na awiri: Wamwanzo, Simawu, anjuwaniwaaye nzina la Pheeturu, na ttwiiye Antere; Tiyaaku, mwaana wa Zepeteewu, na Yaahaya ttwiiye;
Filiipe na Paturumeewu; Tome na Matewuzhu, namariphisa lumpuru; Tiyaaku mwaana wa Alufeeyu, na Tadeewu;
Simawu Zelooti, na Yuuda Eshikariyoote, othuuto anzinkuliyeeyo.
Yinsa khuwaaruma apale khumi na awiri na khuwooza yoori: “Mwiheette wa amalapo, wala mwiheette hatha sitati moote ya a Samariiya.
Ila khapula mweettele pwittipwitthi zawaashikha za Ezirayiilu.
Wakhula vahali mwineettaavo, mwitafusiri hapari epi mwiraka: ‘Ofwalume wa pinkuuni ori kharipu!’
Mwiwaavonisaka anamarati, mwiwaasisimulaka ananfwa, mwiwaatwahareshaka anamaharaja, mwiikare masheethwani. Mweeyo mwapokhera mahala na mwina yawinkha mahala.
Mwihithuule hatha thahapu, wala feeta, wala khoopiri mmwizako mwenu;
Mwihithuule hatha kuwo kiina, wala jampali, wala pakhora, maana nakhaazi eninsuhi wiiyana etthu yoojiwa yawe.
Na wakhula sitati ama mmwanttiwa, mwimweekese ntthu woojishitahi, mwiikhale owawe othuuto mpakha malawelo enu.
Amana mwivira nnyupa, mwichelise.
Nkhama atthu a nyuupa etile eeya oosuhi, heeri yenu mweeyo yiiye vamote na-yo; amana ahisuhi, heeri yenu ti yuuruteleni.
Amana ntthu ahuupokherelini na khuhitakhi osiila mattakhuzi enu, mwitathe lifufu la mmoolu mwenu mwileemo nnyupa mwaya mphule ama nsitati mwaya mphule.
Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori, siikhu ya ophukiwa enttela wiiyavo tthakaraka khwa Sotooma na Komoora zayita sitati ya eto.
“Miiyo kinuurumani mweeyo nkhama pwittipwitthi vakatthi wa miiji; nakataalikha mwiiye alavilavi nkhama nyookha na oohiina zootakhala nkhama jiwa.
Mwiiyane phoole, maana atthu anlawa oottheni nnyupa woophukaniwamo na wuujaphani mmasinakooka mwaya.
Mwaasa wa miiyo, mwinlawa mwalawaniwe vakatthi wa misatoro na afwalume, yoori wiiye oshaahiti anttelaaye orumeyela, yo na amalapo monkoni wa hapari zaka.
Ila amana oofukelani, mwihishanke etthu yoolupa, ama yooretta. Wakathi aya opo, Nluku onttela owinkhani mattakhuzi olupa,
maana khahiyo mweeyo mwinttelaaye ottakhula, ila Rooho ya Papeenu ti enttelaaye ottakhula khwa mweeyo.
“Ttwi mmote onlawa anleve ttwiiye yoori ooliwe, na paapa onleva mwanawe; aana anlawa awaazukuluwele apapa zaya na awoole.
Atthu ooshi anttela owiinani mwaasa wa miiyo, ila otule anttelaaye ovilela mpakha mwiisho ontta wuusurukha.
Amana mwifiya nsitati khulupatthiwa, mwitthirele sitati kiina. Weekhweele miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori khamwinteela wiisha ozukulela Ezirayiilu yooshi Mwaana wa Pinaatamu ahiteeni.
“Nakhiyoni khaninziti mwaaliimu awe, wala karumeya khaninziti mbwana awe.
Nakhiyoni ona yoofurahi amana anfiyela mwaaliimu awe, na karumeya amana anfiyela mbwana awe. Moone, amana mweenyewe nyuupa attukhaniwa khutthajiwa Belezibuuli, khi ajamaaze khatepeeni!
“Nakataalikha mwihiwoove apo aya. Khayiivo yoottiyeleliwa ehinteelaaye othoonyeziwa wala yoovithiwa ehinteelaaye ojuwiwa.
Eti kiniwuuzaani n'yiiza mwilupe nthana. Na etile mwisiiliyeeyo sirini mwaamuuze vatulu wa nyuupa.
Mwihimoove otule anuulaaye mwiili, ahina owahi wa wuula nafusi. Khapula mwimoove otule anwahaaye otapanya mwiili na nafusi khweeselela motthooni.
Anyannyi awiri anuuzanyiwa nzurukhu mmote, ila khina mmote ankwelaaye vathi Papeenu ahitakheeni.
Hatha nyuuli za mmwishwa mwenu zooshi pi za waalakiwa.
Nakataalikha mwihoove! Mweeyo mwinaaye fwayita zayita anyannyi.
“Wakhula otule antukhurwaaye yoori ti waka vakatthi wa atthu, na miiyo kintukhuru khwa ye, vakatthi wa Paapa ariiye pinkuuni.
Ila otule anikikatthalaaye vakatthi wa atthu, na miiyo kinttela onkatthala vakatthi wa Paapa ariiye pinkuuni.
“Mwihaakanyere yoori miiyo katiisa heeri voolumwenku; akitiseeni heeri, katiisa phanka.
Miiyo kata yoori oomane mwaana na papaawe, mwaana wankha na mamaawe, namaraliwa na nkhwewe.
Maatuwi khaamili a ntthu anlankha vakatthi wa ajamaaze.
Otule animphetaaye mamaawe ama papaawe zayita miiyo khansuhi wiiya namalottela aka; otule animphetaaye mwanawe zayita miiyo, khansuhi wiiya namalottela aka.
Otule ahinvikelaaye nsalapa awe akilotta, khansuhi wiiya namalottela aka.
Otule aneekesaaye ohaayi awe ontta omwaashikha, na otule onimwaashikhaaye ohaayi awe mwaasa wa miiyo ontta opattha.
“Wakhula otule anuupwekherelaanini akipwekherela miiyo, na otule anikipwekherelaaye ampwekherela otule akirumiyeeyo.
Otule animpwekherelaaye napiyu mwaasa wa ye wiiya napiyu, ompwekhera tthuvo ya napiyu; otule animpwekherelaaye nashariya mwaasa wa ye wiiya nashariya, ompwekhera tthuvo ya nashariya.
Na wakhula otule animwinkhaaye nsimaana hatha nkhama koopho ya maati oozizima, mwaasa wa ye wiiya nakhiyoni aka, kiniwuuza khweele yoori oto aya onlawa apwekhere tthuvo yawe.”
Paata ya wiisha owaanozela anakhiyoni awe khumi na awiri, Yinsa khusala alawa osomisa na otafusiri sitati za Kalileya.
Yaahaya, paata ya osiila ari nkalapooso vitthu aari orettaazo Al-Masiihu, khuwaaruma anakhiyoni awe olawa omuuzela yoori:
“Ti weeyo otule aari weettelaaye ota, ama nimweekesele nkina?”
Yinsa khuwaajipu araka: “Mwiruti mwamuuze Yaahaya epi mwinsiilaaye na mwinoonaaye:
Ananhooni anoona, anamarakala aneettetta, anamaharaja antta otwahareshiwa, ananhisiili ansiila, ananfwa ansisimuwa, na hapari zooshapweya antafusireliwa asikhini.
Ooparikhiyiwa pi apale ahinikoonanaaye hatha etthu ya owaakwakwanttula.”
Aphano noolaavo anakhiyoni apale a Yaahaya, Yinsa khusala oozela khuntti etile monkoni wa Yaahaya yoori: “Mweetteliye woona-ni n'yaara? Tteketthe yiinisiwaka ti pheevo?
Ama, mweetteliye omoona ntthu awaliye kuwo zooshapweya? Moone, apale anwaalaaye kuwo zooshapweya aniikhala mmanyupa wa afwalume!
Nka khuuzeni, mweetteliye woona niini? Napiyu? Wekhweele, miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori anziti napiyu.
Otu ti otule yaatikhiweeyo monkoni wa ye yoori: ‘Moone, kinlawa kamperekhe karumeya aka omaasho wawo; yoori atthenkeze tarikhi yawo.’
Kiniwuuzani khweele yoori: Khwa aana ooshi avokoliweeyo ti aakha, khapuweenivo hatha mmote wonziti Yaahaya Namoosa. Ila woopushuwa muufwalume wa pinkuuni nwulweene zayita ye.
Waaza siikhu za Yaahaya Namoosa mpakha leelo, Ofwalume wa pinkuuni ontta woojopholiwa, apo aya anjopholaaye anthuula.
Maana Manapiyu ooshi na Kano za Munsa za ahupiri mpakha yenzi ya Yaahaya.
Na amana mwitakha okhupalela, ye ti Aliyaasi otule aari weettelaaye ota.
Otule ariina mashiilo ti asiile!
“Khapila eti kilattanisane niini? Enlattanana asimaana eekhaliye va parasa eettaka osheza na onyakula na ashirikha aya:
‘Fweeyo noovumiselani kuruneetha, ila mweeyo khuhiini; khwiipa liipo la huzuni, ila mweeyo khuhilili.’
Khuta Yaahaya woofuka na ahinnywaaye viinyu, mweeyo mwinri: ‘Ye onaaye masheethwani!’
Ata Mwaana wa Pinaatamu anjaaye na annywaaye, mwinri: ‘Otu nsokho na nnywachi, nshirikha wa anamariphisa lumpuru na anatwampi.’ Ila ojuwa onthoonyezeya khwa khaazi onikholeliwaaye.”
Aphano Yinsa khwaaza omaruwela sitati epile aviriyeemo khurettamo minjuza zawe zawaatta, maana atthu aari wiikhalaamo khathupwiyiye.
“Phoole weeyo, Korazini! Phoole, weeyo Betezayiita! Maana eriwaka Tiiru na Sitooni zeettiye orettiwawo minjuza epi mwiretteliweeyo mweeyo, apale aniikhalaaye ottuukho nka athupwiye raku, khuwala saakhu na khujivaaza fuutha!
Ila miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori siikhu ya ophukiwa enteela wiiyavo tthakaraka khwa Tiiru na Sitooni zayita mweeyo.
Khi weeyo Kafwaranaawu, onttela oweziwa mpakha pinkuuni? Wala, weeyo onttela weeseleliwa motthooni! Eriwaka minjuza zirettiweeyo vakatthi vawo zeettiye orettiwa Sotooma, zaari weettela opharelela mpakha leelo.
Ila miiyo kiniwuuza yoori siikhu ya ophukiwa enteela wiiyavo tthakaraka khwa Sotooma zayita weeyo.”
Wakathi otthuupule Yinsa khulupa yoori: “Miiyo kinuusifu Paapa, Mbwana wa pinkuuni na vathi, maana weeyo wawaavithela vitthu epi ajuwi na asomi, na khuwaathoonyeza apa attiitthi.
Khweele, Paapa, ti nanna waatakhiyeezo.
Vitthu zooshi kenkhiwa ti Paapa. Khina aninjuwaaye Mwaana woohiiyi Paapa, na khina aninjuwaawe Paapa woohiiyi Mwaana na otule mwaana anintakhelaaye yoori anthoonyeze.
Mwikiteele miiyo mooshi mweeyo mwiiyiye ooshokhera na oolemeliwa, miiyo kintta wuuvumulisani.
Mwithuule tthentte yaka na mwikeezele, maana miiyo kiwoonyamala na woojipushuwisa nroho, mweeyo mwintta opattha ovumula wa nafusi zenu.
Maana tthentte yaka ti yookhweya na mapwattha aka pi ooveya.”
Wakathi otthuupule Yinsa khusala avira mmashapa wa tiriku, siikhu ya saapatu. Anakhiyoni awe khuwaakhola jala, yo khwaaza okathula misasi za tiriku arafunaka phunje zaya.
Mafwarizeewu nawoona epile zaya, khumuuza Yinsa yoori: “Owoone anakhiyoni awo anretta etthu ekhattaziweeyo orettiwa saapatu.”
Ye khujipu araka: “Mweeyo khamwisomeeni etthu arettiyeeyo Daawuuda wakathi ye na ashirikha awe aakholiweeyo jala?
Ye eettiye Nnyupa ya Nluku, khurafuna phaawu na ashirikha awe enkhiweeyo Nluku, etthu yahaari otakhisiwaaye orettiwa, ila aariina ruhusa yooretta aari mahaakhimu a tiini paasi.
Ama mweeyo khamwisomeeni nkano za Munsa yoori saapatu, anamalokozela a tiini aavonyiye kano Nnyupa Woosifwiwamo, siikhu yaya eto, ila khuhiina hatha paathuli?
Miiyo kiniwuuza yoori apha ata otu azitiyeeyo Nyuupa Yoosifwiwamo.
Ila eriwaka mweeyo mwaari ojuwa maana a mattakhuzi anraaye: ‘Kintakha huruma akintakha twaha,’ khamwaari onhukhumu ntthu ahina paathuli.
Maana Mwaana wa Pinaatamu Mbwana wa saapatu.”
Khulaavo aphale vaya khweetta nsinakooka yaaya atthaapale.
Nttumphule aarimo mwinyi mmote woorakala nkhono. Aphano atthu akina aari otakhaaye onlokoveza Yinsa yoori: “Ti ya halaali monkoni wa kano ovonisa saapatu?”
Ye khuwaajipu yoori: “Paani wa mweeyo, amana eeyana pwittipwitthi yawe ekwela valiphotto saapatu, ahinlawaaye okhola alazavo?
Ntthu ona fwayita khuluyeene zayita pwittipwitthi! Nakhataalikha ewaapho ruhusa yooretta etthu yooshapweya saapatu.”
Aphano khumuuza mwinyi otule yoori: “Wookole nkhono awo.” Ye khookola, khuvonisiwa, khwiiya sawasawa na opu nkina.
Ila mafwarizeewu apale khusaruwa khusala awaza shawuri za omuula Yinsa.
Yinsa noojuwa shawuri zaya epile, khulaawo okhule waya. Atthu enkeene khusala anlotta, ye khuwaavonisa alwele ooshi aariivo vakatthi wa atthu aya apale,
na khuwooza yoori ahilupe hatha etthu monkoni wa ye.
Eto yaarettikhaniye yoori eretteye etile yaalupiweeyo ti napiyu Ezaaya yoori:
“Otu ari apha karumeya aka, kinthawuliyeeyo, mphetani aka, anfurahisaaye rooho yaka, kanttheela nafusi yaka, ye onteela olaleya ophukiwa wa atthu ooshi.
Khanteela okeetisana wala onyakula, khina anttelaaye osiila huula yawe mmatarikhi.
Khanteela ovuja tteketthe yoomanyeya, wala khanteela ozimisa mweeke wootthuwela, mpakha athuule oshintta khwa shariya.
Amalapo ooshi anttela wiiyana nroromelo khwa nzina lawe.”
Paata ya toowo, khutiiseliwa namasheethwani woohooni na khaari ottakhula, Yinsa khunvonisa, khwaaza woona na ottakhula.
Atthu ooshi khwiiya ooshanka channu khusala oozelana yoori: “Khahi mwaana wa Daawuuda otu?”
Mafwarizeewu akina noosiila toowo khuri: “Otu oniikara masheethwani paasi khwa owahi wa Belezibuuli, mfwalume wa masheethwani.”
Aphano Yinsa noojuwa etthu aari wuupuwelaaye yo, khuwooza yoori: “Wakhula ofwalume wa waawanyeya khusala wuumana otthuuporu oniiya wootapanyeya, na wakhula sitati ama nyuupa yawaawanyeya ethiitoru khiniiyavo.
Nkhama Epiliisi onimwiikara Epiliisi, eetta ojaawanya otthweru. Toowo ofwalume awe onteela wiiyavo toovi?
Nkhama miiyo kiniikara masheethwani khwa owahi wa Belezibuuli, khi aaneenu aniikara toovi? Tiito aaneenu atthaapo ti anttelaaye wuuphukani mweeyo.
Ila nkhama kiniikara masheethwani khwa Rooho ya Nluku, eto enthoonyeza yoori Ofwalume wa Nluku woofiyelani.
“Ama ntthu onvira toovi nnyupa wa nwali khuthuulamo maali zawe ahaazeeni khapula onfuka? Toowo phi oniwahaavo wiiya vitthu za nnyupa mwawe.
“Otule ahi vamote na miiyo ontta okuumanana, na otule ahinkusanyaaye khwa miiyo ontta omwaza.
Etthiipo miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori: Twampi na kufuru zooshi za anaatamu zinswamihiwa, ila okufurwela Rooho Ttakatthiifu khunswamihiwa.
Wakhula otule anlupaaye nttakhuzi la omuumanana Mwaana wa Pinaatamu onswamihiwa, ila otule anttakhulaaye wawuumananavo Rooho Ttakatthiifu khanswamihiwa, waaza nasaapi eti mpakha okhu ninttaawo.
“Muutthi wooshapweya oniima mishumo zooshapweya, muutthi wootakhala oniima mishumo zootakhala, maana wakhula muutthi onjuwiwa khwa mishumo zaya.
Ojama wa nyookha, enretteya mweeyo ootakhala rooho, ottakhula vitthu zooshapweya? Maana milomo enttakhula etile eniiyaaye varoho.
Ntthu wooshapweya rooho, mmujuju mwawe ensarulamo vitthu zooshapweya, wootakhala rooho mmujuju mwawe ensarulamo vitthu zootakhala.
Ila miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori, siikhu ya ophukiwa, atthu anlawa arettiwe hisapu mwaasa wa mattakhuzi ooshi ohiina fwayita aari olupakaaye.
Maana khwa mattakhuzi enu mwinteela wonkokha na khwa atthaapo mwinteela ohukhumwiwa.”
Aphano mafwarizeewu akina na anamanozela a kano khulupa yoori: “Mwaaliimu, nintakha woona alama ya minjuza yoorettiwa ti weeyo.”
Ye khujipu araka: “Khapila yootakhala na yooraruwa enveka alama ya minjuza, ila khinteela winkhiwa hatha moote ya ohiiyi alama ya napiyu Yuunusa.
Maana nkhama etthiipo Yuunusa ekhaliyeeyo siikhu ttatthu nthana na osikhu mmatthupo wa swi, khwa etthiipo Mwaana wa Pinaatamu onttela wiikhala siikhu ttatthu nkhapuri.
Atthu a Neniive anlawa alankhe siikhu ya ophukiwa, ookwiseleni paathuli mweeyo, maana yo athupwiya twampi zaya paata ya osiila tafusiiri ya Yuunusa, na aphano ori apha otule eeyiyeeyo nwulweene zayita Yuunusa.
N'hano wa Kusini onlawa alankhe siikhu ya ophukiwa ookwiseleni paathuli mweeyo, maana ye alankha peetiwene oteela osiila ojuwa wa Seleyimaana, ila nasaapi otu ariiye apha anziti Seleyimaana.
“Amana sheethwani anlawa ntthu, onvira nhali woohiimo maati eekesaka vahali woovumulavo, ila amana ahipatthivo.
Aphano onri: ‘Kinrutela nyuupa ethiitile kilankhiyeeyo.’ Noofiya khusikana nyuupa eheettiweenimo, ori wooseeliwamo wawaattaleliwamo saana.
Ontta oruti khulawa khuwaatana masheethwani sapa ootepa otakhala, khweettamo khusala eekhala nttumpho, ntthu otule khweetta wootepa khuziti khiima etile aariyeeyo raku. Na enttela orettikhana etthiipo khwa khapila eti.”
Yinsa nalelo eettaka ottakhula na khuntti etile, mamaawe na attwiize aarettiye ari vaje, antakhaka yoori anttakhulane.
Ntthu mmote khumuuza yoori: “Mamaawo na attwiizo ari vaje antakha ottakhulana weeyo.”
Ye khujipu yoori: “Maama ti paani? Wala attwiizaku ti paani”?
Khookolela nkhono awe phantte ya anakhiyoni awe khulupa araka: “Maama na attwiizaku pi apa ariiye apha.
Maana otule anrettaaye matakhelo a Paapa ariiye pinkuuni, oto ti ttwiiyaku, nlupwaaka na ti maama.”
Siikhu ethiitile Yinsa khulankha owawe khulawa nshini wa ntthatta.
Khuzukuleliwa pi atthu awaatta, aphano ye khupakhira mmwaatiya khwiikhala. Atthu apale khweemela vapatari.
Ye khusala awaasomisa khwa milikaniso, araka: “Namalima aalawiiye ozala.
Amwazaka peewu yawe, phantte kiina khukwela nshini wa tarikhi, anyannyi khuta khuja.
Kiina khukwela vahali aariivo mawe, vahali laarivo nttophe vattitthiiru; nasaapiru khoottha, ila wiiya nttophe ntthile khaleechiye.
Aphano noopuwa njuwa khulukula na khuuma; maana khazaarina mitathaari.
Peewu kinoko khukwela vanyiiwa, khuwula vamote na nyiiwa, khurapeliwa pi nyiiwa.
Kiina khukwela vanshaka wooshapweya, khwiima mishumo zooshapweya, miiya, mikina siithiini na talaathiini wakhula mmote!
Otule ariina mashiilo ti asiile.”
Anakhiyoni awe khunsusela khumuuzela yoori: “Mwaasa aya niini atthu apa owaattakhulelaka khwa milikaniso?”
Ye khuwaajipu: “Mweeyo mwenkhiwa ojuwa siiri za Ofwalume wa pinkuuni, ila yo wala.
Maana, otule ariina, onttela winkhiwa, oniiyana zawaatta. Ila otule ahina,hatha etile ariinaaye ontta onyakanyiwa.
Tiito miiyo kiniwoozaaye khwa milikaniso: maana yo ana maasho ila khanoona, ana mashiilo ila khansiila, na wala khiniweeleya.
Khwa yo wamariseleya ohupiri wa Ezaaya onlupaaye yoori: ‘Hatha nkhama mwasiila khiniweeleyani; hatha nkhama moona khamwinjuwa.
Maana rooho za atthu apa pi zookhijili, attiyela mashiilo aya na khuphunya maasho aya, eriwaka khayaari ethiito, aari owahi woona na maasho aya, na osiila na mashiilo aya na oweeleya va rooho vaya khurutela mmakhono mwaka, keetta owaavonisa.’
Ila ooparikhiyiwa maasho enu mweeyo, maana anoona; na maashiilo enu, maana ansiila.
Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori: manapiyu enkeene na anashariya aatakhiye woona epi mwinoonaazo, ila khuhooni, na osiila epi mwinsiilaazo ila khuhisiili.
“Nakataalikha mwisiile na mwijuwe maana a nlikaniso wa namazala:
Amana ntthu asiila nttakhuzi la Ofwalume khuhimweeleyi, Ntakhali ti antaaye khulazavo etile yaazaliweeyo nroho mwawe. Eto peewu etile yaakweliyeeyo nshini wa tarikhi.
Etile yaakweliyeeyo vahali aariivo mawe pi apale ansiilaaye nttakhuzi nasaapiru khupokherela na furaha.
Ila mwaasa wa ohiina mitathaari eenyeweru, anlipalipa khwa wakathi vattitthiiru. Amana epuwelela miswipa ama lupattha mwaasa wa nttakhuzi la Ofwalume anlikha nasaapiru amini yaya.
Etile yaakweliyeeyo va nyiiwa, pi apale ansiilaaye nttakhuzi, ila mwaasa wa tafwawuthi za ohaayi, na ottettekha wa maali entta owaakhupa, ahifiyelelaka wiima mishumo.
Ila etile yaakweliyeeyo vahali wooshapweyavo pi apale ansiilaaye nttakhuzi khuweeleya, khwiima mishumo miiya, khwiima siithiini, talaathiini khwa muutthi mmote.”
Yinsa khuwooza nlikaniso nkina araka: “Ofwalume wa pinkuuni ori nkhama ntthu mmote azaliyeeyo peewu yooshapweya mmashapa mwawe.
Osikhu mmote, atthu ooshi eettaka olala, khuta atuwi vakatthi wa tiriku khuzalavo ntakhatakha, khulawa.
Wakathi tiriku ewuliyeevo khupuwa misaasi zaya, naye ntakhatakha khupuwa misaasi zaya.
“Akarumeya a mweenyewe nshapa khulawa wa mweenyewe khumuuza yoori: ‘Mbwana, mweeyo mwaazaliye peewu yooshapweya mmashapa mwenu. Khi aphano ntakhatakha lapuwa vayi?’
Ye khujipu yoori: ‘Atuwi ti arettiye epo zaya.’ Akarumeya apale khumuuzela yoori: ‘Mbwana mwintakha fweeyo nalazemo?’
Ye khujipu yoori: ‘Wala, maana, amana mwikhulakamo ntakhatakha nttho, mwintta okhula vamote na tiriku.
Mwilikhe ziwulele vamote mpakha wakathi wa wuurula. Kintta owooza anamuurula yoori: “Mwikusanye khapula ntakhatakha mwifuke mashittha likhoziwe; mwikusanye tiriku mwitthe va sakafu vaka.’”
Na khuwooza nlikaniso nkina araka: “Ofwalume wa pinkuuni ori nkhama phunje ya samuli, ntthu anthulaaye khuzala mmashapa mwawe.
Eto ttiitthiiru zayita peewu zooshi, amana owula onziti miitthi zooshi za mmashapa, anta anyannyi ojeka vijaaro n'virapi mwaya.”
Khuwooza nlikaniso nkina araka: “Ofwalume wa pinkuuni ori nkhama fwaramento muukha anthuulaaye khuphakanya na ofu wa tiriku wa waatta, wooshi khujakhuwa.
Yinsa aari wuuza khuntti etile, khwa nlikaniso. Weekhweele, khina etthu moote aari owoozaaye woohiiyi khwa nlikaniso.
Eto yaari orettikhana yoori eretteye etile yaalupiweeyo ti napiyu yoori: “Kinteela ofunula milomo zaka khwa nlikaniso, na olaleya vitthu zoovitheya waaza wumpiwa wa olumwenku.”
Aphano ye khuwaalikha atthu apale khulawa owawe. Anakhiyoni awe khumwaattama khunvekela yoori: “Oneeleze nlikaniso wa ntakhatakha.”
Ye khujipu yoori: “Otule aazaliyeeyo peewu wooshapweya ti Mwaana wa Pinaatamu.
Nshapa olumwenku, peewu yooshapweya aana a Muufwalume. Ntakhatakha aana a sheethwani.
Atuwi aazaliyeemo ti sheethwani. Wuurula, mwiisho wa wakathi, akarumeya a wuurula malayikha.
Nkhama etthiipo ntakhatakha linuuruliwaazo khukhoziwa va moottho, enttela wiiya etthiipo mwiisho wa olumwenku.
Mwaana wa Pinaatamu onttela oruma malayikha awe, alazemo muufwalume mwawe zooshi epile zookwakwanttula, na apale anrettaaye vitthu zootakhala.
Aweeselele va njocho la moottho, attaapho onttela wiiyavo olila na oluma meeno.
Aphano anashariya anttela waara nkhama njuwa muufwalume wa Papaaya. Ariina mashiilo, ti asiile.”
Ofwalume wa pinkuuni ori nkhama njuju loovithiwa mmashapa. Ntthu mmote, khulawa khusikana, na ye khuvitha opheya. Mwaasa woofurahi khulawa khuuzanyisa vitthu zawe zooshi aarinaazo khuuzanya nshapa ntthile.
Theenya Ofwalume wa pinkuuni ori nkhama nakusiyanti aneekesaaye mawe ootafikhana.
Noosikana liwe la fwayita khuluyeene, khuuzanyisa vitthu zooshi aariinaazo khuuzanya.”
“Ofwalume wa pinkuuni ori nkhama ntthavi laweesiwa mpahari khuula wakhula jaati ya swi.
Amana liitaala, anamajiya anfutthela vathi. Aphano yo khukusanya swi epile zooshapweya khuttha mmakapaja, ila epile zoohishapweyi khweesela.
Enttela orettikhana etthiipo mwiisho wa olumwenku. Malayikha anteela owaaphakula ootakhala rooho na anashariya,
aweeselele va njocho la moottho apale ootakhala rooho, attaapho onttela wiiyavo olila na oluma meeno.”
Aphano Yinsa khuwoozela yoori: “Zaweeleyani vitthu zooshi kilupiyeeyo?” Yo khujipu yoori: “Aaa!”
Ye khuwooza yoori: “Tiito wakhula namanozela a kano anozeliweeyo monkoni wa Ofwalume wa pinkuuni onlattanana mweenyewe nyuupa anlazaavo va njuju vawe vitthu pheeya na vitthu zaraku.”
Paata ya Yinsa wiisha olupa milikaniso epile, khulaawo okhule waya.
Khufiya sitati yawe, ohali aari wiikhalaawo. Ye khwaaza owaasomisa atthu nsinakooka. Atthu ooshi khwiiya ooshankisiwa, khusala oozela yoori: “Ojuwa opu apattha vayi na owahi wa oretta minjuza?
Khahi mwaana wa kalapinteero? Nzina la mamaawe khahi Mariyamu? Attwiize khayi Tiyaaku, Yuusufu, Simawu na Yuuda?
Alupuwe ooshi khaniikhala nttumphu? Khi vitthu epi apattha vayi?”
Atthu ooshi khuhinkhupali. Ila ye khulupa yoori: “Napiyu ti wooshitahiwa phantte zooshi, ila mmuti mwawe na owawe khanshitahiwa.”
Yinsa khaarettiye minjuza zawaatta mmuti mphule, maana yo khaarina amini.
Wakathi aya opule Herooti Antiipa, nsatoro wa Kalileya, khusiila olupiwa monkoni wa Yinsa.
Ye khuwooza akarumeya awe yoori: “Oto ti Yaahaya Namoosa; eetta osisimuwa muufwa! Tiito ariinaaye owahi wa oretta minjuza.”
Maana aarettiye Herooti antthiiye Yaahaya nkalapooso, mwaasa wa Herotiiya, muukha wa Filiipe, ttwiiye,
mwaasa wa Yaahaya omuuza yoori: “Khahi halaali weeyo onrala ye.”
Herooti aari otakha omuula, ila khusala awoova atthu, maana yo aari ojuwa yoori Yaahaya napiyu.
Va njampo la oretta mwaakha Herooti, mwaana wa Herotiiya khwiina vakatthi wa atthu ooshi, khuntuvelisa Herooti,
ye khumwaahiti khwa olapha omwinkha wakhula etile aari weettelaaye onvekela.
Khwa shawuri za winkhiwa ti mamaawe, mwaana otule khulupa yoori: “Mwikitiisele mparathu eeshwa ya Yaahaya Namoosa.”
Mfwalume khwiiya wooshukulikha, ila mwaasa wa olapha na mwaasa wa anamalaleyiwa, ye khuruma yoori enkhiwe etile mwaana otule avekiyeeyo.
Khuruma olawa oshijiwa eeshwa ya Yaahaya Namoosa nkalapooso.
Eeshwa yawe khuthuuliwa mparathu khulawa khwinkhiwa mwaana otule, ye khuthuula khulawa khumwinkha mamaawe
Anakhiyoni a Yaahaya khuta, khuthuula mwiili awe khulawa khuzikha. Nawiisha khulawa onthatelela Yinsa.
Noosiila vitthu zaarettikhaniyeezo, Yinsa khupakhira mmwaatiya khulaawo okhule waya, khweetta ohali yaariiwo yaara otthwe. Ila atthu noojuwa, khulankha nsitati mphule khusala anlottelela mwentto.
Yinsa noopakhuwa khuwoona atthu awaatta, khuwoonela huruma, khuwaavonisa alwele aariivo.
Njuwa-looveva, anakhiyoni awe khunsusela khumuuza yoori: “Mphu n'yaara na ontta oripa. Owaamwaze atthu apa eette mmamuti mpho oozanye etthu yoojiwa.”
Yinsa khuwaajipu araka: “Khinihithajiya yo olawa. Mweeyo ena mwiwenkhe etthu yoojiwa.”
Yo khulupa yoori: “Fweeyo ninaaye phaawu thaanu na swi piiri.”
Aphano ye khulupa yoori: “Mwikitiisele.”
Khuruma yoori atthu apale eekhale va nyaani, khuthuula phaawu epile thaanu na swi epile piiri, khweekesa otulu, khuparikhiya. Khumeya phaawu epile. Khuwenkha anakhiyoni awe, yo khusala awenkha atthu.
Ooshi khuja khurupala, anakhiyoni khulokotthela khelenke khumi na piiri nyeenye zoosala.
Atthu aajiyeeyo aari alume alufu thaanu, ohiwaatthiimo aakha na asimaana.
Nasaapiru Yinsa khuwaaruma anakhiyoni awe yoori apakhire mmwaatiya alokoze eette phantte kiina, ye aasaliye awaaleezaka atthu apale.
Paata ya owaaleeza atthu, khuwela va mwaako olawa olompa. Khuripa ye ari attaaphale otthwe,
ila wakathi aya opule mwaatiya waari peetiwene na vathi, weettaka opiiwa ti mawipi venkivene maana pheevo eetta wiinyula.
Lifwajiri, Yinsa khusala eetta attaaphale aarivo anakhiyoni awe eettettaka vatulu a maati.
Noomoona eettaka weettetta vatulu a maati yo khwiiya oosuthuwa khulupa yoori: “Opu nshitapehe!” Yo khusala anyakula na woova.
Ila Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Mwiminyale! Ti miiyo. Mwihoove!”
Khujipu Pheeturu yoori: “Nkhama ti weeyo khweele Mbwana, okirume kite attaapho oriivo, keettettaka vatulu a maati.”
Yinsa khunjipu, araka: “Ote.” Aphano Pheeturu khulaamo mmwaatiya, khusala eettetta vatulu a maati eettaka phantte etile aariiwo Yinsa.
Paata ya woona khiima pheevo etile yaari ovumaazo, khoova khusala azama vattiitthi-vattiitthi, ettaka onyakula araka: “Mbwana, okuusuru!”
Nasaapiru Yinsa khookola nkhono awe khunkholelela. Khumuuza yoori: “Ntthu woopushuwa amini, ohaaminaka mwaasa aya niini?”
Paata ya owela mmwaatiya, pheevo etile khwiisha.
Apale aari mmwaatiya khumwaaputu alupaka yoori: “Khweele weeyo o Mwaana wa Nluku.”
Paata ya olokha pahari, khufiya Jenezare.
Wakathi atthu a mmuti mphule anjuwiyeevo yoori ti Yinsa, khumwazela hapari mmuti mphule wooshimo, atthu akina khusala awaatana alwele.
Anvekelaka yoori nenkawu asape nshaka la ajapi yawe; ooshi asapiyeeyo aavoniye.
Aphano khulankha Yeruzaleemu, Mafwarizeewu akina na anamanozela a kano khuta omuuzela Yinsa yoori:
“Mwaasa aya niini anakhiyoni awo akhijilelaka zowera za attunkhulu a tiini, oja ahinaweeni?”
Yinsa khuwaajipu araka: “Mwaasa aya niini mweeyo mwikhijilelaka kano za Nluku, mwaasa wa zowera zenu?
Maana Nluku alupa yoori: ‘Onshitahi papaawo na mamaawo’ na ‘antakhaaye onlaani papaawe na mamaawe ona ya ohukhumweliwa ofwa.’
Ila mweeyo mwinkhupalela yoori amana ntthu amuuza papaawe ama mamaawe yoori: ‘Wakhula etthu kiniwinkhaanini miiyo zaakha ya omwinkha Nluku;
ye khankhanyareliwa theenya onshitahi papaawe khwa nanna nkhama eto.’ Khwa etthiipo, mwaasa wa zowera zenu, mweeyo mwimpeepheyisa nttakhuzi la Nluku.
Manaafikhi! Ezaaya ahupiri saaneene monkoni wa mweeyo araka:
‘Atthu apa anikaaputu na milomo, ila rooho zaya ziri peetiwene khwa miiyo.
Mweeyo mwinikaaputu mahala, mwisomisaka zowera za anaatamu.’”
Yinsa khuwaakhuwela atthu apale khuwooza yoori: “Mwisiile na eweeleyeni.
Khahiyo etile entthiwaaye nkhanyo eninharamushaaye ntthu; ila etile enlankhaaye nkhanyo ti eninharamushaaye.”
Aphano anakhiyoni awe khulawa khumwaattama khumuuzela yoori: “Wajuwa yoori mafwarizeewu noosiila hapari epile eephiriwa?”
Yinsa khuwaajipu yoori: “Miitthi zooshi zihizaliweeni ti Paapa wa pinkuuni zinttela okhuliwa na mitathaari zaya.
Mwiwaalikhe, maana yo khanoona na aniweettettisa ananhooni. Amana ntthu woohooni amweettettisa nahooni nzaawe ooshi antta okwela nliphotto.”
Aphano Pheeturu khunvekela Yinsa yoori: “Onuuze maana a nlikaniso opo.”
Yinsa khuwaajipu yoori: “Kiri na mweeyo nalelo khiniweeleyani?
Yoori zooshi zintthiwaaye nkhanyo zineetta mwiijohojoho na khunyiwa?
Ila vitthu zinlankhaaye nkhanyo zinlankha va rooho na piitthiipo eninharamushaaye pinaatamu.
Maana nroho ti zinlankhaamo shawuri zootakhala nkhama epi: wuula, oraruwa, oshawi akhapa, wiiya, olokova na ohankawaani.
Epo pi eninharamushaaye ntthu. Ila oja ohinaweeni khininharamusha ntthu.”
Paata ya Yinsa olaavo aphale vaya, khusala alawa nti wa Tiiro na Sitooni.
Muukha wa Kanaani aari wiikhalaaye nti otthuupule, khuta okutthanana Yinsa eettaka okhuwa yoori: “Mbwana, Mwaana wa Daawuuda, koonele huruma! Mwanaka etta wiiyana masheethwani na ontta ohoowa channu.”
Ila Ye khuhinjipu hatha nttakhuzi, anakhiyoni awe khulupa yoori: “Omuuze alawe, ontta onyakula nyuma wetthu.”
Yinsa khujipu yoori: “Miiyo kaperekhiwa paasi khwa pwittipwitthi epile zawaashikha za Ezirayiilu.”
Muukha otule khuta khukokhora na khuri: “Mbwana, okaawuni!”
Aphano Yinsa ajipwaka khuri: “Khahiyo yooshapweya othuula phaawu ya aana khuwenkha aana aanapwa.”
Muukha otule khujipu yoori: “Khweele Mbwana, ila na aana aanapwa anja tathela zinkwaaye vameeza wa mweenyewe.”
Aphano Yinsa khumuuza yoori: “Oo muukha, amini yawo khuluyeene! Ti erettikhane etile ontakhaaye.” Na wakathi otthuupule mwanawe khwiiya woovona.
Yinsa khulaawo okhule waya khulawa mpakha nshini wa pahari ya Kalileya. Khuwela va mwaako khwiikhala attaapho.
Khusala ata atthu awaatta, awaatanaka anamarakala, ananhooni, anamakhumuwa, ananhittakhuli na akinoko aya, khuwaalikha nshini wa Yinsa, ye khuwaavonisa.
Atthu khwiiya ooshanka wakathi awooniyeevo ananhittakhuli eettaka ottakhula, anamarakala ari oovona, anamakhumuwa eettaka weettetta na ananhooni eettaka woona. Yo khunsifu Nluku wa Ezirayiilu.
Yinsa khuwaakhuwela anakhiyoni awe na khuwooza yoori: “Kinaaye tthakaraka na atthu apa; zavira siikhu ttatthu ari vamote na miiyo na khana hatha etthu-yoojiwa. Akintakha owaalikha olawa na jala zaya, maana kinoona yoori antta ozileya ntarikhi.”
Anakhiyoni awe khujipu yoori: “Ninttela opattha vayi phaawu zoofiyela, atthu apa waatta na mphu n'yaara?”
Ye khuwoozela yoori: “Mwina phaawu kavi?” Yo khujipu yoori: “Sapa, na mattaatta vattitthiiru.”
Yinsa khuruma yoori atthu apale eekhale.
Khuthuula phaawu epile sapa na swi khushukhurwela khumeya khuwenkha anakhiyoni awe, khusala awaawanyeza atthu.
Ooshi khuja khurupala. Anakhiyoni apale khukusanya khelenke sapa za pattaasu zasaliyeeyo.
Atthu aajiyeeyo aari alufu nne, ohiwaalaki aakha na asimaana.
Paata ya oleezanana atthu apale, Yinsa khupakhira mmwaatiya khulokhela nti wa Makata.
Mafwarizeewu na masatukhi khumwaattama Yinsa khusala amweeza anvekelaka alama moote yoolankha pinkuuni.
Ye khuwaajipu araka: “Amana njuwa liveva, mweeyo mwinraka, ‘Onttela wiiya wakathi wooshapweya, maana pinku ti yookhuttuwa.’
Na leelo supu, ‘Enttela opuwa pheevo, maana pinku ti yookhuttuwa na eetaalawo mawiku.’ Mweeyo mwinjuwa otaphulela nanna ya pinku, ila khamwinjuwa otaphulela alama za wakathi!
Khapila yootakhala na yooraruwa anveka alama ya minjuza, ila hatha alama khanlawa winkhiwa yoohiiyi alama ya Yuunusa.” Aphano Yinsa khuwaalikha khulaavo aphale vaya.
Paata ya olokhela phantte kiina ya pahari, anakhiyoni khusophela yoori asahawu othuula phaawu.
Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Mwiiye wa woona na mwiiyane phoole na fwaramento za mafwarizeewu na za masatukhi.”
Anakhiyoni apale khwaaza onyakulisana atthaaporu, araka “mwaasa aya ohithuuli phaawu.”
Asiiliyeevo onyakulisana opule, Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Atthu oopushuwa amini, mwaasa aya niini mwinnyakulisana mweeyena-ru? Mwaasa woohiina phaawu?
Nalelo khina weeleyeni? Khamwimfikhirela phaawu epile thaanu miiyo kawaawanyeziyeeyo atthu alufu thaanu? Khelenke kavi mweetaaziyeeyo?
Wala khwa phaawu sapa aarafuniyeeyo atthu alufu nne, na zaari khelenke kavi mwilokottheliyeeyo?
Nanna-ni ehiniweeleyaanini yoori akaari owuuzani monkoni wa phaawu? Mwiiyane phoole na fwaramento ya mafwarizeewu na za masatukhi.”
Aphano khuweeleya yoori khaari owooza wiiyana phoole na fwaramento ya phaawu, ila khwa masomi a Mafwarizeewu na masatukhi.
Yinsa afiyeevo nti wa Sezareeya ya Filiipe, khuwoozela anakhiyoni awe yoori: “Atthu aninlupeza niini Mwaana wa Pinaatamu?”
Yo khujipu yoori: “Akina anri o Yaahaya namoosa; akina, anri o Aliyaasi, akina anri o Jeremiiya ama mmote wa manapiyu.”
Khurutela owoozela theenya yoori: “Khi mweeyo mwinri ki paani?”
Simawu Pheeturu khujipu yoori: “Weeyo o Al-Masiihu, Mwaana wa Nluku haayi.”
Yinsa khujipu yoori: “Wooshapweyiwa ti weeyo, Simawu mwaana wa Yoona! Maana vitthu zaya epi khuthoonyeziweeni ti pinaatamu, ila khwa Paapa ariiye pinkuuni.
Miiyo kiniwuuza yoori weeyo o Pheeturu, khwa liwe nttintthi kinjekana ojama wa Nluku na milako za motthooni khazinlawa oshintta.
Miiyo kiniwinkha efukulo ya Ofwalume wa Pinkuuni; etile onfukaaye vathi apha na pinkuuni entta ofukiwa, na etile weeyo onfukulaaye vathi apha na pinkuuni entta ofukuliwa.”
Aphano khuwooza anakhiyoni awe yoori ahiwooze akinoko yoori ye aari Al-Masiihu.
Waaza wakathi otthuupule, Yinsa khwaaza oweeleza anakhiyoni awe araka: Yaari ohithajiya olawa Yeruzaleemu ahoochaniwe vitthu zawaatta mmakhono wa attunkhulu a tiini, mahaakhimu a tiini na anamanozela a kano, ooliiwe, siikhu ya ttaatthu asisimuwe nkhapuri.
Aphano Pheeturu, khunkhuwelela othetekele khusala amuuza yoori: “Wala Mbwanaaka aka! Khinteela wuurettikhanela!”
Yinsa khuzukuluwa khumuuza Pheeturu yoori: “Weette nyuma waka Sheethwani! Weeyo ori nkhama liwe liriiye ntarikhi mwaka yoori likikwakwattule, maana onuupuwela nkhama pinaatamu woohiiyi nkhama anuupuwelaazo Nluku.”
Aphano Yinsa khuwooza anakhiyoni awe yoori: “Nkhama ntthu ontakha okilotta, ajikatthale mweenyewe, athuule nsalapa awe akilotte.
Maana otule antakhaaye wuusuru ohaayi awe ontta ompwetheya, ila otule onimpwetheyaaye ohaayi awe mwaasa wa miiyo ontta wuusurukha.
Ena fwayita-ni ntthu opattha fwayita olumwenku wooshi na khumwaashikha ohaayi awe? Ama niini pinaatamu antakhaaye opatilana ohaayi awe?
Apho Mwaana wa Pinaatamu onlawa ate nnuuru wa Papaawe na malayikha awe, amwinkhe phakari wakhula ntthu khwa etile arettiyeeyo.
Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori, awaapho apha atthu akina ahinttelaaye ofwa ahimooneni khapula Mwaana wa Pinaatamu ataka nkhama mfwalume.”
Ziviriyeevo siikhu sitha, Yinsa khunthuula Pheeturu, Tiyaaku na Yaahaya ttwiiye Tiyaaku, khuwaalawana othetekele va mwaako woolepa.
Attaaphale Yinsa khuzukulisiwa vakatthi vaya. Wuuso awe khwaara nkhama njuwa kuwo zawe khwiiya zoolakala nkhama nuuru.
Wakathi otthuupule khupuwelela omaasho waya Munsa na Aliyaasi apiyaka mwaasa na Yinsa.
Aphano Pheeturu khumuuza Yinsa yoori: “Mbwana, ti yooshapweya wiiya attaapha. Amana otakha, kintta ojeka heema ttatthu; moote yawo, moote ya Munsa, kiina ya Aliyaasi.”
Pheeturu eettaka ottakhula nalelo, khupuwa liwiku lawaara khuwaafinikha, nttumpho khupuwamu huula yaari oraaye: “Otu mwanaka wompheta na wookituvela channu. Mwinsiileze!”
Asiiliyeevo mattakhuzi apale anakhiyoni awe khukokhora khufiisa ajihi zaya vathi na khuwaapattha woova.
Ila Yinsa khuwaattama, khuwaasapa na khuwooza yoori: “Mwilankhe, mwihoove!”
Afunuliyeevo maasho khuhimooni hatha ntthu, khusala amoona Yinsa paasi.
Eettaka wiishukha vamwaako aphale, Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Mwihimuuze hatha ntthu epile mooniyeeyo, mpakha Mwaana wa Pinaatamu asisimuwe muufwa.”
Anakhiyoni apale khumuuzela yoori: “Aphano mwaasa aya niini anamanozela a kano anlupaaye yoori enhithajiya Aliyaasi ota khapula?”
Yinsa khujipu yoori: “Wekhweele Aliyaasi onta arutisele vitthu zooshi.
Ila miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori Aliyaasi ata, yo khuhinjuwi, ila khunrettela zooshi epile atakhaziyeeyo. Khwa nanna etthiipo Mwaana wa Pinaatamu onttela ohoochiwa pi atthaapo.”
Aphano anakhiyoni apale khuweeleya yoori Yinsa aari olupa monkoni wa Yaahaya namoosa.
Wakathi afiyeevo aphale yaariivo khuntti etile ya atthu, mwinyi mmote khulawa aphale aariivo Yinsa khunkokhorela,
khumuuza yoori: “Mbwana, omoonele huruma mwanaka! Eetta wiiyana jilejile entta onhoocha. Swaafu zinki onkwela vamoottho ama mmaati.
Miiyo kawaatiseliye anakhiyoni awo, ila khuhiwahi onvonisa.”
Yinsa khuwaajipu yoori: “Oo khapila yootakhala na yoohiina amini! Mpakha lini kinttelaaye wiiya vamote na mweeyo? Mpakha lini kuuvilelakani? Mwikitiisele mwanenu apha!”
Aphano Yinsa khuruma yoori masheethwani ansaruwe, wakathi otthuupule mwaana otule khwiiya woovona.
Paata ya toole, anakhiyoni awe khunsusela Yinsa othetekele, khumuuzela yoori: “Mwaasa aya niini nahaakhitireliyeeyo wiikara?”
Ye khuwaajipu yoori: “Maana mweeyo amini mwiriina ttiitthiiru. Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori eriwaka mweettiye wiiyana amini nkhama phunje ya samuli, mweetta owahi wuuza mwaako opu yoori: ‘Oleevo apha weette aphale’ weetta olawa, na khina etthu moote ya haari weettelaaye owaheya khwa mweeyo.”
Ila vitthu epo zinta nkatthi wa lompa na ofuka paasi.
Siikhu moote Yinsa na anakhiyoni awe aakusanyeyiye Kalileya, ye khuwooza yoori: “Mwaana wa Pinaatamu onlawa enkheleliwe mmakhono wa atthu.
Yo anttela omuula, siikhu ya ttaatthu asisimuwe.” Anakhiyoni awe khuwaapattha huzuni.
Wakathi Yinsa na anakhiyoni awe afiiyeeyo Kafwaranaawu, anamariphisa lumpuru khulawa omuuzela Pheeturu yoori: “Mwaaliimu enu khanripha lumpuru la Nnyupa Woosifwiwamo?”
Pheeturu khuwaajipu yoori: “Onripha!” Nawiisha Pheeturu khuvira nnyupa, ahinattakhule hatha etthu, Yinsa khuri: “Simawu, onoona toovi? Paani anriphaaye lumpuru na tthuvo ya mfwalume wa olumwenku opu? Atthu a mmuti nttumphu ama aletto?”
Pheeturu khujipu yoori: “Aniiya aletto,” Yinsa khumuuza yoori: “Eto enthoonyeza yoori aana a mmuti ana yoohiriphi.
Ila yoori nihiweephirise, olawe mpahari wamweese nanjoolo awo. Swi ethiito ya mwanzo onttelaaye olowa, ofunule milomo zaya, ontta osikanamo nzurukhu mmote. Aphano olawe wariphe lumpuru laka na lawo.”
Wakathi otthuupule anakhiyoni khuta aphale aariivo Yinsa khumuuzela yoori: “Nwulweene zayita akina aya, ti paani muufwalume wa pinkuuni?”
Ye khunkhuwela nsimaana khunttha vakatthi vaya,
khuwooza yoori: “Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori, mweeyo noohithupwiyi na khuhijiretti wiiya nkhama nsimaana otu, khamwinteela weettamo muufwalume wa pinkuuni.
Wekhweele anjipushuwisaaye nkhama nsimaana otu, oto ti nwulweene aya muufwalume wa pinkuuni.
“Animpwekherelaaye nsimaana nkhama otu khwa nzina laka, onikipwekherela miiyo.
Wakhula otule aninkosisaaye mmote wa asimaana apa akikhupaliyeeyo, afwataali ofukeleliwa liwe loovalaza mmwisiko khutupweeziwa nkhilintti ya pahari.
Phoole olumwenku, mwaasa wa vitthu za okosisa. Maana khinivonyela ohirettikhani vitthu zaya epo, ila atakhaliwa ntthu otule anttelaaye wiiyana paathuli.
Nakataalikha nkhama nkhono awo ama muulu awo onuukosisa, oshije weesele! Maana afwataali weeyo weetta muuhaayi wa mileele ori woorakala ama woovujeya ehiiyeeni wiiyana makhono mawiri na moolu mawiri weeyo aya khweeseleliwa va moottho wa mileele.
Nkhama liisho lawo limote linuukosisa, olazemo weeselele peetiwene! Maana afwataali weeyo weetta muufwalume wa pinkuuni na liisho limote ehiiyeeni weeseleliwa motthooni na maasho mawiri.
“Phoole, mwihintarawu hatha mmote wa asimaana apa! Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori malayikha aya anoona wuuso wa Paapa wa pinkuuni wakhula wakathi.
Wekhweele Mwaana wa Pinaatamu ateela wuusuru etile yaashikhiyeeyo.
Niini onuupuwelaaye weeyo? Amana ntthu eeyana pwittipwitthi zawe miiya khumwaashikhavo moote, khanlikha epile tiisiya wa tiisiini omwaako alawa weekesa etile yaashikhiyeeyo?
Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori, amana asikana oniiya woofurahi mwaasa wa pwittipwitthi yawe etile, zayita epile tiisiya wa tiisiini zoohaashikhi.
Etthiipo theenya Paapeenu ariiye pinkuuni khanintakhela hatha nsimaana mmote waashikha.
“Amana ttwiiyo ookosa, olawe wanthoonyeze etile avonyiyeeyo, ila orette epo zaya weeyo na ye paasi. Amana ye asiila shawuri zawo, wamwaawuni ttwiiyo.
Ila amana ahuusiili, onthuule ntthu mmote ama awiri, ‘yoori khwa oshaahiti wa atthu awiri ama attatthu yoori nttakhuzi lihakikheye.’
Amana ye akatthala wuusiila, walupe vakatthi wa ojama wa Nluku. Amana ye akatthala osiileza theenya ojama wa Nluku, ontthantte nkhama kaafiri ama namariphisa lumpuru.
Kiniwuuzani khweele yoori, zooshi epile mweeyo mwinfukaaye vathi apha, ziniiya zoofukiwa pinkuuni, na zooshi mwinfukulaaye vathi apha ziniiya zoofukuliwa pinkuuni.
kiniwuuzani theenya yoori awiri a mweeyo amana mwikhupalelana vathi apha khwa wakhula etthu etile mwintakhaaye oveka, eniiya yoorettiwa ti Paapa ariiye pinkuuni.
Maana vahali ankusanyeyaavo atthu awiri ama attatthu khwa nzina laka, na miiyo kiniiya attaapho.”
Aphano Pheeturu khumwaattama Yinsa khumuuzela yoori: “Mbwana, amana ttwiiyaku akikosa kinswamihi swafu kavi? Swaafu sapa?”
Yinsa khunjipu araka: “Miiyo kiniwuuza yoori, khahiyo swaafu sapa, ila swaafu saapiini orutela swaafu sapa.
“Khwa toowo, Ofwalume wa pinkuuni ori nkhama mfwalume aari otakhaaye waattalela vitthu zawe na karumeya awe.
Wakathi aaziyeevo waattalela, khutiiseliwa mwinyi aari omwiilaaye milikhi za nzurukhu wa feeta.
Mwaasa wa ohiina nanna yonripha mbwana awe otule aari omwiilaaye, khuruma yoori; ye na muukhaawe, aanaawe na vitthu zawe zooshi, zuuzanyisiwe ariphe teeni.
Karumeya khukokhora omaasho wa mbwana awe khunvekela yoori: ‘Okivilele, kintta wuuripha.’
Mbwana awe khunhurumiya, khufuja teeni etile na khunlikha olawa.
Ila karumeya otule noosaruwa khukutthanana nshirikhaawe wa vakhaazi aari omwiilaaye nzurukhu miiya paasi. Ye khunzola nshirikhaawe mmwisiko khusala anvinya araka: ‘Okiriphe!’
Aphano nshirikhaawe otule khukokhora khusala anvekela yoori: ‘Okivilele, kintta wuuripha.’
Ila ye khuhikhupaleli, khurumisa olawa otthiiwa nkalapooso mpakha ariphe teeni yawe.
Wakathi ooniyeevo akarumeya apale akinoko vitthu epile zaarettikhaniyeeyo, khukatipukha channu na khulawa khumuuza zooshi mbwana aya.
Mbwana khunkhuwela karumeya otule khumuuza yoori: ‘Karumeya woohifwayi, weeyo wakivekela miiyo khuuswaamihi teeni yawo.
Weeyo khawaarina ya omoonela huruma nshirikhaawo nkhama miiyo kiwooneliyeezo?’
Mbwana awe khwiiphiriwa khunttha nkalapooso yoori ahukhumwiwe mpakha ariphe teeni yawe.
Paapa wa pinkuuni onttela oretta etthiipo, amana mweeyo mwihinswaamihi ttwiiyenu na rooho yenu yooshi.”
Yinsa eeshiyeevo olupa mattakhuzi apale, khulaawo Kalileya khweetta Yudeya kaapu kiina ya Yorotaani.
Khuntti khuluyeene khusala enlotta, atthaapale ye khuwaavonisa alwele.
Mafwarizeewu akina khuta aphale aariivo Yinsa yoori amweeze khumuuzela yoori: “Halaali nlume omwaasha muukhawe khwa wakhula kiiswa?”
Yinsa khuwaajipu araka: “Mweeyo khamwisomeeni yoori omwanzo, Nluku amumpa nlume na muukha,
na khulupa yoori: ‘Tiito, nlume onlikha papaawe na mamaawe khujikusanya na muukhaawe, oowiiri khuretteya wiiya mwiili mmote’?
Khwa etthiipo khaniiya awiri ila aniiya mwiili mmote. Aphano, etile Nluku akusanyiyeeyo ahiiyevo antakhaaye ophakula.”
Mafwarizeewu apale khumuuzela theenya yoori: “Aphano mwaasa aya niini Munsa enkhaka ruhusa ya nlume omwinkha talakha muukha awe na khumwaasha?”
Yinsa khuwaajipu yoori: “Munsa aruma yoori mweeyo mwimwaashe muukha enu mwaasa wa wuuma wa rooho zenu. Ila khazaari toowo omwanzweene.
Miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori: wakhula otule animwaashaaye muukha awe, woohiiyi mwaasa wa oraruwa, khunrala muukha nkina ontta oraruwa.”
Anakhiyoni a Yinsa khuri: “Nkhama pi etthiipo muukha na nlume, afwataali ohilooli.”
Yinsa khujipu yoori: “Khiriweeni atthu ooshi eetta wiiyana matakhelo ookhupalela mattakhuzi aya apa, ila otule enkhiweeyo paasi.
Alume akinoko afwa nkuwo, maana avokoliwa etthiipo; akinoko arettisiwa pi atthu azaaya; akina eetta ojirettisa mwaasa wa Ofwalume wa pinkuuni. Otule anwahaaye okhupalela vitthu epi, ti akhupalele.”
Paata ya vitthu epile, atthu akina khusala awaathuula asimaana nontanela Yinsa yoori awaattheele makhono na awaalompele. Ila anakhiyoni awe khusala awaamaruwela.
Aphano Yinsa khuri: “Mwiwaalikhe akiteele miiyo asimaana wala mwihiwaakhattaze; maana Ofwalume wa pinkuuni pi wa apale eeyiye nkhama atthaapo.”
Paata ya owaattheela makhono khulaavo aphale vaya khulawa.
Ntthu nkina khumwaattama Yinsa khumuuzela yoori: “Mwaaliimu, kirette niini yooshapweya yoori kipatthe ohaayi wa mileele?”
Yinsa khunjipu yoori: “Mwaasa aya niini weeyo okuuzelaka etthu yiiyiye yooshapweya? Owaapho ntthu mmote paasi eeyiyeeyo wooshapweya. Nkhama weeyo ontakha weetta muuhaayi wa mileele, oshututele mirumo.”
Ntthu otule khumuuzela Yinsa yoori: “Piivi?” Yinsa khunjipu araka: “Ohuule, ohiraruwe, ohiiye, ohilaze oshaahiti woovonyeya,
onshitahi papaawo na mamaawo, na omphete namwaattamanana awo nkhama etthiipo onjiphetaazo omweenyewe.”
Shapu otule khujipu yoori: “Miiyo kinshututelaka mirumo zooshi. Khi niini enikisaleelaaye nalelo?”
Yinsa khunjipu yoori: “Nkhama weeyo ontakha wiiya khaamili, olawe woozanyise zooshi oriinaaye, nzurukhu aya owenkhe asikhini, orettaru toowo ontta wiiyana njuju pinkuuni. Nawiisha, ote okilotte.”
Noosiila mattakhuzi apale shapu otule khwiiya woohuzunikha, maana aarina maali zawaatta.
Aphano Yinsa khuwooza anakhiyoni awe araka: “Kiniwuuzani khweele yoori, ti yoolipa thaajiri weetta muufwalume wa pinkuuni.
Ila ti yookhweya enkamiiya ovira valiphotto wa sikano zayita thajiri weetta muufwalume wa Nluku.”
Anakhiyoni a Yinsa asiiliyeevo mattakhuzi apale, khwiiya ooshanka na khumuuzela yoori: “Khwa nanna nkhama eto paani anttelaaye wuusurukha?”
Yinsa khuweekesa na khuwaajipu yoori: “Khwa pinaatamu khinwaheya, ila wa Nluku vitthu zooshi zinwaheya.”
Aphano Pheeturu khujipu yoori: “Fweeyo nalikha zooshi yoori nuulotte. Ninttela wiiya niini fweeyo?”
Yinsa khuwooza araka: “Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori, amana ofiya wakathi Nluku anttelaaye waattala zooshi opheeya na Mwaana wa Pinaatamu eekhala va khukulu ya siifwa zawe, mweeyo mwinikilottaaye mwinttela wiikhalela khukulu khumi na piiri yoori mwiphuke mahimo khumi na mawiri a Ezirayiilu.
Ooshi apale alikhiyeeyo vaje vaya, attwi zaya, alupu aya, apapazaya, aanaaya ama mashapa aya, mwaasa wa miiyo, anlawa apwekhere swaafu miiya na orithi ohaayi wa mileele.
Khwa etthiipo, apale amwanzo anttela wiishela, na apale awiishela anttela wiiya amwanzo.
“Maana Ofwalume wa pinkuuni ori nkhama mweenyewe nshapa alankhiyeeyo supuyeene olawa oweekesa atthu yoori akhole khaazi mmashapa mwawe.
Ye khusiilanana yoori awaariphe nzurukhu mmote wa feeta wakhula siikhu, khuwaaruma olawa omashapa wawe.
Wakathi opule wa sattaatthu, ye khulankha khusala alawa khuwoona atthu akina ari ohiina khaazi eekhaliye vaparasa.
Aphano khuwooza yoori: ‘Mwilawe mweeyo theenya mwakhole khaazi mmashapa mwaka la wuuva, miiyo kintta wuuriphani etile enttelaaye wiiya ya shariya.’
Apale khulawa, khulankha theenya wakathi opule wa atuhuri na wakathi opule wa saakhentta, khuretta nanna nkhama etthiipile.
Etthiipo wakathi wa sakhumi na monsi, ye khurutelawo khuwaasikana theenya akina ahaariina khaazi na khuwoozela yoori: ‘Mwaasa aya niini mweeyo mwiiyaka apha mwihikholaka khaazi siikhu yooshi?’
Khunjipu yoori: ‘Maana khina mmote aninkhiyeeyo khaazi’. Aphano khuwooza apale aya yoori: ‘Ettani na mweeyo mwakhole khaazi mmashapa mwaka.’
Weettelaka oripa, mweenyewe nshapa khumuuza waziri awe yoori: ‘Owaakhuwele anakhaazi na owaariphe phakari yaya, owaazaka apale awiishela mpakha apale a mwanzo.’
Khuta anakhaazi apale aattakhulaniweeyo wakathi wa saakhumi na monsi na wakhula ntthu khupwekhera nzurukhu mmote wa feeta.
Wakathi atiiyeevo apale aattakhulaniweeyo mwanzo, aari weekesela opwekhera wawaatta, ila wakhula mmote aari opwekhera nzurukhu moote.
Apwekheriyeevo khwaaza omwaapa mweenyewe nshapa,
amuuzaka yoori: ‘Mamwinyi apa wawaattakhulana yoori akhole khaazi ya wakathi mmote, weeyo mbwana onnilikanisana fweeyo nivileliyeeyo olemela wa khaazi na haari ya nthana wooshi.’
Ila ye khujipu yoori: ‘Swaahipu, akiniwiimana shariya. Khawaakhupaleliye okhola khaazi ya opwekhera nzurukhu moote?
Opwekhere etile yiiyiye yawo olawe. Miiyo kintakha omwinkha otule kaattakhulaniyeeyo wawiishela nkhama etthiipo kiwinkhiyeeyo.
Akina ruhusa ya orettela etile kintakhaaye nzurukhu aka? Ama weeyo ona nrima mwaasa wa miiyo wiiya nkemaani?’
Aphano Yinsa khumarisa araka: Apale amwanzo anttela wiishela na apale awiishela anttela wiiya amwanzo.”
Awelelaka Yeruzaleemu, Yinsa khuwaakhuwela othetekele anakhiyoni awe apale khumi na awiri, khuwooza yoori:
“Mwisiile! Ninwelela Yeruzaleemu, Mwaana wa Pinaatamu onttela winkheleliwa mmakhono wa mahaakhimu a tiini na anamanozela a kano, yo anhukhumwele wuuliiwa,
enkheleliwe mmakhono wa amalapo anveyise, anjaphe na akhomeliwe. Ila siikhu ya ttaatthu asisimuwe.”
Aphano maama wa aana a Zepeteewu khumwaattama Yinsa na khukokhora khusala anvekela.
Yinsa khumuuzela yoori: “Weeyo ontakhani?” Maama otule khujipu yoori: “Kintakha yoori muufwalume mwawo aanaaka apa awiri mmote eekhale nkhono nlume nkina nkhono nkha.”
Yinsa khunjipu yoori: “Mweeyo khamwinjuwa etthu mwinvekaaye. Mwinwahi onywela koopho ethiiti kinttelaaye onywela?” Yo khujipu, “ninwahi.”
Aphano Yinsa khuri: “Weekhweele mweeyo mwinteela onywela koopho yaka, ila wiikhala nkhono nlume aka ama nkhono nkha khahiiyo miiyo kinlupaaye. Maana puuro eto ti yawe otule aattaleliweeyo ti Paapa.”
Wakathi apale akina khumi asiiliyeevo mattakhuzi apale, khwiiya ookasirikha khwa attwi apale awiri.
Aphano Yinsa khuwaakhuwela khulupa yoori: “Mwijuwe yoori anamalokozela a khapila anshintta, na attunkhulu aya anthoonyeza ofwalume khwa yo.
Mweeyo mwihiiye toowo, ila otule antakhaaye wiiya wa fwayita awaarumeyele azaawe;
na otule antakhaaye wiiya wa mwanzo eeye mwiitthwaana enu mweeyo.
Nkhama etthiipo, Mwaana wa Pinaatamu khateleeni orumeyeliwa, ila orumeya na winkha ohaayi awe khwa owaakaphula atthu awaatta.”
Yo alankhaka Yeriko, atthu awaatta khusala awaalotta.
Atthu awiri oohooni eekhaliye nshini wa tarikhi, wakathi asiiliyeevo yoori Yinsa ontta ovira, khwaaza onyakula araka: “Mbwana, Mwaana wa Daawuuda, noonele huruma!”
Atthu apale awaatta khusala awaakhattaza, awaatakhelaka yoori anyamale, ila khusala atepa onyakula araka: “Mbwana, Mwaana wa Daawuuda, noonele huruma!”
Yinsa khweemela khuwaakhuwela khuwoozela yoori: “Mweeyo mwintakha yoori miiyo kuuretteleni niini?”
Yo khujipu yoori: “Mbwana, nintakha noone.”
Yinsa khuwoonela huruma na khuwaasapa maasho aya, nasaapiru khwaaza woona khusala anlotta.
Ari kharipu ya Yeruzaleemu, khufiya Betifwaaje, va mwaako Oluveera, Yinsa khuwaaruma anakhiyoni awe awiri khuwooza yoori:
“Mwilawe nti opo mwinoonaaye omaasho wenu okho, mwinlawa mwansikane mwaana wa puuru weekha afukiwe vamote na weelume. Mwinfukule mwikitiisele.
Amana apuwa ntthu awuuzelani, mwimuuze yoori Mbwana ontta owaatakha, ontta wuulikhani nasaapiru mwiwaathuule.
Vitthu epo zarettikhana yoori emarisele etile alupiyeeyo napiyu yoori:
“Muuze sitati ya Siyooni yoori: ‘Omoone, mfwalume awo ontta wuuteela, woojipushuwisa, aweliye va mwaana wa puuru, nyama yoopakhira.’”
Anakhiyoni khuretta etile aarumiweeyo ti Yinsa.
Khuntiisa puuru yeekha na mwaana aya nttitthiiru, aphano khutthiiwavo kuwo zawe, ye khuwelavo.
Atthu apale awaatta aari onlottaaye khusala attattikha ajapi zaya ntarikhi, akina khusala ashija virapi za miitthi na ottattikha ntarikhi.
Apale aalokoziyeeyo na apale aari onlottaaye eetta onyakula araka: “Ozaana khwa mwaana wa Daawuuda! Wooparikhiyiwa ti otule antaaye khwa nzina la Mbwana! Ozaana wa pinkuuni.
Wakathi Yinsa aviriyeevo Yeruzaleemu, sitati yooshi khutapanyeya, atthu khusala oozeliwa yoori: “Paani otu aya?”
Yo khusala ajipu yoori: “Otu ti Yinsa, napiyu wa Nazareeti ya Kalileya.”
Yinsa khuvira Nnyupa Woosifwiwamo, khuwiikaramo ooshi apale aari wuuzanyisaye na apale aari wuuzanyaaye. Khukurumula meeza a anamapatilisa nzurukhu na khateera za apale aari wuuzanyisaaye jiwa.’
Khuwooza araka: “Yaatikhiwa yoori; ‘Nyuupa yaka enttela wiitthiwa nyuupa yoosifwiwamo, ila mweeyo mwaretta wiiya puuro ya anamwiiya.
Ananhooni na anamarakala khumwaattama Yinsa Nnyupa Woosifwiwamo, ye khuwaavonisa.
Mahaakhimu a tiini na anamanozela a kano ooniyeevo vitthu zootikinisa Yinsa aari orettaazo na aasimana aari okhuwaaye araka: “Ozaana mwaana wa Daawuuda!” khushanka khusala oozela yoori:
“Onsiila epi anlupaazo apa?” Yinsa khuwaajipu yoori: “Aaa; mweeyo khamwina some yoori: ‘Khwa nlimi la asimaana na apale anamwaaye antthenkeza siifwa khaamili?’”
Yinsa khuwaalikha, khulaamo nsitati mphule khulawa Betaaniya ottuukho aalaliiyeewo.
Mmeesho mwaya supuyeene, arutelaka ositati, khunkhola jala.
Khoona nfikeera nshini wa tarikhi, khwaattama ila khuhisikanani hatha mishumo, khusikanamo mathaparu paasi, aphano khuri: “Weeyo khunteela wiima theenya mishumo!” Nfikeera opule khuuma nasaapiru.
Anakhiyoni awe ooniyeevo epile zaarettikhaniyeeyo, khwiiya ooshanka na ootikinisiwa alupaka yoori: “Wooma toovi nasaapiru nfikeera opu?”
Yinsa khuwaajipu yoori: “Kiniwuuzani khweele yoori, amana mwiiyana amini na woohiina nshikili, mwinttela oretta woohiiyi epi zirettikhaniyeeyo khwa nfikeera opu paasi, ila hatha wuuza mwaako opu yoori okhuleye ojeeselele mpahari, zintta orettikhana.
Amana mwiiyana amini mwinpwekhera zooshi mwinttelaaye oveka khwa lompa.
Paata ya Yinsa ofiya Nnyupa woosifwiwamo, eettaka osomisa, mahaakhimu a tiini na attunkhulu a tiini khumwaattama khumuuzela yoori: “Vitthu epi onrettana ofwalume-ni? Wala ti paani awinkhiyeeyo ofwalume aya opu?”
Yinsa khuwaajipu yoori: “Miiyo kintta owuuzelani theenya; amana mwikijipu, kintta owuuzani ofwalume kinrettanaaye vitthu epi.
Woosa wa Yaahaya waari wa vayi? Wa pinkuuni ama wa anaatamu?” Yo khusala akheetisana atthaapo-ru araka: “Amana niri waari wa pinkuuni, ye ontta onuuzela yoori ‘khi mwaasa aya niini mwihikhupalelaka?’
Ila amana nilupa yoori pi wa anaatamu, niniwoova atthu, maana ankhupalela yoori Yaahayanapiyu.”
Yo khunjipu Yinsa yoori: “Khanijuweeni.” Ye khuwooza theenya yoori: “Hatha vattitthiiru akiniwuuzani owahi kinrettanaaye vitthu epi.”
Mwinoona toovi? Aarivo mwinyi mmote aariina aana awe awiri. Khumweettela otule wa mwanzo khumuuza yoori: ‘Mwanaka, etta wakhole khaazi leelo omashapa.’
Khujipu yoori: ‘Akeepu!’ Ila khuupuwela khulawa okhola khaazi etile ooziweeyo.
Paapa otule khumwettela mwanawe otule nkina khumuuza nkhama etthiipo amuziyeeyo otule nkina. Mwaana otule khujipu yoori: ‘Kintta olawa mbwana aka!’ Ila khuhilawi.
Khwa aana apale awiri ti tuuvi arettiyeeyo matakhelo a papaawe?” Khujipu yoori: “Otule wa mwanzo.” Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Kiniwuuzani khweele yoori, anamariphisa lumpuru na amalempe antta weetta muufwalume wa Nluku mweeyo mwihineettemu.
Maana Yaahaya ata yoori oothonyezeni tarikhi ya shariya, mweeyo khuhinkhupaleli, ila anamariphisa lumpuru na amalempe ankhupalela. Mweeyo moona vitthu epile khuhithupwiyi na wala khuhinkhupaleli.
“Mwisiile nlikaniso nkina: Aarivo thaajiri mmote wa mmuti nttumphule aalimiyeeyo nshapa lawe la wuuva. Khujekelela looshi, khwaattala kulaathayini ya onluwatthelamo wuuva na khujeka korofwa ya namweekesela. Khuwaalikhela anamalima apale akina, khulaamo mmuti mphule, khusala alawa safwari yawe.
Ofiyeevo wakathi wa wuurula, khuwaaperekha akarumeya awe khwa anamalima apale, yoori apwekherele mishumo zawe.
Anamalima khuwaakhola akarumeya a mweenyewe nshapa apale; mmote khunvulalisa, nkina khumuula, wattaatthu khunvonya na mawe.
Aphano khuwaaperekha akarumeya awe akina awaatta, anamalima apale khuwaatthantta nkhama etthiipo awaatthanttiyeezo apale akina.
Omwiisho khumperekha mwanawe alupaka yoori: ‘Mwanaka otu antta onshitahi.’
Ila anamalima amoniyeevo mwaana otule, khulupa yoori: ‘Otu namarithi. Mwite, nimuule nithuule eritho yawe.’
Attaaphale yo khunkhola khumweeselela othetekele wa nshapa khumuula.
Amana ata mweenyewe nshapa, onttela owaarettela niini anamalima apale?”
Yo khujipu yoori: “Wekhweele ontta owoola anamalima apale ootakhala rooho na awenkhe anamalima akina nshapa laya. Apa nka amwinkhaka phantte ya mishumo wakathi wa wuurula.”
Yinsa khuwoozela yoori: “Khamwinasome zawaatikhiwa Ttakatthiifu yoori: ‘Liwe anamajeka akatthaliyeeyo, nttho tthi liyiiyeeyo liwe linkhomaazaaye; eto enta wa Mbwana, na etthu yooshapweya khwa fweeyo.’
Paata ya toowo kiniwuuzani yoori Ofwalume wa Nluku mwinttela onyakanyiwa enkhiwe apale animaaye mishumo za Ofwalume.
Otule anttelaaye okwela liwe laya ntthi ontta othapateya, na otule linttelaaye onkhwela ontta othatuwa lifufu.
Mahaakhimu a tiini na mafwarizeewu, asiiliyeevo milikaniso za Yinsa, khuweeleya yoori aari ottakhula monkoni wa yo.
Khusala eekesa nanna ya onkhola ila khusala awoova atthu, maana aari onjali nkhama napiyu.
Yinsa khurutela owooza milikaniso araka:
“Ofwalume wa Pinkuuni onlattanana mfwalume mmote atthekeziyeeyo njampo la harusi ya mwanawe.
Aphano khuwaaruma akarumeya awe olawa owaakhuwela anamalaleyiwa yoori ate onjampo; ila yo khuhitakhi ota.
Khuwaaruma theenya akarumeya akina araka: ‘Mwawooze anamalaleyiwa yoori: Njampo lalikana; mompe zaka na aana aya ooneneva kashija na zooshi zalikana. Mwite onjampo la harusi.’
Ila yo khuhijali khusala alawa, mmote omashapa wawe, mmote nzanshara mwawe,
apale asaliyeeyo khuwaakhola akarumeya khuwaahukhumu na khuwoola.
Ila mfwalume khwiiya wawiiphiriwa, khuwaaruma anajanka awe olawa owaatapanya anamahusuti apale na khulukuza sitati yaya etile.
Aphano khuwooza akarumeya awe yoori: ‘Njampo lalikana, ila anamalaleyiwa khaari osuhi.
Mwilawe mmizukulowo za tarikhi mwawaalaleye ooshi apale mwinttelaaye owaasikana.’
Aphano akarumeya apale khulawa mmatarikhi na khuwaakusanya atthu ooshi apale awasikaniyeeyo, atthu ooshapweya rooho na atthu ootakhala rooho, nsana waari ojiwaavo njampo khwiiya wawiitaala pi anamalaleyiwa.
“Wakathi mfwalume aviriyeevo yoori awoone anamalaleyiwa apale, khumoona mwinyi mmote ahaawaliyeeyo kuwo za njampo.
Khumuuzela yoori: ‘Swaahipu, wavira toovi ohiwaleeni kuwo za njampo?’ Mwinyi otule khwiiya woonyamala.
Aphano mfwalume otule khuwaaruma akarumeyaawe yoori: ‘Mwinfuke moolu awe na makhono awe mwimweeselele vaje, n'yiiza; nttumpho oniiyamo olila na oluma meeno’.
Maana awaatta pi ookhuweliwa, ila vattitthiiru pi oothawuliwa”.
Mafwarizeewu khulaavo aphale vaya, khusala awaza shawuri zonvithaalela khwa mmattakhuzi awe.
Khuwaaruma anakhiyoni aya na atthu akina a khuntti ya Herooti khusala amuuza Yinsa yoori: “Mwaaliimu, fweeyo najuwa yoori weeyo onlupa khweele na onsomisa na khweele tarikhi ya Nluku, khunjilikha othowelelisiwa ti ntthu, wala khuniwaaphuka atthu khwa nanna ariizo.
Nkanuuze, ona shawuri ni? Ti ya shariya onripha lumpuru Seezari ama wala?”
Yinsa khujuwa thwapiya zaya zootakhala khuwaajipu yoori: “Manaafikhi, mwaasa aya niini mwikeezaka?”
Mwikithoonyeze nzurukhu onriphiwaaye lumpuru.” Khutiiseliwa nzurukhu mmote wa feeta.
Ye khuwoozela yoori: “Ratarato eti na nzina ntthi laatikhiweeyo apha tthi laani?”
Khujipu yoori: “Seezari”. Aphano khuwooza yoori: “Mwimwinkhe Seezari etile yiiyiye ya Seezari na mwimwinkhe Nluku etile yiiyiye ya Nluku.”
Asiiliyeevo mattakhuzi apale, khwiiya ootikinisiwa na khulikha wuuzela khusala alawa.
Siikhu ethiitile, khunteela masatukhi akina anlupaaye yoori khawiivo osisimuwa, khusala amuuzela yoori:
“Mwaaliimu, Munsa alupa yoori: ‘Amana ntthu afwa, muukha awe ahinvokoleleeni mwaana, ttwiiye ona ya onrala namafweliwa ti mannawe yoori amwinkhe aana ttwiiye otule afwiiyeeyo.
Fweeyo naari attwi sapa. Wamwanzo khuloola na khufwa. Muukha awe khanvokoleliye mwaana, khuraliwa ti ttwiiye.
Khurettikhana nkhama zanrettikhaneliyeeyo otule wa mwanzo na wa ttaatthu mpakha otule wa saapa.
Omwiisho waya paata ya ooshi ofwa, na muukha khufwa.
Aphano, wakathi woosisimuwa, khwa alume apale sapa ti tuuvi anttelaaye wiiya mannawe? Maana ooshi anraliye.”
Yinsa khuwaajipu yoori: “Mweeyo mwathowelela, maana khamwinjuwa Zawaatikhiwa Ttakatthiifu wala owahi wa Nluku.
Maana wakathi woosisimuwa atthu khanloola wala khanlooziwa; anttela wiiya nkhama malayikha pinkuuni.
Khwa osisimuwa wa ananfwa, mweeyo khamwisomeeni etile Nluku alupiyeeyo yoori:
‘Miiyo ki Nluku wa Eburahiima wa Esiyaakha na wa Yaakhumpa?’ Ye khahiyo Nluku wa ananfwa, ila wa atthu awoona.”
Asiiliyeevo mattakhuzi apale, atthu khwiiya ooshanka khwa osomisa wawe.
Paata ya mafwarizeewu ojuwa khuwaanyamaza masatukhi, khukusanyeya.
Mmote wa yo, namanozela kano khweeza omuuzela yoori:
“Mwaaliimu, nrumo nwulu pi puuvi?”
Yinsa khunjipu yoori: “Omphete Mbwana Nluku awo khwa rooho yawo yooshi, khwa nafusi yawo yooshi na akhili zawo zooshi.
Opu pi wiiyiyeeyo oruma wa mwanzo na wootepa owula.
Waphiiri onlattanana otthuupu: omphete nzaawo nkhama etthiipo onjiphetaazo omweenyewe.
Kano zooshi za Munsa na masomi ooshi amanapiyu anrumeyela mirumo etthiipi miwiri.”
Mafwarizeewu apale nalelo ari okusanyeya, Yinsa khuwoozela yoori:
“Mwinuupuwelani monkoni wa Al-Masiihu? Mwaana waani?” Yo khujipu yoori: “Mwaana wa Daawuuda.”
Yinsa khuwoozela theenya yoori: “Aphano, khi toovi Daawuuda khwa Rooho Ttakatthiifu omwiittha yoori Mbwana, alupaka yoori:
‘Mbwana amuuza Mbwana aka yoori: “Wiikhale nkhono nlume aka mpakha maatuwi awo kiwaatthe vathi wa moolu awo?”’
Nkhama Daawuuda onimwiittha yoori Mbwana, enrettikhana toovi eeyaka mwanawe?”
Khuhiivo mmote awahiyeeyo onjipu, na waaza siikhu ethiitile khina nkina awahiyeeyo omuuzela theenya.
Aphano Yinsa khuwooza atthu apale na anakhiyoni awe yoori:
“Anamanozela a kano na mafwarizeewu eekhalela khukulu ya Munsa.
Mwiwaashututele na mwithokorele zooshi epile aniwuuzaanini. Ila mwihiweezele vitthu anrettaazo. Maana khanrumeyela epile anlupaazo.
Yo anfuka maphuta oolemela na ottikha mmafuzi wa atthu, ila yo khantakha hatha oshashula na yaala.
Zooshi anrettaazo antakha yoori ooniwe pi anaatamu. Yo anjifukela hirizi mmwishwa mwaya, na olepisa mashaka a ajapi zaya.
Owaatuvela puuro zooshapweya za vanjampo na wiikhala wiilokozi nsinakooka,
owaatuvela ochelisiwa vamwanttiwa na wiitthiwa Mwaaliimu.
Mweeyo khamwinlawa wiitthiwa Mwaaliimu, maana Mwaaliimu enu mmote paasi, mweeyo mooshi mwa attwi.
Ahiiyevo vathi apha mwinttelaaye omwinkha khalamu ya ‘opaapa’, maana Papeenu ori mmote paasi, otule ari pinkuuni.
Wala ahiiyevo anttelaaye omwinkha khalamu ya namanozela maana namanozela ori mmote paasi, Al-Masiihu.
Ila otule eyiiye nwulu vakatthi venu eeye karumeya.
Otule anjiwulisaaye ontta opushuwisiwa; otule anjipushuwisaaye ontta owulisiwa.
Olaanikha pi weenu mweeyo anamanozela a kano na mafwarizeewu, manaafikhi, maana mwiniwafukela atthu Ofwalume wa pinkuuni, ila na mweeyo khuheettimo na khamwintakha owaalikha weettamo apale antakhaaye!
Olaanikha pi wenu mweeyo anamanozela a kano na mafwarizeewu, manaafikhi, maana mwimpala maali za anamfweliwa pi amannazaya na ojitapwatelana oretta lompa zoolepa; khwa etthiipo mwinteela ohukhumwiwa saaneene.
Olaanikha pi wenu mweeyo anamanozela a kano na mafwarizeewu, manaafikhi, maana mweeyo mwinlokha pahari na mwineettetta nti wooshi mweekesaka owaathuula atthu mwiwaatthe ntiini mwenu. Na amana mwimpattha ntthu aya oto onretteya swaafu piiri wiiya mwaana wa motthooni zayita mweeyo.
Olaanikha pi wenu mweeyo, anamalokozela oohooni! Maana mwinlupa yoori: ‘Amana ntthu alapha khwa omwimpari, eto khina maana. Ila amana ntthu alapha khwa thahapu ya omwimpari oto ona sharuthi ya oretta etile alaphiyeeyo.’
Alolo oohooni! Eriina fwayita ti tiivi, thahapu ama mwimpari opule onttakatthisaaye thahapu?
Mweeyo mwinlupa theenya yoori: ‘Amana ntthu alapha khwa nzina la alitaari, olapha waya opo khuna maana, ila ntthu amana alapha khwa zaakha etile eriiye vatulu vaya, oto ona yoorumeyela olapha wawe.’
Atthu oohooni, eriina fwayita ti tiivi, zaakha ama alitaari anttakatthisaaye zaakha?
Nakataalikha otule anlaphaaye khwa alitaari onlapha khwa alitaari na yooshi etile eriivo.
Amana ntthu alapha khwa mwimpari, onlapha khwa mwimpari na khwa otule aniikhalaaye nttumpho.
Na otule anlaphaaye khwa pinku onlapha khwa khukulu ya Nluku na khwa otule ekhaleliyeeyo.
Olaanikha pi wenu mweeyo anamanozela a kano na mafwarizeewu, manaafikhi, maana mweeyo mwinimwinkha Nluku lifunku la khuumi mpakha vitthu za nwoorotha na mwinimwinkha nyaani zootuva na samuli, ila mwinkhijilela oruma wa fwayita wa kano, wiiyiye: Shariya, huruma na waamineya, nakataalikha mwaarina ya oretta epo zaya woohiweraweri epile kiina.
Anamalokozela oohooni! Mwinshuja kuuku, ila khumiza enkamiiya.
Olaanikha pi wenu mweeyo, anamanozela a kano na mafwarizeewu, manaafikhi, maana mweeyo mwinoosa pilawuri na parathu oje waya, ila nkatthi mwenu weetaalamo wiiya na omaashokopho.
Mafwarizeewu ohooni, moose khapula pilawuri nkatthi mwaya, aphano phantte etile ya oje entta wiiya yooshapweya.
Olaanikha pi wenu mweeyo, anamanozela a kano na mafwarizeewu, manaafikhi, maana mweeyo mwiri nkhama vilalo yoovaaziwa khinampo, oje waya enumpuwaaye nkhama yooshapweya, ila nkatthi mwaya eetaaliyemo makhonkolo alupa ofwa na wakhula nanna ya vitthu zoovutta.
Oje wenu mwinuupuwa nkhama anashariya, ila nkatthi mwenu mweetaala onaafikhi na vitthu zootakhala.
Olaanikha pi wenu mweeyo, anamanozela a kano na mafwarizeewu, manaafikhi, maana mwinjeka khapuri zooshapweya za manapiyu, khuretta wiiya vilalo za akemaani.
Mwinlupa yoori: ‘Eriwaka neettiye wiiyavo wakathi wa amarehemu apapazetthu, khanaari wiiyana phantte khwa yo ya owoola manapiyu?
Etthiipo, mweeyo mwinjilawela oshaahiti yoori mwa aana a apale awooliyeeyo manapiyu.
Mwilikhe wiitaaza mphimo wa twampi za amarehemu apapazenu.
Nyookha! Ojama wa evili! Mwinttela owerawera toovi hukhumu ya motthooni?
Tiito miiyo kooperekhezani manapiyu, ajuwi na anamanozela a kano. Akina mwiwoole, mwiwaakhomele, mwiwaajaphe nsinakooka mwenu na mwiwaalupatthe sitati khwa sitati.
Khwa etthiipo eniwiittikhelani taamu yooshi ya anashariya yiittikheliyeeyo vathi, waaza taamu ya nashariya Apeele, mpakha taamu ya Zakariiya mwaana wa Barakiiya, mwimuuliyeeyo vakatthi wa omwimpari na alitaari.
Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori, zooshi epo ziniwateela atthu aleelo.
Yeruzaleemu, Yeruzaleemu, weeyo oniwuula manapiyu na owaavonya apale aperekhiweeyo! Swaafu kavi miiyo kitakhaka owaakusanya aana awo nkhama mwanakhu aniwaakusanyaazo aana awe mmapaphelo, ila mweeyo khuhitakhi.
Moone, yoori nyuupa yenu enttela wiiya yoothamiwa.
Maana miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori, mweeyo khamwinteela okoona theenya, mpakha mwilupe yoori: ‘Wooparikhiyiwa ti otule antaaye khwa nzina la Mbwana.’”
Yinsa khusaruwa Nnyupa Woosifwiwamo, khusala alawa, anakhiyoni awe khumwaattama yoori anthoonyeze manyupa apale ooshapweya.
Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Mweeyo mwinoona ooshi apa? Weekhweele miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori khalinsalavo apha liwe vatulu wa liwe lihinttelaaye opwechiwa.”
Wakathi Yinsa eekhaliyeevo va mwaako Oluveera, anakhiyoni khulawa khwiitthaalana othetekele na khunvekela yoori: “Nkanuuze, zinttela orettikhana lini vitthu zaya epo, wala amana otaaka, alama-ni enttelaaye wiiyavo na alama-ni ya mwiisho wa olumwenku?”
Ye khuwaajipu yoori: “Phoole, ti ahiiyevo hatha ntthu anttelaaye wuuttettekhani!
Maana atthu awaatta anlawa ate khwa nzina laka, alupaka yoori: ‘Miiyo ki Al-Masiihu’ na owaattettekha atthu awaatta.
Amana mwisiila hapari za viittha ama nzuuzu la viittha, mwihoove.
Khapila enttela wuumanana khapila kiina, ofwalume na ofwalume nkina, enttela opuwa esikinyaatthi na jala phantte zawaatta.
Zooshi epo yaazo ya vitthu za olwaaza.
Aphano yo anteela owinkhelelani yoori mwilupatthiwe na muuliwe, mwinlawa mweeniwe ti khapila zooshi mwaasa wa nzina laka.
Wakathi aya opo, atthu awaatta anteela wanswi amini anttela wiiya anamazinkula, na wiinana mmote na nzaawe.
Anlawa apuwe manapiyu awaatta oojipanka na awaattettekhe atthu awaatta.
Vitthu zootakhala zinttela weekezeleya, na pheta ya atthu awaatta enttela ovukuwa.
Ila otule anttelaaye ovilela mpakha mwiisho ontta wuusurukha.
Enttela olaleyiwa hapari epi za Ofwalume wa Nluku olumwenku wooshi, nkhama oshaahiti khwa khapila zooshi aphano osala ota mwiisho.
“Mwinteela woona okufuru wa woopisa wa pala onttelaaye opuwa Puuro Ttakatthiifu, etile alupiyeeyo napiyu Daniyeele - osome na eweeleye.
Aphano apale anttelaaye wiiya Yudeya atthirele omwaako.
Otule anttelaaye wiiya vatulu wa nyuupa ahishukhe yoori alazemo etthu nnyupa mwawe,
na otule anttelaaye wiiya omashapa ahirutele onti weettela ajapi yawe.
Siikhu etile ti ya woopisa khwa apale awiimittha na anaamwisaaye.
Mwilompe yoori miswipa epo ehirettikhane mwiita ama jumwa-monsi.
Maana wakathi aya opo onlawa wapuwe ohoowa nwulweene, thanku mwanzo wa olumwenku, na khunteela opuwa nkina nkhama otthuupo.
Eriwaka wakathi aya opo wa ohoowa khawaavukuliwe, khina aari weettelaaye wuusurukha, ila mwaasa wa apale oothawuliwa, siikhu zaya epo enttela wiiya zoovukuliwa.
Aphano amana ntthu awuuzani yoori: ‘Otu ari apha Al-Masiihu!’ ama: ‘Otule ari okhule!’ mwihinkhupalele.
Maana anlawa apuwe a al-Masiihu oojipanka na manapiyu oojipanka anttelaaye oretta alama khulukhulu na vitthu zootikinisa yoori awaahate hatha apale oothawuliwa.
Miiyo kawuuzani khapula zihinarettikhane epo zaya.
Nakataalikha, amana muuziwa yoori: ‘Ori n'yaara,’ mwihilawe, ama oriwa: ‘Ori nnyupa,’ mwihikhupali.
Maana, nkhama etthiipo taari enlankhaaye malawa-juwa, na ojithoonyeza okhu lintupweelaawo njuwa, etthiipo onttela wiiya ota wa Mwaana wa Pinaatamu.
Vahali aniiyaavo muufwi, akhwaazi ankusanyeya attaapho.
Paata ya mashakha a siikhu epo, njuwa linttela ozima na mweezi onttela olikha waara, matthottowa anttela okwa otulu na owahi wa pinkuuni onttela osakhinyeya.
Aphano epuwe pinkuuni alama za Mwaana wa Pinaatamu; khapila zooshi za vatuniya enttela ojikhupanyisa na enttela omoona Mwaana wa Pinaatamu ataaka mmawiku a pinkuuni khwa owahi na siifwa yawaatta.
Ye onttela operekha malayikha awe na ovuma nwulweene wa malope, yo anttela owaakusanya ananthawuliwa aya ooshi khwa phantte nne zinlankhaawo pheevo, phantte khwa phantte kiina ya pinku.
Mwijinozele osomisa wa nfikeera: Amana virapi zaya zootthelaka mathapa mwinjuwa yoori onsaleela ofiya mwiita.
Etthiipo na mweeyo, amana moona vitthu epo zooshi, mwijuwe yoori wakathi wafiya, ensaleela waaza.
Weekhweele kiniwuuzani yoori, khanteela ovira atthu apa aleelo zihirettikhaneene vitthu zaya epo.
Pinku na vathi zooshi zinteela ovira, ila mattakhuzi aka khanviraru.
Ila monkoni wa siikhu na wakathi khina anjuwaaye, wala malayikha a pinkuuni, wala Mwaana, ila Paapa paasi.
Nkhama etthiipo zaarettikhaniyeeyo wakathi wa Nuuhi, enttela wiiya etthiipo etelo ya Mwaana wa Pinaatamu.
Nkhama etthiipo siikhu ziviriyeezo za nnyeri, atthu aari oja na aari onywa, aari oralana na aari oloozana, mpakha ofiya siikhu Nuuhi eettiyeemo mmwaaraka.
Yo kaajuwiyevo hatha etthu mpakha wakathi otiiyeevo nnyeri na khuwaathuula ooshi. Enttela wiiya etthiipo ota wa Mwaana wa Pinaatamu.
Aphano awiri anttela wiiya omashapa; mmote athuuliwe, alikhiwe mmote.
Aakha awiri achilaka tiriku; mmote athuuliwe, mmote alikhiwe.
Mwaasa wa ethiito, mwijeekesele, maana khamwinjuwa siikhu anttelaaye ota Mbwana enu.
Ila eweeleyeni vitthu zaya epo; maana, mweenyewe nyuupa eriwaka eetta ojuwa wakathi antaavo anamwiiya, eetta ojeekesela na khaari olikhelela opwechiwa nyuupa yawe.
Tiito, mweeyo theenya mwiiye woojilikanisa, maana wakathi antaavo Mwaana wa Pinaatamu pi opule mwihinaakhipwelaaye.
“Ti tuuvi karumeya wawaamineya na waakhili, otule Mbwana awe amwinkhiyeeyo osala vaje vawe yoori asala awenkha atthu etthu-yoojiwa wakathi khaamili?
Wooparikhiyiwa karumeya otule mbwana awe ataaka anttelaaye onsikana arettaka etthiipo.
Weekhweele kiniwuuzani yoori onttela olikheliwa weettettisa maali zooshi za mbwana awe.
Ila karumeya otule amana eeya wootakhala rooho, ajilupezaka mweenyewe yoori: ‘Mbwana aka ontta orupaza,’
na khusala awaapiya ashirikhaawe na oja na onywa na ananhapaliwa,
onttela ota mbwana wa karumeya otule khwa siikhu ahaari waakhipwelaaye na wakathi ahinjuwaaye.
Ye onta onhukhumu saaneene antthe puuro ya manaafikhi, ottuukho onttelaaye wiiyawo olila na oluma meeno.
“Siikhu yaya eto, Ofwalume wa pinkuuni onttela wiiya nkhama aamwari khumi athuuliye makhompe aya, khulawa okutthanana mposi.
Athaanu khwa apale khumi aari alolo, athaanu aari akhili.
Apale oololo khuthuula makhompe aya, khuhinthuuli patarooya,
ila apale a akhili olikha othuula makhompe-ru khunthuula theenya patarooya nttopwiyo.
Mposi khurupaza ofiya, na ooshi khuwaakhola osikizi khulala.
Ila osikhu layili, khusiileya nkhuwo waari oraaye: ‘Mposi afiya! Mwisaruwe mwampwekherele.’
Aamwari apale ooshi khulankha khusala atthenkeza makhompe aya.
Apale oololo khusala awooza apale awiiyana akhili yoori: ‘Mwinimeele patarooya enu vattitthiiru, maana makhompe eetthu antta osizila.’
Yo khujipu yoori: ‘Wala, khanfiyela onrumeyela mweeyo na fweeyo. Mwilawe mwamuuzanye patarooya.
Wakathi alawiyeevo omuuzanya patarooya, mposi khufiya, aamwari apale ajitthekiyeeyo khuvira vamote na mposi olawa oja njampo la harusi na nlako khufukiwa.
