Mweeyo khamwina some nkithaapu ya Munsa etthu yaatikhiweeyo monkoni wa osisimuwa? Wakathi aari ottakhulaaye va muutthi opule waari okholelaaye, yaatikhiwa yoori Nluku aamuuziye Munsa yoori: “Miiyo ki Nluku wa Eburahiima, wa Esiyaakha na wa Yaakhumpa.”
Moone, Nluku khahiyo wa ananfwa, ila Nluku wa atthu haayi. Mwattettekheya venkivene.
Namanozela wa kano mmote noowasiila akheetisanaka khunsusela, ajuwiyeevo yoori ajipu saana, khumuuzela yoori: “Khi oruma wamwanzo khwa zooshi pi puuvi?”
Yinsa khujipu yoori: “Oruma wamwanzo khwa zooshi pi opu: Osiileze, Ezirayiilu, Mbwana Nluku eetthu ti eeyiye Mbwana otthwe paasi.
Omphete paasi Mbwana Nluku awo khwa rooho yawo yooshi na nafusi yawo yooshi na akhili zawo zooshi na kuvu zawo zooshi.
Waphiiri pi opu: ‘Omphete nzaawo nkhama etthiipo onjiphetaazo omweenyewe. “Khawiivo nrumo nkina nwulu nkhama opu.’
Namanozela wa kano otule khuri: “Kemaani, Mwaaliimu, walupa na haakhi yoori ye mmote paasi, na khaavo nkina woohiiyi ye,
na omphete na rooho yawo yooshi na akhili zawo na kuvu zawo zooshi na omphete nzaawo nkhama etthiipo onjiphetaazo ti yooziti zaakha yoolukuziwa na twaha.
Yinsa amooniyeevo yoori ajipu waakhilivo, khumuuza yoori: “Weeyo khuri peetiwene na ofwalume wa Nluku.” Elottelanaka, khuhiivo hatha mmote aari omuuzelaaye.
Yinsa eettaka osomisa nnyupa ya Nluku, khuwoozela yoori: “Anlupa toovi anamanozela kano yoori Al-Masiihu mwaana wa Daawuuda?
Daawuuda aya alupa khwa Rooho Ttakatthiifu yoori: ‘Mbwana amuuza Mbwana aka yoori wiikhale nkhono nlume aka, mpakha miiyo kiwaatthe maatuwi awo vathi wa moolu awo.’
Daawuuda aya onimwiittha yoori ‘Mbwana’. Toovi anttelaaye wiiya mwaanawe?” Khuntti khuluyeene yaari osiileza wootuveliwavo.
Yinsa eettaka owaasomisa, aari owooza yoori: “Phoole na anamanozela kano. Yo oniwaatuvela weettetta awaliye ajapi zoolepa na opwekherela mwacheliwa vaparasa,
owaatuvela wiikhala wiilokozi nsinakooka na puuro zooshitahiwa mmajampo,
atthaapo antapanya mmanyupa ananfweliwa pi amannazaya na ojihakikhi khwa oretta lompa zoolepa; apa aya anttela ohoowa khwa ophukiwa woolwaazavo!”
Yinsa eekhaliye waattamela puuro etile eninkhiwaavo zaakha, aari woona nanna khuntti etile yaari otthaamo nzurukhu n'yoopo ya zaakha. Mathaajiri awaatta aari otthaamo wawaatta.
Khumoona muukha namafweliwa ti mannawe mmote wa masikhini, atthaakamo ttoosu piiri.
Yinsa khuwaakhuwela anakhiyoni awe khusala awooza yoori: “Kiniwuuzani khweele yoori namafweliwa otu ti mannawe atthaamo n'yoopo wa zaakha zayita akina aya.
Maana ooshi enkha tathela, ila otu na osikhini awe enkha wooshi aari ororomelaaye.
Wakathi Yinsa aari osaruwaavo nnyupa yoosifwiwamo, nakhiyoni awe mmote khumuuza yoori: “Mwaaliimu nkoona! Maweni mawulweene toono na manyupa ooshapweyisana toono!”
Yinsa khunjipu yoori: “Woona manyupa mawulumawulu apa? Khalinlawa liwe wiiya vatulu wa liwe nzaaya lihinttelaaye opwechiwa.”
Yinsa aarettiye eekhaliye vamwaako Oluveera omaasho wa nyuupa yoosifwiwamo, Pheeturu, Yaakhumpa, Yaahaya na Antere khumuuzela othetekele yoori:
“Onuuze, wakathi-ni enttelaaye orettikhana vitthu zaya epo, na enttela wiiyavo alama-ni yoothoonyeza yoori zooshi zasaleela orettikhana?”
Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Phoole yoori mwihihatiwe ti hatha ntthu.
Maana awaatta anta khwa nzina laka alupaka yoori: ‘Miiyo ki Al-Masiihu!’ na aniwaahata atthu awaatta.
Amana mwisiila viittha ama hapari za viittha, mwihoove maana epo ena zoorettikhana, ila nalelo kinttela wiiya mwiisho.
Khapila moote enlawa yoomanane khapila kiina, na ofwalume onlawa woomanane ofwalume nkina. Zinlawa zeeyevo visikinyaatthi khwa phantte zoofwarikhana na jala. Epo zaya yaazo ya vitthu za olwaaza.
Mweeyo mwiiyane phoole, maana mwinlawa mwenkheleliwe wa anamaphuka na mwinlawa mwajaphiwe mmasinakooka, na mwilawaniwe wa misatoro na wa afwalume, mwaasa wa miiyo, yoori mwiiye mashaahiti.
Ila enihithajiya olaleyiwa hapari zooshapweya khapula khwa khapila zooshi.
Amana mwithuuliwa olawa ofukiwa na ophukiwa, mwihishukulikhe etthu yoolupa, ila ethiito mwinttelaaye winkhiwa wakathi aya otthuupo mwilupe ethiito, maana khahiyo mweeyo mwinttakhulaaye, ila Rooho Ttakatthiifu.
Ttwi mmote onlawa anleve ttwiiye yoori ooliwe, na paapa onleva mwanawe. Aana anlawa awaazukuluwele apapa zaya awoole.
Atthu ooshi anttela owiinani mwaasa wa miiyo. Ila otule anttelaaye ovilela mpakha mwiisho, ontta wuusurukha.
Amana moona okufuru wa woopisa wa pala nhali woohifwayi wiiyamo (ansomaaye ti emweeleye), aphano apale anttelaaye wiiya Yudeya atthirele omwaako.
Otule anttelaaye wiiya vatulu wa nyuupa ahiishukhevo yoori alawe owawe, wala ahivire othuula etthu ya nnyupa mwawe.
Otule aniiyaaye ntthuttu ahirutele onti yoori athuule juupa yawe.
Ootakhaliwa aakha apale anttelaaye osikaniwa ari awiimittha ama eettaka waamwisa!
Mwinvekele Nluku yoori vitthu zaya epo ehirettikhane mwiita.
Maana, siikhu zaya epo onttela wiiyavo ohoowa ohineeyekevo thanku Nluku ompe olumwenku, na khunteela opuwa nkina nkhama opo.
Eriwaka Nluku khaafupheyisiye siikhu zaya epo, khaavo aari weettelaaye wiiya haayi, ila mwaasa wa apale awathawuliyeeyo, afupheyisa siikhu zaya epo.
Aphano, amana ntthu awuuzani yoori: ‘Al-Masiihu otu ariiye apha!’ ama ‘Moone, otule ari okhule!’ mwihikhupali.
Maana anlawa apuwe Al-Masiihu oojipanka na manapiyu oojipanka anttelaaye othoonyeza alama na vitthu zootikinisa yoori kusapi awahi owaattettekha ananthawuliwa.
Mweeyo mwiiyane phoole! Miiyo kiniwuuzani zooshi epo zihinarettikhane.
Ila siikhu zaya epo, paata ya pala eto ya ohoowa, njuwa linttela oriipa na mweezi onttela olikha waara.
Matthottowa akhwe pinkuuni na kuvu ziriiye pinkuuni zinttela osakhinyeya.
Aphano, mwinttela omoona Mwaana wa Pinaatamu mmawiku na owahi nwulweene na siifwa.
Ye onttela oruma malayikha awe khwa phantte nne zooshi za nkerekhere wa olumwenku mpakha nkerekhere ya pinkuuni yoori awaakusanye ananthawuliwa awe.
“Mwijinozele nlikaniso wa nfikeera. Amana virapi zaya zinyoowela na mathapa khwaaza ophutuwela enthoonyeza yoori mwiita ontta waattamela.
Etthiipo theenya mweeyo, amana moona vitthu epo zeettaka orettikhana, mwijuwe yoori ye ori kharipu ya va milako.
Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori khapila eti kinvira vitthu epi zihirettikhaneeni.
Pinku na vathi zooshi zinteela ovira, ila mattakhuzi aka khanviraru.
Ila monkoni wa siikhu ama wakathi khina anjuwaaye; wala malayikha pinkuuni wala Mwaana, woohiiyi Paapa.
Phoole, mwiiye woojeekesela, maana khamwinjuwa ofiya wa wakathi aya opo.
Eri nkhama ntthu anlikhaaye nyuupa yawe khuretta safwari ya peetiwene; ila ahinalawe, khuwaalikhela ofwalume, akarumeya awe wakhula mmote sharuthi yawe, khunruma namweekesela yoori asale aweekeselaka.
Tiito, mwijeekesele, maana mweeyo khamwinjuwa wakathi mweenyewe nyuupa anttelaaye oruti; enttela wiiya njuwa looveva, osikhu layili, lifwajiri ama supu.
Amana ye ata woohileezi, ti ahiwaasikane eettaka olala.
Epile kiniwuuzaanini, kiniwuuzani mooshi: ‘Mwijeekesele!’”
Zaari osaleela siikhu piiri paasi yoori efiye siikhu ya Paashikowa na siikhu ya Njampo la Phaawu Zoohiina Fwaramento. Mahaakhimu a tiini na anamanozela a kano aari weekesa nanna ya onkhola Yinsa sirini yoori amuule.
Yo aari olupa yoori: “Khanininkhola vanjampo yoori nihipuwise nzuuzu vakatthi wa atthu.”
Yinsa ari Betaaniya, eekhaliye vameeza owawe mwinyi mmote anitthiwaaye Simawu namaharaja, khutawo muukha aataniyeeyo suupha ya mafuttha oonukhela awaatta nzurukhu. Khupwecha suupha etile khumwiitthela Yinsa veeswa vawe.
Apale aari attaaphale khwiiya ookatipukha khusala oozana atthaaporu yoori: “Aharipwela-ni mafuttha apale.
Maana aari owahi wuuzanyisa miiya ttatthu za nzurukhu wa paratha, aari weettelaaye winkhiwa asikhini.” Yo khunshowera muukha otule.
Ila Yinsa khuwaalikhisa araka: “Mwinlikhe muukha otu khwa heeri, Mwanvelaveliselani? Ye akirettela miiyo etthu yooshapweya.
Maana asikhini mwina mweeyo mileele, na mwinwahi owaawuni mwitakharu. Ila miiyo akinteela wiiya vamote na mweeyo mileele.
Ye aretta etile awahiyeeyo. Avaaza mafuttha oonukhela mwiili aka raku zeene, atthenkezaka ozikhiwa waka.
Kiniwuuzani khweele yoori: wakhula vahali lintafusiriwaavo nttakhuzi la Nluku khwa olumwenku wooshi, epi arettiyeeyo muukha otu, zeettaka olupiwa noofikhiriwa ye.”
Aphano Yuuda Eshikariyoote, mmote wa apale khumi na awiri, khulawa wa mahaakhimu a tiini khwa shawuri za onzinkula Yinsa.
Yo wakathi ansiliyeevo khwiiya oofurahi na khumwaahiti Yuuda omwinkha nzurukhu. Khwa wakathi aya opo Yuuda aari weekesa kiphenyo saana yoori anzinkule.
Siikhu ya mwanzo ya Njampo la Phaawu Yoohiina Fwaramento, wakathi waazoweriweeyo orettiwa twaha pwittipwitthi yoojeliwa paashikowa, anakhiyoni a Yinsa khumuuzela yoori: “Ontakha yoori neette vayi nootthenkesele etthu yoojiwa ya paashikowa?”
Yinsa khuwaaruma anakhiyoni awe awiri khuwooza yoori: “Mwilawe mpakha ositati, ottuukho mwinlawa mwansikane mwinyi athuuliye yuuku ya maati. Mwinlotte othuuto,
mwimuuze mweenyewe nyuupa ethiito anttelaaye oviramo yoori ‘Mwaaliimu ontta wuuzela: Orivayi nsana aka wa omaka-vo, kinttelaaye onja-vo paashikowa na anakhiyoni aka?’
Aphano ye ontta wuunozani mweeyo khwa nyuupa ya vatulu nsana nwulweene na zooshi mwinihithajiyaaye. Mwitthenkeze attaapho njampo letthu.”
Anakhiyoni apale awiri khulawa mpakha ositati, khusikana zooshi nkhama etthiipile Yinsa aalupiyeezo na khuntthekeza paashikowa.
Wakathi oripiyeevo, Yinsa khuta na anakhiyoni awe apale khumi na awiri.
Ari vameeza eettaka oja Yinsa khuri: “Weekhweele kiniwuuzani yoori mmote wa mweeyo anjaaye na miiyo onkizinkula.”
Ooshi khwiiya oohuzunikha na khwaaza wuuzela wakhula mmote khwa zwaamu yawe yoori: “Talili khahiyo miiyo?”
Yinsa khujipu yoori: “Mmote wa khumi na awiri anjanaaye miiyo parathu moote.
Mwaana wa Pinaatamu onlawa afwe, nkhama etthiipo yaatikhiweeyo monkoni wa ye. Ila wootakhaliwa ti otule anttelaaye onzinkula Mwaana wa Pinaatamu! Afwataali ahivokoliweeni!”
Eettaka oja, Yinsa khuthuula phaawu, khuparikhiya, khumeya, khuwenkha anakhiyoni awe na khuwooza yoori: “Mwithuule; opu mwiili aka.”
Elottelanaka, khuthuula jiikira, khushukhurwela, khuwenkha anakhiyoni awe na ooshi khunywa.
Khuwooza yoori: “Eti ti taamu yaka ya wahati yiitthiweeyo khwa zwaamu ya atthu ooshi.
Miiyo kiniwuuzani khweele yoori akinteela onywa theenya nshumo wa nrayi wa wuuva, mpakha siikhu kinttelaaye onywa theenya na mweeyo muufwalume wa Nluku.”
Paata ya yo wiipa liipo, khulankha khusala alawa omwaako Oluveera.
Aphano Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Mooshi mweeyo mwinlawa mwakanswi. Maana yaatikhiwa yoori: ‘Kininvulalisa nshuki aya, na pwittipwitthi zaya zinttela omwazeya.’
Ila paata ya osisimuwa waka, kinttela olokoza Kalileya.”
Aphano Pheeturu khutukhuru araka: “Hatha nkhama ooshi eetta wuutthira, miiyo akinuutthira.
Yinsa khunjipu yoori: “Weekhweele kiniwuuza yoori leelo osikhu otthuupu, likukhuwi lihineekhe swaafu piiri, onteela okikhana swaafu ttatthu.”
Ila Pheeturu khusala akhanyarela channu araka: “Hatha nkhama kintakha wuuliwa vamote na weeyo, akinteela wuukhana.” Ooshi khulupa etthiipo.
Aphano khulankha khulawa puuro eniitthiwaaye Yetemaani, khuwooza anakhiyoni awe yoori: “Mwiikhale apha, miiyo kinttela olompa.”
Khunthuula Pheeturu, Tiyaaku na Yaahaya khwaaza oshukulikha, othunkuwikha na ohuzunikha.
Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Nafusi yaka ti ya ohuzunikha venkivene woosaleela ofwa; mwisale apha na mwijeekesele.”
Yinsa khuwaasusa vattitthiiru khukokhora na khusala alompa yoori nkhama enwaheya aattuwananisiwe wakathi opu wa ohoowa.
Aari olupa toono: Oo Paapa zooshi khwa weeyo zinwaheya. Okaattuwananise miiyo jiikira eti ya ohoowa. Ila ehirettikhane khwa matakhelo aka, ila khwa matakhelo awo.
Apho khurutela aphale aariivo anakhiyoni awe, khuwaasikana eettaka olala. Khumuuza Pheeturu yoori: “Simawu, ontta olala? Khuwaheeni ojeekesela nenkawu wakathi mmote?
Mwijeekesele na mwilompe, yoori mwihikwele muuzayiniwa; rooho ti yookhomaala, ila mwiili pi woottettheya.”
Yinsa khuwaasusa opheya khusala alompa, arutelaka mattakhuzi mamoteru.
Wakathi arutiyeevo khuwaasikana eettaka olala theenya, mwaasa maasho aya eetta owaalemela; khaari ojuwa etthu yoojipu.
Khuta swaafu ya ttaatthu khuwooza yoori: “Nalelo mwintta olala na ovumula? Zafiyela! Wafiya wakathi wa Mwaana wa Pinaatamu winkheleliwa mmakhono wa anatwampi.
Mwilankhe, nilawe! Mwimoone namazinkula ori kharipu.
Yinsa nalelo eettaka ottakhula, khusala ata Yuuda mmote wa anakhiyoni apale khumi na awiri. Aari ota na atthu awaatta athuuliye phanka na kolomontto, aarumiweeyo ti mahaakhimu a tiini, anamanozela a kano na attunkhulu a tiini.
Namazinkula aawooziye alama araka: “Otule kinttelaaye ompatikha, ti othuuto; mwinkhole mwinthuule saana.”
Wakathi afiyeevo, ye khumwaattama khumuuza yoori: “Mwaaliimu!” na khumpatikha.
Atthu apale khunkhola Yinsa na khunkholelela.
Aphano mmote wa anakhiyoni awe aariina kharipu, khufuttha phanka khunvavela khushija nshiilo la karumeya wa haakhimu nwulu wa tiini.
Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Mwakiteela na phanka na mikokontto yoori mwikikhole nkhama nantarawu?
Siikhu zooshi kaari vamote na mweeyo kisomisaka Nnyupa Woosifwiwamo, khuhikikholi; ila zooshi epi zaariye yoori emarisele zawaatikhiwa ti manapiyu.
Anakhiyoni awe ooshi khumwanswi na khutthira.
Ila shapu mmote, aajifinikhiyeeyo nkhumi woolakala paasi aari onlottaaye Yinsa. Yo khunkhola,
ila khuvula nkhumi opule, khutthira waazu.
Khunthuula Yinsa khunlawana wa haakhimu nwulu wa tiini na khuthukumana mahaakhimu a tiini ooshi, attunkhulu a tiini na anamanozela a kano.
Pheeturu khusala awaalotta ari peetiwene mpakha nlikokoro wa haakhimu nwulu wa tiini, na khulawa khwiikhala na anamarumeyela, ootthaka moottho.
Mahaakhimu a tiini na Mashawuriiya ooshi aari weekesa onsikanana Yinsa paathuli moote yoori anhukhumwele ofwa, ila khuhinsikanani hatha moote.
Maana awaatta aari olawela oshaahiti woovonyeya khwa Yinsa, ila tukhuru zaya khazaari sawasawa.
Aphano khulankha atthu akina na onlupeza vitthu zoovonyeya.
“Fweeyo nansiila alupaka yoori: ‘Kimpwecha Nyuupa eti Yoosifwiwamo yoojekiwa pi makhono a anaatamu, na siikhu ttatthu kijeke kiina, yoohijekiwi pi makhono eenaatamu.’”
Ila hatha nkhama piitthiipo, mattakhuzi aya khaari wiiya sawasawa.
Khulankha haakhimu nwulu wa tiini khumuuzela Yinsa yoori: “Khunjipu mattakhuzi apa onlokoveziwaaye?”
Ila Yinsa khwiiya woonyamala, khuhijipu hatha etthu. Haakhimu nwulu wa tiini khurutela omuuzela theenya yoori: “Weeyo o Al-Masiihu, mwaana wa Nluku Wooparikhiyiwa?”
Yinsa khujipu yoori: “Miiyo ki othuuto, na mwinlawa mwamoone Mwaana wa Pinaatamu eekhaliye nkhono nlume wa Nluku wa owahi zooshi, na ataaka mmawiku a pinkuuni.”
Aphano haakhimu nwulu wa tiini khuvarula kuwo zawe na khuri: “Khi ninrettanna oshaahiti nkina!
Mweeyo mwasiila okufuru wawe. Mwinuupuwela niini?” Atthu ooshi anri onsuhi wuuliwa.
Aphano akina khwaaza ontthemela khunfinikha omaasho wawe khusala ampwakula na amuuzela yoori: “Ti paani oopiyeeyo? Onlupe!” Anamweekesela khunkhola na khumpwakula.
Pheeturu aarettiye ari vathi nlikokoro wa nyuupa etile wakathi atiyeeyo njaazi wa haakhimu nwulu wa tiini.
Amooniyeevo Pheeturu eettaka woottha moottho khuri: “Weeyo waari na Yinsa wa Nazareeti.”
Ila Pheeturu khukhana araka: “Akininjuwa, na wala akinsiila etthu onlupaaye.” Khusaruwela nlako wa nlikokoro.
Wakathi njaazi otule amooniyeevo theenya, khuwooza apale aariina attaaphale yoori: “Otu mmote wa atthaapo.”
Ila khukhana theenya. Oviriyeevo wakathi vattitthiiru, apale aariina atthaapale theenya khumuuza Pheeturu yoori: “Weekhweele, weeyo o mmoteru na atthaapo, maana onkalileya.
Ye khwaaza onlaani na olapha yoori: “Akininjuwa pinaatamu aya oto oninlupaaye.”
Nasaapiru likukhuwi khwiikha swaafu ya phiiri. Pheeturu khuupuwela mattakhuzi Yinsa amuuziyeeyo yoori: “Likukhuwi lihineekhe swaafu piiri, onikikhana swaafu ttatthu.” Khulaavo aphale vaya khusala alila.
Supuyeene, khukusanyeya Mahaakhimu a tiini, attunkhulu a tiini, anamanozela a kano na Mashawuriiya ooshi, khunfuka Yinsa khunthuula khumwinkha Pilaatu.
Pilaatu khumuuzela yoori: “Weeyo o mfwalume wa mayaahuuti?” Ye khujipu yoori: “Weeyo ti onlupaaye.”
Mahaakhimu a tiini khunlokoveza vitthu zawaatta Yinsa.
Pilaatu khurutela omuuzela theenya yoori: “Weeyo khunjipu? Nkoona vitthu kavi anuulokovezaaye.”
Ila Yinsa khuhijipu hatha etthu Pilaatu khwiiya wooshanka.
Yaari zowera yaya, wakathi wa Njampo la Paashikowa, Pilaatu onfukulela napherezu mmote, otule aari ovekiwaaye ti atthu.
Mwinyi mmote anitthiwaaye Baraba aafukeliwe vamote na anamakhijili mwaasa wa omuula ntthu wakathi wa nzuzu.
Khuntti ya atthu etile khuta na khunvekela Pilaatu yoori arette etile awaazoweziyeeyo owaarettela.
Aphano Pilaatu khuwoozela yoori “Mweeyo mwintakha yoori kinfukulele mfwalume wa mayaahuuti?”
Maana ye aari ojuwa saaneene, yoori mahaakhimu a tiini anleviye Yinsa mwaasa wa nrima.
Ila mahaakhimu a tiini awaakhanyareliye atthu apale yoori anvekele Pilaatu aaze onfukulela Baraba khwa otakha waya.
Pilaatu khuwoozela theenya yoori: “Kinrettele niini mwinyi otu mweeyo mwinimwiitthaaye mfwalume wa mayaahuuti?”
Yo khunyakula araka: “Akhomeliwe!”
Ila Pilaatu khuwoozela yoori: “Niini arettiyeeyo yootakhala?” Ila yo khusala atepa onyakula araka: “Akhomeliwe!”
Pilaatu eekesaka otuvelisa khuntti etile ya atthu, khunfukulela Baraba na khuruma ojaphiwa Yinsa na olawa okhomeliwa.
Anajanka khunthuula Yinsa, khunlawana nlikokoro wa nyuupa khuulu ya nsatoro khukusanya khuntti khuluyeene ya anajanka.
Khunwalisa juupa yookhuttuwa, khuvaasha khaara ya miiwa khunwalisa mmwishwa.
Khusala anchelisa araka: “Wiiye haayi, mfwalume wa mayaahuuti!”
Khusala ampiya veeshwa vawe na nthala na ontthemela, akokhoraka na omwaaputu.
Paata ya onttukhana, anajanka apale khunvula kuwo yookhuttuwa khunwalisa kuwo za wiiya zawe. Aphano khunsarulela vaje yoori alawe ankhomele.
Khukutthanana mwinyi mmote wa Sireene aari wiitthiwaaye Simawu, papaawe Alishantere na Ruufu, aari olankhaaye omashapa. Khunkhanyarela othuula nsalapa wa Yinsa.
Yo khunthuula Yinsa khunlawana puuro eniitthiwaaye Kolokoota, eriina maana a puuro ya likurakuza la eeshwa.
Khusala atakha omwinkha viinyu yoophakanyaniwa mafuttha oonukhela, ila ye khuhinywi.
Aphano khunkhomela na khwaawanyana kuwo zawe khwa weekesa nasipu yoori ajuwe wakhula ntthu phantte ari weettelaaye osalana.
Aakhomelaniwe wakathi wa saa-ttaatthu, supu.
Pi etthiipo yaatikhiweeyo khwa olokoveziwa wawe yoori: MFWALUME WA MAYAAHUUTI.
Vamote na ye aakhomeliwe manantarawu awiri, mmote nkhono nlume, nkina nkhono nkha,
[na khurettikhana epile zawaatikhiwa zaalupiyeeyo yoori: “Ye aatthanttiwe nkhama namatapanya.”]
Apale aari oviraaye attaaphale, eetta onttukhana na osakhinya viishwa zaya araka: “Haya, weeyo ompwechaaye Nyuupa Yoosifwiwamo, khwa siikhu ttatthu khujeka.
Wiishukhe vansalapa apho na ojuusuru omweenyewe!”
Khwa nanna etthiipile, mahaakhimu a tiini na anamanozela a kano khusala alupa atthaaporu anveyisa yoori: “Awoosuru akina, ila khanwahi ojuusuru mweenyewe.
Wiishukhe vansalapa apho O Al-Masiihu, mfwalume wa Ezirayiilu, wiishukhe yoori niwoone na nuukhupali.” Apale aakhomeliweeyo, na yo eetta onttukhana theenya.
Yaapuwiye yiiza olumwenku wooshi, waaza atuhuri mpakha alaasiri.
Payina ya alaasiri, Yinsa khukhuwa na huula ya onyakula, araka: “Elooyi, Elooyi, Lama sabatani?” Eto ena maana ya “Nluku aka, Nluku aka, mwaasa aya niini okanswaka?
Wakathi atthu apale aari attaaphale asiiliyeevo mattakhuzi apale, khulupa yoori: “Mwisiile, oninkhuwela Aliyaasi!”
Mmote aari attaaphale khutthira khulawa khunaanisa shiponja na vinaakiri, khupweha va muutthi na khumwinkha Yinsa yoori anywe na khuri: “Mwinlikhe, nimoone nkhama Aliyaasi onta anlazevo aphale vaya.
Ila Yinsa khunyakula channu khwiittha phuumu.
Phazira ya Nnyupa Woosifwiwamo khuvaruwa khwaawanyeya phantte piiri, waaza vatulu mpakha vathi.
Wakathi namalokozela wa anajanka aariiye omaasho wa Yinsa, ooniyeevo nanna afwiyeeyo, khuri: “Wekhweele mwinyi otu aari Mwaana wa Nluku!”
Aakha akina aari oretta eettaka woona vitthu epile zaari orettikhanaaye ari peetiwene. Khwa atthaapo aarivo Mariyamu Mataleena, Mariyamu mamaawe Tiyaaku, nsimaana wa Yuusufu, na Salome.
Aakha aya apo amperekhiye Yinsa na omwaawuni wakathi ariiyo Kalileya. Owaalikha apo aya, aarivo aakha akina awaatta aalawaniyeeyo Yeruzaleemu.
Njuwa leettelaka otupweela, mwaasa wa wiiya siikhu ya otthenkeza Saapatu,
Yuusufu wa Arimateeya, mwinyi wa fwayita na aari oretta phantte ya Mashawuriiya, oto naye aari oweja ota wa ofwalume wa Nluku, khulawa woominyalavo wa Pilaatu na khuveka mwiili wa Yinsa.
Pilaatu khwiiya wooshanka noosiila yoori Yinsa afwa. Khunkhuwela namalokozela wa anajanka khumuuzela nkhama Yinsa afwa.
Wakathi ooziweevo ti namalokozela wa anajanka, khumwinkha mwiili wa Yinsa Yuusufu.
Aphano Yuusufu khuuzanya kuwo yoolakala yoopeepheya, khwiishusha mwiili wa Yinsa vansalapa aphale, khumputaputela va kuwo etile yoolakala na khunttha nkhapuri yaathipiweeyo va mwaako. Nawiisha, khutthaavo liwe vanlako vaya.
Mariyamu Mataleena na Mariyamu mamaawe Yuusufu, aarettiye eettaka woona na khoona mwiili wa Yinsa vahali waatthiiweevo.
Paata ya ovirisa Saapatu, Mariyamu Mataleena, Salome na Mariyamu mamaawe Tiyaaku, khuuzanya mafuttha oonukhela yoori eetthele mwiili wa Yinsa.
Siikhu ya mwanzo ya sumana supuyeene, njuwa leettelaka opuwa, aakha apale khulawa okhapuri.
Ntarikhi khusala oozelana yoori: “Paani anttelaaye onilazelavo liwe lifukaniweeyo nlako wa khapuri?”
Maana liwe laya laari liwululene. Ila noofiya okhule, khoona liri loolaziwavo.
Aviriyeevo nkhapuri mphule, khumoona shaapu awaliye kuwo zoolakala eekhaliye nkhono nlume, na khwiiya awoova.
Khuwooza yoori: “Mwihoove, mweeyo mwinimweekesa Yinsa wa Nazareeti, aakhomeliweeyo. Ye asisimuwa! Khaamo mphu, moone puuro aattattikheliwevo.
Mwilawe na mwawooze anakhiyoni awe na Pheeturu yoori: ‘Ye alokoza eettaka Kalileya.’ Ottuukho mweeyo mwinlawa mwamoone, nkhama etthiipo awuuziyeenini.”
Eettaka othukumela na osuthuwa, aakha apale khulaawo na khutthiramu nkhapuri mphule. Na khuhimuuzi hatha ntthu, maana aari awoova.
Wakathi Yinsa asisimuwiyeevo lifwajiri la siikhu ya mwanzo ya sumana, khumpuwelela omwanzo ene Mariyamu Mataleena, otule eekariweeyo mmwiili mwawe masheethwani sapa.
Ye khulawa owooza ashirikha awe Yinsa, maana yo aari oohuzunikha na olila.
Wakathi asiiliyeevo yoori Yinsa ori haayi na ampuweleliye Mariyamu Mataleena yo khuhikhupali.
Paata ya vitthu epile, Yinsa khujithoonyeza khwa wuuso nkina vakatthi wa anakhiyoni awe awiri alottaka tarikhi ya omashapa.
Yo khuruti khuta khuwooza mattakhuzi apale azaaya; ila theenya apale khuhikhupali.
Omwiisho waya Yinsa khuwaapuwelela apale khumi na mmote, wakathi aariiyo vameeza, na khuwaashowera mwaasa woohikhupali na wuuma rooho zaya, maana khawaasileziye apale aamoniyeeyo wakathi asisimuwiyeevo.
Khuwooza yoori: “Mwilawe olumwenku wooshi mwawalaleyele atthu ooshi hapari zooshapweya.
Otule ankhupalelaaye na khoosiwa ontta wuusurukha, ila otule ahinkhupalelaaye oniiyana paathuli.
Alama epi enttela owaalokoza apale anikikhupalaaye miiyo: khwa nzina laka aniikara masheethwani, anlawa attakhule luuka pheeya,
ankhola nyookha na onywa amali ya wuula, ila khuhiwaaretti hatha etthu na owaattheela atthu makhono khuvona.”
Paata ya owooza mattakhuzi apale, Mbwana Yinsa khuweziwa pinkuuni khwiikhala nkhono nlume wa Nluku.
Aphano anakhiyoni apale khulankha khulawa olaleya phantte zooshi, Mbwana aari owaawuni ahakikhaka mattakhuzi aya na alama zaari owaalottaaye.
Weeyo Tiyoofilu woohishimiwa, atthu a waatta aajilipisiye waatikha hatiithi ya vitthu ziviriyeeyo vakatthi vetthu.
Apale aari mashaahiti ooniyeeyo omwanzweene zirettikhanaka, khwiiya anamalaleya a hapari zooshapweya za nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku, atthaapo pi anifiseliyeeyo fweeyo.
Na miiyo zaamu yaka khusala kitholathola woohilazeli varanka epile zirettikhaniyeezo zaazaka, khulakela owaatikhela zooshi woolotteyavo,
yoori wiiyane nroromelo khwa mattakhuzi apa a haakhi osiiliyeeyo.
Wakathi Herooti ari nsatoro wa Yudeya, aarivo haakhimu wa tiini mmote wa khuntti ya Abiiya aari wiitthiwaaye Zakariiya. Muukhaawe aari wiitthiwa Elizabeeti aari woojama wa mahaakhimu a tiini.
Oowiiri aya aari atthu ookhweele nkatthi wa mwentto wa Nnyizinku na ooshututela wa waamineyavo kano na oruma wooshi wa Mbwana.
Elizabeeti khaarina mwaana mwaasa woohiina mavokozi na oowiiri aya aari awuuluvala.
Siikhu moote Zakariiya aari okhola khaazi yoohaakhimu wa tiini Nnyuupa wa Nnyizinku Yeruzaleemu, mwaasa yoori yaari zwaamu ya khuntti yawe okhola khaazi yaya etile.
Nkhama etthiipo aazowereliyeeyo attunkhulu a tiini, ye aathawuliwe nkatthi wa nasipu yoori asala akhoza ovupa puuro ttakatthiifu ya Mbwana.
N'oofiya wakathi wookhoza ovupa, atthu ooshi apale aari vaje aari ovira alompaka.
Aphano nlayikha la Mbwana khunteela Zakariiya nkhono-nlume vaalitaari onkhoziwaavo ovupa.
Wakathi ye ooniyeevo nlayikha ntthile, khwiiya wooshanka na wa woova channu.
Nlayikha khumuuza yoori: “Ohoove Zakariiya! Nnyizinku asiila lompa yawo; muukhaawo Elizabeeti onteela ompattha mwaana. Weeyo onteela ontthaja nzina la Yaahaya.
Ye onttela wiiya furaha yootuveliwa wawo, atthu a waatta anteela ofurahela ovokoliwa wawe,
maana ye onteela wiiya nttunkhulu mmakhono wa Mbwana Nnyizinku. Khanteela onywa viinyu wala onywa vitthu zoohapala. Onttela wiiya wa wiitaazaniwa Rooho Ttakatthiifu ari mwiirukulu wa mamaawe.
Onteela owaatana atthu awaatta a Ezirayeele wa Mbwana Nnyizinku aya.
Onteela operekhiwa ti Mbwana na onttela wiiya wookhomaala na woowahi nkhama napiyu Aliyaasi, yoori azukulise rooho za apaapa eeyane osiilana na aanaaya, na yoori awaazukuluse anamakhijili eettettise haakhi, toowo phi anttelaavo ozukulisa rooho zaya yoori ampokherele Mbwana ataaka.”
Aphano Zakariiya khuuzela nlayikha ntthile yoori: “Kinteela ohakikhi toovi etthu yaya eto? Miiyo kooluvala na muukhaaka ooluvala.”
Khujipu nlayikha liraka: “Miiyo ki Jipiriilu, kiniiya vamote na Nnyizinku, akiruma yoori kite kiwuuze hapari epi zooshapweya.
Wiiya khukhupaleeni mattakhuzi apa kiwuuziyeezo, onttela wiiya woohittakhuli mpakha siikhu zinttelaaye orettikhana vitthu epi. Zinteela orettikhana wakathi aya otthuupo.”
Nalelo atthu aari onwejaaye Zakariiya khushanka mwaasa woorupaza Nnyupa wa Nnyizinku.
N'oosaruwa, khuhisala awahi ottakhulana atthu apale. Yo khujuwa yoori wanteeliye wahayi Nnyupa wa Nnyizinku. Khwiiya woohittakhuli khusala attakhula na makhono.
Wakathi eeshisiyeevo siikhu zookhola khaazi z'oottunkhulu wa Nnyupa wa Nnyizinku, khurutela owawe.
Paata ya toole, muukhaawe Elizabeeti khwiimittha, khuhisala asaruwa nnyupa mpakha nyeezi mithaanu.
Khuri: “Aphano Mbwana ajipu lompa yaka, eeshisa haaya etile kaariina na atthu.”
Mweezi wasiitha wa erukulu ya Elizabeeti, Nnyizinku khuruma nlayikha Jipiriilu olawa sitati ya Kalileya nti wa Nazareeti
yoori lilawe wa mwaari mmote woohijansiliwi aari wiitthiwaaye Mariyamu, aaposiweeyo ti shapu mmote aari wiitthiwaaye Yuusufu woojama wa mfwalume Daawuuda.
Nlayikha ntthile n'onsikana khumuuza yoori: “Heeri yiiye vamote na-weyo Mariyamu! O wooziti oshapweyiwa, Mbwana ori vamote na-weyo.”
Ye khwiiya woozinkireya mwaasa wa mattakhuzi apale, khuvira aphelelezaka maana a hapari zaya epile.
Nlayikha khurutela omuuza liraka: “Ohoove Mariyamu, wapattha rehema omaasho wa Nnyizinku.
Onteela wiimittha ompatthe mwaana wanlume ontthaje nzina la Yinsa.
Ye onteela wiiya nttunkhulu, nka eetthiwaka Mwaana wa Nnyizinku Nwulu wa Pinkuuni. Mbwana Nnyizinku onteela omwinkha ofwalume wa papaawe Daawuuda.
Na onteela wiiya mfwalume wa Ezirayeele khwa mileele, ofwalume awe khunteela wiisha.”
Aphano Mariyamu khuuzela nlayikha yoori: “Zinttela orettikhana toovi na miiyo akininjuwa nlume?”
Nlayikha khujipu liraka: “Rooho Ttakatthiifu ontta owiishukhela, owahi wa Nnyizinku Nwulu wa Pinkuuni onttela wuufinikha na mwiivuuli awe. Ti eto Mwaana onttelaaye ompattha, onteela wiitthiwa Ttakatthiifu, Mwaana wa Nnyizinku.
Omoone jamaayo Elizabeeti, otule yaari oriwakaaye khanvokola, ila apha na wuuluvala wawe nasaapi eti eemittha opu mweezi wasiitha.
Maana, mmakhono wa Nnyizinku khayiivo etthu moote ehinwaheyaaye.”
Mariyamu khuri: “Kiri raati miiyo karumeya wa Mbwana; mattakhuzi apa onlupaaye phi arettikhane khwa miiyo.” Nlayikha ntthile khulaavo khulawa.
Ziviriyeevo siikhu, Mariyamu khujilokotthela khusala alawa na waakuva sitati moote yaari nti wa nnyaako za Yudeya.
N'oofiya khuvira nnyupa owawe Zakariiya khunchelisa Elizabeeti.
Ye n'oosiila mwacheliwa etile ya Mariyamu, mwaana aari mwiirukulu mwawe khujisakhinya. Elizabeeti khwiiya wa wiitaazaniwa Rooho Ttakatthiifu.
Khukhuwa na kuvu araka: “Wooparikhiyiwa ti weyo Mariyamu vakatthi wa aakha, na wooparikhiyiwa mwaana oto ariiye mwiirukulu mwawo!
Miiyo ki paani wooteela wooniwa ti maama wa Mbwanaaka?
N'oosiila mwacheliwa yawo, mwaana ariiye mwiirukulu mwaka eetta ojisakhinya wafurahavo.
Wooparikhiyiwa ti weyo okhupaliyeeyo yoori anteela orettikhana mattakhuzi apa wuuziweeyo a phantte ya Mbwana.”
Aphano Mariyamu khuri: “Nafusi yaka enlaleya owula wa Mbwana,
Rooho yaka ti yomfurahela Nnyizinku namuusuru aka,
mwaasa yoori Ye akuupuwela miiyo karumeyaawe woohiitaali mmaasho. Waaza attaapha, peewu za atthu ooshi zinttela okiittha yoori muukha wooparikhiyiwa,
mwaasa yoori Nnyizinku Woowahi aretta vitthu khuluzeene muuhaayi mwaka; nzina lawe ttakatthiifu.
Ye oniwaahurumiya atthu a peewu zooshi apale animoovaaye.
Aretta vitthu khuluzeene na makhono awe, khuwaamwaza apale oojikhupali khwa shawuri za nroho mwaya.
Awaalaza afwalume ohaakhimu aya khuwaalansa atthu apale oojipushuwisa.
Aweetaaza vitthu apale ariina jala, na khuweekara mathaajiri makhonoru.
Amwaawuni karumeyaawe Ezirayeele, oopuwelaka huruma aarinaaye
na Eburahiima na peewu yawe khwa mileele, nkhama etthiipo aawooziyeezo amarehemu apapazetthu.”
Mariyamu eekhaliye nyeezi mittatthu wa Elizabeeti nawiisha khurutela owawe
Khufiya wakathi wa Elizabeeti opattha ekumi, khunvokola mwaana wanlume.
Anamwaattamanani awe na ajamaaze khusiila elupiwaka huruma khuluyeene Mbwana amooneliyeeyo Elizabeeti, khulawa khufurahi vamote na-ye.
Efiiyeevo siikhu yanaane, mwaana otule khulawa khukhiriyisiwa khusala atakha otthajiwa nzina la papaawe Zakariiya.
Ila mamaawe khujipu araka: “Ii wala! Nzina lawe linttela wiiya Yaahaya.”
Yo khulupa yoori: “Weeyo khuna jamaayo ariina nzina laya nttho!”
Aphano khwinkhiwa alama papaawe yoori lijuwiwe nzina aari otakhaaye ontthaja mwaana otule.
Zakariiya khuveka lipawu nttitthiiru, khwaatikhavo yoori: “Nzina lawe ti Yaahaya.” Atthu ooshi khushanka.
Nasaapiru Zakariiya milomo zawe khufunuwa na nlimi lawe khushashuwa, khwaaza ottakhula ansifwaka Nnyizinku.
Anamwaattamanani awe ooshi khwiiya awoova, hapari epile khumwazeyela nti wooshi wa nnyaako wa Yudeya.
Atthu ooshi aasiiliyeeyo khusala oopuwela oozelanaka yoori: “Mwaana aya otu onttela wiiya paani?” Nkhono wa Mbwana ori vamote na-ye.
Zakariiya paapa wa mwaana otule, khumwiitaala Rooho Ttakatthiifu khwaaza olaleya mattakhuzi a Nnyizinku araka:
“Asifwiwe Mbwana Nnyizinku, Nluku wa Ezirayeele, ateeliyeeyo owaawuni na owaataphula atthu awe.
Nnyizinku aninkha nusura yookhomaala khwa ojama wa karumeyaawe mfwalume Daawuuda,
nkhama aalupiyeezo rakuzeene khwa manapiyu awe oottakatthiifu.
Ye aanaahitiye onuusuru nkatthi wa maatuwi etthu, anitaphulaka mmakhono wa apale aniiphiiriwaaye ti fweyo,
awaathoonyezaka huruma amarehemu apapazetthu, na oopuwelaka wahati woottakatthiifu aarettiyeeyo na-yo.
Na olapha aalaphisaniyeeyo na marehemu papeetthu Eburahiima,
alaphaka yoori aari oteela onoopola mmakhono wa maatuwi etthu, yoori ninrumeyele Ye woohoovi,
woottakatthifuvo na washariyavo omaasho wawe siikhu zooshi zoohaayi etthu.
Weeyo mwanaka onteela wiitthiwa oriwa napiyu wa Nnyizinku Nwulu wa Pinkuuni, onttela wiiya namalokozisiwa wa Mbwana yoori omwaattalelele tarikhi zawe,
owaalaleyelaka atthu awe nusura entaaye khwa nswammaha wa twampi zaya,
maana Nnyizinku etthu ti wa huruma. Onteela othoonyeza nuuru yawe vakatthi vetthu,
ewaamwasikhele apale ari n'yiiza na vamwiivuuli woofwa, yoori eneettettise ntarikhi ya heeri.”
Mwaana otule khuvira awulaka na rooho yawe khusala ekhomaala, khwiikhala makuluttu mpakha siikhu apuweleliyeevo vakatthi wa atthu a Ezirayeele.
Wakathi aya opo Seezari Akuushitu mfwalume nwulu, aarumiye yoori atthu ooshi apale a nkatthi woofwalume wa Rooma aarina yoolawa waatikhiwa nwarakha ya afwalume.
Waatikhiwa opo wamwanzo waarettikhaniye Kureeniyo ari mfwalume wa Siiriya.
Wakhula ntthu khusala alawa nti aavokoliweewo olawa waatikhiwa.
Yuusufu na-ye khulankha Kalileya sitati ya Nazareeti, khusala alawa Yudeya sitati ya Belemu ottuukho aavokoliweewo wa mfwalume Daawuuda. Ye eetteliye waatikhiwa maana aari woojama wa Daawuuda.
Aalawiye na mposaawe Mariyamu ari wa wiimittha.
Siikhu zaya epo ari Belemu ottuukhule, Mariyamu khumfiyela siikhu zoopattha ekumi.
Khumpattha mwaana w'oomwanzo awe wanlume, khumputaputela vakuwo, khunttattikhela nkashothi zaari ojaamo nyama, mwaasa yoori khaarina puuro yoomaka.
Nti otthuupule aariwo amakhampuzi aari wiikhalaaye ntthuttu ashukisaka pwittipwitthi zaya na weekesela osikhu wooshi.
Nlayikha la Mbwana khwiishukhela attaaphale aariivo amakhampuzi apale. Nuuru ya Mbwana khuwaamwasikhela, khwiiya awoova channu.
Ila nlayikha ntthile khuwooza yoori: “Mwihoove! Miiyo kateela owuuzani hapari zooshapweya za furaha khuluyeene, enttelaaye wiiya ya atthu ooshi.
Leelo ethiiti, sitati ya Daawuuda mwavokoleliwa Namuusuru eeyiye Al-Masiihu, Mbwana.
Alama yenu ti eto: mwininsikana mwaana aputaputeliwe vakuwo, attattikheliwe nkashothi enjakaamo nyama.”
Nasaapiru khupuwa malayikha a waatta, khuphakanyeya na ntthile lamwanzo, khusala ansifu Nnyizinku araka:
“Asifwiwe Nnyizinku otulu, na vathi apha heeri yiiye vamote na atthu ooshi awaatakheliyeeyo osaana.”
Wakathi malayikha apale aruteliyeevo pinkuuni, amakhampuzi khuuzana yoori: “Nlaweni Belemu noone etthu erettikhaniyeewo, etile Mbwana anuuziyeeyo.”
Yo khuhirupazi, khulawa khunsikana Mariyamu na Yuusufu na mwaana otule attattikheliwe nkashothi zinjakaamo nyama.
N'oomoona mwaana otule, yo khusala alupa epile ooziweezo ti nlayikha monkoni wa Ye.
Ooshi apale aasiiliyeeyo hapari aari olupaaye amakhampuzi apale, khwiiya ooshanka.
Ila Mariyamu aatthiiye varoho vawe vitthu epile aari osiilaazo, khusala apheleleza maana aya.
Paata ya toole, amakhampuzi apale khurutela ntthuttu anttitthimisaka Nnyizinku na ansifwaka khwa zooshi aasiiliyeezo na ooniiyeezo, etthiipile nlayikha laawooziyeezo.
N'oofiya siikhu naane, mwaana otule khukhiriyisiwa, khutthajiwa nzina la Yinsa, nttintthile aalupiyeeyo nlayikha ahineemitthiwe.
N'oovira siikhu zootwahareshiwa Mariyamu na Yuusufu, nkhama etthiipo zaari olupaazo kano za napiyu Munsa, khunthuula mwaana otule khunlawana Yeruzaleemu yoori enkheleliwe mmakhono wa Mbwana
maana yaatikhiwa nkano wa Mbwana yoori: “Mwaana wamwanzo wanlume ona yoophakuliwa khwinkhiwa Mbwana.”
Yuusufu na Mariyamu khwinkha twaha nkhama etthiipo zinrumaazo kano za Mbwana: “makhoko mawiri ama jiwa piiri.”
Wakathi aya opo Yeruzaleemu aariwo mwinyi mmote aari wiitthiwaaye Simiyooni, aari wa shariya na woomoova Nnyizinku. Ye aari owejela wuusurwiwa wa atthu a Ezirayeele. Rooho Ttakatthiifu yaari vamote na-ye
na khunthoonyeza yoori khaari ofwa ahimooneeni Al-Masiihu wa Mbwana.
Simiyooni khweetta Nnyupa wa Nnyizinku alokoziwe ti Rooho Ttakatthiifu, wakathi apapaze antaniyeevo Yinsa yoori aretteliwe etile yaalupiweeyo nkano,
Simiyooni khunthuula mwaana otule mmakhono mwawe khunshukhurwela Nnyizinku araka:
“Mbwanaaka, aphano kimfwa na heeri maana yarettikhana etile waahitiyeeyo.
Koona nusura yawo
owaattaleleliyeeyo atthu ooshi.
Ye nuuru yoomwaasikhela khapila zooshi za amalapo na siifwa ya atthu awe a Ezirayeele.”
Papaawe na mamaawe khwiiya ooshanka mwaasa wa mattakhuzi apale aari onlupezaaye Simiyooni mwaana otule.
Simiyooni khuwaaparikhiya, khumuuza Mariyamu maama wa mwaana yoori: “Mwaana otu Nnyizinku anthawula yoori atthu awaatta a Ezirayeele ajikwise ama awoosuru. Ye alama ya Nnyizinku ila atthu a waatta anlawa ankatthale.
Mwaasa wa ethiito, wuupuwela wa nroho wa atthu a waatta onteela osaruwa; weeyo Mariyamu enteela wuupattha huzuni khuluyeene nkhama phanka yoonoliwa yoori eshije nafusi yawo.”
Attaaphale aarivo sharifwa mmote aari wiitthiwaaye Aana. Aari mwaana wa Fwanuweele wa lihimo la Asheeri, aari wa wuuluvala. Eekhalaniye mannawe nyaakha sapa,
paata yomfwela mannawe, khuhiraliwi mpakha opattha nyaakha thamaaniini na mine. Khaari olaamo Nnyupa wa Nnyizinku nthana na osikhu, khaazi yawe yaari omwaaputu Nnyizinku ofuka na olompa.
Wakathi otthuupo khwaaza onshukhurwela Nnyizinku attakhulaka monkoni wa mwaana otule, awoozaka atthu ooshi apale aari owejelaaye wookhowa wa Yeruzaleemu.
Yuusufu na Mariyamu nawiisha oretta zooshi epile zaari orumaazo kano ya Mbwana, khurutela Kalileya sitati ya Nazareeti owaya.
Mwaana khusala awula saaneene na khwiiya njuwi nwulweene, rehema ya Nnyizinku yaari vamote na-ye.
Wakhula mwaakha Mariyamu na Yuusufu aari weettaka Yeruzaleemu onjampo la Paashikowa.
Wakathi Yinsa apatthiyeevo nyaakha khumi na miwiri, Mariyamu na Yuusufu khulankha khusala alawa onjampo la Paashikowa nkhama etthiipile aazowereliyeezo, alawaka anthuuliye Yinsa.
N'oofiya khuretta njampo ntthile khwiisha, khusala arutela owaya. Yinsa khusala Yeruzaleemu, mamaawe na papaawe woohijuwi.
Yo aari woona yoori ori khuntti etile yaari orutelaaye onti, khuvira siikhu ntero eettaka weettetta, aphano khwaaza omweekesa awoozelaka ajamaaze na ashirikhaawe.
Khuhisala ampattha, khurutela Yeruzaleemu olawa omweekesa.
Eviriyeevo siikhu ttatthu, khunsikana ari Nnyupa wa Nnyizinku eekhaliye na anamasomisa awulu a tiini eettaka onsiila na omuuzela.
Ooshi apale aari onsiilaaye khunshankela mwaasa woojuwa wawe na nanna aari owaajipwaazo.
Aphano apapaze n'oomoona khushanka, mamaawe khumuuzela araka: “Mwanaka! Niini epi oniretteliyeezo? Miiyo na papaawo naari wa wantipweya naaza raku oweekesa.”
Ye khujipu yoori: “Mwaari okeekesela-ni? Khamwaari ojuwa yoori miiyo kaarina ya wiiya Nnyupa wa Paapa?”
Yo khuhiweeleyi etthu aari olupaaye.
Yinsa khurutela nti wa Nazareeti na papaawe na mamaawe khusala awaashututela. Mamaawe aari oretta athokorelaka vitthu epile zooshi nroho mwawe.
Yinsa khusala avira awulaka nkatthi wa ojuwa, hirimu na nrehema ya Nnyizinku na atthu.
Mwaakha wakhuumi na thaanu Seezari Tibeeriyu ari mfwalume nwulu wa Rooma, Pontiyu Pilaatu ari liwaali wa Yudeya. Herooti ari nsatoro wa Kalileya na ttwiiye Filiipe na-ye ari wa Itureeya na Tarakhoniiti, Lusaaniya ari nsatoro wa Abileeni.
Anaasi na Khayiifwa aari mahaakhimu awulu a tiini. Mwaakha aya pi otthuupo enkhiweeyo mattakhuzi a Nnyizinku Yaahaya mwaana wa Zakariiya makuluttu.
Ye khuzukulela miti zooshi zaattameliyeeyo muuttho Yorotaani, awoozaka atthu yoori athupwiye twampi zaya aswaamihiwe ti Nnyizinku na oosiwe.
Nkhama etthiipo zaatikhiweezo nkithaapu ya napiyu Ezayiiya: “Owaapho ntthu ankhuwaaye n'yaara araka: ‘Mwaattalele tarikhi ya Mbwana, na mwishapweyise miphiitelo zaya.
Makunte ooshi asireliwe, nyaako na kulu zooshi zipwejiwe, tarikhi zoonyokowa zookoleliwe, epile zoothipeya zishottheliwe.
Atthu ooshi anteela woona nusura ya Nnyizinku.’”
Yaahaya khusala awooza atthu apale aari otaaye woosiwa araka: “Khapila za nyookha! Paani awuuziyeenini otthira hukhumu ya Nnyizinku entaaye?
Mwirette vitthu enthoonyezaaye yoori khweele mwathupwiya, khahiyo ojilupeza yoori ‘Eburahiima ti papeetthu’. Miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori khwa liwe ntthi Nnyizinku onwahi owaattala aana a Eburahiima.
Nshokha latthiiwa nshini wa mitathaari za miitthi, wakhula muutthi ohiniimaaye mishumo zooshapweya ontta oshijiwa weeseleliwe vamoottho.”
Atthu khusala amuuzela araka: “Apho nirette niini?”
Ye khuwaajipu yoori: “Otule ariina hempe piiri, moote amwinkhe otule ahina. Otule ariina etthu-yoojiwa awaameele apale ahina.”
Khulankha anamariphisa lumpuru yoori alawe oosiwe khumuuzela Yaahaya yoori: “Mwanliimu, khi fweeyo nirette niini?”
Ye khuwaajipu araka: “Mwihiriphise mwizitisa hisapu mwirumiweeyo.”
Anajanka na-yo khumuuzela yoori: “Khi fweeyo niri toovi?” Khuwaajipu yoori: “Mwihiwaanyakanye atthu mwiroromelaka kuvu zenu, wala mwihiwaalokoveze vitthu zoohiiyi etthiipo, mwishukhurwele ethiito mwimpatthaaye.”
Nroromelo wa atthu khusala ovira weekezeleyaka oonaka yoori Yaahaya ti Al-Masiihu.
Ye khuwooza ooshi apale aariivo yoori: “Weekhweele miiyo kiniwoosanani maati, ila onta nkina ariina owahi wookiziti miiyo, wala akinsuhi ofukula mikhoyi za jampala zawe. Ye onteela owoosani na Rooho Ttakatthiifu na moottho.
Onaaye fosholo mmakhono mwawe anttelaaye ophakulana tiriku na maveya. Athuule tiriku atthe vantthala vawe, maveya aya eeselele vamoottho ohinzimaaye.”
Khwa mattakhuzi makina a waatta, Yaahaya aari owaahirimiza na owaatafusirela atthu hapari zooshapweya.
Na khunshowera nsatoro Herooti mwaasa wonrala Herodiya muukha wa ttwiiye na oretta vitthu zootakhala za waatta.
Elottelanaka Herooti khweekezela zooshi epile, khuruma ofukeliwa Yaahaya nkalapooso.
Wakathi Yaahaya aari owoosaavo atthu ooshi apale, Yinsa na-ye khuta attaaphale oteela woosiwa. Ye alompaka pinku khufukuwa,
Rooho Ttakatthiifu khumwiishukhela nkhama jiwa. Khusiileya huula yoolankha pinkuuni eraka: “Weeyo o mwanaka kinuuphetachaaye na wookituvela channu.”
Yinsa wakathi aaziyeevo olaleya hapari zooshapweya, aarettiye arina nyaakha talaathiini. Ye aari mwaana wa Yuusufu nkhama etthiipo atthu aari waakanyeraazo, Yuusufu aari mwaana wa Heeli,
Heeli aari mwaana wa Mataati, Mataati aari mwaana wa Leevi, Leevi aari mwaana wa Melikhi, Melikhi aari mwaana wa Yanaayi, Yanaayi aari mwaana wa Yuusufu.
Yuusufu aari mwaana wa Matathiiya, Matathiiya aari mwaana wa Amooshi, Amooshi aari mwaana wa Nahuumu, Nahuumu aari mwaana wa Heshiili, Heshiili aari mwaana wa Nakhaayi,
Nakhaayi aari mwaana wa Maathi, Maathi aari mwaana wa Matathiiya, Matathiiya aari mwaana wa Shemeeni, Shemeeni aari mwaana wa Yosheekhi, Yosheekhi aari mwaana wa Yuuda,
Yuuda aari mwaana wa Yohanaani, Yohanaani aari mwaana wa Reesa, Reesa aari mwaana wa Zorobabeeli, Zorobabeeli aari mwaana wa Sheyalitiyeeli, Sheyalitiyeeli aari mwaana wa Neeri,
Neeri aari mwaana wa Meelikhi, Meelikhi aari mwaana wa Aadi, Aadi aari mwaana wa Kosaamu, Kosaamu aari mwaana wa Elimadaamu, Elimadaamu aari mwaana wa Eeri,
Eeri aari mwaana wa Yoshuwa, Yoshuwa aari mwaana wa Eliyezeeri, Eliyezeeri aari mwaana wa Yoriimu, Yoriimu aari mwaana wa Mathaati, Mathaati aari mwaana wa Leevi,
Leevi aari mwaana wa Simiyooni, Simiyooni aari mwaana wa Yuuda, Yuuda aari mwaana wa Yuusufu, Yuusufu aari mwaana wa Yonaamu, Yonaamu aari mwaana wa Eliyakhiimu,
Eliyakhiimu aari mwaana wa Meleeya, Meleeya aari mwaana wa Meena, Meena aari mwaana wa Matatha, Matatha aari mwaana wa Nathaani, Nathaani aari mwaana wa Daawuuda,
Daawuuda aari mwaana wa Yeese, Yeese aari mwaana wa Obeedi, Obeedi aari mwaana wa Bowaazi, Bowaazi aari mwaana wa Salimooni, Salimooni aari mwaana wa Nashooni,
Nashooni aari mwaana wa Aminadabu, Aminadabu aari mwaana wa Adimiini, Adimiini aari mwaana wa Ariini, Ariini aari mwaana wa Hesherooni, Heshorooni aari mwaana wa Pereezi, Pereezi aari mwaana wa Yuuda,
Yuuda aari mwaana wa Yaakhumpa, Yaakhumpa aari mwaana wa Esiyaakha, Esiyaakha aari mwaana wa Eburahiima, Eburahiima aari mwaana wa Teera, Teera aari mwaana wa Nahoori.
Nahoori aari mwaana wa Serukhi, Serukhi aari mwaana wa Reewu, Reewu aari mwaana wa Peleekhi, Peleekhi aari mwaana wa Ebeeri, Ebeeri aari mwaana wa Saala,
Saala aari mwaana wa Kayinaamu, Kayinaamu aari mwaana wa Arifwakisaati, Arifwakisaati aari mwaana wa Sheemu, Sheemu aari mwaana wa Nuuhi, Nuuhi aari mwaana wa Lameekhi,
Lameekhi aari mwaana wa Methusaleemu, Methusaleemu aari mwaana wa Henookhi, Henookhi aari mwaana wa Yareeti, Yareeti aari mwaana wa Mahalaleeli, Mahalaleeli aari mwaana wa Kayinaamu.
Kayinaamu aari mwaana wa Enooshi, Enooshi aari mwaana wa Seethi, Seethi aari mwaana wa Adamu, Adamu wa Nnyizinku.
Yinsa aarutiye omuttho Yorotaani ari wa wiitaala Rooho Ttakatthiifu, aalokoziwe ti Rooho Ttakatthiifu ethiito mpakha makuluttu.
Nttumpho khuzayiniwa ti Sheethwani siikhu arupayiini. Siikhu zaya epile khaari oja etthu, nawiisha khunkhola jala.
Sheethwani khumuuza yoori: “Nkhama o mwaana wa Nnyizinku orume liwe nttho lithatuwe liiye phaawu.”
Ila Yinsa khunjipu araka: “Yaatikhiwa nkithaapu yoori: ‘Khahiyo phaawu paasi enimwinkhaaye ohaayi pinaatamu’.”
Sheethwani khunweza vatulu, nasaapiru khunnoza ofwalume wooshi w'oolumwenku.
Khumuuza yoori: “Kintta owinkha ofwalume na siifwa z'oolumwenku opu wooshi, mwaasa yoori zooshi kenkhiwa miiyo, na miiyo kinimwinkha otule kinintakhelaaye.
Amana okikokhorela miiyo na khukaaputu, zooshi zintta wiiya zaawo.”
Yinsa khunjipu yoori: “Nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku lalupa yoori: ‘Omwaaputu Mbwanaawo Nnyizinku na onrumeyele othuuto paasi.’”
Aphano Sheethwani khunlawana Yeruzaleemu khunweza vatulu woolepavo wa Nyuupa ya Nnyizinku khumuuza yoori: “Nkhama o mwaana wa Nnyizinku ojeeselele vathi aphale,
maana yaatikhiwa nkithaapu yoori: ‘Ye ontta oruma malayikha awe awiinanele.
Atthaapo antta wuukholelela na makhono aya yoori ohikwakwanttuwe valiwe.’”
Yinsa khunjipu yoori: “Nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku lalupa yoori: ‘Ohimweeze Mbwana Nnyizinku awo.’”
Sheethwani nawiisha onzayini wooshi, khumwaattuwa khusala awejela wakathi wonkhweyela.
Aphano Yinsa khurutela Kalileya, owahi wa Rooho Ttakatthiifu ori vamote na-ye. Hapari zaari olupaaye monkoni wa ye khumwazeyela miti zooshi za nkerekhere.
Aari osomisa mmanyupa woosifwiwamo Nnyizinku, atthu ooshi khusala anttottopela.
Khulawa mpakha sitati ya Nazareeti ohali aleliweewo. Siikhu ya saapatu khweetta nnyupa woosifwiwamo Nnyizinku nkhama etthiipo aazowereliyeezo. Khulankha yoori asome.
Khwinkhiwa kithaapu ya napiyu Ezaaya. Khufunula khusala athola khusikana vahali yaatikhiweevo yoori:
“Rooho ya Mbwana eri vamote na-miyo, akithawaza yoori kiwaatafusirele hapari zooshapweya asikhini na olaleya otaphuliwa wa anamahuzunikha, owoonisa apale oohooni, owaavumulisa apale oohukhumwiwa,
na olaleya yoori wafiya mwaakha wa rehema ya Mbwana.”
Yinsa khufinikha kithaapu etile khumwinkha karumeya wa nnyupa woosifwiwamo Nnyizinku, Ye khwiikhala. Atthu ooshi apale aariimo khusala amweekesa.
Ye khuwooza yoori: “Leelo zarettikhana epile zaatikhiweeyo, etthiipi mwinttaaye wiisharu osiila.”
Atthu ooshi khusala anttottopela, na khwiiya ootikinisiwa mwaasa wa mattakhuzi a rehema aari olankhaaye nkhanyo mwawe, khusala oozelana yoori: “Khahi mwaana wa Yuusufu otu?”
Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Khweele khweele mweeyo mwinlawa mwakuuze kittaphi mmote enraaye toono: ‘Tothoro ojivonise omweenyewe! Orette mmuti mwawo mphu minjuza nisiiliyeeyo epile orettiyeezo Kafwaranawu.’”
Khulupa theenya yoori: “Wookhweele kiniwuuzani yoori khaavo napiyu mmote ankhupaliwaaye mmuti mwawe.
Na weekhwele wakathi wa napiyu Aliyaasi, Ezirayeele aariwo aakha oofweliwa pi amanna zaya wakathi yaafukiweevo pinku nyaakha mittatthu na nyeezi sitha, yaapuwiye jala miti zooshi.
Ila Nnyizinku khuhinrumi Aliyaasi Ezirayeele, okhule aari wiikhalaawo apale aya, khunruma Sarefathi tuniya ya Sitooni aariiwo muukha mmote woofweliwa ti mannawe.
Siikhu za napiyu Elizeewu, Ezirayeele aariwo anamakuttula a waatta, khuhiivo hatha mmote aavonisiweeyo ila Naamani wa nti wa Siiriya ti ye aavonisiweeyo otthwe.”
Atthu ooshi aari nnyupa woosifwiwamo Nnyizinku, n'oosiila mattakhuzi apale aari olupaaye Yinsa yo khwiiphiiriwa.
Khwiikariwamo nsitati mphule khulawaniwa vamwaako yaajekiweevo sitati yaya etile, yoori ansukhumele vathi.
Ila Yinsa khuvira vakatthi vaya khusala alawa.
Paata ya toole Yinsa khwiishukhela sitati ya Kafwaranawu, nti wa Kalileya, khusala awaanozela siikhu ya saapatu.
Yo aari ooshankisiwa na onozela wawe, mwaasa yoori nttakhuzi lawe laarina ofwalume.
Nnyupa woosifwiwamo Nnyizinku aarimo ntthu mmote aariina sheethwani. Aphano sheethwani khunyakula na kuvu zawe zooshi araka:
“Eeee! Onnitakhela-ni weeyo Yinsa wa Nazareeti? Wateela onankameza? Miiyo kinuujuwa weeyo yoori o Ttakatthiifu wa Nnyizinku!”
Yinsa ansukisiye sheethwani araka: “Nyamala, mwaattuwe ntthu oto!” Attaaphale sheethwani khunkwisela vathi ntthu otule atthu eettaka omoona, khuhinvulalisi khumwaattuwa.
Atthu ooshi aari ooshankisiwa, khusala oozana atthaaporu: “Nttakhuzi-ni ntthi? Khwa ofwalume na owahi wawe otu onruma masheethwani khusaruwa!”
Aphano siifwa ya Yinsa yaamwazeyeliye miti zooshi za nkerekhere.
Yinsa khusaruwamo nnyupa woosifwiwamo Nnyizinku khweetta owawe Simawu. Nkhwewe Simawu aari nlwele hooma, yo khunvekelaza Yinsa yoori anvonise.
Ye khwiinama khwiikara hooma etile khunlikha, nasaapiru nunu otule khulankha khusala awaarumeyela.
Njuwa litupweelaka atthu ooshi apale aariina marati khusala atiiseliwa Yinsa, Ye n'oowaattheela makhono n'oowaavonisa.
Theenya aarivo atthu a waatta aari owaasaruwaaye masheethwani anyakulaka araka: “Weeyo o mwaana wa Nnyizinku!” Yinsa khusala amaruwa alikhisaka masheethwani apale ottakhula, maana yo aari ojuwa yoori ye ti Al-Masiihu.
N'oocha Yinsa khulankha khusala alawa mmakuluttu. Atthu a waatta khusala amweekesa, n'onsikana khuhisala atakha onlikha olawa.
Ye khuwooza yoori: “Enhithajiya theenya miiyo olawa sitati kiina olaleya hapari zoofwalume wa Nnyizinku, kaperekheliwa etthiipo.”
Ye aari otafusiri mmanyupa woosifwiwamo Nnyizinku a Yudeya.
Siikhu moote, Yinsa aari nshini wa ntthatta la Kalileya, khuzukuleliwa pi atthu a waatta yoori asiile nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku.
Ye khoona nyaatiya miwiri ziri vapatari wa ntthatta nttintthile, zaalikhiweevo pi anamajiya aari woosaaye matthavi aya.
Yinsa khupakhira mmwaatiya mmote waari wa Simawu khunvekela yoori asusisele mpahari, khwiikhala khusala awaanozela atthu.
Nawiisha onozela khumuuza Simawu yoori: “Othuule mwaatiya awo mwilawe vahali wa wiichavo mwajiye.”
Simawu ajipwaka khuri: “Mbwana, najiya osikhu na osikhu khuhipatthi etthu, wiiya walupa yoori neese, nintta weesa.”
Yo khulawa khweesa matthavi aya khuula swi za waatta mpakha khusala avaruwa matthavi aya.
Khuwaakhuwela ashirikhaaya aari mwaatiya nkina yoori ate arinkaanyele, khwiitaaza nyaatiya zaya zoomiwiri mpakha osaleela ozama.
Simawu Peeturu nawoona etthu etile yaarettikhaniyeeyo, khunkokhorela Yinsa amuuzaka yoori: “Mbwana, okisuse maana miiyo ki natwampi.”
Simawu na ashirikhaawe khuzinkuwa mwaasa wa swi epile za waatta apatthiyeezo.
Yaakhumpa na Yaahaya, aana a Zebedayo, ashirikha a Simawu aari ojiyanaaye khwiiya ootikinisiwa. Aphano Yinsa khumuuza Simawu yoori: “Ohoove, waaza nasaapi eti onttela wiiya namajiya wa atthu.”
Khuwelelisa nyaatiya zaya nkulu, khulikha vitthu zaya zooshi khusala anlotta Yinsa.
Yinsa ari sitati moote, khuvira mwinyi mmote aariina makuttula. N'oomoona Yinsa khukokhora khusijiti khumuuza araka: “Kinuuvekela yoori nkhama watakha Mbwanaaka, kivonise.”
Ye khookola nkhono awe khunsapa khumuuza yoori: “Katakha vona!” Wakathi otthuupule khweele khuvona.
Yinsa khumuuza yoori: “Vitthu epi ohimuuze hatha ntthu, ila olawe wajithoonyeze wa haakhimu wa tiini, othuuto oorettele twaha yoovonisiwa wawo nkhama etthiipile alupiyeezo napiyu Munsa, yoori wiiye oshaahiti vakatthi wa atthu aya apale.”
Aphano hapari zawe zaari ovira zimwazeyaka. Atthu a waatta khusala ata oteela osiila hapari, na oteela ovonisiwa marati aya.
Yinsa aari olaakavo n'oolawa makuluttu olompa.
Siikhu moote Yinsa eetta onozela, apho vaya aari onozelaavo aarivo mafwarizeewu na anamanozela a kano aalankhiyeeyo miti mikina za Kalileya na Yudeya mpakha Yeruzaleemu. Owahi wa Mbwana waari vamote na-ye woowaavonisa alwele.
Aphano atthu akina khuntana mwinyi aariina supiyaani anttattikheliye vanrepa, yo aari otakha omphenyisa ampwehe omaasho wa Yinsa.
Ila nawoona yoori khayiivo kiphenyo mwaasa wa atthu waatta, khuwela vatulu wa nyuupa khutamula liphala khumwiishushela vakatthi wa atthu omaasho wa Yinsa.
Ye nawoona amini aariina atthu apale, khumuuza nasupiyaani otule yoori: “Swaahipu twampi zawo zaswaamihiwa.”
Aphano mafwarizeewu na anamanozela a kano khusala attettha araka: “Otu aya paani ankufurwaaye? Ti paani anwahaaye oswaamihi twampi woohiiyi Nnyizinku?”
Yinsa khujuwa etthu aari ofikhiraaye, khuwoozela yoori: “Mwashukulikhela-ni nroho mwenu?
Yookhweya ti tiivi omuuza yoori twampi zawo za swaamihiwa ama yoori olankhe weettette?
Apho mwijuwe yoori Mwaana wa Pinaatamu onaaye owahi wooswaamihi twampi vathi apha.” Khumuuza nasupiyaani otule yoori: “Olankhe othuule nrepa lawo olawe owawo.”
Nasaapiru ntthu otule khulankha vakatthi wa atthu khuthuula nrepa lawe ntthile aattattikheliweevo khusala alawa owawe ansifwaka Nnyizinku.
Atthu ooshi aariivo khwiiya ooshanka na woova channu, khusala ansifu Nnyizinku araka: “Leelo noona vitthu zootikinisa.”
Paata yawiisha vitthu epile, Yinsa khulankha khusala alawa, khunsikana mwinyi mmote aari oriphisaaye lumpuru aari wiitthiwaaye Leevi eekhaliye vahali aari oriphisaavo malumpuru awe, khumuuza yoori: “Okilotte.”
Ye khulikha khaazi zawe zooshi khusala anlotta.
Leevi khuretta njampo liwululene owawe vamote na Yinsa, aarivo theenya anamariphisa lumpuru akinoko aya na atthu akina eekhaliye vamote na-ye.
Mafwarizeewu na anamanozela a kano khusala a waattakhula anakhiyoni a Yinsa araka: “Mwaasa aya niini mweeyo mwijanaka na mwinywanaka anamariphisa malumpuru na anatwampi?”
Yinsa khuwaajipu araka: “Akumi khanlawaniwa wa tothoro ila alwele,
miiyo akaawaateeliye anashariya kaawaateeliye anatwampi yoori alikhe oretta twampi.”
Atthu akina khumuuza Yinsa yoori: “Anakhiyoni a Yaahaya Namoosa na anakhiyoni a mafwarizeewu amfuka na anlompa, ila awo weeyo khamfuka, antta oja na onywa.”
Yinsa khuwaajipu yoori: “Enrettikhana toovi owooza anamalaleyiwa harusi ofuka namaposa arivo?
Ila onteela ofiya wakathi mposi anttelaaye olaziwavo vakatthi vaya, wakathi aya opo, anteela ofuka.”
Elottelanaka Yinsa khulupa nlikaniso mmote araka: “Khaavo anshijaaye patakha ya kuwo pheeya yoori arette yaapa ya kuwo yoovutta, n'ooretta toowo etile pheeya entta oharipweya, mwaasa wa patakha etile ya kuwo pheeya etthiiweevo oheezani na etile yoovutta.
Khaavo anthuulaaye viinyu pheeya ottha nttompwiyo ya shapala ya raku. N'ooretta toowo entta ophutuwa, viinyu ya yiittikhe ttompwiyo zaya ziharipweye.
Viinyu pheeya entthiiwa nttompwiyo pheeya.
Khaavo anraaye anywiye viinyu ya raku khutakha onywa viinyu pheeya, maana ontta olupa yoori: ‘Poora etile ya raku.’”
Saapatu moote, Yinsa eetta ovira nshini wa nshapa la tiriku. Anakhiyoni awe khusala avurula asusuraka na makhono arafunaka phunje zaya.
Mafwarizeewu khusala awoozela yoori: “Mwaasa aya niini mwirettaka vitthu ziiyiye mwiikho orettiwa saapatu?”
Ye khuwaajipu araka: “Khamwinasome etthu aarettiyeeyo Daawuuda wakathi yankholiyeevo jala na ashirikha awe?
Ye aaviriye Nnyupa wa Nnyizinku khuthuula phaawu zoohalaalishiwa khurafuna kiina khuwenkha ashirikhaawe, ila alupa aarina ruhusa yoorafuna aari mahaakhimu a tiini paasi.”
Yinsa khulupa araka: “Mwaana wa pinaatamu ti Mbwana mwennyewe saapatu.”
Saapatu kiina, Yinsa khuvira nnyupa woosifwiwamo Nnyizinku khusala awaanozela, aarimo mwinyi mmote waarakaliyeeyo nkhono nlume.
Anamanozela a kano na mafwarizeewu eetta omweekesela yoori amoone Yinsa nkhama aari onvonisa siikhu ya saapatu, yoori ankwisele paathuli.
Ila ye aari ojuwa etthu aari wuupuwelaaye atthu apale. Khumuuza mwinyi otule woorakala nkhono nlume yoori: “Olankhe ote vakatthi apha.” Mwinyi khulankha khweemela.
Aphano Yinsa khuwoozela yoori: “Ensuhaaye orettiwa saapatu ti tiivi? Yooshapweya ama yootakhala, wuusuru ama wuula?”
Khuweekesa atthu ooshi apale aariivo khumuuza mwinyi otule yoori: “Wookole nkhono awo.” Ye khookola, khuvona.
Anamanozela a kano na mafwarizeewu khwiiphiiriwa khusala awaza etthu yonrettela Yinsa.
Siikhu zaya epile Yinsa khulankha khusala alawa omwaako olompa, khwiisha osikhu wooshi eettaka olompa.
N'oocha khuwaakhuwela anakhiyoni awe khuwaathawula khumi na awiri, atthaapo theenya khuwenkha nzina la owaaswihaapa.
Simawu antthajiye nzina la Pheeturu, Antere ttwiiye Simawu, Yaakhumpa, Yaahaya, Filiipe, Paturumeewu.
Mateewuzhu, Tome, Yaakhumpa mwaana wa Alufayo na Simawu aniitthiwaaye Zelooti,
Yuuda mwaana wa Yaakhumpa, na Yuuda Iskariyooti otule aari weettelaaye onkholisa Yinsa.
Yinsa khwiishukha vamwaako na maaswihaapa awe khweemela nshini wa mwaakho vahali aariivo anakhiyoni awe na khuntti ya atthu a Yudeya yooshi na a Yeruzaleemu, mpakha apale a miti za waattamela pahari, Tiiro na Sitooni.
Apale aateeliyeeyo osiila na ovonisiwa moolwele aya, mpakha na apale aari wantipwiwaaye ti masheethwani aari ovonisiwa.
Atthu ooshi aari otakha onsapa Yinsa mwaasa yoori waari onsaruwa owahi khusala owaavonisa ooshi.
Aphano Yinsa khulansa maasho khuweekesa anakhiyoni awe khuwooza yoori: “Ananshapweyiwa ti mweyo mwiiyiye asikhini, maana Ofwalume wa Nnyizinku pu weenu.
Ananshapweyiwa ti mweyo enuukholaanini jala aphano, maana mwinlawa mwarupale. Ananshapweyiwa ti mweyo mwinlilaaye aphano, maana mwinteela otheya.
Ananshapweyiwa ti mweyo, mmana atthu eephiiriwaka ti mweyo, awiikarani, oottukhanani na khuwoonani ohifwayi mwaasa wonlotta Mwaana wa Pinaatamu.
Wakathi aya otthuupo, mwiiye woofurahi na mwitthape, maana tthuvo yenu eniiya khuluyeene pinkuuni. Maana wa nanna etthiipi, apapa zaya na-yo aawaaretteliye manapiyu.
Ila olaanikha pu weenu mweeyo mwaamathaajiri, maana mwapokhera tthuvo yenu vathi attaapha.
Olaanikha pu weenu mweeyo ziwiitaaleliyeenini vitthu-zoojiwa, maana mwinteela okholiwa ti jala. Olaanikha pu weenu mweeyo mwiriina furaha eleelo eti, maana mwinteela ojikhupanyera na olila.
Olaanikha pu weenu mweeyo mmana mwittottopeliwaka pi atthu ooshi, maana apapa zaya aawaaretteliye etthiipo manapiyu oojipanka.
Nakataalikha mweeyo mwinikisiilaaye, kiniwuuzani yoori mwiwaaphete maatuwi enu, mwiwaarettele saana apale aniiphiiriwaaye ti mweyo.
Mwiwaaparikhiye apale anuulaanaanini na mwiwaalompele apale anuurettelaanini zootakhala.
Nkhama ntthu oopwakula nlaku limote, na ntthi likina ontheteezele. Nkhama ntthu oovula juupa yawo, ohinkhattaze othuula hempe yawo.
Omwinkhe wakhula otule anuuvekelaaye, nkhama ntthu athuula etile yiiyiye yaawo, ohinkhanyarele wuurutisela.
Epile mweeyo zinuutuvelaanini oretteliwa pi azeenu, na-mweyo mwiwaarettele azeenu etthiipo.
Amana mwiwaaphetaka apale anuuphetaanini paasi, fwayita-ni mwineekeselaaye mmakhono wa Nnyizinku? Hatha anatwampi atthaapo aniwaapheta apale na-yo aniwaaphetaayo.
Amana mwiwaarettelaka saana apale na-yo anuurettelaanini saana paasi, fwayita-ni mwinteelaaye wiiyana? Hatha anatwampi atthaapo na-yo anretta etthiipo.
Amana mwiweepaashaka paasi apale mwinkhupalaaye wuurutiselani, fwayita-ni mwinteelaaye wiiyana? Hatha anatwampi atthaapo aniipaashana aroromelaka orutiselana.
Mwiwaaphete maatuwi enu, mwiwaarettele zooshapweya, mwiweepaashe mwiheekeselaka wuurutiselani. Toowo tthuvo yenu enttela wiiya khuluyeene na mwinttela wiiya aana a Nnyizinku Wooziti, maana Nnyizinku oniwaashapweyela rooho hatha na apale ahininshukhurwaaye na alupa ootakhala rooho.
Mwiiye woohurumiya nkhama etthiipi Papeenu wa pinkuuni na-ye eeyiye wa huruma.
Mwihimphuke ntthu nzeenu na Nnyizinku khanuuphukani, mwihinhukhumu ntthu nzeenu na Nnyizinku khanuuhukhumuni. Mwinswaamihi ntthu nzeenu na Nnyizinku ontta wuuswaamihini.
Mwiwenkhe azeenu na Nnyizinku ontta owinkhani: na mphimo khwaamili, wookhitteleliwa na wa wiitaala mpakha wiittikha. Maana mphimo otthuupo mwimphimanaaye na-mweyo mwinteela ophimeliwa otthuupo.”
Yinsa khulupa nlikaniso mmote araka: “Atthu oohooni khanlokozana, antta okwiselana nliphotto.
Nakhiyoni khaninziti mwanliimu awe, ila wakhula otule ansomiseyaaye saana oniiya nkhama mwanliimu awe.
Onri je woona etutu eriiye mmaasho wa nzaawo ohoonaka muutthi opule oriiye mmaasho mwawo?
Enrettikhana toovi weeyo omuuzaka nzaawo yoori: ‘Ttwiiyaku, nkankaani kuulaze etutu eto eriiye mmaasho mwawo,’ na khupe weeyo ohiwahaka woona muutthi opule oriiye mmaasho mwawo? Naafikhi! Olazemo khapula muutthi oriiye mmaasho mwawo, toowo ontta woona saana, na phi onlazaamo etutu eriiye mmaasho wa nzaawo.”
“Khawiivo muutthi wooshapweya oniimaaye mishumo zootakhala, wala muutthi wootakhala oniimaaye mishumo zooshapweya.
Maana wakhula muutthi onjuweya mwaasa wa mishumo zaya; nnyiiwa khinshumiwamo mishumo za muuyu, mmutthalala khanshumiwamo wuuva.
Ntthu wookemaani, nroho mwawe onsarulamo vitthu zooshapweya, na ntthu wootakhala rooho, nroho mwawe onsarulamo vitthu zootakhala, maana milomo zawe zinttakhula etthiipile ziitaaliyeeyo nroho mwawe.
Mwinkikhuwelela-ni yoori ‘Mbwana, Mbwana’, mwihirettaka epile kiniwuuzaanini?
Miiyo kinuuthoonyezani ntthu anlikananaaye otule ansiilaaye mattakhuzi aka na khushututela.
Onlikanana ntthu ajekaka nyuupa yawe khuthipa khwiichisa saaneene khutha vanchina la mawe woozivalavo. Khuta nnyeri khupiya nyuupa etile ila khuhisakhinyeyi mwaasa woozivalisiwa.
Ila otule ansiilaaye mattakhuzi aka khuhishututeli onlikanana ntthu ajekiye nyuupa yawe vanshaka woohizivalivo. Khuta nnyeri khupiya nyuupa etile nasaapiru khukwa, khupwecheya khuhisali hatha etthu.”
Eeshiyeevo mattakhuzi apale aari owoozaaye atthu, khweetta sitate ya Kafaranawu.
Ottuukho aariwo namalokozela mmote wa anajanka w'eerooma, aariina karumeyaawe wompheta aari olwaaziwaaye khusala asaleela ofwa.
Wakathi namalokozela wa anajanka otule asiiliyeevo monkoni wa Yinsa, khuwaaperekha attunkhulu akina amayaahuuti yoori anvekele Yinsa ate anvonise.
Yo n'onsikana khunvekela wookhanyarelavo araka: “Mwinyi oto onsuhi waawuniwa,
mwaasa yoori oniiya owaapheta atthu etthu na anijekela nyuupa yoosifwiwamo Nnyizinku.”
Aphano Yinsa khulankha khusala alawa vamote na-yo, asaleelaka ofiya, namalokozela otule khuwaaruma ashirikha awe olawa omuuza yoori: “Mbwana, ohijantipu khinsuhi weeyo ovira nnyupa mwaka.
Ti eto miiyo kinoona yoori akinsuhi okutthanana weeyo, ila olupe nttakhuzi limote paasi karumeyaaka ontta ovona.
Miiyo kinaaye afwalume akizitiyeeyo, ila na miiyo theenya kinaaye anajanka ankishututelaaye. Kinimuuza najanka mmote yoori: ‘Olawe’, khulawa; nkina yoori: ‘Aruti’, khuruti. Kinimuuza karumeyaaka yoori: ‘Retta eti’, ye khuretta.”
Yinsa asiiliyeevo mattakhuzi apale khwiiya wooshanka, khuzukuluwa khuwooza atthu apale aari omperekhaaye yoori: “Hatha Ezirayeele ottuukho akooneeniwo amini nkhama eti.”
Ashirikha apale aarumiweeyo khurutela owawe namalokozela otule, khunsikana karumeya otule avoniye.
Mmeesho mwaya Yinsa khulankha khusala alawa sitati ya Nayiini, anakhiyoni awe na khuntti ya atthu a waatta khusala enlotta.
Asaleelaka ofiya vanlako wa sitati etile, khusala asaruwa atthu aari weettelaaye ozikha. Otule aari weettelaaye ozikhiwa aari mwaana wa nunu mmote woofweliwa ti mannawe, ye aarina mwaana mmote othuuto paasi; atthu a waatta aari olawa vamote na-ye.
Wakathi Mbwana Yinsa amooniyeevo nunu otule, khumoonela huruma khunkhuwela khumuuza yoori: “Ohilile!”
Aphano khuwaasusela khusapa janaayiza, apale aathuuliyeeyo khweemela. Yinsa khulupa araka: “Shapu! Kinuuruma yoori olankhe!”
Shapu otule khulankha khwiikhala khusala attakhula; Yinsa khumwinkha mamaawe.
Atthu ooshi khwiiya awoova khusala ansifu Nnyizinku araka: “Napiyu nwulweene aniteela, ninoona yoori Nnyizinku aateeliye owuusuru atthu awe.”
Hapari epile za Yinsa khumwazeyela Yudeya yooshi mpakha miti epile zaattamananiyeeyo.
Yaahaya khuuziwa pi anakhiyoni awe vitthu epile zooshi. Ye khuwaakhuwela awiri,
khuwaaruma yoori alawe amuuzele Mbwana yoori: “Weeyo ti otu naari onwejaaye ama ninweje nkina?”
Yo khulawa mpakha ottuukhule aariiwo Yinsa khumuuza yoori: “Neetta orumiwa ti Yaahaya yoori nite niwuuzele nkhama otule naari onwejaaye ti weyo, ama nivire ninwejaka nkina?”
Wakathi otthuupule Yinsa khuwaavonisa alwele a waatta, anamarakala, apale aariina masheethwani, khuwaafunula maasho apale oohooni.
Aphano Yinsa khuwaajipu yoori: “Mwilawe mwamuuze Yaahaya etthiipo mooniyeezo na mwisiiliyeezo; apale oohooni antta woona, apale oorakala antta weettetta, anamakuttula antta otwahareshiwa, apale oohisiili ansiila, anamfwa asisimuliwa, na hapari zooshapweya antta olaleyeliwa asikhini.
Wooshapweyiwa ti otule ahiniphiiriwaaye ti miiyo.”
Anakhiyoni a Yaahaya n'oolaavo, Yinsa khusala owoozaka atthu monkoni wa Yaahaya yoori: “Makuluttu mweetteliye woona niini? Tteetthe yiinisiwaka ti pheevo?
Ama moona niini? Mwinyi mmote awaliye kuwo zooshapweya? Apale anwalaaye kuwo zootafikhana aniiya nraaha na aniikhala nkorofwa y'oofwalume.
Khi moona niini? Napiyu? Pi etthiipo kiniwuuzani yoori, Yaahaya awaaziti manapiyu akinoko aya.
Otu ti otule laari onlupaaye Nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku yoori: ‘Kinlawa kamperekhe karumeyaaka omaasho wawo yoori aattalele tarikhi yawo.’
Miiyo kiniwuuzani yoori vakatthi wa apale avokoliweeyo pi aakha, khina mmote anzitiyeeyo Yaahaya; ila otule eeyiye nttitthiiru muufwalume wa Nnyizinku, nwulweene zayita ye.”
Atthu ooshi mpakha anamariphisa lumpuru khusiila mattakhuzi a Yinsa. Yo khukhupalela shariya ya Nnyizinku, maana aari awoosiwa ti Yaahaya.
Ila mafwarizeewu na anamanozela a kano khukhijilela matakhelo a Nnyizinku khuhoosiwi ti Yaahaya.
“Anaatamu apa a leelo eti kiwaalattisane niini?
Alattanana khuntti ya asimaana eekhaliye vaparasa akhuwelanaka araka. ‘Fweeyo n'oovumiselani phivi za vaharusi mweeyo khuhiini; khwiipa liipo la huzuni mweeyo khuhilili.’
Khuta Yaahaya Namoosa woofuka na ahinnywaaye viinyu, mweeyo mwinri: ‘Ye onaaye masheethwani.’
Ata Mwaana wa Pinaatamu onja na onnywa, mweeyo mwinri: ‘Mmoone nsokho otu! Nanhapaliwa, nshirikha wa anamariphisa lumpuru na anatwampi.’
Apale anlottaaye ojuwa wa Nnyizinku, anthoonyeza yoori pi wookhweeli.”
Mfwarizeewu mmote anvekeliye Yinsa yoori alawe aje owawe. N'oofiya Yinsa khwiikhala yoori aje.
Omuuta otthuupule muukha mmote wa natwampi wa sitati ethiitile, khujuwa yoori Yinsa ontta oja wa mfwarizeewu, khuthuula suupha yawe ya mafuttha oonukhela.
Khulawa khweemela onyoko wa Yinsa nshini wa moolu awe khusala alila. Mishozi zawe khusala zittonkela moolu a Yinsa. Khusala akukuttha na nyuuli zawe na opejari moolu a Yinsa avaazaka mafuttha oonukhela.
Aphano mfwarizeewu otule nawoona vitthu epile khusala alupa nroho mwawe araka: “Otu eriwaka aari napiyu eetta ojuwa yoori mwanankha otu aninsapaaye natwampi.”
Yinsa khumuuza Simawu yoori: “Kintakha owuuza etthu.” Simawu khujipu yoori: “Kuuzeni mwanliimu.”
Yinsa khumuuza yoori: “Atthu awiri eetta wiiliwa nzurukhu ti mwinyi mmote aari wiipaashisakaaye, otu mmote aari wiiliwa miiya thaanu, otu nkina aari wiiliwa hamusiini.
Ila oowiiri khuhiivo mmote aawahiyeeyo onripha, ye khuwaaswaamihi oowiiri. Atthu apa awiri amphetachiyeeyo ti tuuvi?”
Simawu khujipu araka: “Kinoona yoori ti otule aswaamihiweeyo wa waattavo.” Yinsa khumuuza yoori: “Walikanisa.”
Ye khumuuza Simawu anthoonyezaka muukha otule araka: “Onimoona mwanankha otu? Miiyo kata vaje vawo apha khuhikinkhi hatha maati yoori koose moolu aka, ila ye oosa moolu aka na mishozi zawe khukukuttha na nyuuli zawe.
Khukipokhereleeni na peeju, ila ye khalikheleleeni opejari moolu aka.
Khukivaazeeni mafuttha oonukhela mmwishwa mwaka, ila otu avaaza mafuttha moolu aka.
Pi apho kiniwuuzaaye yoori twampi zawe epile za waatta ariinaazo za swaamihiwa; mwaasa woophetacha wawe. Ila otule aswaamihiweeyo vattitthiiru opheta wawe vattitthiiru.”
Yinsa khumuuza mwanankha otule yoori: “Twampi zawo za swaamihiwa.”
Apale eekhaliyeeyo khusala oozelana yoori: “Otu paani anwahaaye owaaswaamihi twampi atthu.”
Ila Yinsa khumuuza muukha otule yoori: “Waamini wawo wa wuusuru: olawe na heeri.”
Paata ya toole, Yinsa khusala eettetta sitati khwa sitati na nti khwa nti alaleyaka hapari zooshapweya zoofwalume wa Nnyizinku. Anakhiyoni awe apale khumi na awiri aari vamote na-ye,
na aakha akinoko aya apale aavonisiweeyo masheethwani na marati: Mariyamu aari wiitthiwaaye Mataleena, otule ansaruwiyeeyo masheethwani sapa,
na Zhuwaana muukha wa Kuuza, nsatoro wa Herooti, Suzaana na aakha akinoko aari ontthanttaaye Yinsa na vitthu zaya vamote na anakhiyoni awe.
Phantte za waatta za miti aari otawo atthu enkeene oteela okutthanana Yinsa. Aphano ye khulupa nlikaniso mmote araka:
“Aarivo namazala mmote aalawiiye ozala peewu zawe. Amwazaka, kinoko khukwela nshini wa tarikhi, khuluwatthiwa na khujiwa pi anyannyi.
Peewu kinoko khukwela vahali aariivo mawe, khoottha ila khuuma mwaasa woohiivo maati.
Peewu kinoko khukwela vanyiiwa, khuwula vamote na nyiiwa, khurapeliwa pi nyiiwa khufwa.
Ila peewu kinoko khukwela vanshaka wooshapweya, khuwula khwiima mishumo miiya wakhula peewu.” Alupiyeevo toole, ye khukhuwelela araka: “Ariina mashiilo ti asiile!”
Anakhiyoni awe khumuuzela maana a nlikaniso aya opule.
Yinsa khuwaajipu yoori: “Mweeyo mwenkhiwa ojuwa zootikinisa zoofwalume wa Nnyizinku, ila akinoko anuuzaniwa nlikaniso yoori oonaka ahisala ajuwa, asiilaka ehisala eweeleya.”
Maana a nlikaniso opu pi toono: peewu eti enthoonyeza nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku.
Peewu zaakweliiye ntarikhi, zinlikanisaniwa atthu apale ansiilaaye nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku ila sheethwani khulazavo varoho vaya nttakhuzi ntthile yoori ahaamini apattha wuusurukha.
Peewu epi zaakweliiye vamawe, zinlikanisaniwa atthu apale ansiilaaye nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku khupokherela na furaha. Ila mwaasa woohiina mitathaari, wakathi vattitthiiru nawootootiwa ti sheethwani anlikha waamini waya.
Peewu epi zaakweliiye vanyiiwa, zinlikanisaniwa atthu apale ansiilaaye nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku, ila mwaasa wooshukulikhela opattha tuvela na haali za meekhazi, yo waamini waya vattiitthi-vattiitthi onzima, ahifiyelelaka wiima mishumo.
Peewu epi zaakweliiye vanshaka wooshapweya, zinlikanisaniwa atthu apale ansiilaaye nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku khuthokorela nroho mwaya khushututela na khwiiyana niiya, apo aniima mishumo zooshapweya.
Khaavo ankhozaaye khantteya khufinikha na enyipo wala khupweha nlivuku. Entthiiwa vahali onooneyaavo yoori esala ewaamwasikhela apale anviraaye nnyupa.
Khayiivo envithiwaaye ehinttelaaye osaruwela oje, zooshi epile za siiri enttela wiiya payana.
Apho mwiyane ophoole wa nanna yoosiila, otule ariina ontta weekezeliwa, ila otule ahina hatha na etile anuupuwelelaaye wiiyana ontta onyakanyiwa.
Mamaawe na attwiize Yinsa khulankha yoori amoone, ila khuhisala ewaheya mwaasa yoori aarivo atthu a waatta.
Khuuziwa Yinsa yoori: “Vaje apho atavo mamaawo na attwiizo.”
Ye khuwaajipu araka: “Maama na attwiizaku pi apale ansiilaaye Nttakhuzi la Nnyizinku khushututela.”
Siikhu moote, Yinsa khuwooza anakhiyoni awe yoori: “Olawa neette phantte ya kaapu kinoko.” Khupakhira nkalawa khusala alawa.
Aphano eettaka olawa Yinsa khusala alala, khupuwa pheevo ya waatta kalawa khusala esaleela ozama.
Anakhiyoni apale khoova khusala anlansa Yinsa araka: “Mwanliimu, Mwanliimu nasaleela ozama!” Yinsa khulankha khunyamaza pheevo na mawipi, khupuwa nreke.
Nawiisha khuwoozela anakhiyoni awe yoori: “Waamini wenu ori vayi?” Yo khwiiya awoova na ooshanka khusala oozelana, araka: “Otu aya paani anrumaaye pheevo na mawipi khunshututela?”
Yinsa na anakhiyoni awe khulankha khulokhela Keraaza, kaapu ya Kalileya.
Wakathi Yinsa apakhuwiweevo nkalawa, khuta nlume mmote wa sitati ethiitile aariina masheethwani a waatta. Ye eekhaliye siikhu za waatta ahiwalaka kuwo na ahiikhalaka vaje, aari wiikhala mvilalo.
N'oomoona Yinsa khunyakula, khunkokhorela khukhuwa araka: “Onkitakhela-ni, Yinsa mwaana wa Nnyizinku Nwulu wa Pinkuuni? Safwatali ohikihukhumu.”
Ye aalupiye mattakhuzi apa mwaasa yoori Yinsa aarumiye onsaruwa masheethwani. Masheethwani apale eekhaliye siikhu za waatta mmwiili wa nlume otule. Na afukaniwaavo makwinjili khwinkhiwa atthu oomweekesela, eetta ottumulaka n'oothuuliwa pi masheethwani n'onlawana makuluttu.
Aphano Yinsa khumuuzela yoori: “Weeyo nzina lawo o paani?” Ye khujipu yoori: “Miiyo nzina laka ki omathi,” mwaasa yoori ntthu otule aamweettiye masheethwani a waatta mmwiili mwawe.
Masheethwani apale khusala anvekela Yinsa yoori ahiikarele khilintti.
Liphanko liwululene la kuluwe laari oshukisiwa vamwaako, masheethwani apale khunvekela ruhusa Yinsa yoori eette nkuluwe, ye khukhupalela.
Wakathi aliiyeemo masheethwani apale mmwiili wa nlume otule khweetta nkuluwe, aphano kuluwe khusala zitthira ziishukhela vantthatta khutupweela.
Apale aari oshukisaaye kuluwe epile nawoona vitthu epile zaarettikhaniyeezo, khutthira khulawa khulupa hapari epile nsitati mphule na miti mikinoko zaya.
Khulawa atthu a waatta olawa woona vitthu epile zaarettikhaniyeezo. Wakathi amwaattamiyeeyo Yinsa, khumoona nlume otule ansaruwiyeeyo masheethwani eekhaliye nshini wa moolu a Yinsa awaliye kuwo zawe na atthiiyemo akhili zawe, yo khwiiya awoova.
Apale ooniiyeeyo, khulawa khuwooza atthu nanna aavonisiweezo nlume otule.
Aphano atthu ooshi apale a nti opule wa Keraaza khunvekela Yinsa yoori aleemo mmuti mwaya mwaasa wa woova channu, Ye khuwela nkalawa khulaawo.
Nlume otule ansaruwiyeeyo masheethwani khusala anvekela Yinsa amuuzaka yoori anlikhe alawe vamote na-ye. Ila Yinsa khumuuza olawa araka:
“Orutele owawo wawooze atthu etile Nnyizinku ooretteliyeeyo.” Nlume otule khulankha khusala alawa owawe alaleyaka sitati yooshi etile aaretteliweeyo ti Yinsa.
Wakathi Yinsa arutiyeevo, khuntti khuluyeene ya atthu ooshi atthaapale aari onwejaaye khumpokherela na furaha.
Aphano mwinyi mmote aari wiitthiwaaye Yayiiru namalokozela wa nyuupa yoosifwiwamo Nnyizinku, khuta khunkokhorela Yinsa nshini wa moolu awe anvekelaka yoori alawe owawe,
mwaasa yoori mwanawe aariina mmote paasi wa nyaakha khumi na miwiri aari osaleela ofwa. Yinsa alawaka, atthu khusala aphunyana-phunyana.
Attaaphale khutavo muukha aariina nyaakha khumi na miwiri ari nlwele, yaari omwiittikhaaye taamu wakhula siikhu. Khuharipu nzurukhu awe wooshi aariina nkatthi wa akulukhala, ila khuhiivo mmote aawahiyeeyo onvonisa.
Ye khuta mpakha onyoko wa Yinsa khusapa ajapi yawe vattitthiiru, omuuta otthuupule khulikha wiittikha taamu etile.
Yinsa khuuzela yoori: “Paani akisapiyeeyo?” Atthu ooshi khusala akhana, Pheeturu khulupa yoori: “Mbwana, atthu pi a waatta pa yo anuuphunyaaye na wuusukhuma!”
Ila Yinsa khusala avira akhanyarelaka yoori: “Nna akisapiyeeyo keetta woona okisaruwiye owahi waka.”
Aphano muukha otule ooniyeevo yoori khaari owahi ojivitha, khuta eettaka othukumela khunkokhorela Yinsa vakatthi wa atthu ooshi khusala alupa wa nanna ansapiyeezo na avoniyeezo nasaapiru.
Attaaphale Yinsa khumuuza yoori: “Mwanankha waamini wawo woovonisa! Olawe na heeri.”
Attakhulaka etthiipile Yinsa, khuta karumeya mmote wa vaje vawe Yayiiru khumuuza yoori: “Ohimwantipu Mbwana olawa vamote na-weyo, maana mwanawo aya afwa.”
Yinsa n'oosiila khumuuza Yayiiru yoori: “Ohoove, wiiyane amini, mwanawo ontta wiiya nkumi.”
N'oofiya owawe Yayiiru, Yinsa khuhinlikhi hatha ntthu ovira nnyupa mphule, khuvira na Pheeturu, Yaahaya, Yaakhumpa, papaawe mwaana na mamaawe.
Atthu ooshi aasaliye vaje eettaka olila, Yinsa khuwooza yoori: “Mwihilile, otu khafweeni ontta olala.”
Yo khusala antheya Yinsa mwaasa wa ojuwa yoori afwa.
Ye khuntheteezela nkhono awe khumuuza yoori: “Mwaari, lankha!”
Rooho yawe khunrutela khulankha nasaapiru. Aphano Yinsa khumuuza papaawe yoori amwinkhe etthu-yoojiwa.
Papaawe na mamaawe khwiiya ooshanka, ila Yinsa khuwooza yoori mwihimuuze hatha ntthu vitthu epi zirettikhaniyeezo.
Yinsa khuwaakusanya maaswihaapa awe khumi na awiri khuwenkha owahi na ofwalume wa wiikara masheethwani a wakhula nanna na woovonisa.
Khuwaaruma olawa olaleya ofwalume wa Nnyizinku na owaavonisa alwele.
Khuwooza yoori: “Mwilawaka mwihithuule hatha etthu, wala pakhora, wala mfukho, wala phaawu, wala nzurukhu, wala ajapi yaphiiri.
Nyuupa ethiito mwinttelaaye opokhereliwa, mwimake attaapho mpakha olaavo.
Amana mwihipokhereliwi saana, mwilaakamo nsitati mwaya mpho mwitathe lifufu la mmoolu mwenu khwa oshaahiti waya yo.”
Aphano yo khulankha khusala alawa aviraka mmamiti alaleyaka hapari zooshapweya na awaavonisaka alwele wakhula phantte.
Nsatoro Herooti khusiila vitthu zaari orettikhanaazo ye khwiiya wootikinisiwa mwaasa atthu akina aari olupa yoori Yaahaya ti ye asisimuwiye muufwa.
Akina aari olupa yoori Aliyaasi ti ye awaapuweleliye, akina aari olupa yoori oto napiyu mmote wa raku eetta osisimuwa.
Ila Herooti khulupa yoori: “Yaahaya miiyo kaarumiye yoori ashijiwe, khi oto kininsiilaaye alupiwaka na anrettaaye vitthu epo ti paani?” Khusala atakhacha yoori amoone.
Maaswihaapa apale n'ooruti khumuuza Yinsa zooshi aarettaziyeezo. Aphano, ye khuwaathuula khusala alawa sitati moote yaari wiitthiwaaye Betesayita.
Ila khuntti ya atthu n'oojuwa khusala anlotta. Ye khuwaapokherela khusala awooza monkoni woofwalume wa Nnyizinku na awaavonisaka apale aari ohithajiyaaye ovonisiwa.
Njuwa leettelaka oveva, apale khumi na awiri khumwaattama Yinsa khumuuza yoori: “Owooze atthu apa alawe mmamiti mpho amake eekesaka etthu-yoojiwa, maana mphu niriimo makuluttu.”
Ye khuwaajipu yoori: “Mweeyeena mwiwenkhe etthu-yoojiwa.” Yo khunjipu araka: “Niriinaaye apha, phaawu thaanu na swi piiri paasi, woohiiyi olawa wuuzanya etthu-yoojiwa khiniwaafiyela atthu ooshi apa.”
Alume aariivo aari etthu ya alufu thaanu, ila ye khuwooza anakhiyoni awe yoori: “Mwiweekhaze atthu hamusiini wakhula khuntti.”
Yo khuretta etthiipo khuweekhaza ooshi.
Khuthuula phaawu thaanu na swi epile piiri khweekesa otulu, khuparikhiya khumeya khuwenkha anakhiyoni awe yoori awaawanyeze atthu apale.
Ooshi khuja khurupala, epile zaasaliiye khulokottheliwa khwiitaala khelenke khumi na piiri.
Siikhu moote, Yinsa eetta olompa otthwe, anakhiyoni awe ari kharipu, nawiisha khuwoozela yoori: “Atthu anri miiyo ki paani?”
Yo khunjipu yoori: “Akina anri weeyo o Yaahaya Namoosa, akina Aliyaasi, akina theenya anlupa yoori weeyo o napiyu mmote wa raku weetta osisimuwa.”
“Khi mweeyo mwinri ki paani?” Pheeturu khujipu araka: “Weeyo o Al-Masiihu wa Nnyizinku.”
Yinsa khuwaahirimiza yoori vitthu epile ahimuuze hatha ntthu.
Khuwooza araka: “Mwaana wa Pinaatamu ona yoohoowa nkatthi wa vitthu za waatta na okatthaliwa pi anamalokozela a tiini na attunkhulu a mahaakhimu a tiini mpakha anamanozela a kano; onlawa afwe, siikhu yattaatthu asisimuwe.”
Khuvira awoozaka atthu ooshi yoori: “Nkhama ntthu atakha okilotta miiyo, ona yoojikatthala mwennyewe, khuvikela nsalapa awe wakhula siikhu khusala akilotta.
Amana ntthu atakha wuusuru ohaayi awe, ontta ompwetheya; ila otule onimpwetheyaaye ohaayi awe mwaasa wa miiyo, oto onteela wuusurukha.
Ona fwayita-ni ntthu opattha vitthu zooshi z'oolumwenku, ila khujipwetecha ama khujitapanya mwennyeweru?
Otule anikoonelaaye haaya miiyo na mattakhuzi aka, na Mwaana wa Pinaatamu onteela omoonela haaya mmana ataaka nnuuru mwawe na nnuuru wa Paapa na malayikha oottakatthiifu.
Kiniwuuzani khweele yoori awaapo apha akina ahinteelaaye ofwa mpakha oone ofwalume wa Nnyizinku.”
Ziviriyeevo etthu ya siikhu naane paata yoolupa mattakhuzi apale, Yinsa khunthuula Pheeturu, Yaahaya na Yaakhumpa, Ye khuwela vamwaako olawa olompa.
Alompaka etthiipile omaasho wawe khuzukuluwawo, kuwo zawe khwiiya zoolakala na za waara nkhama ozerima.
Nasaapiru khumpuwelela atthu awiri khusala attakhulana, aari Munsa na Aliyaasi.
Aatiiye nnuuru ya pinkuuni khusala amuuza Yinsa khwa nanna aari weettelaazo ohoowa na ofwa Yeruzaleemu nkhama etthiipo Nnyizinku asharutheliyeeyo.
Pheeturu na ashirikha awe aarettiye eettaka olala, wakathi asisimuwiyeevo khoona nuuru ya Yinsa na atthu awiri amweemeleliye.
Atthu apale eettaka olawa Pheeturu khumuuza Yinsa yoori: “Mwanliimu, ti yooshapweya wiikhala attaapha! Nintta ojeka mapantta mattatthu, limote laawo, limote la Munsa, na limote la Aliyaasi.” Pheeturu khaari ojuwa etthu aari ottakhulaaye.
Attakhulaka etthiipile, khuta liwiku khuwaafinikha, anakhiyoni apale khwiiya awoova wakathi ooniyeevo liwiku liwaafinikhaka atthu apale.
Mmawiku mphule khupuwamo huula yaari oraaye: “Otu mwanaka woothawuliwa; mwinsiileze etile anlupaaye.”
Paata yoonyamala huula etile Yinsa khusalavo otthwe. Siikhu zaya epile anakhiyoni apale khwiiya oonyamala, khuhimuuzi hatha ntthu vitthu epile ooniyeezo.
Mmeesho mwaya nawiishukha vamwaako, khuta khuntti ya atthu a waatta oteela okutthanana Yinsa.
Vakatthi wa khuntti ya atthu atthaapale khupuwavo mwinyi aari okhuwaaye araka: “Mwanliimu, kinuuvekela yoori wamoone mwanaka, maana kina mmote othuuto paasi.
Sheethwani eetta onvelavelisa khusala anthukumelisa, onnyakulisa na onkwisela vathi n'oolaza maphovu, khaninlikha ahinvulaliseeni.
Kaawaavekeliye anakhiyoni awo yoori amwiikare sheethwani aya oto, yo khumoojeela.”
Yinsa khujipu araka: “Oo! Atthu oohaamini na ootakhala rooho! Mpakha lini kiiyaka vamote na-mweyo na kuuvilelakani? Ontiise apha mwanawo aya oto.”
